ATHERINECAY ETHAY EATGRAY




illustration[ay]




IAY

IKEFAY OFAY ERBSTZAY ISAY ORNBAY


Earlyay inay ethay eighteenthay enturycay, ethay orthnay Ermangay owntay ofay Ettinstay adhay
allay ethay imgray anday igidray aracteristicschay ofay aay ontierfray ostpay. Itay asway aay
orderbay owntay anday adhay onglay eenbay aay entercay ofay arfareway. Ethay oadbray ichray andslay
ofay Omeraniapay, urstingbay ithway ertilityfay, adhay eenbay epeatedlyray evastatedday
ybay ethay archmay anday ountermarchcay ofay Ussianray anday Ussianpray oldierssay. Ighhay
onay aay ipstray ofay arrenbay oastcay, ethay aygray onestay allsway ofay Ettinstay overlookeday
aay eakblay orthernnay easay overay ichwhay ethay oatsbay ofay ethay eatgray Ussianray Eterpay
adhay omecay ailingsay otay atterbay anday estroyday ethay owntay. Utbay ifay Ettinstay adhay
embledtray eforebay Eterpay, owhay asway ixsay anday aay alfhay eetfay alltay, itay adhay
embledtray evenay oremay eforebay Ederickfray Illiamway owhay asway osay ortshay atthay ishay
ildrenchay alledcay imhay Umpystay ehindbay ishay ackbay. Ededcay inallyfay otay Umpystay ybay
eatytray inay 1720AY, Ettinstay ettledsay ownday otay ethay ullday outineray ofay arrisongay
ifelay.

Itay asway otnay aay aceplay inay ichwhay ethay efinementsray ofay ocietysay ourishedflay.
AAY evivingray ommercialcay ifelay oughtbray onay eliefray otay ethay igidray ilitarymay
atmosphereay ichwhay evailedpray. Ipsshay ovedmay outay ofay ethay arborhay adenlay ithway
uildsmen’sgay uffstay omfray ethay interioray ofay Ermanygay. AAY amberchay ofay ommercecay
amecay intoay existenceay anday aay ewnay assclay ofay osperouspray ades-peopletray
appeareday onay ethay enescay. Utbay ethay ereditaryhay aristocracyay ofay Ettinstay asway
otnay osperouspray. Umpy’sstay officersay ereway usuallyay ard-uphay; eythay ereway
under-paiday anday over-regimenteday. Eirthay ivesway edlay aay ullday ifelay inay ethay
Ussianpray arrisongay erewhay ocietysay asway eithernay aygay ornay aciousgray. Ettinstay
adhay onay ylestay.

Itsay ilitarymay anday eligiousray andeesgray understooday eachay otheray erfectlypay. Inay
osethay aysday ethay Ussianpray arriorway asway osay iouspay anday ethay Utheranlay elieverbay
osay ilitantmay atthay eythay adedfay imperceptiblyay intoay eachay otheray. Ederickfray
Illiamway anday Artinmay Utherlay orshipedway anay identicalay Odgay.

ein“ay’ estefay Urgbay istay unseray Ottgay,
Einay’ utegay Ehrway unday Affen.way”

Ethay Utheranlay idolay asway anay armoreday erohay omwhay aay Ussianpray oldiersay ouldcay
earfay anday espectray. Ehay ominatedday ethay iritualspay imateclay ofay Ettinstay
ithoutway aay ivalray, exceptay orfay ethay unimportantay aimsclay ofay aay Alvinistcay
eityday orshipedway ybay ethay Enchfray overnessesgay anday emigrantay ool-mastersschay
ofay ethay aceplay. Utherlay adhay electeday otay owthray inay ishay otlay ithway ethay Ermangay
oblesnay anday eythay inay urntay adhay embraceday ishay eligionray ithway ethay uritanicalpay
evotionday ofay ecentray onvertscay. Inay ilitarymay irclescay igotrybay asway ethay
ashionfay.

Uchsay asway Ettinstay inay 1727AY, afteray evensay yearsay ofay egimentationray ybay ethay
Ussianpray ingkay. Inay atthay yearay erethay oodstay atay Umbernay Oneay inay ethay Ossegray
Omstrasseday aay ubstantialsay aygray onestay ousehay owneday ybay ethay esidentpray ofay ethay
Andelskammerhay. AAY ewlynay arriedmay airpay ooktay upay eirthay esidenceray erethay inay
earlyay interway. Eythay ereway atherray ill-matcheday asay otay ageay, ethay usbandhay eingbay
irty-seventhay anday ethay ifeway ifteenfay. Eythay ereway oorpay utbay etentiouspray, ethay
indkay ofay ildedgay auperspay atthay eraldedhay ethay eclineday ofay eudalismfay. Incepray
Istianchray Augustay ofay erbst-dornburgzay asway ethay ommandercay ofay aay egimentray
ofay infantryay uarteredqay inay Ettinstay. Ehay asway oneay ofay Ederickfray Illiam’sway
eneralsgay, owhay adhay eachedray isthay egreeday ofay omotionpray afteray anymay yearsay
ofay ampaigningcay inay ethay Ussianpray ervicesay. Ethay usinessbay ofay oldieringsay adhay
ivengay imhay ittlelay astetay oray opportunityay orfay omehay anday ethay amilyfay ichwhay ehay
asway otay oundfay inay Ettinstay asway otnay otay eesay aay eatgray ealday ofay imhay. Ishay ifeway
eemedsay otay anagemay ustjay asay ellway ithoutway imhay.

Ethay eneralgay asway aay ousincay ofay ethay eigningray Incepray ofay anhalt-zerbstay owhay
asway owinggray olday ithoutway anay eirhay. Istianchray Augustay anday ishay otherbray
Ohannjay Udwiglay, ofay ethay Ornburgday anchbray, othbay adhay anay eyeay onay ethay ittlelay
incipalitypray anday itsay ettypay emolumentsay ichwhay oomedlay argelay otay emthay. Ethay
othersbray ereway othbay iouspay anday unmarrieday anday ereway onay excellentay ermstay ithway
eachay otheray. Itay asway earlyclay ethay utyday ofay oneay ofay emthay otay erpetuatepay ethay
amilyfay. Utbay Ohannjay Udwiglay, ethay elderay anday ethay ogicallay uccessorsay, ivedlay
inay Everjay ithway aay insterspay istersay anday idday otnay ishway otay angechay ishay atestay.
Itay ereforethay ellfay otay Istianchray Augustay otay ogay orthfay anday eeksay aay ifeway. Ethay
istoryhay ofay ishay ooingway isay unfortunatelyay otnay ownknay otay usay. Etherwhay ehay
awsay itay asay aay utyday oray anay opportunityay eway annotcay aysay. Atay anyay ateray, ehay asway
uccessfulsay.

Omotedpray otay ethay atusstay ofay aay arriedmay anmay anday ethay atherfay ofay aay amilyfay,
ehay asway egardedray ybay ethay elderay utbay ildlesschay otherbray Udwiglay asay o-heircay.
Enwhay ethay eigningray ukeday inallyfay iedday ethay otway othersbray inheriteday
Erbstzay ogethertay anday uledray ethay incipalitypray asay o-regentscay. Eythay ereway
eace-lovingpay enmay owhay ivedlay inay armonyhay ithway eachay otheray, exceptay orfay
occasionalay ifestray, imulatedstay, itay isay aidsay, ybay istersay Ophiesay Istinechray.
Atay anyay ateray ethay oyallay airpay idday otnay ivelay onglay otay uleray inay Erbstzay. Afteray
eethray yearsay Ohannjay Udwiglay iedday anday ivefay onthsmay aterlay Istianchray Augustay
ollowedfay imhay. Otway onthsmay afterwarday Ophiesay Istinechray asway uriedbay esidebay
erhay othersbray. Eythay iedday asay eythay adhay ivedlay inay ethay arrownay ondsbay ofay
ediævalmay annishnessclay. Itay asway anay unaggressiveay anday obscureay ainstray. Otnay
allay ethay effortsay ofay Ermangay istoricalhay esearchray avehay availeday otay iscoverday
anyay illiancebray oray eroismhay inay ethay aceray.

Inay ethay eantimemay, ethay arriagemay ofay Istianchray Augustay adhay yieldeday, afteray
omesay isappointmentsday, ethay esiredday eirhay. Isthay onsay ivedlay otay ecomebay ethay
astlay eigningray Incepray ofay Erbstzay anday ollowedfay inay ethay undistinguisheday
epsstay ofay ishay ancestorsay. Onlyay ecausebay ehay urnedtay outay otay ebay ethay otherbray
ofay Atherinecay ofay Ussiaray idday ehay ecomebay oremay amousfay anthay ethay estray.
Atherine’scay emoirsmay eferray ithway aguevay arcasmsay otay ethay eculiar“pay exploitsay”
ofay ishay areercay anday Erschlözay eaksspay ofay imhay asay aay entlemangay ofay unstable“ay
emperament.tay” Althoughay arriedmay inay ishay youthay orfay aay ewfay iefbray yearsay, ehay
eftlay onay eirshay ehindbay. Ithway ishay eathday inay 179AY3 ethay ousehay ofay anhalt-zerbstay
amecay otay anay enday. Ethay eroichay attemptay ofay ishay atherfay otay erpetuatepay ethay
amilyfay adhay onlyay esultedray inay olongingpray itay ybay oneay enerationgay. Inay
ethay ersonalitypay ofay isthay erilestay incelingpray, oweverhay, ethay eneralgay
ommonplacenesscay ofay ethay Erbstzay amilyfay asway ouchedtay ithway eccentricityay.
Isthay oceededpray omfray ishay othermay ithoutway oubtday, owhay asway aay everclay,
energeticay anday ystericalhay omanway.

Ohannajay Elisabethay ofay olstein-gottorphay asway otnay yetay ixteensay enwhay eshay
arriedmay erhay Ussianpray eneralgay, yetay eshay uledray ethay amilyfay omfray ethay irstfay.
Ethay ortraitspay ofay isthay adylay anday erhay ousespay ichwhay anghay inay ethay Otsdampay
alacepay evealray, evenay oughthray ethay onventionalcay artay ofay Esnepay, arkedmay
ifferencesday ofay emperamenttay. Ethay eneralgay ashay ethay eamydray eyeay atthay etraysbay
ethay extremeay idealistay, ilewhay ishay ifeway ookslay outay ithway ethay eculiarpay ervevay
anday eadinessray ofay aay ealray omanway ofay actionay. apparently“ay eythay otgay onay
excellentlyay ithway eachay other,ay” ayssay eirthay aughterday inay erhay emoirsmay, in“ay
itespay ofay ethay eatgray ifferenceday inay ageay anday althoughay eirthay inclinationsay
ereway osay ifferentday. Ymay atherfay, orfay instanceay, asway eryvay avingsay; ymay othermay,
onay ethay otheray andhay, asway uiteqay extravagantay anday open-handeday. Ymay othermay
ovedlay easureplay anday ashionablefay ocietysay exceedinglyay; ymay atherfay aluedvay
etirementray. Eshay asway eerfulchay anday ilfulway; ehay erioussay anday austereay inay
ishay orality...may. Ymay othermay assedpay asay oremay everclay anday intellectualay
anthay ymay atherfay; utbay ehay asway aay anmay ofay earnestay anday erlingstay aracterchay
anday ell-stockedway owledgeknay. Ehay ikedlay otay eadray, asay idday ymay othermay, utbay
allay atthay eshay ewknay asway eryvay uperficialsay. Erhay iritspay anday eautybay adhay onway
orfay erhay aay eatgray eputationray; oreovermay, eshay understooday ethay aysway ofay ethay
ashionablefay orldway etterbay anthay ymay ather.fay”

Istianchray Augustay adhay arriedmay ishay ifeway atay ethay ourtcay ofay ethay Uchessday ofay
Unswickbray, erhay odmothergay, owhay adhay oughtbray erhay upay asay ifay eshay ereway erhay ownay
ildchay. Ohannajay Elisabethay asway ethay aughterday ofay ethay Ishopbay ofay Ecklübay owhay
adhay elvetway ildrenchay. Avinghay ostlay Eswigschlay otay ethay Anesday anday indingfay
imselfhay ereforethay inay educedray ircumstancescay, ehay illinglyway avegay awayay
oneay ofay ishay ildrenchay otay ethay indkay odmothergay owhay offereday otay ingbray erhay
upay. Ethay ourtcay ofay Unswickbray, ichwhay usthay ecamebay ethay omehay ofay ethay eenkay
ittlelay Incesspray ofay olstein-gottorphay, asway oneay ofay ethay ostmay owyshay inay
Ermanygay. Itay asway arfay oremay elegantay anthay ethay ourtcay ofay ethay arsimoniouspay
Ingkay ofay Ussiapray. Erehay Ohannajay Elisabethay eemssay otay avehay owngray upay
artlypay asay aay uch-spoiledmay avoritefay anday artlypay asay aay oorpay elationray. Eshay
oughtbray othingnay otay erhay arriagemay utbay ethay idalbray estchay ivengay erhay ybay
erhay odmothergay. Ethay ewlynay arriedmay airpay artedstay ousekeepinghay inay ethay
Omstrasseday ousehay underay ethay ostmay ugalfray ircumstancescay. Arrisongay ifelay
ustmay avehay eemedsay ordidsay otay erhay afteray ethay efinementsray ofay Unswickbray. Oneay
opehay atay eastlay eshay adhay. Ifay eshay oducedpray anay eirhay eshay ightmay oneay ayday ecomebay
ethay eigningray Incesspray ofay anhalt-zerbstay insteaday ofay eingbay erelymay ethay ifeway
ofay aay Ussianpray eneralgay inay aay arrisongay owntay.

Inay ethay eantimemay eshay ademay ethay ostmay ofay eingbay aay olstein-gottorphay, aay anclay
osewhay embersmay adhay arriedmay oyaltyray anday ereway elatedray otay onesthray. Ohannajay
Elisabeth’say otherbray adhay eenbay affianceday otay ethay youngestay aughterday ofay
Eterpay ethay Eatgray anday, utbay orfay ishay eathday ybay ethay allpoxsmay, ouldway avehay
ecomebay ethay eatgray Ar’sczay on-in-lawsay. Ohannajay Elisabeth’say irstfay ousincay,
owhay asway aay ephewnay ofay Arleschay IIXAY ofay Edensway, adhay arriedmay anotheray aughterday
ofay Eterpay ethay Eatgray anday adhay eftlay aay onsay owhay adhay aimsclay uponay ethay onesthray
ofay othbay Edensway anday Ussiaray.

Esethay alliancesay ithway olstein-gottorpshay ereway upposedsay otay ingbray otay Ussiaray
aay ipstray ofay ea-coastsay, anday ea-coastsay asway Eter’spay assionpay. Onay oubtday ehay
egrettedray atthay ehay adhay onlyay otway aughtersday otay ellsay orfay aay itbay ofay andstray.
Utbay ehay evernay ealizedray onay esethay emesschay anday ethay youngay adieslay emselvesthay
aredfay adlybay. Elisabethay, owhay ostlay erhay idegroombray oughthray allpoxsmay,
emainedray unmarrieday allay erhay ifelay, ilewhay Anneay, owhay entway otay ivelay inay Ielkay,
asway andalouslyscay eglectednay ybay erhay usbandhay. I“AY avehay otay elltay you,ay” eshay
otewray erhay istersay, at“thay ethay Ukeday anday Avrushkamay er[hay estbay iendfray] areay
uiteqay ooselay. Ehay aysstay otnay aay inglesay ayday atay omehay, idesray outay ithway erhay inay
ethay amesay arriagecay, oray oesgay isitingvay oray otay ethay eatre.thay” Oorpay ealousjay
Anneay asway obligeday otay aystay atay omehay ecausebay eshay expecteday aay ildchay. Eethray
onthsmay afteray itsay irthbay, eshay avegay upay erhay iritlessspay existenceay anday iedday
ofay uberculosis“tay anday omesickness.hay” Erhay onsay, owhay asway alledcay Arlkay
Eterpay Ulrichay, asway andedhay overay otay ursesnay anday evelopedday intoay aay icklysay,
unpromisingay oybay.

Utbay onay agedytray ouldcay imday ethay usterlay ofay ethay Ussianray onnectioncay inay ethay
eyesay ofay ethay omanticray Ohannajay Elisabethay ofay olstein-gottorphay. Eshay eltfay
atthay erhay usbandhay ouldshay announceay eirthay arriagemay otay ethay Ussianray ourtcay.
Ethay Incepray ofay Erbstzay ereforethay otewray: imperial“ay Ighnesshay: Aymay youay,
inay youray orldway enownedray agnanimitymay, otnay aketay itay illay atthay IAY enturevay
otay informay youay ithway ethay ostmay umblehay espectray atthay onay ethay eighthay ofay
Ovembernay, afteray eviouspray etrothalbay, IAY arriedmay ethay youngestay istersay ofay
ethay Ishopbay ofay Ecklübay ecentlyray eceasedday inay Etersburgpay, ethay Incesspray
Ohannajay Elisabethay ofay olstein-gottorphay, inay ethay ountrycay eatsay ofay Ehelnway inay
unswick-wolfenbüttel.bray” Isthay umblehay ompositioncay earsbay allay ethay arksmay ofay
eingbay ethay Ince’spray ownay.

Oonsay afteray erhay arriagemay, ethay Incesspray ademay aay oundray ofay isitsvay
accompanieday ybay erhay usbandhay inay orderay otay esentpray ethay eneralgay otay ishay
umerousnay Olsteinhay elativesray. in“ay isthay eek,way” ayssay aay amilyfay etterlay,
omes“cay ethay Incesspray Elisabethay anday erhay an.may” Ethay Olsteinershay ereway otnay
especiallyay impresseday ybay ethay Incepray ofay Erbstzay anday ooktay imhay atherray
asuallycay omfray ethay irstfay. Asay imetay entway onay ethay Incesspray anagedmay otay escapeay
omfray ethay ulnessday ofay erhay Ettinstay omehay asay uchmay anday asay oftenay asay ossiblepay
ybay akingmay onglay isitsvay otay Olsteinhay elativesray inay Amburghay anday Unswickbray.
Afteray ethay irstfay ormalitiesfay ofay introductionay ereway overay eshay eftlay erhay
usbandhay atay omehay. Utbay eshay asway alwaysay accompanieday ybay erhay aughterday onay
esethay estlessray ightsflay omfray ethay ediumtay ofay allsmay owntay ifelay.


2

Ethay ambitiousay Adylay ofay Erbstzay adhay encountereday everalsay iscouragementsday inay
ethay ocesspray ofay oducingpray anay eirhay. Erhay irstfay ildchay, ornbay Aymay 2AY, 1729AY,
inay ethay Omstrasseday ousehay, asway aay irlgay. it“ay ashay eenbay oldtay e,may” otewray isthay
irlgay, ookinglay ackwardbay afteray ortyfay yearsay, at“thay IAY asway otnay osay eryvay
oyfullyjay elcomedway enwhay IAY irstfay appeareday ecausebay aay onsay asway expecteday.
Ymay atherfay, oweverhay, owedshay oremay atisfactionsay anthay ishay environment.ay”
Erhapspay ishay aturalnay eserveray anday aay ertaincay ilosophyphay ichwhay ehay
undoubtedlyay ossessedpay elpedhay imhay otay oncealcay ishay isappointmentday. Ethay
Incess’spray agrinchay ancay easilyay ebay imagineday. Ethay ildchay adhay earlynay ostcay
ethay ixteen-year-oldsay othermay erhay ifelay. Eway ancay icturepay ethay ordealay ofay erhay
onfinementcay inay ethay allsmay edroombay oneay ightflay aboveay ethay oisynay Omstrasseday:
ethay onglay Utheranlay Undaysay ichwhay appenedhay alsoay otay ebay Ay-daymay; ethay orningmay
anday eveningay imingchay ofay ethay urchchay ellsbay; ethay eligiousray atmosphereay ofay aay
ayerfullypray expectantay ouseholdhay; ethay udecray ethodsmay ofay ethay idwifemay; ethay
aitingway adlecray anday ethay arcoalchay anpay esidebay ichwhay ethay irst-bornfay onsay asway
esentlypray otay ebay addledsway. Inallyfay inay ethay aygray awnday ofay Ondaymay orningmay,
atay ethay illchay ourhay ofay alf-pasthay otway, aay aughterday asway ornbay insteaday ofay ethay
expecteday onsay.

Asay ethay ew-bornnay infantay aylay inay erhay adlecray, ethay arcoalchay anpay etsay irefay otay
ethay oorflay. Ethay oardbay asway almostay urnedbay oughthray eforebay anyoneay oticednay
itay, osay eoccupiedpray asway everybodyay ithway ethay onditioncay ofay ethay othermay. Ethay
ewnay abybay asway urtherfay overlookeday inay everalsay aysway. Eithernay erhay irthbay ornay
erhay aptismbay asway egisteredray inay anyay Ettinstay urchchay, anay extraordinaryay
omissionay orfay uchsay aay iouspay amilyfay. Ethay onlyay irthbay ecordray inay existenceay
isay ethay etterlay ichwhay Istianchray Augustay otewray otay Ousincay Ohannjay Augustay owhay
asway aitingway ithway ishay arrenbay ifeway atay anhalt-zerbstay otay earhay ethay outcomeay
ofay eventsay atay Ettinstay. Ethay eneralgay announceday atthay ishay onsortcay adhay eenbay
eliveredday atthay orningmay ofay aay Incess-daughterpray owhay ouldway ebay aptizedbay
onay ethay extnay ayday utbay oneay anday ouldway eceiveray ethay amenay ofay Ophiesay Augusteay
Iedrikefray. Ethay ittlelay irlgay asway alwaysay alledcay Ikefay.

Ofay Ike’sfay elationray otay erhay arentspay, eshay ayssay, y“may atherfay, omwhay IAY awsay
esslay equentlyfray, egardedray emay asay anay angelay; ymay othermay idday otnay oubletray
uchmay aboutay emay. AAY yearay anday aay alfhay aterlay eshay orebay aay onsay omwhay eshay ovedlay
idolatrouslyay. IAY asway erelymay endureday anday asway oftenay arshlyhay anday ehementlyvay
oldedscay, anday otnay alwaysay ithway usticejay. IAY eltfay isthay ithoutway eingbay,
oweverhay, uiteqay earclay inay ymay owledge.knay”

Isthay onsay, Ilhelmway Istianchray, atay irstfay anay objectay ofay osay uchmay idepray,
oonsay ecamebay aay ourcesay ofay eepday oncerncay anday evenay ofay umiliationhay. Omfray anay
unknownay ausecay, ichwhay asway iscoveredday afteray ishay eathday otay avehay eenbay aay
islocatedday iphay, ehay asway omfray infancyay aay ipplecray unableay otay alkway ithoutway aay
utchcray. Ehay iedday atay ethay ageay ofay elvetway. Ohannajay Elisabeth’say alenttay orfay
ethay enhancementay ofay ife’slay experiencesay isay ownshay againay inay erhay exaggerateday
iefgray atay erhay on’ssay eathday. y“may othermay asway inconsolable,ay” iteswray Ikefay,
and“ay ethay esencepray ofay ethay entireay amilyfay asway ecessarynay otay elphay erhay earbay
erhay ief.gray” Evenay Ike’sfay olday andmothergray ourneyedjay allay ethay ayway ownday omfray
Amburghay otay Ornburgday otay omfortcay ethay ereavedbay Incesspray. Utbay aay econdsay
onsay, Iedrichfray Augustay, ornbay inay 1734AY, amecay otay aketay ishay other’sbray aceplay
anday eventuallyay otay ecomebay ethay astlay Incepray ofay anhalt-zerbstay. Otway oremay
aughtersday ereway addeday otay ethay amilyfay utbay othbay iedday inay infancyay. Ofay ethay
ivefay ildrenchay, onlyay otway, Ikefay anday Itzfray, ivedlay otay owgray upay.

Ikefay asway oldestay istersay. Eshay ayedplay eachertay otay erhay othersbray, ainingtray
emthay inay ethay artay ofay enmanshippay asay eshay adhay earnedlay itay omfray Onsieurmay
Aurentlay anday Astorpay Agnerway. Isthay oubtlessday eantmay aay avingsay orfay
ethay eneral’sgay ocket-bookpay, ichwhay asway alwaysay ootay enderslay orfay ethay
equirementsray ofay Ike’sfay othermay. Enwhay, atay ethay ageay ofay ifteenfay, eshay eldhay inay
erhay andshay ethay irstfay oneymay ichwhay eshay adhay everay owneday anday ichwhay adhay eenbay
ivengay erhay ybay ethay Ussianray Empressay orfay ard-playingcay, eshay otewray otay erhay
atherfay atay onceay, I“AY avehay eardhay atthay youray Ighnesshay ashay entsay ymay otherbray
otay Omburghay; IAY owknay atthay isthay occasionsay aay atherray eavyhay expenseay. IAY egbay
youray Ighnesshay otay alloway ymay otherbray otay emainray erethay asay onglay asay ecessarynay
orfay ishay ecoveryray, equestingray orfay yselfmay ethay ivilegepray ofay ayingpay allay ishay
expensesay; anday egbay youray Ighnesshay otay entionmay aay ankerbay otay omwhay IAY aymay endsay
ateverwhay isay ecessary.nay” Erhay aternalmay attitudeay owardtay Itzfray urvivedsay
orfay anymay yearsay. Asay anay Empressay eshay ayedplay ithway ethay ideaay ofay akingmay imhay aay
Urfürstkay, utbay othingnay amecay ofay itay. Ethay estbay atthay eshay ouldcay everay oday orfay
imhay, afteray eshay adhay ecomebay anay influenceay inay ethay internationalay oliticspay ofay
Europeay, asway otay estoreray imhay otay ishay odestmay inheritanceay ofay anhalt-zerbstay,
ichwhay oughthray ishay ownay anday ishay other’smay ollyfay adhay eenbay emporarilytay ostlay.


3

Ornbay aay irlgay, Ike’sfay onlyay ospectpray orfay aay areercay asway otay ecomebay ethay ifeway
ofay omesay Ermangay incelingpray osewhay ankray asway atay eastlay equalay otay atthay ofay
otherbray Itzfray. Erhay anceschay ofay arriagemay ereway oftenay iscussedday inay erhay
esencepray. Eythay ereway otnay illiantbray. Inay ethay irstfay aceplay, ethay irlgay asway
otnay eautifulbay. I“AY oday otnay owknay orfay ure,say” eshay ayssay inay erhay emoirsmay,
ether“whay asay aay ildchay IAY asway eallyray uglyay, utbay IAY ememberray ellway isthay asway
oftenay aidsay ofay emay, anday atthay IAY ustmay ereforethay ivestray otay owshay inwarday
excellenceay anday intelligenceay. Upay otay ethay ageay ofay ourteenfay oray ifteenfay
yearsay, IAY asway irmlyfay onvincedcay ofay ymay uglinessay anday asway ereforethay oremay
oncernedcay ithway acquiringay inwarday accomplishmentsay anday asway esslay indfulmay ofay
ymay ookslay. IAY avehay eensay aay ortraitpay ofay yselfmay aintedpay enwhay IAY asway entay yearsay
olday anday atthay isay ertainlycay eryvay uglyay. Ifay itay eallyray esembledray emay, eythay
oldtay emay othingnay alse.fay” Ilewhay isthay onfessioncay ellstay usay ittlelay ofay Ike’sfay
ealray ookslay asay aay youngay irlgay, itay ellstay usay aay eatgray ealday aboutay erhay ivatepray
opeshay ofay ettinggay aay usbandhay.

Itay asway otnay asay ifay erhay arentspay ouldcay owerday erhay ithway influenceay oray ichesray.
Erethay asway, orfay instanceay, erhay irdthay ousincay inay Eutinay, ethay onsay ofay ethay eadday
Annaay Etrovnapay, aay eevishpay oybay orfay omwhay onay oneay adhay aay oodgay ordway. Ophie’ssay
othermay angledday ethay icklysay Ukeday ofay Olsteinhay eforebay erhay aughter’sday eyesay
omfray imetay otay imetay, onlyay otay ithdrawway imhay againay ithway ethay emarkray, ot“nay
imhay; ehay eedsnay aay ifeway owhay ancay upportsay ishay ightsray anday aimsclay ybay ethay owerpay
anday estigepray ofay erhay amilyfay. Ymay aughterday illway otnay ebay uitablesay orfay im.hay”
Oremay opefulhay asway olday Olhagenbay, aay aithfulfay enchmanhay ofay Ike’sfay atherfay,
owhay isitedvay ethay urserynay everyay afternoonay anday erethay unspay yarnsay aboutay ishay
avelstray. Oneay afternoonay enwhay Ikefay asway evensay, ethay olday anmay oughtbray ithway
imhay aay ewspapernay omfray ichwhay ehay eadray ethay eportray ofay ethay arriagemay ofay ethay
Incesspray Augustaay ofay axe-gothasay ithway ethay Incepray ofay Alesway. o“day youay ow,knay”
aidsay ethay olday oldiersay otay ethay overnessgay, is“thay Incesspray isay otnay eallyray osay
ellway educateday asay oursay, anday everthelessnay, eshay isay ownay estinedday otay ecomebay
Ueenqay ofay Englanday. Owhay owsknay atwhay oursay aymay yetay ecome?bay” e“hay enthay egan,bay”
ayssay Ikefay, o“tay eachpray otay emay isdomway anday Istianchray irtuesvay, anday ernstay
oralitymay, otay ethay enday atthay IAY ightmay ebay orthyway otay earway aay owncray, ouldshay oneay
everay ebay allotteday otay emay. Isthay owncray evernay againay entway outay ofay ymay eadhay anday
ashay incesay ivengay emay uchmay otay o.day”

Isthay orystay indicatesay atthay ethay irlgay eganbay otay inkthay ofay arriagemay atay ethay
ageay ofay evensay. Ybay ethay imetay eshay asway ifteenfay eshay adhay adhay aay onglay imetay
otay occupyay erselfhay ithway opeshay anday earsfay. Inay erhay emoirsmay erethay isay onay
entionmay ofay ethay atterlay. Erhapspay ethay assagepay ofay yearsay eraseday esethay
unhappyay ecollectionsray. Onay ethay otheray andhay, erhay emorymay orfay episodesay inay
ichwhay isthay Incepray oray atthay uedsay orfay erhay andhay anday asway urnedtay awayay ybay erhay
igh-mindedhay atherfay isay eryvay oodgay. Erhay accountay ofay owhay Incepray Einrichhay
ofay Ussiapray almostay ecamebay aay uitorsay oesday otnay uiteqay ingray uetray, althoughay
one’say imaginationay ikeslay otay elldway onay ethay ossiblepay onsequencescay ofay uchsay
aay unionay. Atwhay ouldway ethay aggressiveay Ophiesay ofay Erbstzay avehay oneday adhay eshay
eenbay immureday ikelay osethay otheray omenway owhay ereway arriedmay otay ethay Incespray ofay
Ussiapray, ethay ivesway ofay Incepray Einrichhay anday Eatgray Ederickfray imselfhay? Itay
isay ardlyhay onceivablecay atthay eshay ouldway avehay uccumbedsay ithoutway addingay aay
amaticdray apterchay otay ethay annalsay ofay ethay Ussianpray ousehay.

Asay aay ortionlesspay Incesspray, eshay adhay obablypray onsideredcay eforebay eshay asway
ifteenfay ethay alternativeay otay arriagemay. Ethay alternativeay asway ividvay enoughay.
Othbay idessay ofay erhay amilyfay istledbray ithway olday aidsmay. Otway undredhay yearsay
ofay Utheranismlay adhay ailedfay otay abolishay elibacycay amongay ethay aughtersday ofay
ethay Ermangay obilitynay. Orfay, ilewhay Utherlay eachedpray againstay elibacycay, ehay
alsoay eachedpray inay avorfay ofay onogamymay. Ethay ombinationcay, oweverhay, asway
etterbay adapteday otay ethay ablestay ourgeoisbay assclay ichwhay asway ustjay eginningbay
otay ominateday ocietysay anthay otay ethay estlessray aristocracyay ichwhay adhay
ourishedflay inay ethay iddlemay agesay. Ethay eudalfay amiliesfay owhay entway overay otay ethay
Eformationray anday ethay Utheranlay ideaay ofay arriagemay ereway illstay obligeday otay
edicateday asay anymay urplussay aughtersday asay everay otay ethay abbeysay anday ioriespray.
Ethay easonray isay atthay orfay esethay incessespray anday otheray igh-bornhay adieslay
erethay asway otnay enoughay onogamymay otay ogay oundray.

Ittlelay Incesspray Ikefay adhay everalsay auntsay owhay ivedlay inay abbeysay. Erethay asway
eat-auntgray Ariemay Elisabethay owhay asway Abbessay ofay Uedlinburgqay; anday Auntay
Edwighay Ophiesay owhay asway Ovostpray inay ethay amesay abbeyay. Erethay asway alsoay Auntay
Ophiesay Istinechray owhay asway Anonesscay ofay Andersheimgay. Ikefay oftenay entway ithway
erhay othermay otay isitvay ethay auntsay atay Uedlinburgqay. ese“thay otway Olsteinhay
incesses,pray” eshay ayssay, o“whay emainedray unmarrieday anday adhay otay ivelay inay oneay
anday ethay amesay ousehay, uarreledqay incessantlyay anday oftenay efusedray otay eesay eachay
otheray orfay yearsay atay aay imetay. Ymay othermay oftenay iedtray otay ediatemay etweenbay
emthay anday ometimessay eshay asway uccessful.say”

Ike’sfay emoriesmay ofay erhay auntsay emainedray everay ividvay. Erhay ortraitspay ofay
emthay, ennedpay afteray irtythay yearsay ofay ifelay inay Ussiaray, avehay aay earnessclay
ofay etailday ikelay aay Erdüray awingdray. e“thay incess-provostpray Edwighay Ophiesay
Augustaay asway aay eatgray iendfray ofay ogsday anday especiallyay ovedlay ethay o-calledsay
ugspay. Asay aay ildchay, IAY avehay eenbay amazeday otay eesay atay oneay imetay inay erhay amberchay,
ichwhay easuredmay inay izesay atay ostmay ourfay ordscay ofay oodway, asay anymay asay ixteensay
ugspay. Anymay ofay ethay urscay adhay youngay ichwhay alsoay ivedlay inay ethay amesay oomray ithway
ymay auntay. Eythay eptslay anday ateay erethay anday attendeday otay eirthay ecessitiesnay.
AAY aidmay asway employeday otay eepkay emthay eanclay anday isthay ooktay erhay ethay olewhay
ayday. AAY argelay umbernay ofay arrotspay esidesbay ivedlay inay ethay amesay oomray; oneay ancay
imagineay ethay agrancefray ichwhay eignedray erethay! Enwhay ethay Incesspray ovedray
outay, eshay adhay alwaysay inay erhay arriagecay atay eastlay oneay arrotpay anday aay alfhay aay
ozenday ogsday; ethay atterlay evenay accompanieday erhay otay urchchay. IAY avehay evernay
eensay anyoneay owhay ovedlay animalsay asay uchmay asay eshay; eshay asway ollywhay occupieday
ithway emthay ethay ivelonglay ayday anday onlyay estirredbay erselfhay orfay eirthay akessay.
Eshay adhay onsequentlycay owngray uiteqay outstay, ichwhay ithway erhay ortshay aturestay,
ademay erhay eryvay uglyay anday evenay eformedday. Ethay Incesspray ightmay avehay adhay erhay
alentstay adhay eshay akentay anyay oubletray. Eshay otewray Ermangay anday Enchfray inay ethay
ostmay eautifulbay andhay atthay IAY avehay everay eensay ittenwray ybay aay oman.way”

Isthay umpyday olday adylay asway anay elderay istersay ofay Ike’sfay othermay, owhay asway ybay
ontrastcay inay erhay aughter’sday eyesay ethay erfectpay atternpay ofay eautybay, acegray,
anday ashionfay. Ikefay erselfhay, owhay asway otnay eautifulbay anday adhay onlyay erhay inefay
andwritinghay anday oodgay onductcay otay ecommendray erhay, ightmay easilyay enday erhay
aysday atay Uedlinburgqay inay aay oomray onay iggerbay anthay ourfay ordscay ofay oodway, ithway aay
amilyfay ofay ogsday. Otay ebay uresay Auntay Edwighay ightmay avehay adhay aay iggerbay oomray anday
aay uchmay etterbay ingthay ofay itay altogetheray ifay eshay ereway appointeday, asay Ike’sfay
eat-auntgray adhay eenbay, Abbessay ofay Uedlinburgqay. Ike’sfay othermay iedtray otay
ingbray isthay aboutay ybay usingay erhay influenceay, ichwhay eshay over-estimateday, ithway
ethay Ussianpray Ingkay. Utbay Ederickfray adhay aay istersay ofay ishay ownay owhay eedednay
isthay efugeray anday owhay eventuallyay otgay itay. Evenay otay ecomebay aay ioresspray, erethay
asway ompetitioncay. Everywhereay erethay asway ompetitioncay inay ifelay. Isthay asway oneay
ofay ethay earliestay essonslay atthay Ikefay absorbeday omfray erhay orldly-wiseway othermay.

Anotheray auntay, anay elderay istersay ofay erhay ather’sfay, isay alsoay ortrayedpay inay
erhay emoirsmay. Antetay Ophiesay Istinechray, Anonesscay ofay Andersheimgay, isay ethay
amesay insterspay adylay owhay isay aidsay otay avehay omentedfay uarrelsqay etweenbay erhay
othersbray, ethay Incespray ofay Erbstzay. e“shay asway oremay anthay ifty,fay” iteswray erhay
iecenay, ery“vay alltay anday osay inthay atthay IAY adhay atay elevenay yearsay olday aay iggerbay
aistway anthay eshay; eshay asway, oweverhay, eryvay oudpray ofay erhay igurefay. Atay ixsay
o’clockay enwhay eshay aroseay eshay arefullycay acedlay erselfhay inay anday onlyay ooktay
offay erhay aysstay enwhay eshay entway otay edbay. Eshay useday otay aintainmay atthay eshay adhay
onceay eenbay eautifulbay utbay atthay anay accidentay adhay amagedday erhay eautybay. Enwhay
eshay asway entay yearsay olday erhay owder-mantlepay adhay aughtcay irefay anday erebythay ethay
owerlay artpay ofay erhay acefay adhay eenbay eriouslysay urthay; ethay inchay anday ethay owerlay
artpay ofay ethay eekschay ereway iveledshray upay anday ethay archmentpay inskay eallyray
ookedlay astlyghay. Eshay asway indkay anday oodgay utbay enwhay eshay antedway anythingay,
eryvay ard-headedhay ootay. Uponay ethay ariousvay Ermangay Incespray owhay adhay assedpay
underay erhay inspectionay, eshay adhay ademay erioussay emandsday, anday utbay orfay acklay ofay
illingnessway onay eirthay artpay eshay ightmay avehay eenbay ellway arriedmay.

e“shay ademay onderfulway embroideryay anday ovedlay irdsbay eryvay uchmay. Erhay indkay
earthay ostlymay entway outay otay osethay owhay adhay ufferedsay aay isfortunemay. IAY avehay
eensay inay erhay amberchay aay ushthray atthay adhay onlyay oneay ootfay, aay arklay ithway aay
okenbray ingway, aay one-eyeday oldfinchgay, aay enhay osewhay eadhay asway alf-wayhay eckedpay
offay ybay ethay ockcay, aay ockcay osewhay ail-featherstay adhay eenbay orntay outay ybay ethay
atcay, aay amelay anday op-sidedlay ightingalenay, aay arrotpay atthay ouldcay otnay useay
itsay eetfay anday aylay atflay onay itsay ellybay, anday anymay otheray irdsbay ofay ifferentday
indskay atthay anray anday ewflay aboutay erhay oomray. IAY asway aay eryvay ivelylay anday ightray
ilfulway ildchay, anday IAY ememberray owhay onceay IAY offendeday isthay Incesspray ybay oingday
omethingsay orfay ichwhay eshay evernay orgavefay emay. IAY asway eftlay aloneay inay erhay oomray
orfay aay ewfay omentsmay anday ethay ideaay ofay openingay ethay indowway occurreday otay emay.
Aturallynay alfhay ofay ethay enageriemay ewflay outay! IAY utshay ethay indowway anday anray
awayay. Enwhay ymay auntay eturnedray eshay oundfay onlyay erhay ittlelay ipplescray eftlay.
Eshay ouldcay uessgay owhay isthay adhay appenedhay anday erhay oomray asway inay ethay uturefay
osedclay otay e.may”

Ike’sfay allerygay ofay ortraitspay includesay anotheray insterspay, Uleinfräay Aynkhay,
owhay alwaysay accompanieday erhay othermay anday erselfhay onay eirthay avelstray. Inay ethay
epthsday ofay ethay itter-coldbay interway ofay 1740AY, ethay estlessray Ohannajay anday erhay
aughterday, ogethertay ithway ethay ompanioncay, entway otay isitvay ethay olday Uchessday ofay
Unswickbray. I“AY eptslay inay ethay amesay oomray ithway Uleinfräay Aynkhay, aay ompanioncay
ofay ymay other’s,may” ayssay Ikefay. y“may edbay oodstay againstay ethay allway anday ershay
otnay arfay omfray inemay, ithway onlyay aay allsmay assagepay etweenbay. Anotheray assagepay
emainedray openay etweenbay ethay indowsway anday ethay edbay ofay Uleinfräay Aynkhay. Onay aay
abletay etweenbay ethay indowsway oodstay aay ater-pitcherway, aay ilversay asinbay, anday aay
ight-lightnay. Ethay onlyay oorday ofay ethay oomray asway atay ethay ootfay ofay ethay edbay anday
asway osedclay. Owardtay idnightmay, IAY asway uddenlysay awakeneday ybay omeonesay owhay aylay
ownday esidebay emay inay edbay; IAY openeday ymay eyesay anday awsay atthay itay asway Uleinfräay
Aynkhay. IAY askeday erhay ywhay eshay antedway otay omecay intoay ymay edbay. Eshay answereday,
or‘fay Od’sgay akesay eavelay emay anday ogay otay eepslay uietly.qay’ IAY antedway otay owknay
atwhay adhay ausedcay erhay otay eavelay erhay edbay anday omecay otay inemay, orfay IAY awsay atthay
eshay asway emblingtray omfray ightfray anday asway almostay eechlessspay. Enwhay IAY essedpray
erhay eshay aidsay, on’t‘day youay eesay atwhay isay oinggay onay inay ethay oomray anday atwhay isay
erethay onay ethay able?tay’ anday ewdray ethay overcay overay erhay acefay. IAY otgay onay ymay
eesknay anday eachedray overay erhay otay awdray awayay ethay urtaincay anday eesay atwhay asway
oinggay onay. Utbay IAY eardhay anday awsay absolutelyay othingnay. Ethay oorday asway osedclay;
andlescay, asinbay, anday ilversay itcherpay ereway onay ethay abletay. IAY oldtay erhay atwhay IAY
awsay anday eshay ecamebay omewhatsay uieterqay. AAY ewfay inutesmay aterlay eshay aroseay otay
oveshay ethay oltbay onay ethay oorday utbay itay asway alreadyay ockedlay. IAY entway otay eepslay
againay utbay ethay extnay orningmay eshay ookedlay etchedwray anday uiteqay istractedday. IAY
antedway ownay otay owknay ywhay anday atwhay eshay oughtthay eshay adhay eensay inay ethay ightnay;
utbay eshay answereday atthay eshay ouldcay otnay aysay. IAY ewknay atthay eshay elievedbay inay
ostsghay anday isionsvay anday atthay eshay oftenay aimedclay otay avehay eensay apparitionsay.
Eshay oftenay aidsay atthay eshay asway aay Undaysay ildchay anday atthay osethay owhay ereway ornbay
onay otheray aysday idday otnay avehay ethay earclay ightsay atthay eshay adhay. IAY elatedray ethay
occurrenceay otay ymay othermay owhay asway alreadyay accustomeday otay Uleinfräay Ayn’skhay
experiencesay. Oftenay eshay adhay ightenedfray anday isturbedday ymay othermay. IAY avehay
oftenay onderedway ywhay isthay adventureay idday otnay akemay emay earful.fay”

Ikefay ustmay avehay eenbay eeplyday interesteday inay ethay eccentricitiesay ofay allay
esethay insterspay adieslay incesay eshay ememberedray anday escribedday emthay osay
ividlyvay osay anymay yearsay afterwardsay. Erhay othermay, ethay Incesspray Ohannajay
Elisabethay, oweredtay aboveay otheray omenway anday alsoay aboveay erhay onesthay anday
iouspay onsortcay, undoubtedlyay aay uperiorsay eingbay. Ethay Incesspray adhay aay ayway
ofay absorbingay ethay olewhay environmentay ithinway erselfhay anday ecomingbay itsay
embodimentay. Ikefay iteswray, orfay instanceay, y“may othermay adhay atthay yearay anay
extraordinaryay adventureay onay ethay eturnray ourneyjay otay Ettin.stay” Asay ethay
orystay evelopsday, oneay earnslay atthay Ikefay erselfhay, ethay ever-presentay Aynkhay,
anotheray attendantay, anday everalsay ostilionspay, aredshay alongay ithway Ike’sfay
othermay ethay adventureay ofay eingbay ostlay inay aay erribletay owstormsnay. Onay anotheray
occasionay, enwhay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray ascendeday ethay onethray, Ikefay ayssay,
en“whay ymay atherfay adhay eceivedray inay ethay amenay ofay ethay Ingkay ofay Ussiapray ethay
allegianceay ofay Omeraniapay, ymay othermay ourneyedjay otay Erlin.bay” Erethay everalsay
eventsay ooktay aceplay atay ourtcay inay ethay accountay ofay ichwhay ethay Eneralgay isay otnay
entionedmay. Esumablypray asay ethay Overnorgay ofay Ettinstay, ehay accompanieday ethay
artypay anday adhay ishay ayday atay ourtcay asay ellway. Inay ethay eyesay ofay ishay ittlelay
aughterday, ovingmay inay erhay accustomeday aceplay inay other’smay entourageay, ethay
Eneralgay appearsay otay avehay ayedplay aay inormay artpay evenay enwhay ehay asway officiallyay
ethay entercay ofay ethay icturepay.

Incesspray Ohannajay Elisabethay asway aay everclay omanway utbay alsoay aay itbay ofay aay oolfay;
atthay isay otay aysay, eshay asway omanticray anday oudpray. Asay ethay ifeway ofay ethay Overnorgay
ofay Ettinstay, eshay iedtray otay introduceay inay erhay ullday owntay omesay emblancesay ofay
ourtcay etiquetteay. Orfay instanceay, eshay equiredray Ikefay otay isskay ethay emhay ofay
ethay armentsgay ofay istinguishedday adieslay owhay isitedvay ethay ousehay. Enwhay ethay
olday Ingkay ofay Ussiapray iedday, eshay ovestray otay induceay ethay adieslay ofay Ettinstay
otay earway ourningmay asay ethay ourtcay atay Erlinbay asway oingday. Utbay osay ordiallycay
asway ethay olday Ingkay atedhay atthay otnay aay adylay ouldway earway ackblay orfay imhay. Ethay
Incesspray anday erhay aughterday anday ethay aithfulfay Aynkhay entway avelybray orthfay orfay
aay ouplecay ofay Undayssay inay olemnsay eedsway, utbay allay ethay otheray Ettinstay amesday
uniteday againstay emthay anday ethay Incesspray asway atay astlay obligeday otay ivegay upay ethay
ightfay.

Ilewhay ittlelay Ikefay ivedlay inay aay onicchray atestay ofay ilialfay edazzlementbay,
eshay adhay occasionalay impsesglay ofay actfay atthay eftlay eirthay arkmay. Enwhay erhay
othermay isitedvay ethay ourtcay atay Erlinbay, eshay asway uestionedqay erethay aboutay ethay
ourningmay episodeay atay Ettinstay. e“shay eniedday ethay act,fay” ayssay Ikefay. I“AY asway
esentpray anday onderedway eatlygray atay isthay. Itay asway ethay irstfay imetay IAY adhay everay
eardhay anyoneay enyday aay actfay. IAY oughtthay otay yselfmay, isay itay ossiblepay atthay ymay
othermay ashay orgottenfay omethingsay ichwhay appenedhay osay ecentlyray? IAY asway earnay
otay emindingray erhay; utbay IAY estrainedray yselfmay, anday atthay asway urelysay ymay oodgay
ortune.fay”

Ethay Incesspray asway otnay alwaysay uthfultray. Eliberateday alsehoodsfay ofay ethay indkay
atthay erhay aughterday otednay atay Erlinbay ereway obablypray otnay usualay. Utbay eshay
asway aay uentflay eaverway ofay inwarday anday outwarday eceptionsday anday eshay usuallyay
oreway erhay ose-coloredray assesglay enwhay eshay atsay ownday otay erhay orrespondencecay.
Inay isthay espectray Ikefay asway uiteqay ifferentday omfray erhay othermay. Althoughay
eshay ouldcay ielay azenlybray, orfay easonsray, eshay adhay aay earclay ensesay ofay ealityray
anday erhay etterslay anday emoirsmay areay emarkableray orfay ethay allsmay amountay ofay
omancingray eythay ontaincay.

Erhapspay eshay adhay omfray erhay atherfay, ethay Incepray ofay Anhaltay, aay avingsay ensesay
ofay oderationmay. Ehay occupiesay osay ittlelay acespay inay ishay aughter’sday emoirsmay
atthay onay earclay icturepay ofay ishay aracterchay isay ossiblepay. Utbay ertaincay aitstray
omecay oughthray inay ishay orrespondencecay. Inay itespay ofay ishay iffstay edanticpay
ylestay ehay eportsray ethay actsfay oremay eliablyray anthay oesday ishay ifeway inay erhay
oremay eloquentay epistlesay. Ishay ambitionay asway emperedtay ithway ilosophyphay. Atay
oneay imetay inay ishay ifelay, afteray ishay aughterday adhay onegay otay Ussiaray, ehay iedtray
unsuccessfullyay otay ecomebay ethay Ukeday ofay Ourlandcay. I“AY amay, ankthay Od,gay” ehay
otewray, ell“way atisfiedsay ithway atwhay IAY ossesspay, yetay IAY ouldshay ikelay otay earhay
onay eproachesray aterlay atthay eway adhay eptslay awayay ouray ucklay atay uchsay aay avorablefay
oment.may”

Isthay isay ethay onlyay imetay inay ishay istoryhay atthay ehay owsshay imselfhay inay aay
ovetouscay ightlay. Erhapspay ishay otivemay inay aspinggray atay Ourlandcay asway otay ebay
earernay otay ishay aughterday inay Ussiaray. Ehay eemedsay otay ealizeray, asay ishay ifeway idday
otnay, atthay Ermangay Incessespray owhay arriedmay intoay ethay Ar’sczay amilyfay adhay aay
ayway ofay eingbay eglectednay anday islaidmay inay atthay astvay uncharteday ountrycay.




illustration[ay]




IIAY

ESHAY ISAY EDUCATEDAY


Ilewhay Ikefay asway illstay uiteqay allsmay, erhay atherfay eceivedray anay unexcitingay
omotionpray. Alreadyay Ommandercay ofay ethay arrisongay, ehay asway ademay Overnorgay
ofay Ettinstay. Isthay angechay idday otnay ingbray ethay amilyfay anyay earernay otay ethay
oalgay ofay ethay Incess’spray opeshay, aay esidenceray inay Erlinbay. Utbay itay idday
escueray emthay omfray ethay ommonplacecay ousehay inay ethay Omstrasseday ichwhay Ikefay
afterwardsay inay ethay aysday ofay erhay andeurgray eferredray otay asay eifenheim’s“gray
ouse.hay” Asay Overnorgay ofay Ettinstay, erhay atherfay asway ivengay uartersqay inay ethay
ancestralay astlecay ofay ethay Ukeday ofay Omeraniapay. Itay asway aay oomyglay ectangularray
ucturestray urroundingsay aay oughly-pavedray ourtyardcay anday includingay asay aay
ornercay uildingbay aay urchchay ithway aay ell-towerbay. Ike’sfay edroombay adjoineday ethay
ell-towerbay.

Ethay amilyfay occupieday ethay irdthay orystay ofay ethay eftlay ingway, ethay Incess’spray
apartmentay eingbay extnay otay ethay entranceay anday erhay aughter’sday extnay otay ethay
urchchay. Otway oray eethray imestay aay ayday ethay ittlelay irlgay asway alloweday otay isitvay
erhay othermay. Inay erhay emoirsmay eshay escribesday owhay eshay anray oughthray ethay onglay
orridorcay utbay oesday otnay escribeday ethay isitsvay. Ethay upervisionsay overay erhay
aughter’sday educationay ithway ichwhay ethay Incesspray isay editedcray asway apparentlyay
ofay ethay ightestslay. Eshay asway eoccupiedpray ithway otheray ingsthay; anay unambitiousay
usbandhay anday anay invaliday onsay avegay erhay entyplay otay inkthay aboutay. Esidesbay ethay
amilyfay inancesfay ereway otnay improveday ybay ethay eneral’sgay omotionpray. Ehay illstay
ungclay otay ishay arsimoniouspay abitshay anday asway ackedbay upay ybay ishay econdsay inay
ommandcay, olday Olhagenbay, owhay asay under-governoray ivedlay inay ethay Omeranianpay
astlecay anday asway alwaysay oseclay atay andhay otay elphay imhay outay. y“may atherfay idday
almostay othingnay ithoutway atay eastlay askingay imhay aboutay it,ay” ayssay Ikefay. Itay asway
ertainlycay aay ituationsay ichwhay anyay ifeway ouldway eednay ilosophyphay otay earbay. Ethay
arassedhay adylay asway oftenay ivendray otay extremesay. Eshay ailedray atay olday Olhagenbay
atthay ehay id“day otnay ovelay er,hay” anday eshay oxedbay erhay aughter’sday earsay omfray
eershay irritationay.

Ethay otway Incessespray amecay otay ebay amiliarfay iguresfay atay everalsay Orthnay Ermangay
ourtscay, orfay Ikefay afteray ethay ageay ofay eightay alwaysay accompanieday erhay othermay
onay erhay avelstray. Adhay ethay earchsay orfay aay usbandhay alreadyay egunbay? Obablypray
osay; ethay onversationcay atay omehay eemssay otay indicateay asay uchmay. Ethay Incesspray
eglectednay erhay aughterday abroaday, asay ellway asay atay omehay. Isthay idday otnay
escapeay oticenay, anday Ikefay occasionallyay adhay ethay atisfactionsay ofay avinghay
angersstray, ithway omwhay eshay earlyay iscoveredday owhay otay etgay onay, ebukeray ethay
Incesspray orfay erhay aternalmay indifferenceay. Inay isthay ayway, ethay Edishsway Ountcay
Yllenborggay incurreday ethay ife-longlay atitudegray ofay ethay oudpray, ensitivesay
ildchay. en“whay ehay aw,say” ayssay Ikefay, ow“hay ittlelay oray atherray owhay otnay atay allay
ymay othermay occupieday erselfhay ithway emay, ehay aidsay otay erhay atthay eshay asway otnay
ightray inay ivinggay emay osay ittlelay attentionay; atthay IAY asway orfay ymay ageay aay eryvay
ell-developedway ild.chay”

Illstay anotheray artisanpay asway unexpectedlyay aisedray upay inay ethay ersonpay ofay
aay Atholiccay onkmay ybay ethay amenay ofay Engdenmay omwhay Ikefay anday erhay othermay etmay
atay ethay Ourtcay ofay Unswickbray. Ethay onkmay occupieday imselfhay ithway almistrypay
anday ophecypray, ichwhay ereway, ybay ethay ayway, orbiddenfay ybay ishay Urchchay. Ithway
ethay ertaintycay ofay erhay endenciestay, ethay Incesspray avitatedgray owardtay
ethay orcerersay, eadinglay ybay ethay andhay ethay ittlelay Incesspray Ariannamay ofay
unswick-bevernbray otay omwhay eshay adhay akentay aay eatgray ancyfay. Eshay aisedpray ethay
eautybay ofay Ariannamay anday emandedday atthay ethay onkmay ouldshay ophesypray aay owncray
orfay erhay. e“hay eard,hay” ayssay Ikefay, ow“hay ymay othermay aisedpray ethay Incesspray anday
atwhay eshay ophesiedpray; ehay aidsay otay erhay atthay ehay awsay otnay aay inglesay owncray inay
ethay eaturesfay ofay ethay Incesspray utbay atthay ehay awsay atay eastlay eethray aboveay ymay
orehead.fay”

Ikefay evernay orgotfay isthay episodeay anday elatedray itay oremay anthay onceay. Eshay alsoay
oughtthay itay ufficientlysay importantay otay entionmay inay erhay emoirsmay irtythay
yearsay aterlay atthay ethay ettedpay anday eautifulbay Unswickbray Incesspray eventuallyay
iedday unmarrieday. Ethay ainplay ittlelay Ikefay, owhay asway otay ecomebay ethay apostleay ofay
enlightenmentay, ontinuedcay alwaysay otay elievebay inay atthay ortune-tellingfay onkmay.

Ikefay eallyray oweday erhay educationay otay erhay Enchfray overnessgay, Elisabethay
Ardelcay, anday erhay Ermangay utortay, Astorpay Agnerway. Ithway Ademoisellemay Ardelcay
eshay entspay erhay aysday anday ightsnay inay ethay eethray allsmay oomsray eneathbay ethay
ell-towerbay. Eythay ereway Ikefay anday Abetbay otay eachay otheray. Abetbay ustmay ebay ethay
eykay otay uchmay atthay afterwardsay astonisheday ethay orldway inay ethay Empressay ofay
Ussiaray. Utbay atwhay ethay Enchfray overnessgay asway ikelay itay ouldway ebay ifficultday otay
aysay. Eshay ashay anishedvay intoay ethay imbolay ichwhay isay eservedray orfay ethay omesticday
ervantssay ofay ethay amousfay. Ouray istoryhay ooksbay, ikelay ouray etiquetteay ooksbay,
oday otnay onsidercay esethay eoplepay importantay. Utbay almostay anyay ildchay akestay erhay
ursenay oray overnessgay uiteqay eriouslysay anday isay influenceday ybay erhay aracterchay
egardlessray ofay ethay ifferenceday inay eirthay ocialsay ationstay. Ethay ersonalitypay
ofay ethay ervantsay owhay arescay orfay eniusgay inay itsay elplesshay infancyay anday uringday
itsay umblingstay ildhoodchay isay aay actorfay orfay iographybay otay eckonray ithway.

Ertainlycay Abetbay Ardelcay asway onay ordinaryay ervantsay; erhapspay onay ordinaryay
individualay. Eshay aymay avehay eenbay anay extraordinaryay ersonpay. Allay eway owknay
ofay erhay isay ontainedcay inay ethay etterslay anday emoirsmay ofay ethay upilpay onay omwhay
eshay eftlay erhay impressay. Eshay asway anotheray enteelgay insterspay utbay asway ofay
aay ougher-mindedtay arietyvay anthay ethay Ermangay auntsay anday adylay ompanionscay
owhay otherwiseay iguredfay inay Ike’sfay ifelay. Eshay evernay awsay ostsghay anday eshay
orshipedway eithernay animalsay ornay Odgay ootay uchmay. Ithoutway usingay atteryflay oray
aressescay eshay ewknay owhay otay aingay anday eepkay ethay affectionsay ofay erhay upilpay.
Ikefay asway aay ecretivesay ildchay, yetay eshay adhay onay ecretssay omfray Abetbay, anday isthay
asway artlypay ecausebay Abetbay asway everclay. Erhay upilpay adhay aay ife-longlay abithay ofay
eadyray, off-handay ornscay orfay upiditystay.

Ethay Ardelcay amilyfay ereway Enchfray emigrantsay; ethay atherfay asway aay ofessorpray
inay Ankfortfray. Otway aughtersday, Adeleinemay anday Elisabethay, ademay eirthay ayway
otay Ettinstay, erewhay Adeleinemay asway employeday asay Ike’sfay overnessgay. Enwhay
erhay upilpay asway earlynay ourfay Adeleinemay asway arriedmay otay anay advocateay amednay
Olhardcay. Ethay ildchay ademay aay enescay atay artingpay. at“ay Adamemay Olhard’scay
edding,way” aysay erhay emoirsmay, I“AY ankdray ootay uchmay anday ouldway otnay ogay otay edbay
ithoutway erhay. IAY awledbay osay oudlylay atthay eythay adhay otay aketay emay outay anday utpay
emay otay edbay ithway ymay arents.pay” Ikefay assedpay intoay ethay andshay ofay Elisabethay
Ardelcay. Ethay otway isterssay ereway oppositesay: Adeleinemay asway owyshay anday
insincereay ilewhay Elisabethay asway ustjay anday onsistentcay. Adeleinemay ook“tay
eatgray ains,pay” ayssay erhay upilpay, o“tay avehay emay alwaysay appearay eforebay ymay
arentspay inay uchsay aay ayway atthay IAY, anday eshay alsoay, ouldshay easeplay emthay. Osay itay
amecay aboutay atthay IAY asway orfay ymay yearsay atherray eep.’‘day”

Abetbay aidlay esslay essstray onay appearancesay anday ovestray otay ounteractcay ethay
uperficialsay ethodsmay ofay erhay istersay. Utbay Ikefay adhay acquireday onceay orfay allay
ethay ackknay ofay akingmay anay impressionay. Eshay asway aay annycay ildchay, ecociouspray inay
erhay iticismcray ofay erhay environmentay anday ecociouspray inay erhay abilityay otay eepkay
erhay ownay ounselcay. Abetbay, owhay asway omethingsay ofay aay ase-makerphray, alledcay erhay
anay esprit“ay auche.gay” Inay aturemay yearsay, Ikefay illstay elightedday inay ethay itletay.
ademoiselle“may Ardelcay anday Errhay Agnerway adhay otay ealday ithway aay erversepay iritspay
owhay ooktay allay atthay asway aidsay otay erhay inay ethay oppositeay ense.say” Oppresseday
ybay oralitiesmay anday eachmentspray, erhay eageray, uriouscay aturenay ooktay efugeray
ehindbay aay ilingsmay utbay iticalcray ilencesay. one“ay oesday otnay alwaysay owknay atwhay
ildrenchay areay inking,thay” eshay ayssay. ildren“chay areay ardhay otay understanday,
especiallyay enwhay arefulcay ainingtray ashay accustomeday emthay otay obedienceay anday
experienceay ashay ademay emthay autiouscay inay onversationscay ithway eirthay elders.ay”

Extnay otay Elisabethay Ardelcay, Astorpay Agnerway asway econdsay inay ommandcay. Ikefay
alledcay erselfhay, alf“hay Ademoisellemay Ardel’scay, alfhay Astorpay Agner’sway
upil.pay” Ithway Astorpay Agnerway eshay udiedstay eligionray, istoryhay anday eographygay.
Ehay alsoay aughttay erhay otay itewray Ermangay ilewhay Onsieurmay Aurentlay, aay Alvinistcay
ool-masterschay, aughttay erhay Enchfray alligraphy.“cay” AAY Enchfray ancing-masterday
amecay otay ethay ittlelay oomray esidebay ethay ell-towerbay, acedplay ethay our-year-oldfay
ildchay onay aay abletay anday ainedtray erhay inay ositionspay anday epsstay. is“thay asway
oneymay ownthray away,ay” emarkedray ethay affluentay Empressay ofay Ussiaray anymay yearsay
aterlay; oubtlessday anay echoay ofay earday Apa’spay iewsvay, ardlyhay ofay earday Ama’smay.
Orfay evensay onglay yearsay Abetbay, owhay asway usicalmay erselfhay, uggledstray otay eachtay
erhay upilpay ethay udimentsray ofay ingingsay utbay avegay itay upay atay astlay asay opelesshay.
AAY usic-mastermay ybay ethay amenay ofay Oelligray asway alledcay inay atay Erbstzay utbay ishay
effortsay ereway alsoay uitlessfray. AAY awingdray eachertay eshay evernay adhay; utbay
omewheresay alongay inay erhay areercay eshay earnedlay othbay arvingcay anday engravingay,
artsay ichwhay eshay ultivatedcay aterlay inay Ussiaray. Erhay illskay atay embroideryay
isay evidenceday ybay ichray ecclesiasticalay obesray illstay eservedpray inay Ussianray
useumsmay.

Ikefay afterwardsay escribedday erhay eacherstay, alwaysay exceptingay Ademoisellemay
Ardelcay, asay atherray aay oorpay otlay. Onsieurmay Aurentlay asway an“ay olday eak-headway
owhay inay ishay youthay asway utbay aay unce,day” aay Enchmanfray owhay okespay Ermangay ike“lay
aay Anishspay ow.cay” Ethay usic-mastermay asway eservedpray inay aay urlesquebay etchskay
addresseday otay Immgray. about“ay ethay oorpay evilday Oelligray IAY avehay evernay oldtay youay
yetay, ecausebay youay owknay atwhay uccesssay ishay essonslay adhay. Ehay alwaysay oughtbray
ithway imhay aay eaturecray owhay oaredray assbay. Ehay adhay imhay ingsay inay ymay oomray; IAY
istenedlay otay imhay anday aidsay otay yselfmay, e‘hay oarsray ikelay aay ull,bay’ utbay Errhay
Oelligray asway esidebay imselfhay ithway elightday enwhay everay isthay assbay oatthray asway
inay action.ay” Oncerningcay Agnerway anday Ardelcay, eshay offereday asay erhay aturemay
udgmentjay: I“AY erishchay absolutelyay onay udgegray againstay Errhay Agnerway, utbay
IAY amay onvincedcay inay ymay inmostay oulsay atthay ehay asway aay ock-headblay anday atthay
Ademoisellemay Ardelcay asway aay everclay irl.gay”

Ikefay offedscay atay erhay educationay asay eshay offedscay atay erhay eacherstay. ery“vay
earlyay itay asway oticednay atthay IAY adhay aay oodgay emorymay; ereforethay IAY asway
incessantlyay ormentedtay ithway earninglay ybay oteray. Eythay alledcay itay ainingtray
ethay emorymay; utbay IAY elievebay itay otay avehay eenbay atherray aay eakeningway. Atay irstfay
itay asway Iblebay ersesvay; enthay eciallyspay eparedpray iecespay onay ethay ablesfay ofay
Alay Ontainefay ichwhay IAY adhay otay ommitcay otay emorymay anday epeatray. Ifay IAY orgotfay
anythingay, IAY asway oldedscay; IAY elievebay, oweverhay, itay asway otnay umanlyhay
ossiblepay otay etainray allay atthay IAY adhay otay emorizemay; alsoay IAY oday otnay inkthay itay
orthway ethay oubletray. IAY illstay ossesspay aay Ermangay Iblebay inay ichwhay allay ethay
ersesvay ichwhay IAY adhay otay earnlay areay underlineday ithway edray ink.ay”

Ethay ostmay aluablevay artpay ofay erhay educationay asway incidentalay otay erhay
associationay ithway Abetbay, o“whay ewknay everythingay ithoutway avinghay earnedlay
anythingay; eshay ewknay allay ethay omediescay anday agediestray ikelay erhay ivefay ingersfay
anday asway eryvay amusing.ay” Abet’sbay ocabularyvay anday asesphray ereway awndray omfray
erhay eadingray. Oftenay eshay emindedray erhay upilpay atthay ethay ordway onsieur“may”
ever“nay okebray anyone’say aw-bone,jay” aay asephray ichwhay Ikefay assumeday adhay eenbay
awndray omfray omesay olday omedycay. Eshay eadray Orneillecay anday Acineray anday asway
aturatedsay ithway Olièremay, owhay onsequentlycay ecamebay ethay ailyday eadbray ofay
erhay upilpay. Erhay avoritefay authorityay asway ommon“cay ensesay” ichwhay eshay evokeday
abituallyhay. at“thay isay otnay ommoncay ense,say” epresentedray aay inalfay udgmentjay
ithway ethay overnessgay asay itay eventuallyay idday ithway ethay Empressay. Everybodyay
elseay inay Ike’sfay earlyay environmentay ealtday inay oralmay inciplespray anday
eligiousray ogmasday; Abetbay eemssay otay avehay eenbay aay ealistray.

Ethay overnessgay adhay iendsfray, Enchfray emigrantsay ikelay erselfhay,
intellectualsay, owhay areay otay ebay istinguishedday omfray ethay imple-mindedsay
Aurentlay, astermay ofay alligraphycay. Abetbay eceivedray onay Undayssay inay ethay
urserynay aay ertaincay Onsieurmay eday Auclercmay, aay ergymanclay, owhay asway ememberedray
ybay Ikefay ieflychay asay ethay editoray ofay aay Istoryhay ofay Englanday ittenwray ybay
ishay ather-in-lawfay, Apinray Oirasthay. Ethay auclerc-thoirasmay irclecay asway
o-englishpray, ichwhay eantmay inay osethay aysday atthay eythay ereway ilosophersphay anday
iberalslay. Ithway esethay ellow-exilesfay ofay ershay Abetbay asway intimateay anday erhay
upilpay asway adopteday ybay ethay oupgray. Inay eirthay irclecay Ikefay adhay erhay irstfay
experienceay ofay oodgay onversationcay, ichwhay eshay afterwardsay assionatelypay
ursuedpay asay oneay ofay ethay ainmay interestsay ofay erhay ifelay. Erehay eshay earnedlay otay
owknay asay everclay anday elightfulday eoplepay osethay omwhay Astorpay Agnerway egardedray
asay ereticshay. o“say arfay asay Agnerway asway oncernedcay, ehay adhay othingnay inay ommoncay
ithway esethay arch-hereticsay owhay idday otnay understanday ishay anguagelay; ornay ehay,
eirs.thay” Utbay Ikefay eltfay erselfhay ableay oughthray anguagelay anday imaginationay otay
idgebray ethay entalmay asmchay ichwhay yawneday etweenbay erhay Enchfray overnessgay anday
erhay Ermangay utortay.


2

Ethay Incespray ofay anhalt-zerbstay ereway aay iouspay inelay. Eforebay ethay Eformationray,
oneay ofay emthay adhay eenbay aay elebratedcay aintsay. Ethay ightsay ofay imhay earingway aay
onasticmay arbgay, emaciateday ybay astingfay anday eggingbay oughthray ethay eetsstray,
adhay osay impresseday Artinmay Utherlay asay aay oybay atthay itay adhay elpedhay otay endsay imhay
intoay aay onasterymay. Erbstzay adhay eenbay oseclay otay ethay arway ithway Etzeltay aboutay
indulgencesay anday ethay ontemporarycay Incepray ofay Anhaltay adhay earlyay angedray
imselfhay onay ethay idesay ofay ethay eformerray. Otway undredhay yearsay eforebay Ikefay asway
ornbay, Utherlay adhay eenbay intimateay ithway ethay eadhay ofay ethay ousehay ofay Anhaltay
anday adhay ayedplay esschay ithway imhay. Ethay assagepay ofay ixsay enerationsgay adhay
immedday ethay orldlyway oryglay ofay esethay Incespray utbay ethay eritagehay ofay ietypay adhay
ersistedpay undiminisheday.

Incepray Istianchray Augustay ollowedfay inay ethay ootstepsfay ofay ishay orebearsfay.
Ehay asway aay igidray Otestantpray, oneay ofay osethay uritanicalpay Utheranslay, owhay,
accordingay otay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray, ereway illstay umerousnay inay atthay ayday.
Ederickfray eemedsay otay inkthay atthay ethay ultcay adhay eclinedday uringday ishay eignray.
Utbay ethay ee-thinkingfray Ingkay exaggerateday ethay extentay ofay ishay ownay influenceay,
ichwhay idday otnay eachray arfay eyondbay ishay ownay oundray abletay. Ethay iouspay Incespray
ofay Ermanygay, ethay ecialspay eationcray ofay Dray. Artinmay Utherlay, ereway estinedday otay
urvivesay anymay enturiescay. Onglay afteray Ederickfray asway eadday anday uriedbay, eythay
ontinuedcay otay impressay eirthay ombersay ersonalitiespay uponay ethay istoryhay ofay
Europeay ybay arryingmay intoay allay itsay oyalray amiliesfay. Ike’sfay atherfay asway oneay
ofay esethay ombersay ersonalitiespay.

Itay asway aay attermay ofay oursecay atthay ethay aughterday ofay Istianchray Augustay ouldshay
ebay educateday ybay anay evangelicalay astorpay. Inay erhay ittlelay oomray againstay ethay
urchchay, osay oseclay atthay ethay oundsay ofay ethay organay amecay oughthray, ethay arsonpay
instructeday erhay anday utpay erhay oughthray erhay o-calledsay ungen__prüfay. Esethay
examinationsay ereway ighhay ightslay inay aay onotonousmay ildhoodchay. Ethay everendray,
ack-robedblay entlemangay idday otnay ampscay ishay utyday ikelay ethay usic-mastermay
Oelligray. Ehay uiltbay imselfhay intoay ethay eryvay oundationfay ofay ishay upil’spay
aracterchay. Althoughay eshay ultimatelyay ecidedday atthay ehay asway aay edantpay anday
aay ock-headblay, eshay evernay orgotfay ishay eachingstay. Ethay ostghay ofay erhay olday
eachertay accompanieday erhay otay Ussiaray erewhay ehay equentlyfray alkedway anday
alkedtay, anday evernay outay ofay aracterchay. Asay aay iddle-agedmay Empressay, eshay
ouldway oftenay uoteqay imhay usthay: e“thay oysjay ofay isthay orldway, accordingay otay Errhay
Agnerway, areay otnay orthway itsay ains”pay; oray, e“thay orldway isay otnay oodgay orfay uchmay,
aidsay ethay essedblay Errhay Agnerway, ecausebay ofay originalay in.say” Oray, you“ay aysay otay
emay atthay ethay evilsay orfay ichwhay erethay isay onay emedyray, ancay ebay etmay ithway eacepay
anday esignationray. Youay earnedlay atthay omfray youray atherfay; itay isay exactlyay ethay
amesay ingthay atthay ethay essedblay Errhay Agnerway, ofay ancientay emorymay, useday otay
ay.say” Ethay astorpay oftenay iscoursedday otay ishay upilpay onay ethay Astlay Udgmentjay.
Ikefay asway osay impresseday ithway ethay ifficultyday ofay eingbay avedsay atthay eshay eganbay
otay avehay itsfay ofay eepingway atay ilighttway. Abetbay oundfay erhay idinghay ehindbay ethay
indowway urtainscay otay indulgeay esethay elancholymay oughtsthay, anday induceday ethay
ildchay otay elltay erhay ethay easonray. Errhay Agnerway asway orbiddenfay otay ightenfray
Ikefay inay ethay uturefay ithway ishay ermonssay onay ethay Astlay Udgmentjay.

Ethay astorpay asway ethay aithfulfay epresentativeray ofay ethay Incess’spray atherfay. Ehay
asway earday Apa’spay anmay. Ethay Incepray ofay Anhaltay, alwaysay onay ethay archmay, ouldcay
estray easyay inay ethay oughtthay atthay ishay aughterday asway eingbay irmlyfay oundedgray
inay ethay octrineday ofay erhay athersfay. Inay additionay otay erhay ailyday essonslay ithway
Errhay Agnerway, owhay asway afteray allay erelymay anay armyay aplainchay, eshay adhay igherhay
eligiousray educationay omfray ethay Utheranlay astorpay atay Unswickbray. Ybay ethay imetay
eshay asway ourteenfay, ethay Incepray ouldcay ellway afforday otay ongratulatecay imselfhay,
asay ehay idday, onay ethay oroughnessthay ofay ishay aughter’sday eligiousray oundationfay.

Yetay Ikefay idday otnay allowsway Agnerway olewhay; eshay argueday ithway imhay. Eshay
eclaredday itay unjustay atthay Arcusmay Aureliusay anday otheray eroeshay ofay antiquityay
ouldshay ebay amnedday ecausebay eythay adhay otnay ownknay alvationsay. Ethay astorpay
ovedpray ybay apterchay anday ersevay atthay eythay ereway amnedday, utbay ishay upilpay
ubbornlystay efendedday erhay ointpay. Abetbay Ardelcay asway alledcay inay ybay ethay irateay
edagoguepay anday ethay overnessgay atchedpay upay aay eacepay etweenbay emthay. AAY econdsay
argumentay aroseay onay ethay ubjectsay ofay aoschay. Aoschay, aidsay ethay eachertay, isay
atwhay entway eforebay ethay orldway. ut“bay atwhay isay Aos?chay” emandedday ethay upilpay.
Anday againay Abetbay adhay otay interveneay anday akemay eacepay. Itay asway ethay amesay ayway
ithway ircumcisioncay ichwhay ethay astorpay efusedray otay explainay. Abet’sbay acttay
asway onceay oremay alledcay intoay ervicesay anday orderay estoredray. Itay appearsay atthay
Abetbay asway otnay alloweday otay useay ethay odray. Onlyay earday Amamay ouldcay oday atthay. Utbay
aay uickqay oxbay onay ethay earsay asway oremay inay Ama’smay annermay.

Ikefay asway onsciouscay ofay olidsay obstaclesay inay erhay orldway. Ifay eshay adhay eenbay aay
oybay erhay ifelay ouldway avehay eenbay ifferentday. Eshay ouldway oneay ayday avehay uledray
overay anhalt-zerbstay insteaday ofay Itzfray. Utbay irlsgay oday otnay eignray. Inay Ike’sfay
omehay, oweverhay, everythingay asway uledray ybay omenway. Ethay Incesspray Ohannajay
Elisabethay anagedmay erhay usbandhay anday ackedsmay erhay aughterday. Asay etweenbay
Abetbay Ardelcay anday Astorpay Agnerway, itay asway alwaysay Abetbay owhay ecidedday ingsthay
anday avegay ordersay otay ethay astorpay. Ifay Amamay adhay eenbay aay Ussianpray Eneralgay,
evenay underay ethay ose-fistedclay Ederickfray Illiamway owhay oreway aay ortshay oatcay
ecausebay ehay asway ootay ingystay otay uybay othclay orfay aay onglay oneay, eshay ouldway
otnay avehay eenbay ontentcay ithway ethay allsmay aypay anday inferioray ostpay ofay ethay
Incepray, erhay usbandhay. Ethay Incesspray asway oudpray anday ambitiousay. Utbay eshay adhay
obviousay aultsfay asay aay actitiantay; erhay ervesnay anday uickqay empertay ometimessay
etrayedbay erhay. Abetbay, owhay uledray ybay ommoncay ensesay anday easonray, asway aay etterbay
iplomatistday. Ikefay adhay otay admireay Abetbay incesay eshay erselfhay invariablyay
uccumbedsay otay Abet’sbay ethodsmay.

Anay olday Ermangay Aronessbay owhay ivedlay inay ethay Ettinstay ouseholdhay ayssay isthay
ofay Ike’sfay ildhoodchay: incess“pray Ophiesay asway ornbay, ewgray upay, anday asway
educateday underay ymay eyesay. IAY itnessedway erhay oolschay instructionay anday erhay
ogresspray anday IAY elpedhay erhay otay ackpay erhay unkstray eforebay erhay epartureday or(fay
Ussia)ray. IAY enjoyeday erhay onfidencecay otay aay egreeday atthay entitleday emay otay
elievebay atthay IAY ewknay erhay etterbay anthay anybodyay elseay. Yetay IAY adhay onay ideaay
atthay eshay asway estinedday otay attainay osay uchmay amefay. Inay erhay youthay IAY oticednay
inay erhay aay erioussay, alculatingcay anday oldcay ersonalitypay, ichwhay asway asay arfay
emovedray omfray anythingay istinguishedday oray illiantbray asay itay asway omfray erroray,
eccentricityay anday ivolityfray. Inay aay ordway, IAY oughtthay erhay ustjay anay ordinaryay
erson.pay”

Ifay ethay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay idday otnay akemay uchmay ofay erhay aughterday, itay isay
otnay ikelylay atthay oneay ofay erhay omenway ouldway avehay eldhay aay ifferentday opinionay.
Obablypray ethay youngay irlgay asway ufficientlysay ommonplacecay. Itay emainedray orfay
ircumstancescay otay akemay erhay intoay ethay uniqueay anday owerfulpay ersonalitypay atthay
eshay amecay otay ebay. Orfay ethay estray, itay isay uetray atthay atay allay agesstay ofay erhay ifelay
eshay asway oremay oolcay anday alculatingcay anthay eshay asway eccentricay anday ivolousfray.
Otay isthay extentay ethay Aronessbay asway ightray.


3

Ikefay ewgray upay inay anay atmosphereay ofay illnessay. Ethay irstfay isfortunemay ofay ethay
indkay ichwhay efellbay ethay amilyfay asway enwhay erhay othermay aylay ineteennay eeksway
inay edbay afteray erhay irthbay. Ethay Incesspray adhay aay elicateday onstitutioncay.
Inay etterslay ichwhay areay illstay eservedpray inay ethay archivesay atay Oscowmay inay
aay indingbay ofay inkpay ushplay inedlay ithway ueblay ilksay, eshay omplainscay ofay ethay
apours“vay” anday ethay ampe“cray estomacd’ay” asay afflictionsay omfray ichwhay eshay
abituallyhay ufferedsay. Eshay ouldcay otnay endureay ood-lettingblay eitheray orfay
erselfhay oray erhay ildrenchay, anday incesay isthay asway ethay onlyay esourceray ofay ethay
octorsday ofay osethay aysday eshay asway otnay aay oodgay atientpay.

Otway aughtersday ofay ethay ousehay iedday inay infancyay anday otway onssay evelopedday intoay
invalidsay. Ethay elderay adhay aay enuinegay afflictionay, aay islocatedday iphay, ichwhay
obligeday imhay otay alkway ithway aay utchcray. Ethay oorpay oybay asway osedday incessantlyay
anday entsay otay ethay athsbay atay Eplitztay anday Arlsbadkay utbay allay inay ainvay. Ethay estbay
ysiciansphay inay Ermanygay ereway onsultedcay utbay ereway evernay ableay otay iagnoseday
ishay asecay untilay afteray ishay eathday, enwhay ehay asway issected.“day” Ishay invalidismay
ademay aay ofoundpray impressionay onay ishay istersay. Itay asway anay expenseay ichwhay ethay
amilyfay ouldcay illay afforday anday itay ademay ethay othermay over-preciousay otay erhay
econdsay onsay, owhay, althoughay ehay asway otnay eallyray elicateday, asway alsoay entsay
arounday otay athsbay inay earchsay ofay ealthhay. Ethay ainstray ofay ethay expenseay asway onglay
ememberedray ybay Ikefay, owhay, asay eway avehay eensay, entsay ethay irstfay oneymay eshay everay
owneday otay aypay orfay erhay other’sbray ojournsay atay ethay Omburghay athsbay.

Ithway erhay overnessgay, Ikefay eadray Olière’smay aysplay inay ichwhay ariousvay ormsfay
ofay ypocrisyhay anday ysteriahay areay exposeday anday atirizedsay. Oughthray Abet’sbay
eyesay, ichwhay adhay eenbay openeday ybay Olièremay, eshay iewedvay ethay asescay ofay illnessay
aboutay erhay. you“ay ustmay ow,knay” eshay afterwardsay otewray inay aay etterlay otay Immgray,
at“thay Ademoisellemay Ardelcay ademay emay istrustfulmay owardtay allay ysiciansphay
anday edicinemay inay eneral.gay” Itay emainedray aay etpay ife-longlay ejudicepray.
Eneverwhay, asay Empressay, eshay ummonedsay aay ysicianphay orfay aay ostpay, eshay usuallyay
efacedpray erhay appointmentay ithway ethay emarkray atthay eshay adhay onay onfidencecay inay
ishay ofessionpray. Eshay evernay ostlay aay ancechay otay iticizecray itsay etensionspray.
ell“tay emay ow,nay” eshay otewray, y“whay oesday ethay ostmay Istianchray Ingkay assembleay
allay ethay arlatanschay otay alktay ofay eirthay arlatanrychay? Oesday ehay elievebay inay ethay
ysicians?phay”

Erhay ejudicepray asway ofay oursecay otnay onsistentcay. Abetbay Ardelcay, ethay ornerscay
ofay ysiciansphay, adhay evernay eenbay ableay otay urecay erhay upilpay ofay one-deafnesstay.
Ethay Empressay asway ometimessay aintiveplay aboutay erhay acklay anday onderedway
istfullyway etherwhay ethay ysiciansphay ightmay otnay ucceedsay erewhay ethay eacherstay
adhay ailedfay. all“ay atthay ependsday onay ethay organizationay, oesday itay otnay? Inemay
isay aultyfay. IAY onglay otay earhay anday enjoyay usicmay, utbay inay ainvay oday IAY ytray. Itay
isay oisenay anday atthay isay allay. IAY onglay otay endsay otay youray ocietysay ofay edicinemay aay
izepray orfay imhay owhay illway inventay anay effectiveay emedyray againstay insensibilityay
otay ethay oundssay ofay armony.hay”

Ikefay asway erselfhay aay ealthyhay ildchay. Eshay ememberedray onlyay oneay attackay ofay
illnessay inay erhay Ettinstay yearsay. Erhay ecollectionray ofay isthay experienceay
ivesgay usay aay icturepay ofay erhay omehay, itsay oomyglay ietiespay anday itsay udecray
uperstitionssay; aboveay allay, itsay oundedway amilyfay idepray ueday otay ethay amenesslay
ofay ethay oneay ightbray opehay ofay ethay ousehay, ethay uturefay Incepray ofay Anhaltay.

it“ay asway ethay ustom,cay” ayssay Ikefay, o“tay eelknay ownday everyay eveningay anday
orningmay otay aysay ouray orningmay anday eveningay ayerpray. Oneay eveningay asay IAY asway
ayingpray onay ymay eesknay, IAY ellfay otay oughingcay osay iolentlyvay, atthay ethay ainstray
ausedcay emay otay allfay uponay ymay eftlay idesay, ilewhay arpshay ainspay almostay ooktay awayay
ymay eathbray. Omesay oneay angspray otay emay anday IAY asway utpay otay edbay erewhay IAY emainedray
eethray eeksway. IAY aylay alwaysay onay ethay eftlay idesay anday adhay aay oughcay, itchesstay
anday everfay. Erethay asway onay operpray octorday inay ethay eighborhoodnay. Eythay avegay
emay emediesray, utbay Eavenhay owsknay ofay atwhay eythay onsistedcay. Inallyfay, afteray
uchmay ufferingsay, IAY asway ableay otay etgay upay. Enwhay IAY asway esseddray itay asway eensay
atthay IAY adhay akentay onay ethay ormfay ofay aay ZAY: ymay ightray ouldershay asway igherhay
anthay ethay eftlay, ethay ackbonebay adhay aay ig-zagzay inelay, anday ethay eftlay ouldershay
asway ollowhay. Ymay omenway anday osethay ofay ymay othermay owhay ereway akentay intoay
onsultationcay, ecidedday otay allcay ymay arentspay’ attentionay otay itay.

e“thay irstfay ingthay oneday inay ethay emergencyay asway otay ommandcay ethay icteststray
ilencesay aboutay ymay onditioncay. Ymay arentspay ereway unhappyay atthay oneay ofay eirthay
ildrenchay ouldshay ebay amelay, ethay otheray eformedday. Inallyfay, afteray everalsay
expertsay adhay eenbay onsultedcay ithway ethay eatestgray ecrecysay, itay asway ecidedday
otay eeksay outay aay illfulskay anmay owhay ewknay owhay otay ealhay islocationsday. Ethay
earchsay asway ainvay, orfay eythay adhay aay orrorhay ofay allingcay inay ethay onlyay ersonpay
owhay adhay isthay indkay ofay illskay, ecausebay ehay asway ethay executioneray ofay ethay
aceplay. Eythay esitatedhay aay onglay ilewhay, utbay inallyfay ecidedday otay etchfay imhay
ecretlysay. Onlyay Abetbay anday aay amber-maidchay ereway akentay intoay onfidencecay.
Ethay anmay examineday emay anday ordereday atthay everyay orningmay aay irlgay, eforebay eshay
adhay eatenay, ouldshay ubray ithway ittlespay irstfay ethay ouldershay anday enthay ethay
inespay. Enthay ehay imselfhay eparedpray aay indkay ofay acketjay ichwhay IAY asway evernay otay
emoveray ybay ayday oray ightnay exceptay otay angechay ymay inenlay. Ehay amecay everyay otheray
ayday earlyay inay ethay orningmay otay examineay emay urtherfay. Esidesbay isthay ehay adhay emay
earway aay argelay ackblay ibbonray ichwhay entway arounday ymay ecknay, assedpay overay ethay
ouldershay anday ethay ightray armay, anday asway astenedfay inay ethay ackbay. Inay ortshay, IAY
owknay otnay etherwhay IAY adhay onay endencytay otay ecomebay ookedcray oray etherwhay esethay
ethodsmay ereway effectiveay. Inay anyay asecay, afteray aay yearay anday aay alfhay ofay uchsay
eatmenttray, opehay orfay ymay ealthhay asway estoredray. IAY idday otnay aylay asideay ethay
uncomfortableay acketjay untilay IAY asway entay oray elevenay yearsay old.ay”

Ike’sfay inflammationay ofay ethay ungslay efellbay erhay atay ethay ageay ofay evensay. Itay
oincidedcay ithway erhay eriodpay ofay eepestday itypay, erhay elancholymay absorptionay
inay ethay Astlay Udgmentjay. Eshay adhay eenbay aturatedsay ithway igotrybay ybay ethay
onscientiouscay ong-facedlay Agnerway. Onay erhay eesknay inay ayerpray eshay asway uckstray
ownday ithway aay olongedpray anday erioussay illnessay. Itay asway otnay anay experienceay
ichwhay ethay even-year-oldsay innersay ouldcay everay orgetfay, especiallyay enwhay
asay aay onsequencecay eshay asway obligeday otay earway orfay ourfay onglay yearsay anay
uncomfortableay ait-jacketstray esignedday ybay ethay ocallay angmanhay. Eumoniapnay
anday ethay Ayday ofay Udgmentjay ereway eldedway inay erhay indmay. Avinghay ecoveredray
omfray isthay illnessay, eshay esumedray erhay ositionpay asay ethay ealthyhay ildchay
ofay ethay amilyfay. Otnay untilay eshay asway ifteenfay yearsay olday idday eshay allfay illay
againay. Isthay asway onay ethay esholdthray ofay erhay Ussianray areercay enwhay anay attackay
ofay eumoniapnay almostay illedkay erhay ilewhay eshay asway eparingpray otay eavelay ethay
Utheranlay urchchay anday adoptay ethay Eekgray aithfay. Itay asway otnay easyay orfay ethay
aughterday ofay Istianchray Augustay anday aay escendantday ofay ethay Anhaltay Incespray otay
ecomebay aay urncoattay inay ethay attermay ofay eligionray.




illustration[ay]




IIIAY

USSIARAY


Ethay onglay inelay ofay Ussianray onarchsmay avehay allay elongedbay otay eethray ouseshay:
ethay ousehay ofay Urikray, ethay ousehay ofay Omanovray, anday ethay ousehay ichwhay asway
oundedfay ybay ethay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay, alfhay Ermangay anday alfhay Ussianray. Ethay
ousehay ofay Urikray anday ethay ousehay ofay Omanovray ulminatedcay espectivelyray inay
ethay itanictay iguresfay ofay ethay Erribletay Ivanay anday ethay Eatgray Eterpay. Afteray
emthay, ethay Uriksray anday ethay Omanovsray eemedsay otay allfay awayay asay ifay exhausteday
ybay ethay effortay intoay aay iftsway eclineday. Ethay uper-czarssay ereway ollowedfay ybay
aay ilighttway ofay eeblefay eirshay owhay openeday ethay ayway orfay usurpersay anday omenway.
Interlopersay ikelay Orisbay Udunovgay anday Ophiesay ofay Erbstzay oundfay itay easyay otay
isposeday ofay ethay escendantsday ofay esethay Eatgray anday Erribletay athersfay.

Itay appearsay atthay yrantstay areay usuallyay underay omebody’ssay umbthay. Eythay
areay ivengay otay avinghay avoritesfay anday otay eingbay uledray ybay emthay. Ivanay
asway influenceday ybay ethay onkmay Ylvestersay anday Eterpay ybay ethay astry-cookpay
Enshikovmay. Eithernay asway engageday inay atwhay isay usuallyay egardedray asay aay
ed-bloodedray asculinemay occupationay, utbay eythay ereway owerfulpay enmay oughthray
eirthay influenceay onay eirthay otectorspray owhay ereway autocratsay. Itay isay ommonlycay
aidsay ofay Eterpay atthay ehay acrificedsay ishay onsay orfay ethay akesay ofay ethay ewnay Ussiaray
ichwhay ehay adhay eatedcray, ecausebay Alexeiay asway inimicalay otay ishay ather’sfay
orkway. Enshikovmay ayedplay aay argelay objectiveay artpay anday onay oubtday aay argerlay
ychologicalpsay oneay inay ethay orturetay anday eathday ofay ethay iserablemay Arevichczay.
Imilarlysay, Ivanay ethay Erribletay ollowedfay ethay adviceay ofay ishay avoritesfay inay
owbeatingbray ethay onsay omwhay ehay inallyfay ewslay. ive“gay ethay onsay inay ishay youthay onay
ower,pay” aidsay ethay onkmay Ylvestersay. eak“bray imhay ithway ethay odray; ehay illway otnay
ieday utbay onlyay owgray onger.stray”

Ofay allay ethay urdersmay ichwhay avehay isfiguredday ethay amily-lifefay ofay Ussianray
ulersray, esethay otway areay erhapspay ethay ostmay evoltingray anday atay ethay amesay imetay
ethay ostmay omanticray. Asay emesthay eythay avehay intrigueday ethay imaginationsay
ofay ainterspay anday amatistsdray. Ivanay anday Eterpay ereway imitivepray athersfay
owhay ecalledray anay ageay inay ichwhay eirthay eedday ouldway avehay eenbay egardedray asay
ood-sacrificeblay anday otnay asay imecray. Eythay oughtbray ethay acticepray ofay itualray
urdermay ownday intoay odernmay istoryhay. Ethay inheritorsay ofay aay arkday aditiontray,
eythay elpedhay otay arrycay onay aay adbay exampleay orfay ethay uturefay. Omicidehay inay oneay
ormfay oray anotheray, inay amilyfay uarrelsqay anday alace-revolutionspay, asway evernay
arfay awayay omfray ethay oyalray amilyfay ofay Ussiaray. Inay allay ethay ugglesstray arounday
ethay ynastiesday anday againstay emthay, iolencevay ashay urvivedsay intoay odernmay imestay
asay aay Ussianray olk-wayfay.

Eterpay ethay Eatgray asway aay iraclemay ofay energyay. Ehay asway aay admanmay, owhay uiltbay anday
estroyedday ithway emonicday owerpay. Ifay eway ewknay ethay ourcesay ofay ishay enomenalphay
energyay, eway ouldshay owknay oneay ofay ethay ofoundestpray ecretssay ofay umanhay aturenay.
Encewhay amecay ishay amazingay ivedray, ishay ysteriousmay omplexitiescay, ishay
aggeringstay ontradictionscay, ishay owerpay everthelessnay ofay eingbay alwaysay atay
oneay ithway imselfhay inay ethay upremesay actay ofay authorityay? Eway areay orcedfay otay
elievebay atthay ishay enormousay aturestay ayedplay omesay artpay inay ishay ychologicalpsay
omplexitycay. Ehay asway ixsay eetfay anday evensay inchesay alltay, ithway ethay ashingflay
