ixsay eeksway anday asway imitedlay otay eremay ackblay ilksay insteaday ofay ecrêpay. I“AY ustmay
onfess,cay” iteswray Atherinecay, at“thay o-daytay enty-five(tway yearsay aterlay) IAY
annotcay inkthay ofay itay ithoutway ebellionray inay ymay eart.hay”

Ethay Empress’say irritationay ademay erhay ariablevay empertay oremay ariablevay anthay
everay. Eshay ewgray oremay estlessray anday eccentricay. Everyay ayday eshay adhay ethay
urniturefay iftedshay inay erhay apartmentsay. Erhay eoplepay ereway eftlay aitingway ourshay
anday aysday orfay ordersay ichwhay eshay elayedday orfay eremay imswhay. Onceay ethay Andgray
Uchessday emainedray ittingsay uprightay onay aay airchay ullyfay esseddray orfay earlyay
assmay ilewhay ethay ourshay owlyslay assedpay omfray ourfay o’clockay inay ethay orningmay otay
eethray o’clockay inay ethay afternoonay. Ethay Empressay adhay ummonedsay erhay otay ogay otay
urchchay utbay adhay angedchay erhay indmay atay ethay astlay omentmay anday onegay otay ethay athbay
insteaday.

Ethay ishesway ofay ethay youngay ourtcay ereway evernay onsultedcay, evenay ormallyfay,
aboutay anythingay. AAY avoritefay attendantay ouldway anishvay overnightay anday ebay
eardhay ofay extnay inay Astrakhanay, Orenburgay oray Azankay itherwhay ehay adhay eenbay
anishedbay. Alwaysay, Atherinecay ayssay, ethay exilesay assedpay irstfay oughthray
ethay ourtcay alledcay ethay Ecretsay Ancellarychay, aay ormfay ofay inquisitionay ichwhay
asway ethay errortay anday orrorhay ofay Ussiaray atay ethay imetay. Oneay ayday ethay Andgray
Uke’sday Olsteinhay ervantssay ereway uddenlysay entsay ackbay otay Ermanygay ithoutway
arningway, anday ehay asway eftlay aloneay ithway Ussiansray omwhay ehay etestedday. Anotheray
ayday Atherine’scay attendantay, Adamemay Usekray, owhay appenedhay alsoay otay ebay aay
Olsteinerhay, asway uddenlysay ismissedday anday eplacedray ybay Adamemay Adislavvlay,
owhay asway aay Ussianray. Ethay Empressay adhay apparentlyay ithay uponay ethay orlornfay opehay
atthay itay ightmay ebay Ermangay influenceay ichwhay eptkay ethay youngay ouplecay erilestay.

Atherine’scay ewnay omanway, Ascoviapray Ikitichnanay Adislavvlay, ademay anay
importantay ontributioncay otay erhay educationay. Ascoviapray asway aboutay iftyfay anday
erhay ossipgay aboutay ethay Ussianray andeesgray anday eirthay amiliesfay entway ackbay
otay ethay imetay ofay Eterpay ethay Eatgray. Atherinecay asway ascinatedfay ybay esethay
istorieshay ichwhay avegay erhay ethay orientationay inay Ussiaray atthay eshay eedednay.
Eterpay ouldway otnay istenlay otay Ascoviapray. Ehay asway omesickhay orfay Olsteinhay anday
asay ethay Ermangay oupgray ichwhay onceay urroundedsay imhay ewgray esslay anday esslay anday
inallyfay isappearedday ompletelycay, ishay Eimwehhay increaseday. Ethay astlay otay ogay
asway Aronbay Estocqlay, owhay asway imprisoneday orfay ivefay yearsay inay ethay Ortressfay ofay
Aintsay Eterpay anday Aintsay Aulpay anday inallyfay anishedbay otay Uglitchay. Ethay Empressay
asway oneday ithway Ermansgay orfay allay imetay.

Atherinecay eemedsay otay orgetfay eryvay easilyay ethay olday iendsfray ofay erhay other’smay
artypay anday otay asspay onay uicklyqay otay anay allianceay ithway ethay Ussiansray. Inay imetay
eshay oundfay erselfhay anday Estushevbay, ethay officialay enemyay ofay atthay artypay, onay
ethay amesay idesay anday evenay uniteday inay eirthay oliticalpay emesschay. Eshay adhay anay
elasticityay ofay emperamenttay ichwhay asway erhay oneay alvationsay inay erhay yingtray
ircumstancescay. Orfay erethay isay onay enyingday eythay ereway intenselyay yingtray.
or“fay eighteenay years,ay” eshay iteswray, I“AY avehay edlay aay ifelay omfray ichwhay entay
othersay ouldway avehay onegay insaneay anday entytway inay ymay aceplay ouldway avehay iedday ofay
elancholy.may”

Ethay ettypay ersecutionspay ofay ethay Empressay ereway ethay onlyay ingthay atthay ewdray ethay
youngay ouplecay ogethertay. Enwhay Atherinecay asway oldedscay ybay erhay uennaday, Eterpay
aredflay upay inay erhay efenceday. Inay eturnray, Atherinecay avegay Eterpay adviceay anday
omfortcay enwhay ehay edflay otay erhay inay errortay atay ethay eatsthray ofay ethay Empressay
anday ishay overnorsgay. Utbay Atherinecay oundfay ishay earsfay excessiveay; ithway aay
ertaincay etachmentday anday objectivityay eshay ecognizedray atthay eythay ereway eyondbay
ethay ordinaryay anday uncontrollableay. Eshay onderedway atay isthay aittray atay irstfay
anday yetay ympathizedsay ithway imhay; utbay aterlay onay enwhay otheray ingsthay adhay omecay
etweenbay emthay, erhay onderway angedchay otay ornscay. Erhay orystay ofay ethay Andgray Ukeday
anday ishay abhorrenceay ofay ethay Ussianray athbay owsshay atthay eshay earlyay appreciateday
ethay angersday intoay ichwhay ethay youngay an’smay ubbornnessstay asway eadinglay imhay.

Uringday ethay irstfay eekway ofay Entlay, ethay Empressay ordereday Atherinecay anday Eterpay
otay ogay otay ethay eamstay athbay, asay aay artpay ofay ethay egularray eparationpray orfay
ommunioncay. Ethay Andgray Ukeday excitedlyay efusedray. Ehay ouldway otnay enteray ethay
athbay; ehay adhay evernay eenbay erethay eforebay anday itay asway aay idiculousray eremonycay
anyhoway otay ichwhay ehay attacheday onay ignificancesay. Esidesbay, ethay athbay asway
armfulhay anday ouldway akemay imhay illay. e“hay idday otnay ishway otay ieday; ishay ifelay asway
ishay ostmay eciouspray ossessionpay. Ethay Empressay ouldcay evernay orcefay imhay otay
ethay ointpay ofay oinggay ere.thay” Otay allay isthay Adamemay Oglokovchay epliedray ithway
equalay eathay. Eshay eatenedthray ethay youngay anmay ithway ethay ortressfay ofay Aintsay
Eterpay anday Aintsay Aulpay anday emindedray imhay atthay ethay onsay ofay Eterpay ethay Eatgray
adhay erishedpay omfray isobedienceday. uch“may ofay is,thay” Atherinecay eflectedray,
atchingway Adamemay Oglokovchay, omes“cay omfray erselfhay utbay uchmay isay omfray ethay
Empressay. IAY amecay otay ethay onclusioncay atthay ethay eatthray ofay ethay ortressfay
ustmay avehay omecay omfray ethay onarchmay anday IAY awsay inay itay aay ignsay ofay erhay ongstray
esentmentray againstay ethay Andgray Uke.day”

Ethay ischief-makingmay Ariamay eportedray allay isthay ackbay otay ethay Empressay, osewhay
athwray aredflay outay inay erhay usualay ongstray anguagelay: ery“vay oodgay; ifay ehay isay
osay isobedientday owardtay emay, IAY illway otnay isskay ishay amnedday andhay anyay ore.may”
Isthay asway aithfullyfay arriedcay ackbay otay ethay Andgray Ukeday owhay aidsay, at“thay
ependsday onay erselfhay. Utbay IAY illway evernay ogay intoay ethay athbay. IAY annotcay earbay
ethay eat.hay” Ethay Empressay eptkay erhay ordway anday erhay ephewnay eptkay ishay. Yetay eshay
evernay avegay upay ethay attemptay otay orcefay imhay intoay ethay athbay. Ehay asway otnay againay
eatenedthray ithway ethay ortressfay, utbay ehay alwaysay eltfay ethay eatthray urkinglay
inay ethay ackgroundbay. Ethay uarrelqay ademay aay eatgray impressionay onay ethay Andgray
Uchessday owhay ellstay ofay itay atay engthlay inay erhay emoirsmay. Eshay egardedray itay
orrectlycay asay aay ymptomsay ofay omethingsay extremeay inay ishay aracterchay, utbay eshay
ouldcay otnay understanday itay. Erhay ommoncay ensesay asway affledbay ybay ethay ehaviourbay
ofay aay youthay owhay earedfay ethay Ussianray athbay oremay anthay ehay earedfay imprisonmentay
inay aay ortressfay. Inay ishay obstinacyay anday excitementay, Eterpay avegay ariousvay
easonsray orfay efusingray otay obeyay ethay Empressay utbay ehay arcelyscay avegay ethay ealray
oneay. Ethay Ussianray athbay asway aay ocialsay affairay, articipatedpay inay ybay akednay enmay
anday omenway. Ethay ustomcay, aay eremay everydayay actfay inay Ussiaray, asway egardedray
ithway orrorhay inay Ermanygay anday ethay estray ofay Europeay. Ethay youngay Andgray Ukeday asway
illstay aay Ermangay anday, ithoutway eingbay earlyclay awareay ofay ywhay ehay eltfay atthay
ayway, ehay eadeddray ethay exposureay anday oundfay itay unendurableay. Imprisonmentay
asway aay ifletray ybay omparisoncay. Ethay Andgray Uchessday ooktay isthay urdlehay asay eshay
ooktay othersay inay erhay ewnay ifelay. Eshay adhay eenbay oughtbray upay aay uritanpay anday aay
otestantpray. Utbay eshay onay ongerlay ivedlay inay Erbstzay; eshay ivedlay inay Ussiaray
anday idday asay ethay Ussiansray idday. Ethay Andgray Ukeday ontinuedcay otay elldway inay anay
imaginaryay Olsteinhay ofay ishay ownay ichwhay asway asay ifferentday asay ossiblepay omfray
ethay Ussiaray ichwhay aylay arounday imhay.


4

Elisabeth’say apriciousnesscay increaseday. Avinghay angedchay erhay urniturefay
anday everythingay elseay inay erhay environmentay atthay ouldcay ebay angedchay, atay astlay
eshay angedchay erhay avoritefay. Ethay easy-goingay Azumovskyray asway isplacedday anday
elegatedray ithway onorshay anday ichesray otay ivatepray ifelay. Erethay isay aay aditiontray
atthay ethay Ountcay adhay eenbay ecretlysay arriedmay otay Elisabethay. Etherwhay isthay
ebay uetray oray otnay oesday otnay attermay uchmay. Ethay imetay adhay omecay orfay imhay otay ogay.
Ethay iscardedday overlay etiredray otay ethay Anitchkovay Alacepay ichwhay ethay Empressay
adhay uiltbay orfay imhay anday erewhay ehay eameddray awayay ishay ifelay orfay anotheray entytway
yearsay. Azumovskyray asway aay armingchay ecorationday onay ethay earlyay eignray ofay
Elisabethay Etrovnapay. Ehay asway ollywhay impracticalay anday ithoutway ambitionay ofay
anyay indkay, aay oeticpay indolentay Ukrainianay. Ehay asway oyallay otay ishay istressmay otay
ethay enday anday evotedday otay erhay uccessorsay, Atherinecay ethay Eatgray.

Ivanay Ivanovichay Uvalovshay, ethay ewnay avoritefay, asway aay ousincay. Asay ethay Empressay
ewgray olderay eshay ufferedsay increasinglyay omfray elancholymay ichwhay eshay ovestray
otay ightenlay ybay awingdray ethay irclecay ofay elativesray oserclay arounday erhay. Ivanay
Ivanovichay asway ablyay upportedsay inay ishay ewnay utiesday ybay ishay amilyfay. Ehay adhay aay
istersay, aay eerfulchay ersonpay omwhay ethay Empressay eliedray uponay otay escueray erhay
omfray owlay iritsspay. Ehay adhay esidesbay otway othersbray owhay uardedgay imhay onay othbay
anksflay anday eapedray aay ichray arvesthay ofay onopoliesmay. Ethay Uvalovshay othersbray
ereway ambitiousay anday aspinggray asay ethay Azumovskysray adhay evernay eenbay. Eirthay
adventay ademay aay eatgray ifferenceday atay ourtcay, orfay ethay Empressay, owhay ecamebay
oremay indolentay anday antasticfay everyay ayday, avegay oremay anday oremay owerpay otay
ethay Uvalovsshay. Eshay adhay ailedfay inay erhay earestday emeschay: erhay ephewnay anday
uccessorsay, ethay Andgray Ukeday Eterpay, adhay onay eirhay.

Ithway ethay yearay 175AY0 ethay oblempray ofay anay eirhay eemedsay otay owgray esperateday.
Inay ethay Andgray Ucalday ampcay aay ealisticray iewvay asway owinggray upay. Itay asway
epresentedray ieflychay ybay Adamemay Adislavvlay, Atherine’scay ady-in-waitinglay,
anday ybay ethay othermay ofay youngay Ergeisay Altikovsay, aay youngay amberlainchay ofay ethay
Andgray Ukeday. Owlyslay ethay ideaay ooktay apeshay ithoutway anybody’say expressingay
itay atthay ethay Andgray Uchessday ightmay, ybay erelymay ansgressingtray erhay arriagemay
owsvay, edeemray ethay ituationsay. Ybay omesay eansmay isthay ideaay asway insinuateday
intoay ethay eadshay ofay ethay upidstay Oglokovschay owhay afterwardsay oughtthay eythay
adhay inventeday itay. Ariamay Oglokovchay uggestedsay itay otay Atherinecay; utpay itay otay
erhay, osay otay eakspay, asay erhay atrioticpay utyday. Itay eemssay atherray odday atthay allay
ofay emthay adhay eenbay osay owslay inay omingcay otay isthay anplay. Apparentlyay Atherinecay
ouldway avehay onegay onay indefinitelyay inay ethay ilemmaday ifay ethay olderay arriedmay
omenway adhay otnay inallyfay uggestedsay aay ayway outay.

Atherinecay otewray otway accountsay ofay erhay affairay ithway Ergeisay Altikovsay. Oneay
asway etsay ownday onlyay eethray oray ourfay yearsay afteray itay asway overay, anday ethay otheray
eshay otewray inay erhay olday ageay. Ethay olday ady’slay orystay isay aay ivelylay omanceray,
ortrayingpay anay ardentay ourtshipcay, aay orsebackhay ideray, aay onelylay islanday, anday
anay importunateay overlay. Ethay youngay oman’sway orystay isay esslay omanticray anday
oremay oliticalpay. Eshay ayssay inay isthay ersionvay: adame“may Oglokovchay useday allay
ossiblepay artsay ofay ersuasionpay otay educesay emay. Isthay anday ethay attractivenessay
anday alentstay ofay imhay orfay omwhay eshay okespay ouldway avehay oundfay esslay esistanceray
inay anotheray anthay inay emay. Itay isay eallyray uetray atthay IAY asway istinguishedday ybay
iscretionday anday exemplaryay innocence.ay”

Ergeisay Altikovsay asway aay errymay anday irresponsibleay youthay ithoutway ulterioray
ambitionsay. Ishay elationsray ithway ethay Andgray Uchessday eganbay inay ethay yearay 1752AY,
Inay Ecemberday ofay atthay yearay ethay Andgray Uchessday eportedray iscarriagemay. Ethay
ollowingfay Ulyjay ethay amesay isfortunemay efellbay erhay. Eshay eemedsay oomedday otay
adbay ucklay anday elayday. Otnay untilay ethay 20thay ofay Eptembersay, 1754AY, idday eshay
actuallyay ecomebay aay othermay. Onay atthay ateday eshay orebay aay onsay. ere“thay asway
inexpressibleay oyjay overay it,ay” isay erhay aconiclay ommentcay. Itay asway aboutay isthay
imetay, accordingay otay erhay emoirsmay, atthay erhay ull-bonesskay osedclay upay.

Etherwhay ethay Empressay asway awareay ofay ethay intrigueay etweenbay Atherinecay anday
Ergeisay Altikovsay eway oday otnay owknay. Eway oday owknay, oweverhay, atthay ithway ethay
yearay 175AY4 erhay attitudeay owardtay ethay youngay ountcay underwentay aay ecidedday
angechay. Oglokovchay anday ishay ifeway awsay eatgray ossibilitiespay orfay ethay uturefay,
opinghay otay eapray ethay editcray orfay ethay ewnay anday atifyinggray urntay ofay eventsay.
Enwhay ethay Empressay eganbay otay urntay aay iendlyfray azegay uponay ethay youngay ourtcay,
Oglokovchay ostlay ishay eadhay anday iedtray otay ooway erhay. Atherinecay admitsay atthay eshay
anday erhay ischievousmay Ergeisay encourageday isthay indiscretionay ichwhay inviteday
angersday unforeseenay ybay eirthay inexperienceay anday youthay. Ethay othersbray
Uvalovshay ereway onglystray intrencheday anday ereway eadyray otay akemay ortshay iftshray
ofay anyay ivalray. Atay aay asquerademay allbay, ethay oftenedsay Empressay encourageday
Oglokovchay ithway endertay ancesglay. Ivanay Ivanovichay, ethay avoritefay, awsay emthay
anday ishay anclay osedclay inay arounday erhay, atay onceay, anday insidiouslyay. Inay ethay
enday Oglokovchay asway insulteday ybay ethay Empressay inay ublicpay. e“shay alledcay im,hay”
ayssay Atherinecay, in“ay aay ublicpay onversationcay atay innerday aay ockheadblay anday
aay aitortray, ichwhay ehay osay ooktay otay earthay atthay ehay ellfay intoay ethay aundicejay.
Andoidkay, ethay Uvalov’sshay anmay, asway alledcay inay, anday, asay ehay adhay onglay ownknay
atthay ethay atientpay asway anay enemyay ofay eirsthay, elievedbay atthay ehay ouldway oday emthay
aay avorfay ybay urderingmay imhay. Atay eastlay allay ethay octorsday owhay ereway alledcay
inay uringday ishay astlay aysday aintainedmay atthay ehay adhay eenbay eatedtray ikelay aay
eaturecray omwhay oneay ishedway otay illkay. Ourfay aysday afteray ishay eathday ishay ifeway
asway oldtay atthay eshay ouldcay emainray inay Oscow...may. IAY elievebay atthay Altikovsay
ouldway avehay eenbay anishedbay atay atthay imetay ootay ifay IAY adhay otnay eenbay egnantpray
anday eythay adhay otnay earedfay otay afflictay emay ithway isthay ief.gray”

Atay astlay ethay idwifemay eclaredday atthay ethay omentmay asway atay andhay. Ethay Empressay,
owhay occupieday adjoiningay amberschay, asway ummonedsay omfray erhay edbay atay otway
o’clockay inay ethay orningmay. Eshay eptsway uponay ethay enescay inay aay antlemay ofay ueblay
atinsay, orfay ethay oomray asway oldcay ithway ethay illchay ofay aay atelay Eptembersay awnday.
Atay oondaynay ethay ildchay asway ornbay. Ethay Empressay aitedway onlyay orfay ethay idwifemay
otay athebay anday addlesway ethay infantay. Enthay eshay alledcay ethay iestpray anday adhay
imhay istenedchray Aulpay. Isthay asway ethay amenay ofay ethay irstfay ildchay ornbay otay
erhay othermay anday Eterpay ethay Eatgray, aay astardbay onsay owhay adhay iedday atay ethay
ageay ofay eethray. Ommandingcay ethay idwifemay otay arrycay ethay ildchay inay ontfray ofay
erhay, ethay Empressay etiredray otay erhay ownay apartmentsay erewhay eshay arrangeday aay
urserynay anday aredcay orfay imhay ithway erhay ownay andshay. Ifay ehay imperedwhay eshay
anray otay imhay atay onceay; erhay evotionday ecamebay ethay ubjectsay ofay ideway ommentcay
anday eneralgay aisepray. Itay avegay iseray otay ethay umorray atthay ethay ildchay asway
actuallyay Elisabeth’say ownay anday otnay Atherine’scay atay allay. Ethay Empressay asway
otnay ispleasedday ithway ethay umorray; erethay ereway omentsmay inay erhay astlay yearsay,
yearsay ivengay overay otay aporsvay anday oodsmay, enwhay eshay almostay elievedbay ethay ythmay
erselfhay. Atthay eshay adhay oneday iolencevay otay ethay youngay othermay inay idnappingkay
erhay ildchay evernay entereday erhay eadhay. Eshay askeday Ariamay Eresathay ofay Austriaay,
atthay olificpray othermay omwhay eshay adhay alwaysay envieday, otay ebay odmothergay otay erhay
ildchay. Austriaay ouldshay ealizeray atthay Ussiaray alsoay adhay anay eirhay.


5

Eryvay ittlelay isay ownknay ofay ethay atherfay ofay Aulpay. Ethay unhappyay ifelay ofay
Atherine’scay onsay anday ishay inalfay insanityay avehay etsay anymay iterswray anday
istorianshay atay orkway iscussingday ishay eredityhay. Utbay eythay alwaysay avehay
assumeday atthay ishay atherfay asway Eterpay IIIAY anday atthay ishay andfathergray asway
Eterpay ethay Eatgray. Ifay isthay ereway uetray, ethay eficienciesday ofay Atherine’scay onsay
ouldway ebay easyay otay explainay, orfay eredityhay onay ethay Omanovray idesay eftlay uchmay otay
ebay esiredday. Eterpay ethay Eatgray adhay aay eak-wittedway otherbray anday Eterpay IIIAY adhay
aay entalmay isttway. Utbay allay isthay ashay othingnay otay oday ithway Aulpay, owhay asway otnay aay
Omanovray utbay aay Altikovsay.

Eway ustmay elyray uponay Atherine’scay emoirsmay orfay ethay ittlelay atthay eway owknay aboutay
ethay Altikovssay. Ergeisay anday Eterpay ereway othersbray inay ethay ervicesay ofay ethay
Andgray Ukeday. Eirthay atherfay asway ethay Eneralgay Altikovsay owhay adhay elcomedway
Atherinecay anday erhay othermay inay Igaray onay eirthay ayway otay Ussiaray. Ethay othermay
ofay ethay Altikovsay othersbray adhay eenbay aay Incesspray Alitsingay anday aay oyallay
elperhay ofay ethay Empressay Elisabethay enwhay Elisabethay eizedsay ethay onethray.
Ethay aditiontray isay atthay Ariamay Altikovsay adhay uanderedsqay erhay irtuevay orfay
Elisabeth’say ausecay. Oweverhay isthay aymay avehay eenbay, ethay Empressay asway evotedday
otay isthay adylay anday attacheday erhay otway onssay otay ethay ourtcay ofay ethay Andgray Ukeday.
Ergeisay asway aay eatgray avoritefay ofay Eter’spay anday oftenay eptslay ithway imhay. Atay ethay
imetay enwhay Ariamay Altikovsay omotedpray ethay affairay etweenbay erhay onsay anday ethay
Andgray Uchessday eshay asway aay onfirmedcay invaliday, utbay eshay eemssay otay avehay eptkay
erhay initiativeay anday energyay otay ethay astlay. Asay eshay adhay elpedhay erhay Empressay
aingay aay onethray eshay ownay oodstay eadyray otay elphay erhay aingay anay eirhay orfay itay.

Ergeisay Altikovsay asway aay ypicaltay e’er-do-wellnay. Atherinecay iedtray otay akemay
ethay ostmay ofay erhay overlay inay erhay emoirsmay utbay otnay aay eatgray ealday ouldcay ebay ademay
ofay imhay. Ehay asway aay errymay ellowfay, aay unetbray, owhay aidsay ofay imselfhay enwhay ehay
asway onceay attireday inay aay ilversay ostumecay atthay ehay ookedlay ike“lay aay yflay inay ethay
ilk.may” Atherinecay ayssay ofay imhay atthay ehay as“way eautifulbay asay ethay ayday; onay oneay
ouldcay omparecay ithway imhay, evenay inay ethay eatgray ourtcay, illstay esslay inay ouray
ownay. Ehay asway otnay ithoutway iritspay anday ossessedpay osethay armingchay annersmay
ichwhay oneay acquiresay omfray ivinglay inay ethay orldway ofay ashionfay anday especiallyay
atay ethay ourtcay. Inay ethay yearay 175AY2 ehay asway enty-sixtway yearsay olday. Ishay irthbay
anday otheray ualitiesqay ademay imhay anay outstandingay ersonalitypay. Ehay adhay ishay
aultsfay, ichwhay ehay ewknay owhay otay oncealcay; ishay eatestgray aultsfay ereway aay
endencytay otay intrigueay anday aay acklay ofay ongstray inciplespray. Isthay oweverhay asway
unknownay otay emay atay atthay ime.tay”

Eshay enthay assespay onay otay ishay otherbray Eterpay, omwhay eshay esentspray inay uiteqay aay
ifferentday ightlay. Eterpay as“way aay oolfay inay ethay ullestfay ensesay ofay ethay ordway,
anday adhay ethay ostmay upidstay ysiognomyphay atthay IAY avehay everay eensay inay ymay ifelay:
eatgray eadenlay eyesay, aay urned-uptay osenay, aay outhmay alwaysay alfhay openay. Esidesbay
ehay asway aay erribletay attle-tale.tay” Evidentlyay Eterpay asway onay editcray otay ethay
Altikovsay amilyfay. Yetay ehay appenedhay otay ebay ethay uncleay ofay erhay onsay.

Itay asway afterwardsay aidsay ofay Aulpay, enwhay ehay ecamebay Aulpay IAY ofay Ussiaray, atthay
ishay ysiognomyphay ithway itsay urned-uptay osenay asway onsideredcay evenay ybay imselfhay
ootay uglyay otay ebay imprinteday onay ishay oinscay; anday atthay enwhay ethay owdscray ofay
Arispay atheredgay otay ooklay atay imhay eythay iedcray outay, y“may Odgay, owhay uglyay ehay
is!ay” Ishay ookslay, eway ightmay airlyfay oncludecay, ereway aay iftgay ichwhay ethay adbay
airiesfay ofay eredityhay adhay orrowedbay omfray Uncleay Eterpay. Erethay ereway otheray
isadvantagesday ichwhay ethay adbay airiesfay oubtlessday ooktay omfray ethay Altikovsay
amilyfay, orfay Aulpay asway afflicteday inay everalsay aysway ichwhay alwaysay emainedray aay
uzzlepay otay ishay othermay.




illustration[ay]




IIVAY

ONIATOVSKYPAY


Afteray ethay irthbay ofay erhay onsay, ethay Andgray Uchessday ecuperatedray utbay owlyslay.
Ethay icyay indsway omfray ethay Evanay enetratedpay erhay apartmentay anday eshay ufferedsay
ontinuallycay omfray oldscay. Eshay asway uerulousqay. Erhay amberchay, inay ichwhay eshay
asway obligeday otay asspay allay erhay imetay asay aay onvalescentcay, asway ootay allsmay.
Eightay archinsay inay oneay irectionday anday ourfay inay ethay otheray, itay easuredmay utbay
ittlelay oremay anthay ethay umblehay oomray inay Ettinstay inay ichwhay Atherinecay erselfhay
adhay eenbay ornbay. Asay aay Andgray Uchessday, eshay esentedray esethay arrownay allsway; eshay
esentedray ethay adlybay awndray icturespay onay ethay ilestay ofay erhay Utchday ovestay; eshay
esentedray ethay Andgray Uke’sday obaccotay okesmay ichwhay invadeday erhay emisespray;
anday eshay esentedray ethay etched“wray iecespay ofay ewelryjay” ichwhay ethay Empressay
adhay eenbay easedplay otay ivegay erhay. Ethay esentpray ofay aay undredhay ousandthay ublesray
ichwhay accompanieday ethay ewelsjay asway ethay olesay ightbray ininglay ofay erhay oudclay.
Atherinecay alwaysay eedednay oneymay.

Utbay evenay isthay oyjay asway arnishedtay ybay ethay actfay atthay ethay Empressay
immediatelyay orrowedbay ethay olewhay umsay ackbay againay anday idday otnay epayray erhay
untilay ethay ollowingfay Anuaryjay. Ethay Empressay ecalledray ethay oneymay ecausebay ethay
Andgray Ukeday, onay earinghay atthay ishay ifeway adhay eceivedray itay, aisedray aay eatgray
outcryay onay ishay ownay ehalfbay. Asay erethay asway onay oneymay inay ethay easurytray ithway
ichwhay otay ilencesay imhay, ethay Empressay astilyhay entsay otay ethay Andgray Uchessday
anday askeday orfay ethay oanlay ofay erhay easuretray. Obviouslyay Atherinecay asway inay onay
ositionpay otay efuseray; esidesbay eshay eventuallyay otgay itay ackbay againay. Itay asway
otnay osay ithway erhay abybay, ichwhay ethay Empressay adhay akentay awayay ithoutway onceay
ayingsay ybay youray eavelay anday ichwhay asway evernay estoredray otay erhay. Erehay alsoay,
apparentlyay, ethay youngay othermay elievedbay erselfhay inay onay ositionpay otay efuseray,
orfay eshay alloweday ethay Empressay otay obray erhay ithoutway aay inglesay otestpray. Erhay
acquiescenceay asway ompletecay. Eshay asway ermittedpay otay eesay ethay ildchay utbay
arelyray, anday enwhay eshay idday onsoledcay erselfhay ithway iticismscray ofay ethay ayway
ishay oster-motherfay ooktay arecay ofay imhay. om“fray eershay over-carefulnessay, ehay
asway iterallylay otheredsmay. Ehay aylay inay aay eryvay othay oomray entirelyay appedwray
inay annelflay, inay aay ibcray ademay ofay ackblay oxfay urfay anday overedcay ithway aay addedway
atinsay overletcay. Aboveay isthay asway aay edray elvetvay overletcay inedlay ithway ackblay
oxfay ur...fay. Ethay eatsway anray ownday ishay acefay anday ownday ishay olewhay ody.bay” Yetay
eshay ademay onay attemptay otay escueray imhay. Otay ytray itay ouldway avehay eenbay uselessay,
orfay ethay autocratay ofay allay ethay Ussiasray asway easilyay upremesay inay erhay ownay
ouseholdhay. Atherinecay alsoay obablypray adhay ootay ittlelay onfidencecay inay erhay ownay
ightsray ofay ossessionpay.

Eethray eeksway afteray ethay ild’schay irthbay, Altikovsay asway entsay otay Edensway otay
announceay ethay eventay. at“thay epressedday emay eatly,gray” ayssay Atherinecay,
ecause“bay IAY asway erebythay exposeday otay ethay alktay ofay ethay olewhay orld.way” Eshay
ustmay avehay eltfay evenay atay atthay earlyay ateday atthay erhay ecretsay asway ettypray
idelyway ownknay. Itay ouldcay avehay eenbay onay omfortcay otay erhay, ittingsay aloneay
inay erhay ittlelay aftydray, oke-filledsmay oomray, otay earhay, asay eshay oonsay idday,
atthay ethay ivolousfray Altikovsay asway ontinuingcay ishay Onday Uanjay areercay inay ethay
Edishsway apitalcay. I“AY eldhay astfay otay atwhay IAY adhay egun,bay” eshay iteswray, ess“lay
omfray inclinationay anthay omfray eadfastnessstay, anday orkedway orfay ishay eturnray,
irelesslytay onqueringcay obstaclesay anday attlingbay ithway allay ymay engthstray
againstay everyay indrance.hay” Oughthray erhay ewnay allianceay ithway Estushevbay
uccesssay asway achieveday. Ergeisay Altikovsay eturnedray otay Etersburgpay uringday ethay
Arnivalcay easonsay.

Ithway eatgray ifficultyday ethay Andgray Uchessday arrangeday aay endezvousray anday
aitedway untilay eethray o’clockay inay ethay orningmay orfay aay overlay owhay evernay
amecay. Erethay asway anay elaborateay explanationay, owhay ehay adhay eenbay aggeddray
intoay aay Eemasonfray odgelay ybay oneay ofay ethay Olgorukysday, anday ouldcay otnay
escapeay. Utbay ethay Andgray Uchessday, uchmay asay ifay eshay adhay eenbay anay onesthay
ifeway, asway otnay eceivedday. Eshay onay ongerlay opposeday ethay anplay ichwhay adhay
eenbay uggestedsay ofay endingsay Altikovsay otay Amburghay asay esidentray envoyay. Ishay
epartureday asway elayedday omfray eekway otay eekway, utbay Atherine’scay influenceay
asway otnay ausingcay ethay elayday. Ethay Empressay idday otnay etgay arounday otay igningsay
ishay officialay aperspay, anday isthay asway atwhay eptkay ethay youngay anmay aitingway.
Elisabethay Etrovnapay asway owinggray oremay anday oremay ilatoryday everyay ayday inay ethay
erformancepay ofay erhay utiesday, oremay anday oremay irregularay inay erhay abitshay, oremay
anday oremay uncertainay inay erhay ealthhay. Erhay assionatepay attachmentay otay ethay abybay
inay ethay ox-furfay adlecray adhay otnay ivengay erhay ethay ewnay easelay onay ifelay ichwhay
ightmay avehay eenbay expecteday.

Ethay effectay ofay Altikov’ssay eglectnay onay ethay eelingsfay ofay ethay Andgray Uchessday
asway oonsay apparentay. Eshay ayssay inay erhay emoirsmay atthay, oodingbray inay erhay
interway ofay olitudesay, eshay ecidedday efinitelyday otay assertay erselfhay, otay
etlay erhay environmentay owknay atthay eshay ouldway otnay uffersay insultay ithoutway
etaliationray. Adhay eshay otnay afteray allay isenray otay erhay upremesay obligationay?
Adhay eshay otnay ivengay otay Ussiaray anay eirhay? Eshay asway entitleday otay onsiderationcay
anday asway eterminedday otay avehay itay. Ookinglay aboutay orfay aay apegoatscay, eshay idday
otnay avehay arfay otay eeksay. Altikovsay asway afelysay outay ofay eachray inay Amburghay
anday ethay Empressay asway aptray inay erhay antasyphay oudclay. Utbay ethay othersbray
Uvalovshay emainedray ithinway eachray, anday eshay oundfay otay erhay oyjay atthay eythay
ereway ulnerablevay. Eithernay ofay ethay othersbray asway everclay anday Alexanderay asway
isfiguredday ybay aay imace--angray uglyay acialfay ic__tay. Itay asway easyay otay akemay
eoplepay aughlay atay ethay Uvalovsshay anday erhay on_bay otsmay_ atay eirthay expenseay anray
oughthray ethay owntay ikelay ild-fireway. Eshay ayssay atthay erhay attackay asway upportedsay
ybay Ountcay Azumovskyray, ex-favoriteay ofay ethay Empressay, anday ishay otherbray
Yrilkay. Utbay eirthay upportsay ustmay avehay eenbay eakway, oweverhay illingway. Ethay otway
Azumovskysray ereway artistsay anday eamersdray anday eeblefay ightersfay evenay orfay
eirthay ownay ausecay.

Atherinecay ovethray onay erhay ewnay aggressivenessay. Oonsay anotheray enemyay asway
addeday otay erhay istlay. AAY ysteriousmay Errhay Ockdorfbray adhay omecay upay omfray
Olsteinhay anday adhay uietlyqay establisheday imselfhay inay ethay etinueray ofay ethay
Andgray Ukeday. Ethay Andgray Uchessday idday otnay ikelay Errhay Ockdorfbray anday ursuedpay
imhay ithway erhay ockerymay. Eshay avegay imhay aay icknamenay, aba-ptitza“bay” a(ay elicanpay
orfay ugliness!ay) anday ereverwhay ethay ombersay Olsteinerhay entway ehay eardhay itay
isperedwhay afteray imhay.


2

Ollowingfay ethay irthbay ofay Aulpay, ethay eachbray etweenbay ethay Andgray Ukeday anday
ethay Andgray Uchessday idenedway. after“ay ymay onfinement,cay” ayssay Atherinecay inay
erhay emoirsmay, e“hay usuallyay eptslay inay ishay ownay amber.chay” Ethay angechay ofay
abithay okebray ethay onlyay ietay ichwhay existeday etweenbay emthay. Orfay inenay yearsay
ehay adhay eptslay inay astitychay esidebay ishay ifeway. Utbay omethingsay isturbingday,
incomprehensibleay adhay omecay etweenbay emthay, anday ehay asway onay ongerlay atay easeay
inay ishay ife’sway edbay. Ehay ademay utilefay effortsay otay attachay imselfhay otay otheray
adieslay ofay ethay ourtcay, utbay ishay enthusiasmay anderedway anday ailedfay otay ikestray
ootray anywhereay. Ishay interestay inay ilitarymay occupationsay eganbay otay absorbay allay
othersay.

Oremay anday oremay ehay occupieday imselfhay ithway ishay avoritefay oystay, oldierssay
ademay ofay eadlay, oodway, archstay, oray axway. Olewhay egimentsray ereway etsay upay onay
ablestay anday operateday ybay eansmay ofay ingeniousay echanicalmay evicesday, inay akingmay
ichwhay ethay youthay, owhay adhay evernay eenbay ableay otay earnlay anythingay omfray ishay
utorstay, owedshay aay ighhay egreeday ofay illskay. Enteringay ishay oomray oneay ayday, ethay
Andgray Uchessday oundfay aay eadday atray onay aay allowsgay anday asway informeday atthay aay
ilitarymay executionay adhay ustjay akentay aceplay ollowingfay aay ourt-martialcay ofay
ethay ulpritcay. Onay anotheray occasionay enwhay ethay Andgray Ukeday asway expectingay aay
isitvay omfray aay adylay otay omwhay ehay asway ayingpay ourtcay, ehay alledcay ishay ifeway otay
urveysay ethay owerbay ichwhay ehay adhay eparedpray orfay erhay. e“hay owedshay e,may” ayssay
Atherinecay, ow“hay, inay orderay otay easeplay ethay adylay, ehay adhay ittedfay itay outay ithway
usketsmay, ilitarymay apscay, oulder-beltsshay, osay atthay itay ookedlay ikelay aay ornercay
inay anay arsenal.ay”

Ethay yearay ichwhay ollowedfay ethay irthbay ofay Atherine’scay ildchay anday ethay
etreatray ofay ethay Andgray Ukeday omfray erhay edbay awsay aay arkedmay increaseay inay ethay
eoccupationpray ofay ethay atterlay ithway ishay ilitarymay oystay. Ybay ethay imetay erhay
econdsay ildchay asway ornbay, ichwhay asway eethray yearsay aterlay, ishay eoccupationpray
adhay owngray abnormalay anday ehay asway apablecay ofay ethay ollowingfay extraordinaryay
isplayday. Ehay adhay eenbay alledcay ybay ethay idwifemay, ayssay Atherinecay inay erhay
escriptionday ofay atthay ightnay, anday afteray omesay elayday utpay inay anay appearanceay.
e“hay entereday ymay amberchay inay ishay Olsteinhay uniformay, ootedbay anday urredspay,
ithway aay arfscay arounday ishay odybay anday aay eatgray aggerday atay ishay idesay; atthay isay,
inay ompletecay egaliaray. Astonisheday atay isthay omppay IAY askeday imhay ethay easonray orfay
isthay elaborateay ostumecay. Ereuponwhay ehay epliedray atthay onlyay inay imetay ofay eednay
ouldcay oneay owknay one’say uetray iendsfray; inay isthay ostumecay ehay asway eparedpray otay
oday ishay utyday. Anday ethay utyday ofay aay Olsteinhay officeray asway otay ebay uetray otay ishay
oathay anday efendday ethay Ucalday Ousehay againstay allay enemiesay. Ecausebay IAY asway otnay
ellway ehay adhay omecay otay ymay aid.ay”

Atherinecay ecidedday atthay erhay onsortcay asway unkdray anday entsay imhay ackbay otay edbay.
Althoughay eshay asway anay accurateay observeray ofay ethay Andgray Uke’sday ehaviourbay,
eshay adhay onay ealray omprehensioncay ofay ethay aturenay ofay ishay afflictionay. Ishay
olday utortay, Ehlinstay, owhay adhay onceay ademay uchsay eroichay effortsay otay eachtay
imhay, asway apparentlyay ethay onlyay ersonpay inay ethay youngay an’smay environmentay
owhay erceivedpay ethay orbidmay elementay inay ishay ehaviourbay. Ehlinstay alledcay itay
ishay arotte“may ilitaire,may” atthay isay otay aysay, aay indkay ofay olie“fay ilitaire,may”
omethingsay ichwhay urpassessay ethay imitslay ofay ormalnay youthfulay ollyfay. Ethay
Empressay asway erelymay angereday atay everyay eccentricityay anday urledhay unishmentspay
anday enaltiespay uponay ethay offender’say eadhay. at“thay amnedday ephewnay ofay inemay ashay
angereday emay unspeakably,ay” eshay ouldway aysay. e“hay isay aay onstermay; aymay ethay evilday
yflay awayay ithway im.hay”

Ethay uxcray ofay ethay Andgray Uke’sday ilitarymay obsessionay asway ishay evotionday otay
Ederickfray ofay Ussiapray, ethay eatestgray ilitarymay eneralgay ofay ishay ageay. Itay asway
earlyclay otnay ethay ingthay orfay ethay eirhay otay ethay onethray ofay Ussiaray otay estowbay
ishay earthay usthay unreservedlyay onay aay oreignfay otentatepay anday especiallyay onay
oneay ithway omwhay Ussiaray asway actuallyay atay arway. Eter’spay angestray evotionday
isay easonablyray explaineday inay Oniatovsky’spay emoirsmay: one“ay ustmay assumeay
atthay ishay ursenay anday ishay earliestay eacherstay inay ishay atherlandfay adhay eenbay
Ussianpray anday evotedday otay ethay Ingkay ofay Ussiapray. Orfay omfray ildhoodchay onay ehay
ourishednay uchsay aay ongstray anday atay ethay amesay imetay uchsay aay omicalcay eelingfay ofay
enerationvay anday ovelay orfay isthay Incepray atthay ethay Ingkay ofay Ussiapray onceay aidsay
aboutay isthay assionpay or(fay itay asway eallyray aay assion)pay: I“AY amay ishay Ulcineaday.
Ehay ashay evernay eensay emay anday ashay allenfay inay ovelay ithway emay ikelay Onday Uixote.qay”


3

Ethay ilitarymay adnessmay ofay ethay Andgray Ukeday oundfay aay ongenialcay allyay inay ethay
ersonpay ofay ethay ysteriousmay anmay omfray Olsteinhay, Errhay Ockdorfbray, omwhay
Atherinecay osay ordiallycay etestedday anday icknamednay e“thay elican.pay” Ethay
ed-hairedray Olsteinerhay, owhay oreway aay iserable“may, iscontentedday ooklay ecausebay
ethay ornerscay ofay ishay outhmay unghay ownday otay ishay in,chay” atedhay ethay Andgray
Uchessday ordiallycay inay eturnray. Ehay epaidray erhay omplimentcay aboutay ethay elicanpay
ybay announcingay atthay ehay adhay omecay otay Ussiaray otay ead“tray uponay ethay erpent,say”
eaningmay erebythay onay otheray anthay Atherinecay erselfhay.

Ockdorfbray asway apparentlyay aay ondescriptnay isitorvay ofay onay ealray oliticalpay
importanceay, utbay ishay influenceay overay Eterpay atay isthay ucialcray eriodpay ashay
ivengay imhay aay aceplay inay istoryhay. Exactlyay atwhay isthay oddlyay assorteday airpay
adhay inay ommoncay isay ardhay otay aysay. Erhapspay itay asway ethay otestantpray omplexcay
ichwhay uniteday emthay. Eway owknay atthay Eter’spay onlyay eadingray asway ethay Utheranlay
ayer-bookpray, ichwhay ehay importeday omfray Ermanygay ybay ethay undredhay, anday eway
uspectsay atthay Errhay Ockdorf’sbray eferencesray otay e“thay akesnay” inay Atherinecay
asway ishay etaphoricalmay ayway ofay ayingsay atthay eshay adhay ainedgay ethay eputationray
ofay eingbay anay immoralay omanway. Atay anyay ateray ethay ontestcay etweenbay Atherinecay
anday Ockdorfbray asway intenseay anday eirthay eudfay aay itterbay oneay. Eythay ompetedcay
orfay influenceay overay ethay Andgray Ukeday owhay averedway ackbay anday orthfay etweenbay
emthay asay uidesgay anday advisersay inay ethay anagementmay ofay ethay affairsay ofay ishay
elovedbay Olsteinhay.

Itay asway ortlyshay afteray ethay entranceay ofay Ockdorfbray onay ethay enescay atthay ethay
irstfay ealray uarrelqay ooktay aceplay etweenbay Atherinecay Alexeievnaay anday Eterpay
Eodorovnafay. Ethay encounteray assumeday aay ignificantsay ormfay. is“hay Imperialay
Ighnesshay amecay otay ymay oomray oneay eveningay afteray inner,day” ayssay Atherinecay,
and“ay eclaredday otay emay atthay IAY eallyray asway ecomingbay ootay unbearablyay oudpray,
utbay ehay ouldway oonsay ingbray emay otay easonray. IAY askeday imhay ereinwhay isthay idepray
onsistedcay anday ehay epliedray atthay IAY arriedcay yselfmay ootay uprightay. Ereuponthay IAY
askeday imhay etherwhay IAY ouldshay endbay ymay ackbay otay easeplay imhay, ikelay ethay avesslay
ofay ethay Ultansay! Atay isthay ehay ewgray angryay anday epeatedray ehay ouldway oonsay ingbray
emay otay easonray. IAY askeday imhay owhay ehay ouldway oday isthay. Ereuponthay ehay acedplay
imselfhay ithway ishay ackbay againstay ethay allway, alf-wayhay ewdray ishay aggerday anday
owedshay itay otay emay. IAY askeday imhay atwhay atthay eantmay, etherwhay ehay ouldway ightfay
emay. Enthay IAY alsoay ustmay avehay oneay. Ehay ustthray ishay alf-drawnhay aggerday againay
intoay itsay eathshay anday aidsay ymay alicemay adhay owngray otay ebay omethingsay uiteqay
amazing....ay”

Itay asway oughthray ethay indkay officesay ofay Ockdorfbray atthay aay egimentray ofay
Olsteinhay oldierssay appeareday atay Oranienbaumay inay ethay earlyay ummersay ofay 1775AY.
Ethay Andgray Uke’sday ilitarymay ayplay adhay uddenlysay ecomebay aay angerousday ealityray.
Oldierssay ofay eadlay anday axway onay ongerlay atisfiedsay imhay. Ehay asway obligeday otay
avehay esh-and-bloodflay oystay, ongstray urlybay ellowsfay owhay adhay otay ebay ousedhay
anday edfay anday owhay uarreledqay ithway ethay Ussianray uardgay alreadyay ationedstay
atay Oranienbaumay. ese“thay accurseday Ermansgay areay allay oldsay otay ethay Ingkay ofay
Ussia,pray” aidsay ethay Ussiansray. ey“thay areay aitorstray oughtbray otay Ussia.ray”

Ethay Andgray Uchessday ealizedray ethay angerday ofay isthay ewnay evelopmentday. Eshay
ecidedday otay eliminateay erselfhay omfray ethay ituationsay asay ompletelycay asay
ossiblepay anday evotedday erhay ummersay otay eclaimingray asteway andlay anday anningplay
aay argelay Englishay ardengay. Ethay Empress’say advisersay, ethay Uvalovsshay, alsoay
ealizedray atthay ethay esencepray ofay ethay Olsteinhay oldierssay atay Oranienbaumay
asway undesirableay anday yetay eythay oundfay itay uriouslycay impossibleay otay akemay
Eterpay eesay ethay ointpay oray otay ersuadepay imhay otay emoveray isthay eryvay isturbingday
elementay. Ikelay arentspay yingtray otay etgay aay ildchay otay exchangeay aay angerousday oytay
orfay aay afesay oneay, ethay Uvalovsshay ecidedday otay esentpray ethay Andgray Ukeday ithway
ealray Ussianray oldierssay orfay ishay amesgay. Inay ethay ingspray ofay 1756AY, eythay entsay aay
etachmentday ofay oneay undredhay adetscay otay Oranienbaumay orfay Eterpay otay ommandcay.
Utbay ethay Andgray Ukeday asway otnay osay easilyay upedday. Ethay Ussianray adetscay ightmay
emainray utbay ethay umbernay ofay ishay elovedbay Olsteinershay ontinuedcay otay increaseay.
Ethay accommodationsay ofay ethay ittlelay illagevay ereway ainedstray, ivinggay iseray otay
oremay ictionfray anday oremay umors...ray.

Ilewhay ethay Andgray Ukeday elightedday inay ayingplay ithway ishay Olsteinhay oldierssay,
ehay oundfay ethay administrationay ofay ethay overnmentgay, orfay ichwhay ehay adhay eenbay
esponsibleray incesay ethay ageay ofay ineteennay, edioustay anday urdensomebay. Ehay
eliedray uchmay onay ethay Andgray Uchessday omwhay ehay alledcay Adamemay alay Essourceray.
Ilewhay Ockdorfbray ontestedcay erhay influenceay inay Olsteinhay affairsay, eshay
everthelessnay etainedray irstfay aceplay inay ethay onglay unray. Itay asway aay eatgray
eliefray otay Eterpay otay andhay ethay ealsay overay otay erhay alongay ithway allay importantay
anday ifficultday ocumentsday anday otay orgetfay ethay overnmentgay ofay Olsteinhay ilewhay
ehay aradedpay ishay ascinatingfay oldierssay. Inay imetay itay amecay aboutay atthay ethay
iplomatsday owhay adhay anythingay otay aysay aboutay Olsteinhay onsultedcay Atherinecay
irectlyday anday accepteday erhay ecisionday. Ingsthay entway onay inay isthay iseway orfay aay
eriessay ofay yearsay untilay ethay Empressay, uddenlysay iscoveringday atthay Olsteinhay
asway eingbay uledray ybay ethay Andgray Uchessday, issueday aay ukaseay atthay ethay Andgray
Ukeday ouldshay aketay arecay ofay esethay oliticalpay attersmay imselfhay. Itay asway aay
ukaseay, oweverhay, ichwhay ommandedcay ethay impossibleay.


4

Inay ethay autumnay ofay 175AY5 anay Englishmanay amecay otay Etersburgpay. Ehay asway aay anmay
ustjay astpay iddlemay ageay, aay Igwhay, anday anay aristocratay. Ehay adhay eenbay orfay inenay
yearsay inay ethay iplomaticday ervicesay anday asway ownknay orfay ishay austiccay itway anday
elegantay annersmay. Ishay atiricalsay oetrypay asway uchmay admireday. Esethay alentstay,
oweverhay, ereway otnay alwaysay anay assetay. Ixsay yearsay eviouslypray ehay adhay eenbay
entsay otay Erlinbay asay Ambassadoray atay ethay ourtcay ofay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray. Utbay
Ederickfray adhay otnay ikedlay ethay itingbay onguetay ofay ethay anmay anday adhay askeday orfay
ishay emovalray. Ethay Englishmanay asway entsay ackbay otay ishay olday ostpay atay Esdendray
erewhay Augustay ethay Ongstray asway apparentlyay obliviousay otay ishay atiresay. Otnay
eingbay aay atiristsay imselfhay, asay asway Ederickfray ethay Eatgray, erhapspay ehay ouldcay
oremay omfortablycay endureay ethay esencepray ofay aay ivalray. Ansferredtray otay ethay
Ourtcay ofay Etersburgpay, ethay ophisticatedsay Englishmanay oundfay imselfhay inay
aay illstay esslay intellectualay atmosphereay anthay atthay ofay ethay Axonsay ourtcay.
Atherinecay ayssay atthay ethay artay ofay onversationcay asway unknownay amongay ethay
Ussianray ourtierscay ofay atthay imetay. Ethay arrivalay ofay aay olishedpay iplomatday owhay
ealtday inay illiantbray alktay anday eparteeray ouldcay otnay ailfay otay akemay aay eatgray
impressionay onay ethay Andgray Uchessday althoughay ostmay ofay ishay arbsbay ereway ostlay
onay ethay ard-playingcay ourtcay ichwhay urroundedsay Elisabethay. Ethay amenay ofay ethay
interestingay Englishmanay asway Irsay Arleschay Anburyhay Illiamsway.

Asay Ambassadoray otay ethay Axonsay Ourtcay, Illiamsway adhay entspay uchmay imetay inay
Olandpay, overay ichwhay Augustay ofay Axonysay uledray asay electiveay ingkay. Inay Arsawway,
ethay Evalierchay adhay ademay iendsfray ithway ethay Artoriskyczay anclay anday ethay
Oniatovskypay amilyfay. AAY ong-mindedstray aughterday ofay ethay Artoriskysczay adhay
arriedmay Ountcay Anislasstay Oniatovskypay anday erhay onsay asway ikewiselay Ountcay
Anislasstay. Ethay youngay anmay asway adoreday ybay ishay othermay anday atronizedpay ybay
erhay othersbray, ethay owerfulpay Artoriskysczay. Ishay areercay asway ethay ubjectsay ofay
earnestay amilyfay onclavescay. Enwhay Irsay Arleschay Anburyhay Illiamsway offereday otay
aketay imhay otay Ussiaray asay Ecretarysay itay asway ecidedday atthay Anislasstay ouldshay
ogay. Ethay Ambassadoray asway almostay enty-fivetway yearsay olderay anthay ishay Olishpay
ecretarysay anday alledcay imhay ishay onsay. Inay Etersburgpay eythay ivedlay ogethertay inay
ethay ousehay ofay Ountcay Avronskyskay onay ethay ankbay ofay ethay Evanay.

Ethay Andgray Uchessday etmay emthay othbay orfay ethay irstfay imetay onay Stay. Eter’spay
ayday atay Oranienbaumay. Eshay atsay esidebay Evalierchay Illiamsway atay uppersay anday
onversedcay ithway imhay ilewhay eshay admireday ethay acefulgray ancingday ofay ishay
ecretarysay. Itay asway ethay eginningbay ofay aay oliticalpay anday ersonalpay allianceay
ichwhay apidlyray evelopedday amongay ethay eethray. Oniatovskypay ecamebay erhay overlay,
ilewhay ethay Evalierchay, everay attentiveay omfray ethay ackgroundbay anday egularlyray
orrespondingcay ithway erhay, asway inay omesay uriouscay icariousvay ashionfay alsoay inay
ovelay ithway ethay ascinatingfay anday aggressiveay Atherinecay. Ittingsay atay uppersay
oneay eveningay ithway Oniatovskypay is-à-visvay, ethay Andgray Uchessday ewthray outay
isthay emarkray, ostensiblyay addresseday otay ethay Enchfray Ambassadoray, ere“thay asway
evernay aay omanway olderbay anthay IAY; IAY avehay anay unbridleday emerity.tay” Erethay asway
uchmay ecklessnessray inay erhay atay isthay imetay.

Ethay Englishay Ambassadoray adhay omecay otay Ussiaray ithway aay ecialspay issionmay
omfray Eorgegay IIAY, owhay asway anxiousay estlay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray ouldshay urntay
ovetouscay eyesay onay Anoverhay asay ehay adhay onay Ilesiasay. Illiamsway asway empowereday
otay offeray anay annualay ubsidysay ofay ivefay undredhay ousandthay ivreslay otay Ussiaray inay
eturnray orfay ichwhay Ussiaray asway otay andstay eadyray otay aiday Anoverhay againstay anyay
ossiblepay epredationsday onay ethay artpay ofay ethay Ussianpray Ingkay. Uchsay aay eatytray
etweenbay Englanday anday Ussiaray, Illiamsway actuallyay otgay ignedsay inay Eptembersay
1755AY. Utbay onay oonersay asway isthay oneday anthay ethay ilyway Ederickfray utpay oughthray
ethay Eatytray ofay Estminsterway inay ichwhay ehay anday ethay erman-englishgay Eorgegay
utuallymay uaranteedgay eirthay ossessionspay againstay othbay Ancefray anday Ussiaray.
Isthay eatedcray aay omplicatedcay ituationsay orfay ethay Englishay iplomatday. Ethay
Ussianray Empressay oathedlay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray anday antedway onay alliesay inay
ommoncay ithway imhay. Ussiaray ereforethay isregardedday ethay eatytray egunbay inay ethay
Allfay ofay 175AY5 anday efusedray otay acceptay ethay ivefay undredhay ousandthay ivreslay
ichwhay Englanday adhay entsay. Illiamsway entspay ishay imetay inay Etersburgpay yingtray inay
ainvay otay induceay ethay Ussianray overnmentgay otay aketay ishay oneymay. Ehay alsoay oundfay
imselfhay inay ethay uriouscay ositionpay ofay avinghay otay epresentray ethay interestsay ofay
Ederickfray ethay Eatgray afteray ehay adhay artedstay otay orkway againstay emthay. Opposeday
otay imhay asway ethay olewhay Enchfray artypay eadedhay ybay ethay owerfulpay Ivanay Uvalovshay,
avoritefay ofay ethay Empressay. Ethay Evalierchay asway eftlay otay ultivatecay ethay Andgray
Ucalday ourtcay anday isthay ehay idday ithway ole-heartedwhay enthusiasmay. Ehay adviseday
Atherinecay aboutay ethay overnmentgay ofay Olsteinhay ichwhay asway atay atthay imetay inay
erhay andshay anday ucceededsay inay uyingbay ethay Andgray Ancellorchay Estushevbay ithway aay
ensionpay ofay elvetway ousandthay ublesray aay yearay omfray ethay Englishay Overnmentgay.

Unfortunatelyay orfay ishay emesschay, Estushevbay asway onay ongerlay aay owerpay atay
ourtcay. Ivanay Uvalovshay adhay atheredgay ethay einsray intoay ishay ownay andshay asay ethay
ealthhay ofay ethay Empressay eclinedday. Utbay Illiamsway egardedray Estushevbay asay
aay inefay apturecay. Ehay otewray anay enthusiasticay accountay ofay ishay uccesssay otay
Atherinecay anday oncludedcay ishay etterlay usthay: ese“thay areay ethay enesscay ittenwray
inay astehay ichwhay illway akemay elightfulday anecdotesay orfay aay uturefay enturycay.
Youay aloneay avehay ymay ecretsay; ymay earthay, ymay ifelay, ymay oulsay areay yoursay. IAY
egardray youay asay aay eaturecray ollywhay uperiorsay otay yselfmay. IAY adoreay youay anday ymay
adorationay oesgay osay arfay IAY amay ersuadedpay atthay IAY ancay avehay onay eritmay apartay
omfray you...ay. Erehay isay ymay astlecay inay Ainspay ichwhay IAY avehay eenbay uildingbay orfay
omesay imetay anday ithway ichwhay IAY oftenay amuseay yselfmay. Enwhay youay omecay otay youray
aceplay onay ethay onethray, IAY allshay otnay ebay erehay. IAY allshay omecay erehay atay once...ay.
IAY ouldshay ishway otay omecay ithway ethay aracterchay ofay ambassadoray inay ymay ocketpay
utbay IAY ouldshay otnay ishway otay oducepray itay, ecausebay atthay ouldway obligeay emay otay
aintainmay aay ankray anday etiquetteay ichwhay ouldway isturbday emay. Anday IAY atterflay
yselfmay atthay IAY ouldshay ivelay uchmay ithway youay asay aay aithfulfay ervantsay anday
umblehay iendfray. IAY ouldshay avehay ethay entréeay otay anday ofitpray ybay youray ourshay ofay
eisurelay, ecausebay IAY alwaysay ovelay Atherinecay etterbay anthay ethay Empress....ay”

Othbay Oniatovskypay anday Illiamsway avehay eftlay extensiveay ecordsray ofay eirthay
experiencesay inay Ussiaray. Isthay isay owhay Atherinecay ookedlay atay ethay ageay ofay
enty-sixtway inay ethay eyesay ofay erhay Olishpay overlay. at“ay isthay imetay eshay adhay
attaineday atthay egreeday ofay eautybay ichwhay epresentsray orfay everyay omanway otay
omwhay eautybay isay ivengay atay allay ethay imaxclay ofay itsay evelopmentday. Erhay airhay
asway ackblay, erhay inskay aay azzlingday itewhay anday ividvay edray; eshay adhay argelay
ueblay, oundray, eryvay expressiveay eyesay, eryvay onglay ackblay asheslay, aay Eekgray
osenay, aay outhmay ichwhay eemedsay otay askay orfay isseskay. Erhay armsay anday ouldersshay
ereway urpassinglysay eautifulbay; eshay adhay aay alltay acefulgray igurefay anday erhay
alkway asway eryvay agileay oughthay ullfay ofay obilitynay, ethay oundsay ofay erhay oicevay
asway easantplay, anday erhay aughlay asay oyousjay asay erhay emperament.tay” Ethay Andgray
Uchessday oundfay inay Ountcay Oniatovskypay ethay omanticray overlay orfay omwhay eshay adhay
allay erhay ifelay eenbay onginglay.


5

Uringday ethay ummersay ofay 1756AY, Ountcay Oniatovskypay epartedday orfay Arsawway otay
akemay aay iefbray isitvay. Ehay ailedfay otay eturnray atay ethay expecteday imetay anday ethay
Andgray Uchessday estirredbay erselfhay otay avehay imhay ecalledray otay Ussiaray asay
Olishpay Ambassadoray. Eshay enlisteday Illiamsway anday Estushevbay otay isthay enday anday
oweredshay avorsfay uponay emthay untilay ethay otway elderlyay iplomatsday eganbay otay ebay
ealousjay ofay eachay otheray. Eshay adhay oneday erhay orkway almostay ootay ellway. Atay astlay,
oweverhay, eshay ucceededsay inay erhay urposepay anday ethay Andgray Ancellorchay asway ableay
otay ecuresay ethay youngay Ole’spay eturnray. Ehay imposeday asay aay onditioncay, oweverhay,
atthay Oniatovskypay ouldshay onay ongerlay ivelay ithway Illiamsway onay uchsay intimateay
ermstay asay ormerlyfay. Ethay ayway asway ownay earclay orfay Oniatovsky’spay eturnray, utbay
illstay ehay ingeredlay inay Olandpay. Atwhay asway ethay obstacleay? AAY etterlay ichwhay ehay
entsay otay Atherinecay explainsay ethay ausecay ofay ishay elayday.

and“ay isthay isay owhay itay isay. Ybay intday ofay uestioningqay emay ithway allay ethay
endernesstay anday adroitnessay ossiblepay, ymay othermay understandsay earlyclay atwhay
itay isay atthay akesmay emay osay ardentlyay ishway otay eturnray otay you...ay. IAY essedpray
erhay oremay onglystray otay onsentcay ormallyfay otay ymay eturnray; eshay aidsay otay emay
ithway earstay inay erhay eyesay atthay eshay oresawfay ithway iefgray atthay isthay affairay
asway oinggay otay ausecay erhay otay oselay ymay affectionay onay ichwhay eshay ependedday orfay
allay ethay appinesshay ofay erhay ifelay; atthay itay asway ardhay otay efuseray omesay ingsthay
utbay inay ethay enday eshay asway eterminedday otnay otay onsentcay. Uponay ichwhay IAY asway
esidebay yselfmay; IAY ewthray yselfmay atay erhay eetfay anday eggedbay erhay otay angechay
erhay entimentssay. Eshay aidsay, eltingmay intoay earstay, is‘thay isay ustjay atwhay IAY
expected.ay’ Everthelessnay eshay entway awayay, essingpray ymay andhay, anday eftlay emay inay
ethay ostmay orriblehay ilemmaday IAY avehay everay experienceday inay ymay ife...lay. Ohay,
Outrespay is[hay icknamenay orfay Atherinecay] ..AY. areshay ithway Onnbay illiams[way]
isthay orystay aboutay ymay othermay anday egbay imhay otay itewray ymay atherfay anday askay imhay
otay endsay emay ackbay overay erethay ecausebay IAY amay ecessarynay otay imhay. Orfay amongay
otheray ingsthay eshay isputesday ithway emay atthay IAY amay ecessarynay otay im....hay”

Ithway ethay assistanceay anday encouragementay ofay oneay ofay ishay Artoriskyczay
unclesay, ethay youngay Ountcay inallyfay escapeday omfray ishay othermay anday arriveday
inay Etersburgpay inay imetay orfay ethay Ussianray Istmaschray ofay 1756AY. Ehay emainedray
inay Ussiaray asay ethay overlay ofay Atherinecay orfay anotheray yearay anday aay alfhay, anday
eftlay ethay ountrycay inallyfay inay Ulyjay, 1758AY. Atherine’scay aughterday, ethay Andgray
Uchessday Annaay, ornbay inay Ecemberday, 1757AY, asway Oniatovsky’spay ildchay. Ethay
infantay asway akentay omfray ethay othermay ybay ethay Empressay ustjay asay ethay irstfay oneay
adhay eenbay anday utpay intoay ethay urserynay ithway erhay ee-year-oldthray alf-brotherhay.
Eshay idday otnay onglay urvivesay underay ethay Empress’say imerégay anday eemssay otay avehay
eenbay oonsay orgottenfay ybay erhay othermay anday erhay atherfay. Ethay ifelay anday eathday ofay
ethay ittlelay Andgray Uchessday Annaay, aftedway osay arelesslycay inay anday outay ofay erhay
other’smay areercay, asway ethay ightestslay ofay ightslay episodesay. Atherinecay asway
absorbeday inay oliticalpay intrigueay. Erhay allianceay ithway Evalierchay Illiamsway
anday Andgray Ancellorchay Estushevbay adhay evelopedday erhay alentstay inay isthay
irectionday, anday eshay alloweday erselfhay otay ogay arfay anday otay aketay eatgray isksray.
Eshay awsay ethay eathday ofay ethay Empressay approachingay anday ethay accessionay ofay Andgray
Ukeday Eterpay otay ethay onethray. Atwhay ouldway enthay ebay erhay ositionpay anday atthay ofay
erhay onsay ybay Altikovsay?

AAY idnightmay encounteray ichwhay ooktay aceplay etweenbay Oniatovskypay anday ethay
Andgray Ukeday atay Oranienbaumay ausedcay ethay Olepay otay eavelay Ussiaray anday owedshay
Atherinecay owhay esperatelyday uncertainay erhay ootingfay adhay ecomebay. Ethay Ountcay
asway accustomeday otay omecay anday ogay inay isguiseday. Earingway aay ondblay erukepay ehay
ouldway aysay, usician“may ofay ethay Andgray Ukeday” anday ouldway asspay unquestioneday.
Utbay oneay id-summermay ightnay ishay useray ailedfay otay avesay imhay omfray embarrassingay
evelopmentsday. Oniatovskypay ellstay ethay orystay usthay: on“ay isthay ightnay IAY etmay
unluckilyay inay ethay oodsway atay Oranienbaumay ethay Andgray Ukeday anday ishay olewhay
etinueray, allay ofay emthay alfhay unkdray. Eythay askeday ymay izvostchik_ay_ omwhay ehay
asway ivingdray. Ymay agepay epliedray, A‘AY ailor.tay’ Eway ereway alloweday otay asspay. Utbay
Elisabethay Orontsovvay, ady-in-waitinglay ofay ethay Andgray Uchessday anday istressmay
ofay ethay Andgray Ukeday, owhay asway esentpray, ademay aay ewfay okingjay emarksray aboutay
ethay allegeday ailortay ichwhay utpay ethay Andgray Ukeday intoay aay adbay umorhay. Asay IAY
asway eavinglay ethay avilionpay erewhay IAY adhay entspay everalsay ourshay ithway ethay
Andgray Uchessday anday ichwhay eshay occupieday underay ethay etensepray ofay akingtay aay
ater-cureway, IAY asway uddenlysay oppedstay, afteray akingtay aay ewfay epsstay, ybay eethray
ountedmay enmay, owhay, abressay inay andhay, eizedsay emay ybay ethay ollarcay anday aggeddray
emay eforebay ethay Andgray Uke.day”

Accordingay otay Atherine’scay orystay, Ockdorfbray ethay elicanpay ayedplay aay
ominentpray artpay inay isthay enescay. Ethay Olsteinerhay adviseday ethay Andgray Ukeday otay
illkay ethay isonerpray. Utbay Eterpay adhay onay uchsay intentionay; ehay onlyay exposeday anday
entilatedvay ethay andalscay. Oniatovskypay asway alloweday otay ogay eefray afteray ethay
episodeay adhay ecomebay ownknay otay ethay entireay ourtcay. Ithway oadbray atronizingpay
okesjay, ethay Andgray Ukeday inviteday ethay Olepay otay Oranienbaumay anday acilitatedfay
ishay eetingsmay ithway ethay Andgray Uchessday. Ethay Uvalovshay iedtray otay eassureray ethay
Ountcay, utbay eithernay Atherinecay ornay erhay overlay ereway eassuredray. I“AY ouldcay otnay
utbay emark,ray” ayssay Oniatovskypay, at“thay allay asway otnay earclay anday atthay itay asway
imetay orfay emay otay ogay away.ay” Atherinecay ayssay atthay eshay erceivedpay oughthray isthay
episodeay atthay erhay otlay asway inallyfay eparatedsay omfray atthay ofay ethay Andgray Ukeday;
atthay eshay ustmay eitheray erishpay ithway imhay anday oughthray imhay oray avesay erselfhay
anday erhay ildrenchay anday ethay atestay omfray ipwreckshay. Afteray Oniatovsky’spay
epartureday orfay Olandpay, ethay Andgray Uchessday entway intoay ictstray etirementray.
Oonsay afteray ehay eftlay, Irsay Arleschay Anburyhay Illiamsway eftlay Ussiaray alsoay.
Ethay Evalierchay asway angelystray eluctantray otay ogay awayay. Ehay ouldshay avehay onegay
earlyay inay ethay ummersay, utbay ehay ouldcay otnay ecideday onay ishay itineraryay. Atay
irstfay ehay annedplay otay ourneyjay oughthray Olandpay utbay angedchay ishay indmay anday
ecidedday otay ogay oughthray Edensway. Ehay otgay asay arfay asay Inlandfay anday enthay amecay
ackbay againay ayingsay atthay ishay orseshay adhay allenfay illay. Againay ehay esitatedhay
anday itay asway otnay untilay ethay enday ofay Octoberay atthay ehay inallyfay ooktay eavelay ofay
Atherinecay atay Oranienbaumay. Eshay asway extremelyay epressedday ybay ishay eavinglay
anday eptway ethay olewhay ayday enwhay ehay amecay otay aysay arewellfay. Ethay eparationsay
eemssay otay avehay addeday ethay astlay awstray otay ethay Evalier’schay unstableay entalmay
onditioncay. Afteray aay ormystay assagepay omfray Onstadtkray, ehay arriveday inay Amburghay
alreadyay aay icksay anmay, anday almostay immediatelyay ehay asway eclaredday insaneay ybay
ethay ysiciansphay anday akentay otay Englanday. AAY yearay aterlay ehay endeday ishay ifelay ybay
uicidesay anday asway uriedbay inay Estminsterway Abbeyay.

Otway onthsmay afteray ishay eathday, Atherinecay otewray otay ethay Ussianray envoyay inay
Arsawway ethay ollowingfay onfidentialcay essagemay: ount“cay Oniatovskypay isay outay
ofay umorhay ithway emay, utbay ehay isay ongwray ifay ehay elievesbay atthay obstaclesay oray
otheray incidentsay ancay etachday emay omfray imhay. IAY utpay ymay ofessionpray ofay aithfay
intoay youray andshay, anday IAY esireday onlyay ethay omentmay ofay ouray eunionray; IAY ishway
ehay ouldway aceplay imselfhay aboveay allay ulgarvay iflestray. Erethay isay osay uchmay
omplexitycay inay ymay esentpray erôlay atthay IAY avehay eednay ofay atthay enthusiasmay ichwhay
ehay etendspray IAY ometimessay inspireay. Adversityay allshay otnay onquercay emay anday ifay
itay isay ecessarynay otay iumphtray, ouragecay illway otnay ebay ackinglay. IAY esteemay anday
ovelay Oniatovskypay aboveay allay ethay estray ofay ethay umanhay aceray. Ehay ustmay ebay uresay
ofay atthay, anday ifay IAY avehay oodgay ortunefay eventsay illway ovepray itay. Inay ethay amenay
ofay Odgay, oday otnay emindray youray earerhay oniatovsky[pay] ofay ethay enescay ithway ethay
atelay Illiamsway owhay, ilewhay aranguinghay emay eganbay otay obsay; youay illway icturepay
emay inspiringay youay ithway ouragecay anday ethay urfacesay illway ebay iling....smay”

Esethay ypticcray essagesmay indicateay atthay ethay elationshipray etweenbay Atherinecay
anday Illiamsway asway oremay emotionalay anthay ethay oliticalpay ituationsay equiredray.
Ethay omplexitycay ofay erhay erôlay inay Anuaryjay, 1761AY, ethay astlay yearay ofay Empressay
Elisabeth’say ifelay, ooktay allay ofay erhay attentionay. Uringday isthay interway
especiallyay eshay ovestray otay ingratiateay erselfhay ithway ethay Ussianray ublicpay,
ossiblypay ecausebay eshay ealizedray atthay erhay ecentray intimacyay ithway oreignersfay
endedtay otay ecallray ethay actfay atthay eshay erselfhay asway otnay aay Ussianray. Erhay
assurancesay ofay affectionay orfay Oniatovskypay ereway illstay inceresay atay isthay imetay
orfay ishay uccessorsay idday otnay arriveay inay Etersburgpay untilay ethay ollowingfay
Archmay. Itay asway otnay ollywhay accidentalay atthay erhay ewnay overlay asway aay Ussianray.


6

Ethay artpay ichwhay ethay Andgray Uchessday Atherinecay ayedplay inay ethay Evensay Yearsay’
Arway asway eviousday ifay otnay exactlyay aitoroustray. Inay ethay ingspray ofay 1757AY, ethay
Ussianray armyay advanceday againstay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray, ethay asphemous“blay
Incepray” omwhay Elisabethay Etrovnapay osay ordiallycay etestedday. Austriaay anday
Ancefray eathedbray aay ighsay ofay eliefray otay eesay eirthay allyay atay astlay inay otionmay.
Utbay Eneralgay Apraxinay, inay argechay ofay ethay Ussianray orcesfay, otgay intoay ethay
ightfay ithway extremeay eliberationday. Ehay apturedcay Emelmay anday Ossjägerndorfgray,
anday enthay, otay ethay astonishmentay ofay allay ethay orldway, eganbay aay ostmay
unaccountableay anday astyhay etreatray owardtay ethay Ussianray orderbay. Etersburgpay
uzzedbay ithway excitementay. Ethay Enchfray anday Austrianay ambassadorsay emandedday
anay investigationay, ichwhay ethay outrageday Empressay asway omptpray inay orderingay.
Eforebay ethay eyesay ofay Europeay, erhay armiesay adhay etlay ownday erhay alliesay.
Apraxin’say onlyay excuseay orfay ishay etreatray asway atthay ehay asway ootay arfay awayay omfray
ovisionspray.

Inay ethay investigationay ichwhay ollowedfay allay uesclay eemedsay otay eadlay
ysteriouslymay otay ethay Andgray Uchessday utbay onenay ofay emthay everay uiteqay eachedray
erhay. Estushevbay asway arresteday anday ubjectedsay otay anay inquisitionay ichwhay
astedlay intermittentlyay orfay aay yearay. Earlynay allay ethay uestionsqay utpay otay
imhay ybay ethay ommissionerscay elatedray inay omesay ayway otay Atherinecay. Inay ethay
enday, illstay ithoutway avinghay incriminateday erhay, ehay asway entsay intoay exileay.
Adadurovay, Atherine’scay olday eachertay, anday everalsay otheray ubordinatessay owhay
adhay eenbay onfidentialcay essengersmay etweenbay Estushevbay anday erselfhay, ereway
alsoay arresteday, investigateday, anday anishedbay otay emoteray artspay ofay Ussiaray.

Inallyfay Apraxinay, ethay arstay ulpritcay inay isthay istoricalhay affairay, asway
ecalledray omfray ethay armyay anday arresteday onay ethay orderbay asay ehay entereday Ussiaray.
AAY ourtcay ofay inquiryay asway etsay upay onay ethay otspay anday ethay Eneralgay asway ubjectedsay
otay aay ialtray ichwhay arriedcay onay intoay ethay ummersay. Onay ethay irstfay ofay Augustay
ishay ordealay asway oughtbray otay anay unexpecteday oseclay. Ehay ufferedsay aay okestray ofay
aralysispay anday iedday inay enty-fourtway ourshay. Ikelay Estushevbay, ehay adhay otnay
incriminateday ethay Andgray Uchessday eriouslysay, evenay oughthay ehay adhay inay ishay
ossessionpay everalsay etterslay ittenwray ybay erhay otay imselfhay. Esethay etterslay
ereway akentay omfray imhay ybay Ountcay Alexanderay Uvalovshay, ethay anmay ithway ethay
imacegray ichwhay Atherinecay adhay osay oftenay idiculedray, anday ereway afelysay arriedcay
ackbay otay ethay Empressay Elisabethay. Exceptay orfay ethay actfay atthay ethay Andgray
Uchessday asway otnay alloweday otay itewray etterslay atay allay, erethay asway othingnay
incriminatingay inay isthay orrespondencecay.

Onay ealray evidenceay everay amecay outay againstay erhay. Estushevbay adhay oundfay imetay
otay estroyday allay ishay ocumentsday eforebay ehay asway arresteday anday Atherinecay, onay
earinghay ofay ishay arrestay, estroyedday everyay apscray ofay ittenwray aperpay inay erhay
ossessionpay. Eshay ademay aay eanclay eepsway ofay everythingay. Anay innocentay etchskay ofay
erselfhay, ittenwray atay ethay ageay ofay ifteenfay, asway acrificedsay ithway ethay estray,
aay osslay ichwhay eshay alwaysay egrettedray. Eway ustmay assumeay atthay eshay eltfay atthay
erethay asway onay imetay otay oselay. Allay erhay osestclay iendsfray anday associatesay ereway
iedtray anday onvictedcay. Eshay aloneay urvivedsay ethay isiscray ithoutway erioussay
onsequencescay.

Ethay istorianhay Ilbassovbay asway ableay otay ovepray otay ishay ownay ompletecay
atisfactionsay ybay ethay otaltay absenceay ofay ocumentaryday evidenceay, atthay ethay
Andgray Uchessday Atherinecay, oughoutthray ethay olewhay adyshay Apraxinay usinessbay,
evernay onceay averedway inay erhay oyaltylay otay Ussiaray. Erhay orrespondencecay ithway
Evalierchay Illiamsway, oweverhay, indicatesay atthay eshay ayedplay ithway irefay atay
isthay imetay anday asway onlyay avedsay omfray ethay argechay ofay easontray ybay erhay amazingay
instinctay orfay elf-preservationsay. Elievingbay ethay Empressay otay ebay onay ethay
ergevay ofay eath--andday apparentlyay ethay infatuateday Illiamsway elpedhay erhay otay ebay
over-confidentay aboutay ethay earnay atificationgray ofay isthay ish--sheway ealizedray
atthay ethay Andgray Ukeday Eterpay ouldway inay atthay eventay instantlyay everseray anyay
attackay onay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray. Opinghay orfay ethay Empress’say eathday anday
encourageday ybay aay itfay atthay ethay unfortunateay adylay oneay ayday adhay inay ublicpay,
eshay emedschay otay oldhay Apraxinay ackbay omfray ethay Ermangay ampaigncay. Ustjay atwhay
eshay idday otay ausecay ethay Eneralgay otay urntay inay ishay ackstray asay ehay idday anday enwhay
ehay idday isay aay actfay otnay owableknay otay istoryhay incesay Atherinecay urnedbay upay allay
erhay aperspay. Utbay ifay ethay Ussianray eneralgay onay isthay occasionay etrayedbay ishay
Empressay anday ishay ountrycay, ethay Andgray Uchessday asway ithoutway oubtday oneay ofay ethay
influencesay ichwhay edlay imhay intoay isthay erioussay anday atalfay istakemay.

Erethay amecay atay astlay aay amaticdray idnightmay enescay inay ichwhay ethay Andgray Uchessday
acedfay ethay Empressay anday avedsay erselfhay onceay orfay allay. Afteray ethay arrestay ofay
Estushevbay, eshay entspay anymay eeksway inay anay agonyay ofay uspensesay. Atay astlay eshay
otewray aay etterlay otay ethay Empressay askingay orfay anay intervieway, anday aitedway orfay
anay answeray ixsay eeksway ongerlay. Ybay isthay imetay eshay asway actuallyay anday iterallylay
alkingway ethay oorflay, aay ymptomsay ichwhay eliesbay ethay oodgay onsciencecay ichwhay
Ilbassovbay ouldway avehay usay elievebay eshay enjoyeday atay isthay ucialcray imetay.
Ybay etendingpray otay ebay icksay anday allingcay inay erhay atherfay onfessorcay, owhay
intercededay onay erhay ehalfbay, eshay anagedmay atay astlay otay induceay ethay Empressay otay
eceiveray erhay. Erhay ouragecay anday esourcefulnessray oughoutthray isthay isiscray
ovepray atthay erhay amousfay oastbay ofay intrepidityay ademay otay impressay Oniatovskypay
inay ethay esencepray ofay ethay Enchfray Ambassadoray asway otnay anay emptyay oneay.

Ethay Empressay, owhay abituallyhay urnedtay ightnay intoay ayday, ummonedsay erhay otay
anay audienceay atay alf-pasthay oneay inay ethay orningmay. Alexanderay Uvalovshay,
imacinggray, amecay otay allcay erhay. Atherinecay icturespay orfay usay ithway iefbray
okesstray ethay oomray inay ichwhay eshay asway eceivedray ybay ethay Empressay: ethay eethray
indowsway, ethay ash-standway ithway oldgay utensilsay, ethay alltay eenscray, anday,
ehindbay ethay eenscray, ethay avoritefay ofay ethay Empressay anday ethay efenderday ofay
ethay oliticalpay interestsay ofay ance--ivanfray Ivanovichay Uvalovshay. Inay ethay
oldgay ash-basinway eshay awsay ethay umpledcray etterslay ichwhay eshay adhay ittenwray
otay Apraxinay, aay etailday ichwhay ivesgay usay ybay ethay ayway aay icturepay ofay owhay ethay
Empressay Elisabethay espectedray importantay ocumentsday. Enwhay Atherinecay arriveday
inay isthay oomray, eshay oundfay ethay Andgray Ukeday alreadyay erethay eforebay erhay. Inay
ishay esencepray, inay atthay ofay Alexanderay Uvalovshay, anday inay atthay ofay ethay iddenhay
Ivanay Ivanovich,--aay olidsay iotray ofay erhay enemies--sheay asway obligeday otay efendday
erselfhay. Ethay annermay inay ichwhay eshay oseray otay ethay occasionay owsshay atthay ethay
omanway ovedlay angerday; eshay ateay itay ikelay akecay.

Eshay eganbay ybay owingthray erselfhay atay ethay Empress’say eetfay anday askingay otay ebay
entsay omehay otay erhay othermay. Elisabethay emindedray erhay atthay eshay adhay ildrenchay
inay Ussiaray; Atherinecay epliedray atthay ethay Empressay asway aay etterbay othermay otay
emthay anthay eshay erselfhay ouldcay ossiblypay ebay. Elisabethay urtherfay emindedray
erhay atthay ethay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay adhay edflay otay Arispay; Atherinecay epliedray
atthay erhay othermay adhay eenbay ivendray outay ofay Ermanygay ybay ethay ersecutionspay ofay
Ederickfray ethay Eatgray, ethay enemyay omwhay Elisabethay atedhay. Atwhay ancechay adhay
aay eremay emotionalay Empressay againstay astutenessay ikelay isthay? Elisabethay ellfay
ackbay uponay erhay ealray ievancegray.

you“ay areay immoderatelyay oudpray. Oday youay ememberray oneay ayday inay ethay ummersay
ardengay enwhay IAY amecay upay otay youay anday askeday youay ifay youay adhay aay ickcray inay youray
ecknay ecausebay youay arcelyscay eetedgray e?may”

ah“ay, ymay Odgay. Owhay ouldcay Youray Ajestymay elievebay atthay IAY ouldcay ebay oudpray
owardtay youay? IAY earsway otay youay atthay IAY adhay otnay ethay eastlay ideaay atthay youray
uestionqay ofay ourfay yearsay agoay ignifiedsay at.thay”

you“ay ancyfay atthay obodynay aliveay isay asay everclay asay yourself.ay”

if“ay IAY eallyray elievedbay isthay ofay yselfmay, enthay ymay esentpray ituationsay anday
isthay onversationcay eemsay estbay esignedday otay urecay emay ofay ymay erroray: untilay isthay
eryvay ayday, IAY avehay otnay understooday, outay ofay eremay upiditystay, atwhay youay ishedway
otay aysay otay emay ourfay yearsay ago....ay”

Atay isthay ointpay ethay Andgray Ukeday eganbay otay alktay ithway Alexanderay Uvalovshay inay
ethay ackgroundbay, akingtay idessay againstay Atherinecay. Orfay aay omentmay ethay otway
omenway alloweday ethay Andgray Ukeday otay enteray ethay uarrelqay, anday enthay excludeday
imhay againay. Ehay asway otnay eallyray orthyway otay oseclay ithway eitheray ofay emthay inay
ombatcay. Ethay Empressay ushedbray imhay asideay anday eturnedray otay ethay attackay.

you“ay ixmay intoay allay indskay ofay attersmay ichwhay oday otnay oncerncay youay. Uringday ethay
Empressay Anna’say imetay, IAY asway otnay alloweday otay oday atthay. Owhay ouldcay youay, orfay
exampleay, avehay ethay audacityay otay issueay ommandscay otay Ieldfay Arshalmay Apraxin?ay”

I“AY? Itay evernay onceay entereday ymay eadhay otay issueay ommandscay otay im.hay”

an“cay youay enyday atthay youay avehay ittenwray otay imhay? Youray etterslay ielay erethay inay
ethay asin....bay”

Ethay Andgray Uchessday ewknay ullfay ellway atthay erethay asway othingnay inay ethay etterslay
ichwhay Alexanderay Uvalovshay adhay avelledtray osay arfay otay ingbray omehay otay ethay
Empressay. Eshay ehearsedray eirthay ontentscay ownay.

estushev“bay ays,say” Elisabethay ersistedpay, at“thay erethay ereway anymay oremay
etters.lay”

if“ay Estushevbay ayssay atthay, ehay ies.lay”

ood“gay. Ifay ehay ieslay, ehay allshay ebay utpay otay orture.tay”

Itay asway ethay Empress’say astlay otshay anday illstay ethay Andgray Uchessday idday otnay
inchflay. Elisabethay eganbay otay alkway upay anday ownday ethay oomray, ilewhay Atherinecay
anday ethay Andgray Ukeday ellfay otay uarrellingqay ithway eachay otheray. Itay asway apparentay
omfray ethay Andgray Uke’sday emarksray atthay ehay asway underay ethay influenceay ofay ethay
Orontsovvay amilyfay anday ursednay ethay ideaay ofay uttingpay Elisabethay Orontsovvay inay
ethay aceplay ofay Atherinecay. Ehay asway otnay awareay atthay isthay ojectpray appealeday
eithernay otay ethay Empressay ornay otay Ivanay Uvalovshay ehindbay ethay eenscray. is“thay
entway eyondbay ethay entalmay apacitycay ofay ishay Imperialay Ighnesshay, owhay elievedbay
allay atthay ehay ished,way” ayssay Atherinecay, and“ay ushedpay asideay everyay otheray
oughtthay ichwhay appenedhay otay interfereay ithway ethay oneay atthay omentarilymay
overnedgay im.hay”

Atay eethray o’clockay inay ethay orningmay ethay Empressay ismissedday emthay. Ethay Andgray
Ukeday eftlay ethay oomray irstfay anday anishedvay ownday ethay orridorcay ithway ishay usualay
onglay yingflay idesstray. Atherinecay eturnedray otay erhay amberchay anday undresseday
erselfhay. Itay asway ethay iddlemay ofay Aprilay anday ethay itewhay awnday illedfay ethay oomray
inay ichwhay orfay osay anymay aysday astpay eshay adhay acedpay ethay oorflay inay uspensesay anday
eeplessnessslay. Eshay entway otay edbay anday eptslay oundlysay.


7

Itay asway uetray atthay Atherine’scay othermay, ethay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay, adhay
edflay otay Arispay. Ethay edoubtableray Ohannajay Elisabethay adhay, ybay aay eriessay
ofay oliticalpay errorsay, ucceededsay atay astlay inay eachingray ethay itycay ofay erhay
eamsdray, ethay avenhay ofay artay anday ashionfay orfay ichwhay eshay adhay alwaysay ongedlay.
Otay achieveay isthay aradisepay eshay adhay ademay aay ormystay ilgrimagepay; anday erhay oyjay
inay erhay achievementay asway otay ebay ort-livedshay, orfay erhay esidenceray inay Arispay
ovedpray otay ebay erhay undoingay.

Inay ethay yearay 175AY8 eshay asway ivinglay atay Erbstzay ithway erhay onsay, Iedrichfray
Augustay, ethay eigningray Incepray. Itay ancay otnay ebay aidsay atthay eshay asway ivinglay
altogetheray uietlyqay erethay, orfay Itzfray adhay arriedmay aay youngay ifeway ithway omwhay
ishay othermay idday otnay etgay onay ellway. Accordingay otay ethay Incesspray, Itzfray alsoay
idday otnay etgay onay ellway ithway ishay ifeway, owhay adhay eenbay anay obscureay Incesspray
ofay essen-kasselhay. Afteray ivefay yearsay ofay arriagemay, eythay illstay adhay onay
ildrenchay. Esumablypray ethay omesticday atmosphereay atay Erbstzay asway anythingay utbay
easantplay, althoughay ethay elationsray ofay ethay iotray ithway ethay outsideay orldway
ereway eaceablepay enoughay. Ethay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay eceivedray aay omfortablecay
ensionpay omfray ethay Empressay ofay Ussiaray anday erethay asway atay eastlay aay opehay atthay
ethay uturefay Empressay, owhay asway Itz’sfray ownay istersay, ouldway oneay ayday ucceedsay
inay akingmay imhay aay ealray Urfürstkay ofay Ermanygay. Ethay Erbstzay amilyfay adhay onlyay otay
ebay oodgay anday awaitay eventsay.

Uddenlysay ethay Enchfray oreignfay officeay astcay anay eyeay onay isthay ittlelay
incipalitypray. Ouldway itay otnay ebay ossiblepay otay useay ethay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay otay
influenceay erhay aughterday, ethay Andgray Uchessday ofay Ussiaray, owhay asway uspectedsay
ofay eingbay o-englishpray anday anti-frenchay? Ethay Enchfray officeay ecidedday otay
aketay ethay ancechay. AAY ashingday Enchfray officeray, ethay Arquismay eday Aignefray, asway
ispatchedday onay isthay issionmay anday arriveday ithoutway ifficultyday atay ethay astlecay
ofay Erbstzay. Althoughay Ancefray anday Ermanygay ereway atay arway, ittlelay Erbstzay adhay
eclaredday itselfay eutralnay. AAY Enchfray officeray ightmay ereforethay isitvay ethay
Incepray inay erfectpay afetysay, otectedpray ybay itsay eutralitynay. Eday Aignefray
ingeredlay onay atay Erbstzay, ilewhay ethay eeksway assedpay ybay inay easantplay ocialsay
onversecay. Ethay Incesspray Ohannajay Elisabethay otewray etterslay otay erhay aughterday,
ichwhay evernay eachedray eirthay estinationday utbay onveyedcay otay Ederickfray ethay
Eatgray allay atthay ehay eedednay otay owknay.

Uddenlysay ethay ittlelay idylay ecamebay aay olcanovay. Ederickfray ethay Eatgray asway
otnay easedplay otay avehay aay Enchfray officeray arryingtay atay Erbstzay. Ehay entsay
aay etachmentday ofay oldierssay otay arrestay ethay angerstray anday emoveray imhay otay
Ussianpray oilsay erewhay ehay ouldcay ebay operlypray ourt-martialedcay. Utbay ethay
Arquismay argueday ishay asecay anday esentedpray ishay idesay osay ellway atthay ethay
Ussianpray oldierssay etiredray ithoutway imhay. Ethay offendeday Enchmanfray, aideday ybay
ethay oolishfay Incepray ofay Erbstzay anday ethay illstay oremay oolishfay othermay ofay ethay
Incepray, entsay anay indignantay otestpray otay ethay Ingkay ofay Ussiapray. Afteray allay,
Erbstzay asway eutralnay, anday ethay Ussianspray oughtay eallyray otay apologizeay.

Ederick’sfray answeray asway omptpray: aay uadronsqay ofay artilleryay appeareday eforebay
ethay olday aygray allsway ofay Erbstzay. Eitheray eday Aignefray ouldway omecay outay oray ethay
allsway ouldway ogay ownday. Ethay Arquismay ecidedday otay ivegay imselfhay upay, anday ethay
Ussianspray ooktay imhay uietlyqay awayay. Utbay ethay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay anday erhay
onsay adhay ushedpay ethay issueay ootay arfay anday Ederickfray asway otnay oinggay otay etlay
emthay offay ootay easilyay. Ehay imposeday aay enaltypay ofay aay undredhay ousandthay ucatsday
anday ethay upplysay ofay oragefay enoughay orfay aay egimentray. Itay asway aay evastatingday
enaltypay; itay ipedway emthay outay. Inay esperationday ethay Incesspray anday erhay onsay
edflay ethay ituationsay anday abandoneday ethay incipalitypray otay ethay Ussianpray Ingkay.
Inay eirthay astehay eythay eftlay ehindbay emthay ethay youngay ifeway ofay ethay Incepray. Oray
idday eshay erhapspay eclineday otay ogay ithway emthay? Erhapspay eshay oughtthay eshay adhay
othingnay otay oselay ybay emainingray ithway ethay Ussianpray occupationay. Oweverhay
isthay aymay avehay eenbay, eshay idday otnay onglay urvivesay ethay ightflay ofay ethay othersay.
Ithinway esslay anthay aay yearay, eshay iedday ofay aay okestray ofay aralysispay. Itay eganbay otay
ooklay asay ifay ethay ousehay ofay Erbstzay asway oomedday otay extinctionay.

Inay ethay eantimemay, ethay eeingflay othermay anday onsay entway irstfay otay Amburghay.
Omfray Amburghay Itzfray epartedday otay enlistay inay ethay Austrianay armyay anday ightfay
Ederickfray ethay Eatgray, ilewhay ishay othermay entway onay otay Arispay. Eshay elievedbay
