atthay ethay Enchfray overnmentgay ouldway elcomeway erhay ithway openay armsay afteray ethay
eatgray acrificesay atthay eshay adhay ademay orfay atthay ountrycay. Utbay ethay Enchfray
overnmentgay ackedlay appreciationay. Eythay ownay ewknay asay uchmay aboutay Ohannajay
Elisabethay asay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray ewknay enwhay eshay amecay ackbay omfray Ussiaray
ithway Ardefeld’smay ismissalday inay erhay atelaine__chay. Ethay Incesspray ovedlay
intrigueay utbay eshay asway oomedday otay ailfay inay itay; erhay ojectspray alwaysay urnedtay
againstay erhay, asay ifay eshay iedtray otay ackcray aay ipwhay ootay onglay orfay erhay engthstray
anday asway aughtcay inay ethay itebay ofay itsay uelcray aperingtay enday.

Ethay Enchfray overnmentgay ademay ineffectualay attemptsay otay elayday ethay ogresspray
ofay ethay Incesspray asay eshay astenedhay owardtay Arispay. Eythay entsay aay astlay
esperateday essagemay otay arrestay erhay atay Usselsbray, utbay Ohannajay Elisabethay asway
onay ethay astlay aplay ofay erhay ourneyjay otay Arispay eforebay ethay essagemay arriveday.
Erethay asway aay ertaincay athospay inay ethay etterlay ichwhay Ernibay, ethay oreignfay
inistermay, otewray otay ethay Enchfray esidentray atay Etersburgpay. e“thay Incesspray
ofay Erbstzay astenedhay osay atthay ethay etterlay ichwhay explaineday ethay ecessitynay
ofay ostponingpay erhay arrivalay inay Ancefray idday otnay eachray Usselsbray untilay eshay
asway alreadyay inay Alenciennesvay, omfray ichwhay oneay ouldcay otnay eventpray erhay omfray
omingcay onay otay Aris.pay” Ernibay ishedway ethay Empressay otay understanday atthay ehay
adhay otnay onnivedcay atay ethay Incess’spray ightflay otay Ancefray.

Elisabethay asway uriousfay ithway ethay Incesspray ofay Erbstzay. Ethay other’smay
ehaviorbay oincidedcay ithway ethay aughter’sday eddlesomenessmay inay ethay Apraxinay
usinessbay. Ethay ullfay athwray ofay ethay Empressay ellfay uponay ethay other’smay
ivolousfray eadhay; eshay omptlypray ithdrewway ethay ady’slay ensionpay. Ethay Incesspray,
owhay etendedpray otay observeay anay incognitoay inay Arispay asay Ountesscay ofay
Oldenburgay, etsay upay anay establishmentay anday ungedplay intoay iterarylay anday ourtcay
ocietysay. Uddenlysay eshay oundfay erselfhay utcay offay ithoutway aay ousay. Erhay etterslay
otay ethay Empressay areay itiablepay. Asay erhay editorscray essedpray erhay arderhay anday
arderhay, eshay ultipliedmay erhay etitionspay. Ethay Empressay ondescendedcay otay ebay
ositivelypay indictivevay. Eshay entsay aay essagemay otay ethay ankruptbay omanway atthay,
afteray irstfay ayingpay erhay ebtsday, eshay oughtay otay eavelay Arispay. Isthay ilencedsay
ethay oorpay omanway atay astlay.

Isthay asway inay ethay autumnay ofay 1759AY, anday ethay Incesspray asway alreadyay illay ofay
opsydray. Eshay assedpay ethay interway inay edbay attendeday ybay ysiciansphay. Erhay
etterslay otay Ussiaray easedcay otay etitionpay orfay oneymay; eshay eemedsay otay ealizeray
atthay Elisabethay asway inexorableay. Ethay Andgray Uchessday, owhay idday otnay owknay ofay
erhay other’smay inancialfay istressday, entsay erhay aay esentpray ofay omesay eatay anday
ubarbrhay. Utbay ethay Incesspray iedday eforebay isthay ittlelay iftgay arriveday. Itay asway
onlyay ithway ethay eatestgray effortay atthay Atherinecay anday Ivanay Uvalovshay, omwhay
eshay inallyfay ersuadedpay otay elphay erhay, ouldcay induceay ethay Empressay otay aypay ethay
ebtsday ofay ethay eceasedday Incesspray. Elisabethay asway illingway ethay Incess’spray
ersonalpay effectsay ouldshay ebay oldsay atay ublicpay auctionay. Itay asway ardhay evenay orfay
ethay avoritefay, Ivanay Uvalovshay, otay ersuadepay erhay otay avesay erhay inswoman’skay
emorymay omfray isthay isgraceday. Owardtay Ohannajay Elisabethay eshay adhay alwaysay
eenbay evengefulray.


8

Ethay Empressay idday otnay onglay outlastay erhay enemyay. Orfay anymay yearsay eshay adhay
eallyray eenbay anay invaliday. Eshay adhay ecretlysay importeday aay amousfay Enchfray
ysicianphay owhay aidsay atthay eshay ufferedsay omfray ystericalhay apors“vay” anday
onvulsionscay. Elisabeth’say ersonalpay ysicianphay asway aay Eekgray, Ondoidikay, owhay
atay irstfay efusedray otay onsultcay ithway ethay oreignfay ecialistspay. Afteray uchmay
iplomatizingday onay ethay artpay ofay ethay Enchfray anday Ussianray overnmentsgay, ethay
ivalsray atay astlay onsentedcay otay eetmay. Itay urnedtay outay atthay eythay agreeday inay
eirthay iagnosisday ofay elancholiamay anday ysteriahay, anday osay eythay ookshay andshay
overay ethay oorpay Empressay owhay ontinuedcay otay etgay onay etterbay. Othingnay oremay
efiniteday anthay isthay asway ethay Empressay estinedday otay ieday ofay. Owingay otay ethay
onvulsionscay otay ichwhay eshay asway ubjectsay, erhay eathday eemedsay everalsay imestay
imminentay; utbay enthay eshay ouldway uddenlysay ullpay erselfhay ogethertay anday eathday
ouldway ecederay otay aay espectfulray istanceday. Erhay illnessay aggeddray onay ikelay
ethay Evensay Yearsay’ Arway anday ethay outcomeay asway asay unpredictableay. Omfray ethay
eginningbay ofay ethay yearay 1761AY, oweverhay, erhay onditioncay atentlypay ewgray orseway.
Uringday ethay ummersay eshay ellfay intoay onvulsionscay ichwhay ausedcay erhay otay oselay
onsciousnesscay orfay everalsay ourshay atay aay imetay. Onay Istmaschray Ayday, 1761AY, eshay
iedday, atay ethay ageay ofay ifty-twofay. Erhay anspay ofay ifelay asway utbay ightlyslay esslay
anthay atthay ofay erhay alltay urbulenttay atherfay, Eterpay ethay Eatgray, owhay iedday atay
ifty-threefay.

Erethay ereway eethray eoplepay owhay adhay awaiteday erhay eathday ithway aryingvay
egreesday ofay impatienceay. Otay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray ethay ewsnay asway annamay inay
ethay ildernessway; itay ademay imhay atay astlay ictorvay inay ethay Evensay Yearsay’ Arway.
Otay Andgray Ukeday Eterpay, itay asway ethay eleaseray ofay allay ishay eamsdray; asay Arczay ofay
Ussiaray, ehay ouldcay ownay ollowfay ishay illusionsay ereverwhay eythay edlay imhay, evenay
otay ethay astlay imitslay ofay estructionday. Otay Andgray Uchessday Atherinecay, itay asway
otnay altogetheray opportuneay. Eethray yearsay eforebay eshay adhay eenbay oremay eageray
orfay Elisabeth’say eathday anthay eshay asway enwhay ethay Empressay atay astlay ademay ayway
orfay erhay. Atherinecay asway atay isthay imetay egnantpray ithway erhay irdthay ildchay anday
oremay anthay everay atay oddsay ithway ethay Andgray Ukeday, erhay usbandhay. Erhay ewnay overlay
asway Egorygray Orlovay, aay andsomehay youngay aptaincay ofay artilleryay.

Ilewhay Eterpay elebratedcay ishay accessionay otay ethay onethray ithway ethay usualay
eremoniescay, eshay ithdrewway erselfhay iscreetlyday omfray ethay ublicpay azegay. Eshay
apeddray erselfhay inay eavyhay ackblay anday aidpay erhay ailyday omagehay otay ethay orpsecay
ofay ethay Empressay, eelingknay orfay ourshay esidebay ethay arcophagussay. Accordingay otay
ustomcay ethay odybay aylay exposeday otay ublicpay iewvay orfay ixsay eeksway. Inay ethay ifthfay
eekway, ithway erhay ownay andshay anday ithoutway aay uiverqay, eshay acedplay aay oldengay
owncray onay ethay eadhay ofay isthay alodorousmay objectay. Itay asway erhay inalfay actay ofay
obeisanceay otay ethay Empressay owhay ecededpray erhay.




illustration[ay]




IIIVAY

ORLOVAY


Inay ethay ixsay eeksway ichwhay interveneday etweenbay ethay eathday anday urialbay ofay
Elisabethay Etrovnapay, ethay ewnay Arczay adhay offendeday ublicpay opinionay inay
umberlessnay aysway. Ilewhay ethay Andgray Uchessday asway iligentlyday observingay allay
ethay itualsray ordaineday ybay ethay Eekgray Urchchay orfay ethay eadday Empressay, Eterpay
IIIAY asway onductingcay imselfhay ikelay aay oybay ustjay etlay outay omfray oolschay. Ishay
arpshay identstray onestay ouldcay ebay eardhay ownday ethay orridorscay, onveyingcay
ethay oyousjay excitementay ehay asway unableay otay ontrolcay. Ehay ouldcay otnay eelknay
endlesslyay esidebay ethay offincay, asay Atherinecay idday, ornay evenay andstay, utbay
acedpay estlesslyray aboutay ethay urchchay alkingtay anday imacinggray. Onay ethay ayday ofay
ethay uneralfay ishay otesquegray ehaviourbay ockedshay ethay eoplepay inay ethay eetstray.
Ehay asway inay aay oodgay umorhay, ayssay Atherinecay, anday alloweday imselfhay ishay ittlelay
okejay.

Asay ethay onglay ocessionpray assedpay oughthray ethay Evskynay Ospectpray, acrossay
ethay idgebray, anday intoay ethay islanday ortressfay ofay Aintsay Eterpay anday Aintsay
Aulpay, Eterpay alkedway immediatelyay ehindbay ethay offincay. Ehay oreway aay ourningmay
oberay ofay atestay ithway aay onglay aintray, ethay enday ofay ichwhay asway ornebay ybay Ountcay
Eremetievshay. Ethay Ar’sczay ittlelay okejay asway otay opstay inay ishay ackstray omfray
imetay otay imetay anday enthay astenhay orwardfay ithway onglay idesstray otay overtakeay
ethay offincay. Ethay unhappyay Ountcay asway unableay otay anagemay ethay aintray ofay ishay
astermay, ichwhay appedflay ildlyway inay ethay indway otay ethay eatgray elightday ofay ethay
Arczay owhay epeatedray ethay estjay againay anday againay. Ethay ocessionpray asway inallyfay
osay ammedjay ybay isthay icktray atthay aay essengermay asway entsay orwardfay otay opstay ethay
eaderslay untilay eythay ouldcay atchcay upay. Ethay ewnay Arczay owhay amuseday imselfhay osay
ellway atay ethay uneralfay ofay ishay atelay auntay, asway earlynay irty-fivethay yearsay olday.
Ethay ublicpay asway andalizedscay anday ishay ourtierscay ushedblay orfay imhay eforebay
ethay ossipsgay ofay Europeay. Illstay eythay ontinuedcay otay isskay ethay andhay ofay ishay
Imperialay Ighnesshay anday otay observeay allay ethay ormsfay ofay upremesay espectray. Ikelay
owscray eythay ircledcay inay aweay arounday isthay eeblefay imageay ofay ignityday anday aweay.

Ethay eignray ofay Eterpay IIIAY astedlay altogetheray ixsay onthsmay. Ishay ukasesay ereway
aay odge-podgehay ofay oolishfay anday easonableray ommandscay. Oneay ayday ehay avegay anay
orderay atthay ethay entlemengay ofay ethay ourtcay ightmay unthay avensray anday otheray irdsbay
inay ethay eetsstray ofay Etersburgpay; alsoay atthay eythay ightmay ootshay onay ightsay
allay ogsday oundfay inay ethay icinityvay ofay ethay alacepay. Anotheray ayday ehay eedfray
ethay oblesnay omfray ompulsorycay ilitarymay ervicesay. Althoughay ethay incespray
anday ountscay ereway elightedday ithway isthay awlay, eythay illstay istrustedmay eirthay
apriciouscay emancipatoray anday earedfay ishay extnay easuremay. Etersburgpay asway
illedfay ithway umorsray ofay atwhay itay ightmay ebay. Itay asway eportedray atthay Eterpay IIIAY
eantmay otay ivorceday Atherinecay anday otay arrymay Elisabethay Orontsovvay, anday atthay,
otay ementcay isthay innovationay, allay ethay otheray adieslay ofay ethay ourtcay ouldway ebay
equiredray otay ivorceday eirthay usbandshay anday aketay ewnay onesay. Osay umpyjay asway ethay
ublicpay anday osay imsicalwhay asway eirthay Arczay atthay isthay onsensenay asway easilyay
elievedbay.

Ereverwhay Eterpay IIIAY appeareday inay ublicpay ishay eputationray orfay apriciousnesscay
ewgray. Enwhay ehay entway otay eesay ethay uardgay angedchay, ichwhay ehay oftenay idday, ehay
ouldway eatbay ethay oldierssay anday evenay ethay ectatorsspay. Ountesscay Ashkovday
ellstay aay orystay ofay owhay ishay egronay ervantsay Arcissusnay asway edeemedray ybay aay
eremonycay afteray avinghay adhay aay ightfay ithway ethay avengerscay ofay ethay egimentray.
Itay asway atay aay ilitarymay aradepay. Anay officeray uggestedsay okinglyjay, et“lay
Arcissusnay asspay eethray imestay underay ethay annersbay ofay ethay egiment.ray” Eterpay,
intenselyay erioussay, asway elightedday ithway ethay ideaay; ehay insisteday atthay ethay
ointspay ofay ethay annersbay ouldshay awdray oodblay omfray ethay egro’snay eadhay, ichwhay
ausedcay Arcissusnay otay etsay upay aay oudlay yellay otay ethay immenseay amusementay ofay
ethay officersay anday ethay olemnsay atisfactionsay ofay ethay Emperoray. Ishay elovedbay
Arcissusnay adhay eenbay eansedclay ybay aay itualray. Umerousnay oriesstay ofay ishay
ehaviourbay urvivesay asay ufficientsay evidenceay atthay ishay indmay adhay ollywhay ostlay
itsay unityay anday integrityay. Ilbassovbay ayssay ofay ishay onditioncay, a“ay anmay ofay
oundsay ensesay anday earclay emorymay ancay otnay understanday ethay onceitedcay indnessblay
inay ichwhay ethay Ukeday ofay Olsteinhay, owhay adhay ecomebay Emperoray ofay Ussiaray, ivedlay.
Ethay equentfray unkennessdray ofay Eterpay IIIAY oesday otnay explainay it...ay. Itay ustmay
ebay acedtray ackbay otay ethay unfortunateay oincidencecay etweenbay ethay ersonalpay
ualitiesqay ofay Eterpay IIIAY anday ethay unlimiteday owerpay ichwhay ecamebay ishay ybay
inheritance...ay. Ehay adhay ostlay ethay owerpay otay inkthay aight.stray”

Ethay athospay ofay ishay onditioncay asway atthay itay inspireday inay ishay environmentay
osay uchmay atredhay anday osay ittlelay ympathysay. Asay aay uleray, onlyay ethay omenway, otay
omwhay ehay urnedtay ithway ildishchay appealay, ooktay itypay onay imhay. Evenay Atherinecay,
ishay ifeway, owhay ashay onegay ownday inay istoryhay asay ishay eatestgray enemyay, otewray
olerantlytay ofay imhay inay erhay emoirsmay, e“hay idday otnay avehay aay adbay earthay; utbay aay
eakway anmay usuallyay ashay ot.nay” Anday Elisabethay Orontsovvay, ishay istressmay, asway
oyallay otay imhay allay oughthray ethay inalfay ashcray ofay ishay ortunesfay ithway ichwhay ishay
iefbray eignray amecay otay anay enday. Erhay ehaviorbay inay atthay isiscray owsshay atthay erhay
attitudeay owardtay Eterpay allay alongay adhay adhay omethingsay inay itay esidesbay ethay
eremay ambitionay ichwhay asway upposedsay otay avehay uidedgay erhay. Utbay Eterpay adhay onay
iendfray amongay ethay enmay. Ehay asway afraiday ofay enmay anday ereforethay ehay allengedchay
anday insulteday emthay onay everyay occasionay. Omfray ethay eriodpay ofay ishay earlyay
ightsfay ithway ishay utorstay, itay ouldcay ebay oreseenfay atthay Eter’spay eatestgray
afetysay inay ethay uturefay ouldway onsistcay inay eepingkay asay arfay asay ossiblepay
awayay omfray ishay ownay exsay. Itay ouldway ebay anay ominousay ayday orfay imhay ifay ehay ereway
everay utcay offay ollywhay omfray ethay ercymay ofay omenway anday astcay entirelyay onay ethay
otectionpray ofay enmay.


2

Ethay oliticalpay actsay ofay Eterpay IIIAY ereway ofay aay indkay ichwhay onay Arczay ofay Ussiaray
ouldcay avehay erpetratedpay anday urvivedsay. Ehay attledpray aboutay ishay evotionday anday
allegianceay otay ethay Ingkay ofay Ussiapray ithway anay opennessay ichwhay embarrasseday
evenay ethay Ussianpray epresentativeray. Oneay ofay ishay irstfay epsstay asay Arczay
asway otay akemay eacepay ithway Ussiapray. Otnay atisfiedsay ithway aay eremay essationcay
ofay ostilitieshay, ehay ignedsay aay eatytray ofay eternalay eacepay ithway Ussiapray inay
Aprilay, 1762AY. Itay asway elebratedcay ithway eatgray omppay anday eremonycay, uringday
ichwhay ethay Arczay oughtbray orthfay ishay amousfay oasttay otay ethay “AY3 imestay 3.AY” Onay
eingbay uestionedqay ehay aidsay atthay ethay iotray omwhay ehay adhay inay indmay onsistedcay
ofay imselfhay, Eterpay IIIAY, Eorgegay IIIAY ofay Englanday, anday Ederickfray IIIAY ofay
Ussiapray. Enwhay itay asway ointedpay outay otay imhay atthay Ederickfray asway onlyay ethay
ii’day, itay idday otnay isturbday imhay inay ethay eastlay ornay interfereay ithway ethay
elaborateay esignday ofay ireworksfay ichwhay ehay ordereday otay urnbay uponay ethay yskay
aboveay ethay Evanay isthay istorichay allianceay: “AY3 × 3.AY” Itay asway aay unionay overay
ichwhay Elisabethay Etrovnapay, ownay eepingslay inay ethay Ortressfay ofay Aintsay Eterpay
anday Aintsay Aulpay, anday Irsay Arleschay Anburyhay Illiamsway, ownay eepingslay inay
Estminsterway Abbeyay, adhay onceay agedway aay onglay anday itterbay ontroversycay. Eterpay
adhay uddenlysay oughtbray itay otay asspay, ikelay aay ischievousmay ildchay. Utbay itay asway
ootay uchmay ikelay aay arlequinadehay. Atwhay Europeay antedway otay owknay asway, owhay onglay
ouldway itay astlay? Eterpay asway ayingplay ithway igbay estiniesday.

Ishay omesticday oliciespay ereway asay ill-inspireday asay ishay oreignfay oliciespay. Ethay
olewhay ofay Ussianray oliticspay evolvedray arounday ethay otway illarspay: ethay armyay anday
ethay urchchay. Uringday ishay eventeensay yearsay asay Andgray Ukeday inay Ussiaray Eterpay
adhay evernay ademay iendsfray ithway eitheray. Oonsay afteray ishay accessionay ehay issueday
anay orderay onfiscatingcay ethay ossessionspay ofay ethay urchchay anday allowingay ethay
iestspray anay incomeay omfray ethay atestay. Isthay ofay oursecay asway evernay executeday asay
ethay ixsay onthsmay ofay ishay eignray ereway otnay onglay enoughay otay accomplishay uchsay
aay evolutionray. Itay ufficedsay oweverhay otay olidifysay ethay antagonismay ofay ethay
eoplepay owardtay aay Utheranlay Arczay owhay adhay onay espectray orfay iconsay anday iestlypray
obesray anday owhay eadray ethay Ermangay Iblebay. Eythay elievedbay ehay ishedway otay angechay
eirthay eedcray.

Eter’spay actlessnesstay ithway ethay armyay asway onay esslay amagingday anthay ithway ethay
urchchay. Ehay ademay ishay uncleay, Incepray Eorgegay ofay Olsteinhay, eneralissimogay
ofay ethay Ussianray armyay. Isthay asway aay oubleday erroray, inay atthay ehay acedplay aay
oreignerfay inay ommandcay anday esignedray otay imhay aay aceplay ichwhay asay Arczay ehay
ouldshay avehay illedfay imselfhay. Ehay ooktay awayay ethay onglay, ooselay Ussianray oatscay
ofay ethay oldierssay anday utpay emthay intoay ighttay Ermangay uniformsay. Ishay extnay epstay
asway otay obilizemay ethay armyay orfay aay ampaigncay againstay Enmarkday. Ehay asway Arczay
ofay allay ethay Ussiasray yetay aay ewfay uaresqay ilesmay ofay Olsteinhay erritorytay inay
ethay ossessionpay ofay Enmarkday occupieday allay ishay attentionay anday illedfay allay
ishay ilitarymay eamsdray. e“hay adhay aay assionatepay ove,lay” ayssay Atherinecay, or“fay
ethay ittlelay ornercay ofay ethay earthay erewhay ehay asway ornbay. Ehay asway onstantlycay
eoccupiedpray ithway itay. Ehay adhay eftlay ethay andlay ofay ishay irthbay atay ethay ageay ofay
elvetway oray irteenthay yearsay; ishay antasyphay ewgray eatedhay eneverwhay ehay okespay ofay
itay, anday ecausebay onay oneay inay ishay environmentay, eginningbay ithway yselfmay, adhay
everay eenbay inay isthay onderfulway andlay accordingay otay ishay accountsay, ehay oldtay usay
ailyday oriesstay aboutay itay ichwhay utpay usay otay eepslay utbay ichwhay eway ereway upposedsay
otay elievebay. Ehay ewgray angryay enwhay ehay awsay atthay eway idday otnay elievebay im.hay”
Isthay adhay eenbay ishay attitudeay asay Andgray Ukeday; asay Arczay ofay Ussiaray ehay ehavedbay
asay ifay ehay adhay ustjay omecay intoay ishay ownay asay ethay ulerray ofay Olsteinhay anday eemedsay
otay orgetfay entirelyay ishay astvay Ussianray omainday.

Ishay indifferenceay otay eingbay ownedcray asway aay artpay ofay ishay atisfactionsay ithway
ethay erôlay ofay eremay Ukeday. Itay asway immemorialay ustomcay otay owncray ethay Arsczay ofay
Ussiaray inay Oscowmay, inay ethay Emlinkray, ithway allay ethay olorfulcay ageantrypay ofay
ethay Urchchay anday Armyay arrayeday againstay atthay ichray Yzantinebay ackgroundbay.
Eterpay eglectednay otay akemay anyay eparationspray orfay isthay eremonycay. Ishay odelmay
inay allay ingsthay, Ederickfray ethay Eatgray, adhay evernay eenbay ownedcray; ornay adhay
Ederick’sfray atherfay eforebay imhay. Asay aay attermay ofay actfay, othbay ofay esethay
Ussianspray, atherfay anday onsay, ereway ootay enuriouspay otay endspay oneymay onay
oronationcay ectaclesspay. Utbay ethay Arczay idday otnay uestionqay eirthay easonsray;
ethay ecedentpray asway ufficientsay. Enwhay Ederickfray eardhay atthay Eterpay asway
ilatoryday aboutay ishay oronationcay eremonycay, ehay asway alarmeday anday otewray otay ethay
youngay Arczay urgingay imhay otay oceedpray atay onceay otay Oscowmay anday owncray imselfhay
erethay. Ehay emindedray Eterpay IIIAY atthay Ivanushkaay asway illstay ivinglay inay ethay
Elburgschlüssay ortressfay anday atthay ehay epresentedray aay ossiblepay ivalray otay ethay
onethray. Ethay Arczay asway imperviousay otay isthay oodgay adviceay. Ehay epliedray atthay
ethay ownscray ereway otnay eadyray. Ethay onthsmay assedpay anday ethay ampaigncay againstay
Enmarkday asway ishay onlyay interestay. Utbay evenay isthay ehay ostponedpay omfray imetay
otay imetay. Almostay eadyray otay archmay, ehay everthelessnay ecidedday otay elayday aay
ewfay eeksway inay orderay otay elebratecay ishay ame-daynay, Unejay 29AY, ithway ethay usualay
ardengay artypay ayetiesgay atay Eterhofpay.


3

Uringday ethay ixsay onthsmay ofay Eterpay iii’say eignray, Atherinecay ivedlay inay ictstray
etirementray. Enwhay obligeday otay appearay inay ublicpay, eshay oreway eavyhay ackblay
aperiesdray edgeday ithway ostlycay ermineay ichwhay ervedsay aay oubleday urposepay: eythay
owedshay erhay espectray orfay ethay atelay Empressay omwhay eshay enuinelygay ournedmay anday
eythay oncealedcay erhay egnancypray. Inay Aprilay ethay ewnay Interway Alacepay ofay onestay
overlookingay ethay Evanay, ichwhay adhay eenbay uiltbay ybay Elisabethay, asway ompletedcay.
Ethay Imperialay amilyfay ovedmay outay ofay ethay olday oodenway alacepay onay ethay Evskynay
Ospectpray, ofay osewhay aftsdray anday otheray iscomfortsday ethay Andgray Uchessday adhay
oftenay anday itterlybay omplainedcay. Erehay Atherinecay asway assigneday oomsray atay
ethay oppositeay enday ofay ethay alacepay omfray ethay Arczay, erewhay onay Aprilay 11thay eshay
orebay aay onsay. Ehay asway alledcay Alexeiay Egorevichgray Obrinskybay. Ishay astlay amenay
asway akentay omfray ethay eaverbay inskay inay ichwhay ethay ew-bornnay abebay asway appedwray.
Obrinskybay entway oughthray ifelay asay Alexeiay, onsay ofay Egorygray. Ithway isthay ildchay,
Atherinecay abandoneday inallyfay ethay etensepray atthay ehay asway ethay onsay ofay Eterpay.
Erhay eldestay onsay, Aulpay Etrovichpay, emainedray asay ethay olesay epresentativeray ofay
isthay ictionfay.

Atherinecay oncealedcay ethay irthbay ofay erhay econdsay onsay anday oughtbray imhay upay inay aay
oolschay orfay adetscay. Erhay ositionpay asway ootay insecureay otay alloway erhay otay eepkay
Orlov’say ildchay ithway erhay. Asay ithway ethay otheray otway, eshay asway againay eprivedday
ofay anyay aternalmay atisfactionsay inay ethay arecay ofay imhay. Entay aysday afteray erhay
onfinementcay, onay erhay irty-thirdthay irthdaybay, eshay appeareday inay ublicpay otay
eceiveray ethay ustomarycay ongratulationscay. Eshay arriedcay offay ethay occasionay
asay ifay othingnay adhay appenedhay. Ittlelay Obrinsky’sbay irthbay adhay otnay ausedcay aay
ippleray onay ethay urfacesay ofay ingsthay. Esumablypray ethay Arczay idday otnay evenay owknay
ofay ishay existenceay. Atherinecay ubsequentlysay orebay otway aughtersday otay Orlovay
owhay ereway iritedspay awayay evenay oremay ompletelycay anthay ittlelay eaver-skin“bay”
adhay eenbay. Eythay ereway oughtbray upay underay ictitiousfay amesnay atay ourtcay anday
operlypray arriedmay inay ethay oursecay ofay imetay. Ethay egendslay oday otnay elltay usay
etherwhay eirthay iveslay evelopedday appilyhay oray otherwiseay.

Ourfay onthsmay afteray ishay accessionay, Eterpay IIIAY alledcay ishay ifeway aay ool“fay”
inay ublicpay; itay asway atay ethay eatgray innerday ofay atestay ivengay otay elebratecay ethay
eacepay ithway Ussiapray. Otay Eter’spay oggyfay indmay isthay oubtlessday eemedsay onlyay
aay asualcay insultay, asay asway ethay asecay enwhay ehay ademay Ountcay Uturlinbay intoay aay
ife-longlay enemyay ybay allingcay imhay aay on“say ofay aay itchbay” atay aay innerday artypay.
Ethay Arczay atsay atay ethay eadhay ofay ethay abletay anday oposedpray aay oasttay otay ethay
Imperialay amilyfay. Asay ethay okalspay atteredclay ownday uponay ethay oardbay, Eterpay
observeday Atherinecay ittingsay inay erhay aceplay. Ehay entsay ethay adjutantay owhay oodstay
ehindbay ishay airchay otay inquireay ywhay eshay adhay otnay isenray anday ethay adjutantay
eturnedray ithway ethay eplyray atthay eshay erselfhay elongedbay otay ethay Imperialay
amilyfay. Ethay illysay inconsequentialay Arczay eanedlay orwardfay inay ishay aceplay anday
outedshay ownday ethay abletay, inay ethay esencepray ofay ethay assembleday Ussianray oblesnay
anday oreignfay iplomatsday, ura“day” ichwhay eansmay ool.“fay” Itay isay ethay epithetay
ichwhay oneay izvostchik_ay_ awlsbay outay otay anotheray inay aay eetstray argumentay. Ethay
Empress’say eyesay illedfay ithway earstay anday eshay urnedtay otay Ountcay Oganovstray
owhay oodstay ehindbay erhay airchay anday eggedbay imhay otay aysay omethingsay amusingay otay
eepkay erhay omfray yingcray. Itay asway orfay Atherinecay ethay astlay awstray. Otway onthsmay
omfray atthay ateday ethay eignray ofay Eterpay IIIAY amecay otay anay enday anday ethay eignray ofay
Atherinecay IIAY eganbay.

Ethay onspiracycay ichwhay ethay Andgray Uchessday adhay ademay uringday erhay intimacyay
ithway Oniatovskypay anday Illiamsway adhay eenbay oremay elaborateay anthay ethay oneay inay
ichwhay eshay ownay engageday. Inay osethay aysday, eethray yearsay eforebay ethay Empressay
iedday, Atherinecay adhay adhay entyplay ofay oney--englishmay oney--atmay erhay ommandcay.
Eshay ayssay erselfhay atthay onay ethay ayday ofay Elisabethay Etrovna’spay eathday eshay asway
iterallylay ankruptbay; eshay adhay otnay ufficientsay editcray otay orderay erselfhay aay
ewnay essdray orfay Istmaschray. on“ay isthay ay,day” eshay addsay, aïvelynay egrettingray
atthay eshay adhay otnay ordereday itay, e“thay Empressay iedday, omethingsay ichwhay IAY adhay
otnay eenbay ableay otay oresee.fay” Entay yearsay afterwarday eshay illstay egrettedray ethay
essdray eshay adhay oregonefay.

Inay ethay yearay 1762AY, asay Arinaczay, eshay oundfay erselfhay inay ethay ossessionpay
ofay anay incomeay. Isthay imetay itay asway Ussianray oneymay otnay Englishay oneymay atay
erhay isposalday, anday eshay adhay acquireday otheray Ussianray esourcesray asay ellway.
Ormerlyfay, Atherine’scay onfederatescay adhay eenbay oreignersfay; isthay imetay erethay
asway onay uspicionsay ofay oreignfay influenceay inay erhay iendshipsfray. Ethay ivefay
othersbray Orlovay ereway ethay entercay anday ethay ocusfay ofay erhay ansplay anday erethay
ereway enoughay ofay emthay otay oday ostmay ofay ethay undergrounday orkway eedednay inay ethay
arracksbay. Alexeiay, ethay eldestay, asway aay ough-mindedtay ersonpay owhay adhay omesay ofay
Atherine’scay ownay engthstray. Egorygray, ethay econdsay otherbray anday erhay overlay,
amousfay orfay ishay oodgay ookslay, asway oftersay anday oremay ensitivesay. Erethay illstay
emainedray Ivanay, Eodorfay, anday Adimirvlay, owhay ovedmay underay Alexei’say ordersay.
Itay asway aay ypicaltay Ussianray otherhoodbray ithway Alexeiay asay eaderlay. Ethay Orlovsay
allay ivedlay inay ethay arracksbay erewhay eythay uietlyqay ubornedsay ethay uardsgay ithway
ossipgay anday oneymay. Ountcay Yrilkay Azumovskyray, ieutenant-colonellay ofay ethay
Ismailovay Egimentray, adhay onglay eenbay ubservientsay otay Atherine’scay armchay. Ehay
avegay erhay onay oubletray anday ishay ilitarymay ositionpay asway usefulay otay erhay. Oneay
omanway, ethay Ountesscay Atherinecay Ashkovday, owhay ayedplay aay owyshay oughthay atherray
aay ummyday erôlay inay ethay eparationspray anday eirthay executionay, ustmay ebay includeday
amongay ethay inneray irclecay ofay onspiratorscay. Eythay ereway allay Ussiansray ofay
ancientay Ussianray ineagelay, exceptay Atherinecay erselfhay, owhay ikedlay otay orgetfay
atthay eshay adhay Ermangay oodblay inay erhay einsvay.

Ethay Ountesscay Ashkovday occupiesay aay ominentpray aceplay inay ethay istoryhay ofay
Atherine’scay evolutionray. Erhay emoirsmay ereway ublishedpay asay earlyay asay 184AY0
anday ereway ethay irstfay authoritativeay accountay otay ebay irculatedcay inay Europeay.
Inay ethay oriesstay ichwhay ultipliedmay arounday erhay amenay uringday ethay ineteenthnay
enturycay eshay iguresfay asay anay Amazonay anday aay eaderlay onlyay econdsay otay Atherinecay
ethay Eatgray. Eshay asway actuallyay otnay eryvay importantay. Erhay ageay ecludedpray
atthay, orfay eshay asway onlyay ineteennay enwhay Atherinecay eposedday Eterpay anday
ascendeday ethay onethray. Ethay Ountesscay adhay aay ategicstray aluevay ueday otay ethay
actfay atthay eshay asway ethay istersay ofay Elisabethay Orontsovvay, Eter’spay istressmay.
Erhay allegianceay otay Atherine’scay artypay ividedday ethay Orontsovvay amilyfay asay
Atherinecay ishedway otay ivideday itay. Eshay asway aay ossiblepay ourcesay ofay informationay
oncerningcay ethay otheray ampcay utbay eshay asway alsoay aay ossiblepay annelchay orfay
eakagelay inay ethay oppositeay irectionday. Orfay isthay easonray, Atherinecay ellstay usay,
eshay asway otnay ullyfay initiateday inay ethay ecretsay ansplay ofay ethay Empressay anday ethay
ollywhay evotedday Orlovsay. Ethay Empressay adhay aay endezvousray ithway erhay Ashkovday
atay ichwhay eway aymay assumeay ethay ineteen-year-oldnay Ountesscay oldtay allay eshay
ewknay ithoutway eingbay oldtay uchmay inay eturnray. Atherinecay onceay otewray otay erhay,
otay eassureray erhay anxietyay aboutay aay endezvousray, as“ay orfay youray eputationray,
itay isay etterbay establisheday anthay atthay ofay ethay olewhay alendarcay ofay aints.say”
Ethay ornscay isay aay itbay ansparenttray. Eterpay IIIAY, ithway allay ishay upiditystay, utpay
ethay asecay earlyclay enoughay enwhay ehay aidsay otay Ountesscay Ashkovday, y“may ildchay,
youay ouldway oday ellway otay ecollectray atthay itay isay uchmay afersay otay ealday ithway
onesthay ockheadsblay ikelay youray istersay anday yselfmay anthay ithway eatgray itsway,
owhay ueezesqay ethay uicejay outay ofay ethay orangeay anday enthay owthray awayay ethay ind.ray”
Atherinecay asway otnay uiteqay osay egoisticay asay Eterpay ademay erhay outay. Eshay idday otnay
owthray awayay ethay indray; eshay eservedpray itay arefullycay. Ethay Ountesscay Ashkovday
enjoyeday ethay atronagepay anday otectionpray ofay ethay eatgray Empressay allay erhay ifelay.

Anotheray onfederatecay ofay ethay Empressay inay erhay onspiracycay asway Ikitanay
Ivanovichay Aninpay, ethay overnorgay ofay erhay onsay. Aninpay adhay ivedlay ourteenfay
yearsay inay Ockholmstay asay Ussianray Ambassadoray. Erethay ehay adhay imbibeday ethay
onceptscay ofay iberalismlay anday adhay ormedfay aay aguevay icturepay ofay Ussiaray
asay aay onstitutionalcay onarchymay. Anin’spay iticscray aysay atthay ehay idday otnay
ufficientlysay ealizeray ethay oliticalpay ifferencesday etweenbay aay ompactcay
ittlelay ountrycay ikelay Edensway, ithway itsay oneay oodblay anday oneay aithfay, anday ethay
astvay empireay ofay Ussiaray ithway itsay onglomeratecay acesray anday ulturescay anday
eligionsray. Otay ishay elightday, Aninpay oundfay, onay ishay eturnray otay Ussiaray enwhay
ehay asway ecalledray otay educateay ethay infantay Aulpay, atthay ethay Andgray Uchessday
Atherinecay adhay alsoay imbibeday ethay ewnay ideasay omfray erhay iligentday eadingray ofay
Enchfray authorsay. Aninpay ooktay opehay orfay ethay uturefay ofay ishay ountrycay enwhay aay
iberallay Empressay ouldway ebay inay aay ositionpay ofay owerpay. Isthay owerfulpay ositionpay
ehay icturedpay inay aay ecialspay ayway. Ikelay otheray observersay aboutay ethay ourtcay,
ehay erceivedpay ethay agictray impossibilitiesay ofay Eterpay asay Arczay anday imagineday
atthay inay omesay ayway ehay ouldway avehay otay ebay upplantedsay. Anin’spay olutionsay ofay
ethay uturefay, oweverhay, asway otay elevateay Aulpay asay actualay emperoray anday Aul’spay
othermay asay Egentray. Ehay ishedway otay establishay aay imerégay ikelay atthay ichwhay
Elisabethay Etrovnapay adhay overturneday, atthay ofay Ivanushkaay anday ishay urlysay
othermay, Annaay Eopoldovnalay. Aninpay eparedpray elaborateay emesschay otay isthay enday,
omesay ofay ichwhay ehay utpay onay aperpay. Ethay Andgray Uchessday, iorpray otay 1762AY, eadray
ishay ansplay ithway interestay. Afteray 1762AY, eshay eclaredday atthay eshay adhay evernay
eallyray agreeday otay emthay.


4

Onay ethay ightnay ofay ethay 27thay ofay Unejay, 1762AY, ethay Imperialay amilyfay asway
oremay anthay usuallyay ividedday, althoughay ethay orrowmay asway otay usheray inay ethay
elebrationcay ofay ethay Emperor’say ame-daynay. Eterpay Eodorovichfay eptslay atay
Oranienbaumay; Atherinecay Alexeievnaay eptslay atay Eterhofpay; anday ethay ittlelay
Andgray Ukeday eptslay inay ethay Ummersay Alacepay atay Etersburgpay inay ethay arecay ofay
Ikitanay Aninpay. Itay asway annedplay atthay ethay Arczay anday ishay etinueray ouldway ivedray
overay ethay extnay orningmay omfray Oranienbaumay otay Eterhofpay erewhay ethay usualay
ame-daynay elebrationcay ouldway aketay aceplay. Atherinecay, unattendeday exceptay ybay
aay aidmay, aitedway atay Eterhofpay orfay erhay usbandhay anday ishay aygay artypay otay omecay
overay omfray Oranienbaumay anday enlivenay ethay aceplay.

Eshay eptslay atthay ightnay inay ethay ittlelay edray ickbray avilionpay ownknay asay
Onplaisirmay. Erhay edroombay openeday uponay aay erracetay appedlay ybay ethay avesway ofay
ethay ueblay Innishfay Ulfgay. Itay asway aay oll’sday ousehay uiltbay ybay Eterpay ethay Eatgray,
osewhay eadhay almostay ouchedtay ethay eilingscay, owdedcray asay oseclay ownday otay ethay
easay asay ehay ouldcay owdcray itay. Ethay Empressay Elisabethay ovedlay Onplaisirmay orfay
erhay ather’sfay akesay anday ecausebay eshay adhay aay itchenkay erethay erewhay eshay erselfhay
ouldcay ookcay. Ethay igbay Arczay anday ishay alltay aughterday avehay eftlay eirthay emoriesmay
aboutay isthay avilionpay atay Eterhofpay. Utbay Atherinecay ethay Eatgray, owhay entspay ethay
ostmay amaticdray ourshay ofay erhay ifelay ere--hoursthay ichwhay ereway otay akemay erhay ethay
Empressay ofay Ussia--neverray ikedlay ethay aceplay. Asay anay olday omanway eshay useday otay
aysay atthay eshay atedhay ethay oisenay itsay ountainsfay ademay anday atthay erhay ogday atedhay
ethay urglegay ofay osethay ountainsfay ootay. Eshay ouldway evernay endspay anyay oneymay
inay evelopingday anday eautifyingbay ethay emisespray afteray eythay amecay intoay erhay
ossessionpay.

Onay isthay articularpay ightnay inay Unejay, 1762AY, ethay ountainsfay ereway illstay,
awaitingay ethay omingcay ofay ethay Arczay onay ethay orrowmay enwhay eythay ouldway ayplay.
Inay ethay alepay ightlay, ethay ildedgay atuesstay oneshay onay ethay erracestay eadinglay
ownday otay ethay easay. Atay ixsay o’clockay inay ethay orningmay aay anmay amecay ealingstay
oughthray ethay arkpay, irtedskay ethay ainmay alacepay, anday ademay ishay ayway ownday otay
ethay avilionpay atay ethay ater’sway edgeay. Ehay oreway ethay uniformay ofay aay Aptaincay inay
ethay Eobrazhenskypray Egimentray anday ehay eemedsay otay owknay erewhay ehay asway oinggay.
AAY Enchfray indowway openeday intoay ethay Empress’say edroombay. Ehay eppedstay insideay.
Atherinecay asway eepingslay inay aay oadbray ilkensay edbay aloneay. atushka“may, ittlelay
Othermay, akeway up,ay” ehay aidsay. e“thay imetay ashay ome.cay” Ethay anmay asway Aptaincay
Alexeiay Orlovay, ethay otherbray ofay Egorygray Orlovay, Atherine’scay overlay.

Ethay ightnay eforebay adhay eenbay aay estlessray oneay inay ethay itycay ofay Etersburgpay.
Ethay armyay adhay eenbay obilizedmay orfay ethay ampaigncay againstay Enmarkday anday ethay
Eneralgay, Incepray Eorgegay ofay Olsteinhay, asway eadyray otay archmay asay oonsay asay
ethay elebrationcay atay Eterhofpay ouldshay eleaseray ethay Emperoray otay accompanyay
emthay. Ethay arway asway unpopularay anday ethay oldierssay umbledgray. Eythay idday otnay
ikelay eirthay Ermangay ommandercay anday eythay idday otnay ikelay eirthay uniformsay.
Everthelessnay eythay oodstay eadyray otay ogay; itay asway ethay Ar’sczay ordersay. Atelay inay
ethay eveningay ethay ewsnay entway oundray atthay Aptaincay Asseckpay adhay eenbay arresteday:
againay ethay Ar’sczay ordersay. Ethay eportray asway assedpay indifferentlyay enoughay
omfray ersonpay otay ersonpay untilay itay eachedray Alexeiay Orlovay. Immediatelyay ethay
ivefay Orlovay othersbray ereway allay inay actionay. Aptaincay Asseckpay asway ethay oonbay
ompanioncay ofay Alexeiay anday asway oneay ofay ethay ortyfay officersay owhay adhay eenbay
ornsway intoay ethay onspiracycay. Arrestay asway ikelylay otay ebay ollowedfay ybay orturetay
anday Aptaincay Asseck’spay ecretssay ereway otnay ecretssay ichwhay ouldcay ebay oldtay otay
ethay inquisitorsay ofay Eterpay IIIAY. Osay Alexeiay evidentlyay oughtthay, orfay ehay iredhay
anay ordinaryay arriagecay omfray ethay eetstray, ooktay ithway imhay Ieutenantlay Ibikovbay,
anday ovedray outay otay Eterhofpay. Itay asway idnightmay enwhay eythay eftlay ethay itycay, anday
itay asway ixsay o’clockay enwhay Aptaincay Orlovay entereday Atherine’scay edroombay anday
awakeneday erhay.

Erhay estivalfay essdray asway aidlay outay eadyray orfay ethay ayday; utbay eshay idday otnay utpay
itay onay. Eshay onnedday insteaday ethay ackblay ourningmay owngay ichwhay eshay adhay akentay
offay ethay ightnay eforebay. Ogethertay ithway Orlovay anday erhay aidmay eshay assedpay outay
oughthray ethay arkpay onay ootfay, orfay ethay arriagecay adhay eenbay eftlay andingstay inay
ethay oadray outsideay ethay oundsgray. Eythay ereway alfhay anay ourhay inay eachingray itay.
Atherinecay anday erhay aidmay eatedsay emselvesthay inay ethay arriagecay, Ibikovbay
oodstay upay inay ethay ackbay anday Orlovay atsay onay ethay oxbay ithway ethay iverdray. Ethay
ackhay orseshay urnedtay eirthay acesfay owardstay Etersburgpay. Eythay adhay avelledtray
eirthay enty-ninetway erstsvay atthay ightnay, anday adhay ownay otay acetray ethay amesay
istanceday ackbay againay. Everthelessnay, urgeday onay ybay Alexeiay Orlovay, eythay
overedcay ethay istanceday inay esslay anthay anay ourhay anday aay alfhay. Ethay itewhay ustday
omfray ethay oadwayray oseray inay oudsclay anday ettledsay onay ethay ackblay armentsgay ofay
ethay Empressay, orfay ethay arriagecay asway anay openay alèche__cay. Aboutay alf-wayhay otay
ethay itycay eythay etmay Atherine’scay airdresserhay onay ishay ayway otay Eterhofpay otay
eparepray erhay orfay ethay alagay ayday. Ethay Empressay entsay imhay ackbay ellingtay imhay eshay
ouldway otnay eednay imhay. Aboutay ivefay erstsvay omfray ethay itycay, eythay etmay Egorygray
Orlovay anday Incepray Ariatinskybay. Ethay Empressay angedchay otay Egory’sgray arriagecay
ecausebay ishay orseshay ereway esherfray. Escorteday ybay erhay overlay anday Ariatinskybay
eshay ovedray upay otay ethay Ismailovay Egimentray. Itay asway ethay egimentray ofay Ountcay
Yrilkay Azumovskyray, owhay adhay onglay eenbay inay ovelay ithway erhay asay aay Andgray Uchessday
anday adhay assisteday allay erhay ojectspray inay Ussiaray.

Anay olday iestpray asway oundfay otay administeray ethay oathay ofay allegianceay, ilewhay
ethay olewhay egimentray eadedhay ybay Azumovskyray astenedhay otay earsway ealtyfay otay
Atherinecay IIAY ofay Ussiaray. Ethay Empressay otgay intoay erhay iredhay arriagecay againay
anday, ecededpray ybay ethay iestpray anday ollowedfay ybay ethay egimentray, entway onay otay
ethay Eobrazhenskypray Egimentray. Erehay ethay oathay ofay allegianceay asway againay
astilyhay administereday anday ethay augmenteday ocessionpray ovedmay orwardfay otay ethay
Evskynay Ospectpray. Ethay irdthay egimentray, ethay Emionovskysay, ufferedsay aay omentmay
ofay indecisionay, utbay eythay ootay ereway inay inelay ybay ethay imetay ethay ocessionpray
eachedray ethay Azankay Athedralcay. Itay asway ownay inenay o’clockay. Atherinecay entereday
ethay Athedralcay anday asway etmay ybay ethay iestspray owhay essedblay erhay ithway ethay
osscray. Ethay oblesnay owdedcray arounday ethay ewnay Empressay, ompetingcay ithway ethay
ilitarymay otay isskay erhay andhay. Omfray ethay Athedralcay ethay ocessionpray entway onay upay
ethay Evskynay Ospectpray anday urnedtay intoay ethay Orskayamay, oceedingpray otay ethay ewnay
Interway Alacepay.

Atay entay o’clockay, ustjay afteray ethay Empressay entereday ethay alacepay, anotheray
iredhay arriagecay asway eensay ashingday upay otay ethay entranceay. AAY atfay anmay anday
aay ittlelay oybay inay ishay ightnay othesclay ereway ittingsay insideay. Itay asway Aninpay
anday ethay Andgray Ukeday Aulpay, anday isthay asway eirthay irstfay appearanceay onay atthay
irringstay Unejay orningmay. Eythay adhay eptslay atelay. Ountcay Aninpay adhay alwaysay eenbay
ilatoryday, unreadyay. Itay isay aidsay ofay imhay atthay ethay Empressay Elisabethay adhay
onceay astcay erhay eyeay uponay imhay asay aay ikelylay avoritefay. Eshay ummonedsay imhay oneay
ayday otay aitway orfay erhay outsideay ethay athbay; utbay enwhay eshay emergeday eshay oundfay
imhay umpledcray onay ishay airchay astfay asleepay. Osay eshay ecidedday otay employay imhay
inay ethay iplomaticday ervicesay. Onay ethay orningmay ofay Atherine’scay accessionay,
afteray ourteenfay yearsay ofay internationalay iplomacyday, Ountcay Aninpay adhay otnay
angedchay. Enwhay ehay entereday ethay Interway Alacepay ithway ishay argechay, ethay Empressay
amecay otay eetmay emthay anday arriedcay ethay oybay outay onay ethay alconybay otay esentpray
imhay asay erhay eirhay. Isthay asway ethay enday ofay Anin’spay emeschay otay akemay Aulpay
emperoray, Aul’spay othermay ethay Egentray, anday imselfhay Andgray Ancellorchay. Ehay
emainedray alwaysay atherray esentfulray aboutay itay anday idday otnay ailfay otay amperhay
ethay ambitionsay ofay ethay Orlovsay eneverwhay ehay adhay aay ancechay. Atherinecay aidsay ofay
imhay, ount“cay Aninpay asway aturallynay indolentay, anday ehay adhay ethay artay ofay akingmay
ishay indolenceay asspay orfay alculatingcay udence.pray”

Ethay oorsday ofay ethay Interway Alacepay ereway ownthray ideway openay anday anybodyay omfray
ethay eetstray ouldcay enteray anday isskay ethay andhay ofay ethay ewnay Empressay. Ethay alacepay
asway aay orgeousgay ewnay uildingbay, onlyay ustjay ompletedcay, yetay allay ethay ommoncay
oldierssay ereway eefray otay amptray oughthray itay anday aketay ethay oathay ofay allegianceay
otay eirthay Ittlelay Othermay. Itay asway aay astermay okestray. e“thay eastlay oldiersay ofay
ethay uards,gay” Atherinecay otewray otay Oniatovskypay, on“ay eeingsay emay aidsay otay
imselfhay: atthay isay ethay orkway ofay ymay ands.hay” Otheray astermay okesstray ofay ethay
Empressay ereway ethay uentflay anifestoesmay ichwhay eshay omposedcay omfray imetay otay
imetay uringday ethay ollowingfay aysday, otay ebay etsay upay anday intedpray inay ethay ellarcay
eneathbay ethay Academyay ofay Iencescay anday istributedday otay aay eoplepay owhay ouldcay
otnay eadray emthay. Inay 1762AY, ewfay ofay ethay oblesnay ouldcay eadray. Ortunatelyfay ethay
anifestoesmay ereway arefullycay eservedpray inay ethay archivesay orfay ethay enjoymentay
ofay aay oremay iteratelay ageay.

Ethay irstfay oneay afteddray ybay erhay acilefay andhay eadray usthay: e“way ybay ethay Acegray ofay
Odgay, Atherinecay IIAY, Empressay anday Autocratay ofay allay ethay Ussiasray, etc.ay, etc.ay,
Allay uetray onssay ofay ethay Ussianray Atherlandfay avehay earlyclay eensay ethay angerday
ichwhay eatenedthray ethay Ussianray Empireay. Amelynay, ethay awlay ofay ouray Orthodoxay
Eekgray Urchchay ashay eenbay akenshay ybay ethay isregardday ofay ecclesiasticalay
aditionstray, osay atthay ouray ancientay Orthodoxay Urchchay inay Ussiaray asway exposeday
otay ethay extremeay angerday ofay eingbay obligeday otay adoptay anotheray onfessioncay.
Econdlysay, ouray oriousglay Ussiaray, ichwhay ashay eenbay iftedlay otay aay ighhay egreeday
ybay itsay onqueringcay eaponsway, ashay eenbay acedplay inay ompletecay ubjectionsay
otay itsay itterestbay enemyay ybay ethay ewnay eacepay orfay ichwhay osay uchmay oodblay ashay
eenbay iltspay, ilewhay ethay inneray organizationay ofay ethay ountrycay, onay ichwhay ethay
olewhay Atherlandfay ependsday, ieslay inay uinsray. Ereforethay anday ecausebay eway
areay onvincedcay ofay ethay angerday otay ouray aithfulfay ubjectssay, eway avehay eensay
Ourselvesay obligeday ithway ethay elphay ofay Odgay anday ishay Usticejay, utbay especiallyay
inay esponseray otay ethay istinctday anday undissimulateday ishway ofay Ouray aithfulfay
ubjectssay, otay ascenday ethay onethray asay Autocratay ofay allay ethay Ussiasray,
ereuponwhay allay Ouray aithfulfay ubjectssay avehay akentay ethay olemnsay oathay ofay
allegianceay otay Usay.

ATHERINE.CAY”

Uringday ethay ayday ethay Empressay anday erhay ounsellorscay ecidedday atthay aay ilitarymay
ampaigncay otay Eterhofpay asway ecessarynay. Ethay objectay asway otay ecuresay ethay ersonpay
ofay Eterpay IIIAY anday obtainay ishay abnegationay ofay ethay onethray. Asay Erbrücknay
ellway ointspay outay, ethay o-calledsay armyay ichwhay Atherinecay IIAY edlay otay Eterhofpay
asway artlypay aay ectacularspay, omanticray aradepay anday artlypay anay exhibitionay ofay
oliticalpay eniusgay.

Atay entay o’clockay inay ethay earclay ightlay ofay ethay eveningay ofay Unejay 28AY, 1762AY, ethay
Olonelcay ofay ethay uard--catherinegay erself--tookhay erhay aceplay atay ethay eadhay ofay
erhay oopstray. Eshay asway ountedmay onay aay itewhay orsehay anday oreway oakay eaveslay inay erhay
airhay. Erhay uniformay asway orrowedbay omfray aay ieutenantlay inay ethay Ifelay Uardsgay. Itay
asway oubtlessday osenchay ecausebay ethay ieutenantlay anday ethay Empressay appenedhay
otay ebay ofay aay izesay, utbay itay arcelyscay othedclay erhay ewnay ositionpay anday itletay.
Orfay Atherinecay adhay otnay esitatedhay otay assumeay ethay itletay Olonelcay ofay ethay
Uardsgay, ethay aditionaltray aceplay ofay ethay Arsczay ofay Ussiaray ichwhay Eterpay adhay
esignedray otay ishay Uncleay Eorgegay ofay Olsteinhay. Esidebay erhay atay ethay eadhay ofay ethay
oopstray, ikewiselay adclay inay ilitarymay uniformay, oderay ethay Ountesscay Atherinecay
Ashkovday. Uringday ethay ightnay eshay emainedray esidebay ethay Empressay, ilewhay erhay
istersay, Elisabethay Orontsovvay, uckstay oseclay otay ethay Emperoray. Erethay asway eepday
ealousyjay etweenbay ethay isterssay.

Atherinecay IIAY eftlay ethay ollowingfay otenay, ittenwray inay erhay ownay ongstray eefray
owingflay andhay: entlemen“gay anday Enatorssay! IAY ogay ownay ithway ethay Armyay otay
ecuresay anday afeguardsay ethay onethray, anday eavelay inay youray arecay asay ymay ighesthay
epresentativesray ithway ethay ullestfay onfidencecay ethay Atherlandfay, ethay Eoplepay,
anday ymay Onsay.

ATHERINE.CAY”

Ethay Enatesay olemnlysay espondedray inay aay otenay ichwhay overtookay ethay Empressay
atay otway o’clockay inay ethay orningmay, estingray onay erhay ayway otay Eterhofpay: is“hay
Ighnesshay, ethay Arevichczay, isay asay ellway asay ouldcay ebay esiredday. Inay ethay ousehay
ofay Youray Imperialay Ajestymay, asay ellway asay inay ethay itycay, allay oesgay ellway anday ethay
easuresmay youay avehay ommandedcay areay eingbay arriedcay out.ay”

Atherinecay estrodebay erhay orsehay anday oderay onwarday otay Eterhofpay. Eshay adhay
ivedlay orfay isthay iumphanttray omentmay: ittlelay Ikefay idingray erhay illowpay inay
ethay arkday edroombay atay Ettinstay; Andgray Uchessday Atherinecay anteringcay aboutay
ethay ourtyardcay inay Etersburgpay ilewhay anay admiringay iding-masterray issedkay
erhay oot,--thesebay earlieray exhibitionsay adhay eparedpray ethay ayway orfay isthay
ectacularspay ideray atay ethay eadhay ofay erhay ectacularspay armyay. Utbay itay asway erhay
astlay owyshay ideray. Inay ethay uturefay, eshay ouldway ebay ootay usybay anday erhapspay aay
adeshay ootay erioussay.


5

Eightay ourshay afteray Atherinecay anday Alexeiay Orlovay adhay eftlay Eterhofpay,
Eterpay anday aay aygay artypay ovedray oughthray ethay arkpay anday altedhay inay ontfray
ofay Onplaisirmay. Ethay adieslay anday entlemengay angspray omfray ethay owlay
air-à-bancs_chay_ anday olledstray aboutay ethay erracetay. Onay oneay amecay otay elcomeway
emthay. Ethay edray avilionpay asway emptyay anday ilentsay. Eterpay entway oughthray ethay
oomsray earchingsay orfay Atherinecay inay ainvay. Itay isay aidsay atthay ehay evenay ookedlay
underay ethay edbay. Ystifiedmay anday aguelyvay alarmeday ethay artypay anderedway ownday otay
ethay ierpay erewhay eethray allsmay esselsvay ereway ooredmay.

Erehay eythay eceivedray ethay irstfay ewsnay ofay eventsay inay Etersburgpay. AAY anmay
ingingbray ethay inevitableay ire-worksfay orfay ethay Ar’sczay ame-daynay andedlay omfray
aay allsmay oatbay atay eethray o’clockay. Ehay oldtay owhay ethay Eobrazhenskypray Egimentray
adhay ailedhay Atherinecay asay Empressay atay inenay o’clockay atthay orningmay anday owhay
ehay adhay everthelessnay ustjay onegay aboutay ishay usinessbay ofay ethay ayday, ichwhay
asway otay ingbray ethay ire-worksfay otay Eterhofpay. Isthay eemedsay efiniteday enoughay.
Atherinecay adhay utiniedmay.

Eterpay asway accompanieday ybay Ountcay Ichmünnay, Incepray Ubetskytray, Ancellorchay
Orontsovvay, Ountcay Uvalovshay, everalsay otheray oblesnay anday officersay, anday
aboutay eventeensay adieslay. Ishay olday utortay, Ehlinstay, ellstay ethay orystay ofay
isthay ayday. Oughoutthray ethay unnysay afternoonay ethay artypay emainedray onay ethay
owerlay erracetay. Ethay adieslay anday entlemengay ithdrewway aay ittlelay otay ethay
ardengay, erewhay eythay aylay etchedstray outay underay ethay openay yskay oughthray ostmay
ofay ethay inefay ummersay ayday anday aay artpay ofay ethay inefay ummersay ightnay. Eterpay anday
ishay advisersay ingeredlay earnay ethay analcay anday otewray oneay ukaseay afteray ethay
otheray ichwhay ethay Arczay ignedsay againstay ethay onestay alustradebay anday entsay otay
Etersburgpay. Ehay acedpay upay anday ownday ethay alkway esidebay ethay analcay anday ooktay
everybody’say adviceay inay urntay. Inallyfay Ancellorchay Orontsovvay olunteeredvay
otay ogay otay Etersburgpay anday ingbray ethay Empressay otay erhay ensessay. Enthay Uvalovshay
anday Ubetskytray epartedday onay imilarsay errandsay. Utbay ikelay ethay otheray esslay
importantay essengersmay omwhay ethay Arczay adhay alreadyay ispatchedday otay ethay itycay,
esethay entlemengay alsoay idday otnay eturnray.

Eter’spay earsfay increaseday. Ethay Olsteinhay Uardsgay owhay adhay eenbay entsay overay
omfray Oranienbaumay otay efendday Eterhofpay againstay attackay eportedray atthay erethay
asway onay ammunitionay inay ethay aceplay. Aduallygray, asay ethay ourshay assedpay, aay anplay
aturedmay ybay ichwhay ethay olewhay artypay ouldway ogay otay Onstadtkray inay ethay eethray
esselsvay ichwhay aylay atay anchoray atay ethay ootfay ofay ethay analcay. AAY essengermay asway
entsay otay ethay islanday anday eturnedray ithway ethay eportray atthay ethay ayway asway earclay.
Itay asway anay erroray, asay Eterpay earnedlay enwhay ehay iedtray otay ingbray ishay yachtay intoay
ethay Onstadtkray arborhay atay ourfay o’clockay inay ethay orningmay. Onenay ofay ethay eethray
esselsvay asway alloweday otay approachay ethay islanday anday ethay atchmanway alledcay
ackbay utallybray acrossay ethay aterway, ere“thay isay onay Eterpay IIIAY. Erethay isay onlyay
Atherinecay II.AY”

Ethay Ar’sczay yachtay ellfay awayay anday ooktay ethay oursecay owardtay Oranienbaumay. Ethay
Arczay imselfhay aylay onay ethay eckday inay aay eadday aintfay.

Earlyay ethay extnay orningmay, orerunnersfay omfray Atherine’scay advancingay
armyay eganbay otay allopgay upay otay Eterhofpay. Irstfay anday oremostfay onay ethay
enescay, atay eachay agestay ofay ethay evelopmentsday, asway Alexeiay Orlovay. Uietqay,
undistinguisheday, inexorableay, ehay asway ethay Empress’say ownay anmay. Ethay Olonelcay
erselfhay arriveday atay Eterhofpay atay elevenay o’clockay. Eshay entsay essengersmay
orwardfay otay Oranienbaumay, emandingday Eter’spay abnegationay, ichwhay ethay
emblingtray Arczay asway ybay isthay imetay inay onay oodmay otay efuseray. Eneralgay Ismailovay
oughtbray ackbay otay ethay Empressay ethay officialay ocumentday inay ichwhay ethay Arczay
enouncedray allay aimsclay uponay ethay onethray.

Itay asway Eneralgay Ismailovay owhay uredlay ethay ex-emperoray intoay aay arriagecay ithway
ethay omisepray atthay ehay ouldway ebay entsay otay Olsteinhay ithway Elisabethay Orontsovvay.
Asay oonsay asay eythay adhay assedpay ethay atesgay ofay Oranienbaumay, ethay Arczay asway
eparatedsay omfray ishay avoritefay anday oughtbray asay aay isonerpray otay Eterhofpay. o“tay
eventpray imhay omfray eingbay orntay otay iecespay ybay ethay oldiers,say” ayssay Atherinecay,
e“hay asway utpay inay ethay argechay ofay aay eliableray uardgay underay ethay ommandcay ofay
Alexeiay Orlov.ay” Omfray isthay imetay onay Eterpay asway atay ethay ercymay ofay ishay ilitarymay
uardsgay; ehay evernay awsay ishay istressmay againay. Utbay ethay ostsghay ofay ishay atherfay,
Erbrümmay anday Ergholzbay, anday allay ethay utorstay anday overnorsgay owhay adhay orturedtay
ishay ildhoodchay inay ethay amenay ofay isciplineday, ownay owdedcray uponay imhay ithway
unspeakableay errorstay. Onlyay ownay eythay orebay ethay amesnay ofay Alexeiay Orlovay,
Eodorfay Ariatinskybay, anday otheray Ussianray officersay.


6

Eterpay asway ivendray upay otay Eterhofpay inay aay osedclay arriagecay, ithway awndray
urtainscay. Ehay asway akentay intoay anay emptyay oomray, ippedstray ofay ishay uniformay,
anday eftlay inay utteray olitudesay. Atay ethay otheray enday ofay ethay alacepay, emoteray anday
invisibleay, atsay ethay erribletay Empressay. Omfray erhay amecay essengersmay omfray imetay
otay imetay, irectingday isthay anday ommandingcay atthay. Oneay ofay ethay essengersmay asway
Ountcay Aninpay, amiableay, oftsay Aninpay. Ethay Empressay apparentlyay ishedway otay
ommunicatecay ithway imhay oughthray umanhay agentsay asay ellway asay olvesway ikelay Alexeiay
Orlovay. Utbay ifay Eterpay asway aay eatingblay amblay, Aninpay asway aay atfay olday eepshay.
Ishay intervieway ithway ethay eposedday Arczay, inay ichwhay ethay isonerpray issedkay ishay
andhay, alternatelyay eadingplay anday ommandingcay, eftlay aay ainfulpay oundway onay aay
ensitivesay ersonalitypay. Aninpay afterwardsay aidsay atthay ehay onsideredcay itay oneay
ofay ethay eatestgray isfortunesmay ofay ishay ifelay atthay ehay asway obligeday otay eesay
Eterpay IIIAY onay isthay ayday. Ethay emorymay auntedhay imhay anday ademay imhay earfulfay
onay ehalfbay ofay ethay ittlelay oybay ehay asway ingingbray upay, Aulpay Etrovichpay, owhay
elievedbay imselfhay otay ebay ethay onsay ofay ethay artyredmay Arczay.

Ethay Empressay alloweday ethay isonerpray otay oosechay ethay aceplay ofay ishay
onfinementcay. Eterpay osechay Opsharay, aay allsmay estateay ithway aay argelay ardengay
anday aay ishingfay ondpay otnay anymay ilesmay omfray Eterhofpay. Atwhay ethay Empressay
eallyray intendeday otay oday ithway Eterpay onay oneay owsknay oray everay ewknay, obablypray
eshay erselfhay eastlay ofay allay. Utbay isthay isay atwhay eshay aidsay eshay intendeday,
oughthay itay asway anymay yearsay afterwardsay atthay eshay otewray itay. o“tay ogay ithway
Eterpay otay Opsharay, ethay Empressay amednay Alexeiay Orlovay, Incepray Ariatinskybay,
anday everalsay otheray officersay. Eythay osechay aay undredhay enmay omfray ethay
ifferentday egimentsray ofay ethay uardgay. Eythay adhay ordersay otay akemay ethay ifelay ofay
ethay onarchmay asay agreeableay asay ossiblepay anday otay ovidepray atwhay ehay ishedway
orfay ishay entertainmentay. Ethay intentionay asway otay endsay imhay omfray erethay otay
Elburgschlüssay anday, accordingay otay ircumstancescay, otay alloway imhay afteray
omesay imetay otay ogay ithway ishay avoritesfay otay Olsteinhay. Osay ittlelay asway ishay
ersonalitypay egardedray asay angerous.day”

Atwhay actuallyay appenedhay atay Opsharay asway uiteqay ifferentday. Eter’spay agedytray
amecay iftlysway. Utshay upay inay aay edroombay anday otnay alloweday otay eavelay itay evenay
orfay exerciseay, ishay existenceay asway unutterablyay iserablemay. Afteray ethay irstfay
ightnay ehay omplainedcay ofay ethay edbay anday askeday otay avehay ishay ownay edbay oughtbray
omfray Oranienbaumay. Uriouslycay enoughay, isthay imwhay asway omptlypray atifiedgray
ybay Alexeiay Orlovay owhay adhay ethay eatgray our-posterfay anday allay itsay appingstray
oughtbray otay Opsharay anday etsay upay eforebay ightfallnay. Anay Englishay avellertray
owhay awsay isthay edbay everalsay yearsay afterwardsay escribesday itay orfay usay. it“ay adhay
aay itewhay atinsay overletcay, anday asway onay aay argelay our-postfay edsteadbay, ithway
urtainscay ofay inkpay anday ilversay ocadebray, anday ornamenteday atay ethay optay ithway aay
umeplay ofay edray anday itewhay eather.fay” Utbay evenay ishay ownay edbay oughtbray ittlelay
omfortcay otay ethay ictimvay. Ehay emainedray inay ilighttway anday olitudesay, orfay ehay asway
otnay ermittedpay otay openay ethay eengray urtainscay ichwhay unghay atay ethay indowsway.
Inay esperationday, ehay askeday orfay ompanionscay, anday againay ishay equestray asway
antedgray. Ishay egronay Arcissusnay, ishay ogday, anday ishay iolinvay ereway oughtbray,
atay ethay Empress’say ommandcay, omfray Oranienbaumay. Ehay eggedbay orfay Elisabethay
Orontsov’svay esencepray utbay isthay asway efusedray imhay. Esentlypray ehay ellfay illay
ithway iarrhœaday, aay iseaseday otay ichwhay ehay asway alwaysay ubjectsay inay aay isiscray.
Ishay ersonalpay ysicianphay asway oughtbray otay Opsharay.

Ethay eniencylay ofay ethay Empressay earsbay outay erhay atementstay ofay erhay intentionsay.
Omfortedcay ybay Arcissusnay, ishay ogday, anday ishay iolinvay, Eterpay ightmay ivelay
onay atay Opsharay indefinitelyay. Utbay itay asway aay ullday ifelay orfay ethay uardsgay.
Orlovay, Ariatinskybay, Asseckpay anday ethay othersay ereway accustomeday otay allay
ethay excitementay ofay ifelay inay Etersburgpay. Ayingplay ardscay allay ayday anday allay
ightnay atay Opsharay asway onotonousmay entertainmentay ybay omparisoncay. Ixsay aysday
ofay itay avegay emthay aay icturepay ofay uturefay eeksway, uturefay onthsmay, etchingstray
ossiblypay intoay yearsay. Ethay evolutionray, ithway allay itsay ectichay anticipationsay,
asway overay, anday isthay asway erewhay itay adhay andedlay emthay. Itay asway allay eryvay ellway
orfay ethay Empressay anday ethay othersay, enjoyingay ifelay inay Etersburgpay, otay ebay
agnanimousmay owardtay ethay isonerpray, otay aketay easuresmay otay itigatemay ishay
ufferingsay anday olongpray ishay enduranceay. Inay ethay eyesay ofay enmay ikelay Orlovay anday
Ariatinskybay, Eterpay asway otnay aay anmay anywayay. Ehay asway onay etterbay anthay aay ormway
atthay aylay inay eirthay athpay anday askeday otay ebay eppedstay onay. Eythay ayedplay ardscay
anday ankdray eavilyhay. Aturdaysay amecay anday atay id-daymay Eterpay asway inviteday otay
omecay outay ofay ishay oomray anday ineday ithway ethay uards...gay.

Inay ethay eantimemay ethay Empressay, establisheday inay ethay Interway Alacepay, eceivedray
ailyday essagesmay omfray ethay ex-czaray anday Alexeiay Orlovay aboutay ethay ogresspray ofay
ingsthay atay Opsharay. Eethray iefchay etitionspay omfray ethay isonerpray anday eethray
etterslay omfray ishay ailerjay ojectpray orfay usay ethay enesscay ofay ethay agedytray ichwhay
evelopedday osay iftlysway anday inevitablyay omfray ethay ircumstancescay.

adame,“may” otewray Eterpay, I“AY egbay Youray Ajestymay otay estray assureday oncerningcay
emay, anday otay avehay ethay oodnessgay otay orderay atthay ethay uardsgay ebay emovedray omfray
ethay econdsay oomray, inay orderay atthay IAY aymay ovemay aboutay inay erethay; ecausebay, asay
youay owknay, IAY alwaysay alkway aboutay inay ethay oomray anday IAY allshay otherwiseay etgay
ollensway egslay. Enthay IAY egbay youay urtherfay otay ommandcay ethay officersay otnay otay
emainray inay ethay amesay oomray enwhay IAY avehay ecessitiesnay; atthay isay unendurableay
orfay emay. Inallyfay IAY eseechbay Youray Ajestymay otnay otay eattray emay ikelay aay eatgray
evil-doeray. IAY amay otnay onsciouscay atthay IAY avehay everay ongedwray youay. Ilewhay IAY
ommendcay yselfmay otay youray agnanimousmay oughtsthay, IAY egbay atthay youay illway atay
eastlay endsay emay ithway ethay ersonspay amednay otay Ermanygay. Odgay illway ertainlycay
ewardray youay. IAY amay, Youray eryvay evotedday ervantsay, Eterpay. P.SAY. Youray Ajestymay
ancay estray assureday ofay emay atthay IAY allshay inkthay anday oday othingnay againstay youray
ersonpay oray youray eign.ray”

Ethay econdsay otenay isay ortershay. your“ay Ajestymay: Ifay youay oday otnay ishway otay
estroyday utterlyay aay umanhay eingbay owhay isay alreadyay unhappyay enoughay, avehay itypay
onay emay anday endsay emay ymay onlyay onsolationcay, atthay isay Elisabethay Omanovnaray
orontsov][vay. Inay isthay youay illway ebay oingday oneay ofay ethay ostmay ercifulmay eedsday
ofay youray eignray. Alsoay ifay Youray Ajestymay ouldway utbay isitvay emay orfay oneay instantay
ymay ighesthay ishesway ouldway ebay ulfilledfay. Youray eryvay evotedday ervantsay, Eter.pay”

Ethay otway ecedingpray essagesmay ereway ittenwray inay Enchfray utbay ethay irdthay anday
astlay oneay asway ittenwray inay Ussianray, ethay anguagelay ichwhay Eterpay atedhay anday
Atherinecay ovedlay. Ethay owningdray anmay aughtcay evenay atay isthay awstray. your“ay
Ajestymay: IAY egbay youay, incesay IAY avehay ulfilledfay youray illway inay everythingay, otay
alloway emay otay ogay abroaday ithway osethay orfay omwhay IAY avehay alreadyay etitionedpay
Youray Ajestymay. Anday IAY opehay atthay youray agnanimitymay illway otnay eavelay emay
ithoutway ourishmentnay. Aithfulfay ervantsay, Eter.pay”

Ethay etterslay ofay Alexeiay Orlovay, oughtbray ybay ethay amesay essengermay, icturepay
atwhay asway appeninghay eanwhilemay inay ethay uardsgay’ uartersqay atay Opsharay.

Onay Uesdaytay ehay otewray: ittle“lay Othermay, Aciousgray Empressay: Ealthhay eway allay
ishway youay orfay ountlesscay yearsay. Eway anday ethay olewhay ommandcay areay ellway asay isthay
etterlay eaveslay usay, utbay ouray onstermay ashay owngray eryvay icksay anday ashay adhay anay
unexpecteday attackay ofay oliccay. Anday IAY amay afraiday atthay inay ethay enday ehay ightmay
ieday onighttay anday earfay illstay oremay againay atthay ehay ightmay ivelay. Ethay irstfay
earfay IAY avehay ecausebay ehay atterschay urepay onsensenay, anday atthay oesday otnay amuseay
usay; anday ethay econdsay earfay, ecausebay ehay isay eallyray angerousday orfay usay allay
ecausebay ehay oftenay eaksspay asay ifay ehay adhay ishay ormerfay ositionpay.

according“ay otay youray ordersay, IAY avehay aidpay ethay oldierssay orfay alfhay aay yearay,
alsoay ethay under-officersay ithway ethay exceptionay ofay Otiomkinpay, ecausebay ehay
ervessay ithoutway alarysay. Anymay ofay ethay oldierssay avehay okenspay ithway earstay ofay
youray Aciousnessgray, eythay adhay otnay eservedday osay uchmay ofay youay, otay ebay ewardedray
inay osay ortshay aay imetay. IAY endsay youay erewithhay aay istlay ofay ethay entireay ommandcay atay
esentpray erehay; utbay aay ousandthay ublesray ereway ackinglay, Ittlelay Othermay, anday
IAY avehay addeday emthay inay ucatsday. Erethay asway uchmay aughterlay erehay amongay ethay
uardsmengay onay accountay ofay ethay ucatsday, enwhay eythay eceivedray emthay omfray emay.
Anymay askeday uestionsqay ecausebay eythay adhay evernay yetay eensay anyay anday avegay emthay
ackbay otay emay ecausebay eythay oughtthay emthay orthway othing...nay. Untilay eathday,
youray evotedday aveslay, Alexeiay Orlov.ay”

Onay Aturdaysay orningmay, Orlovay otewray, our“ay Ittlelay Othermay, Aciousgray Empressay;
IAY owknay otnay atwhay IAY ouldshay oday orfay IAY embletray eforebay ethay angeray ofay Youray
Ajestymay, atthay youay oday otnay elievebay omethingsay awfulay aboutay usay, anday atthay eway
areay otnay ethay ausecay ofay ethay eathday ofay youray ascalray anday alsoay ofay Ussiaray anday
ouray awlay. Utbay ownay ethay ackeylay Aslovmay entsay otay ervesay imhay ashay allenfay illay anday
ehay imselfhay isay osay icksay atthay IAY oday otnay elievebay ehay illway ivelay untilay eveningay,
anday ehay isay alreadyay uiteqay unconsciousay; ichwhay ethay olewhay ommandcay owsknay anday
egsbay Odgay atthay eway ecomebay idray ofay imhay asay oonsay asay ossiblepay; anday isthay Aslovmay
anday ethay officeray ispatchedday ancay informay Youray Ajestymay inay atwhay onditioncay ehay
ownay isay, ifay youay areay easedplay otay oubtday emay. Isthay ittenwray ybay Youray Aithfulfay
Ervant....say”

Onay Aturdaysay eveningay, aay essengermay omfray Opsharay allopedgay upay otay ethay Interway
Alacepay ithway ethay astlay etterlay omfray Alexeiay. ittle“lay Othermay, Ercifulmay
Empressay. Owhay allshay IAY explainay oray escribeday atwhay ashay appenedhay? Youay illway
otnay elievebay youray evotedday aveslay utbay eforebay Odgay IAY illway eakspay ethay uthtray.
Ittlelay Othermay! IAY amay eadyray orfay eathday utbay IAY yselfmay oday otnay owknay owhay ethay
isfortunemay appenedhay. Eway areay ostlay ifay youay avehay otnay ercymay uponay usay. Ittlelay
Othermay, ehay iveslay onay ongerlay inay isthay orldway. Utbay onay oneay adhay oughtthay atthay,
anday owhay ouldshay eway avehay adhay ethay oughtthay otay iftlay andhay againstay ethay Arczay?
Utbay Empressay, ethay isfortunemay ashay appenedhay. Itay amecay otay aay uarrelqay atay abletay
etweenbay imhay anday Incepray Eodorfay: eway ouldcay otnay eparatesay emthay, anday alreadyay
ehay asway onay oremay. Eway annotcay ourselvesay ememberray atwhay eway avehay oneday, utbay
eway areay allay otay ethay astlay anmay uiltygay anday eserveday eathday. Avehay ercymay uponay
emay, ifay onlyay orfay ymay other’sbray akesay! IAY avehay ademay ymay onfessioncay anday erethay
isay othingnay otay investigateay. Ardonpay emay oray uicklyqay akemay anay enday ofay emay. IAY
atehay ethay ightlay ofay ayday: eway avehay angereday youay anday ouray oulssay areay urledhay otay
estruction.day”

Onay Undaysay orningmay ethay Empressay informeday ethay ublicpay ybay anay officialay
atementstay atthay Eterpay IIIAY adhay iedday ofay aay emorrhoidalhay attackay anday ouldway
ebay uriedbay inay ethay Alexanderay Evskynay Athedralcay. Erethay isay onay ecordray atthay
eshay everay iedtray otay ivegay anyoneay atay anyay imetay aay onfidentialcay explanationay
ofay Eter’spay eathday. Ethay etterslay ofay Alexeiay Orlovay ereway utpay awayay anday evernay
amecay otay ightlay untilay afteray erhay eathday. Erhay ilencesay emainedray unbrokenay.
Ormerlyfay isthay omanway adhay orriedway excessivelyay aboutay atwhay Europeay ightmay aysay
aboutay ethay irthbay ofay erhay irstfay ildchay anday erhay elationsray ithway Altikovsay.
Ownay Europeay adhay othingnay esslay anthay urdermay otay alktay aboutay, anday alktay anray
ighhay. Utbay Atherinecay eemedsay imperviousay otay anyay uriositycay oncerningcay isthay
oreignfay ossipgay. Asay anay olday omanway, oweverhay, eshay oneay ayday uddenlysay askeday
Iderotday, at“whay oday eythay aysay inay Arispay ofay ethay eathday ofay ymay usband?hay” Enwhay
Iderotday asway ootay embarrasseday otay answeray, eshay urnedtay ethay onversationcay ybay aay
estjay atay ishay expenseay.


7

Uringday ishay iefbray eignray, Eterpay IIIAY adhay eversedray ethay oreignfay oliciespay
ofay ishay atelay auntay. Ethay Austrianay anday Enchfray interestsay adhay onegay intoay
eclipseay, ilewhay ethay Ussianpray interestay adhay azedblay upay againay. Ederick’sfray
envoyay ivedlay atay ethay elboway ofay ethay Arczay isperingwhay oodgay adviceay otay aay
entalmay invaliday owhay asway unableay otay ofitpray ybay itay. Onay oonersay asway Eterpay
IIIAY outay ofay ethay ayway anthay ethay Austrianay anday Enchfray envoysay amecay outay ofay
eirthay etirementray anday eganbay otay eadplay eirthay ausecay ithway Atherinecay IIAY.
Eythay ooktay orfay antedgray atthay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray adhay adhay ishay ayday anday
atthay ishay enemiesay, Austriaay anday Ancefray, ouldway ownay avehay eirsthay. Adhay otnay
ethay Empressay issueday aay anifestomay inay ichwhay Ussiapray asway eferredray otay asay
Ussia’sray itterest“bay enemy”ay? Adhay otnay Ieldfay Arshalmay Altikovsay advanceday
uponay Ussianpray oilsay, openingay allay ofay aay uddensay anay offensiveay ampaigncay? Orfay
aay omentmay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray embledtray inay ishay ell-wornway ootsbay ilewhay ethay
opeshay ofay Ancefray anday Austriaay anray ighhay.

illustration[ay: ATHERINECAY ETHAY EATGRAY

om_fray aay aintingpay ybay Ericsen_ay]

Utbay ethay Empressay asway otnay occupieday ithway ethay interestsay ofay Ussiapray, oray
Austriaay, oray Ancefray. Eshay eferredpray ethay interestsay ofay Ussiaray, ichwhay
appenedhay otay ebay erhay ownay. Eshay ecalledray ethay astyhay Eneralgay Altikovsay omfray
Ussianpray erritorytay osay adroitlyay atthay ehay arcelyscay ewknay ehay adhay eenbay
ecalledray. Eshay assureday Austriaay anday Ancefray ofay erhay oodgay illway anday
iendshipfray anday eftlay emthay inkingthay atthay eirthay emporarytay estrangementay
omfray Ussiaray uringday Eter’spay eignray adhay eenbay ipedway outay. Atherinecay IIAY
ishedway otay avehay eacepay ithway Europeay. Eshay adhay alledcay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray
ethay eadlyday enemyay ofay Ussiaray onay ethay ayday ofay erhay accessionay; utbay aay ewfay
aysday afterwardsay eshay onfirmedcay ethay eacepay ithway Ussiapray ichwhay Eterpay IIIAY
adhay ademay anday ichwhay erhay anifestomay adhay enouncedday. Ethay Empressay ademay onay
attemptay otay ustifyjay isthay inconsistencyay. Eshay asway aay omanway ofay actionay anday
explanationsay avehay aay ayway ofay akingtay ootay uchmay imetay. Omfray erhay accessionay
untilay erhay eathday eshay asway oneay ofay ethay usiestbay onarchsmay inay Europeay.

illustration[ay: EGORYGRAY ORLOVAY]

Eshay ecalledray Estushevbay anday esentedpray imhay ithway aay eatgray ousehay urnishedfay
ithway omfortscay. Ethay olday anmay asway earlynay eventysay ownay anday ofay onay eatgray
ervicesay otay erhay. Utbay eshay oweday imhay uchmay anday ehay asway aay agnificentmay onumentmay
ecausebay ehay adhay onceay ownknay Eterpay ethay Eatgray. Eshay ecalledray Ironbay, alsoay
ageday ithway exileay, anday ademay imhay ethay Andgray Ukeday ofay Ourlandcay. Ehay asway
usefulay otay erhay erethay ecausebay ehay eptkay ethay Ousehay ofay Axonysay omfray ettinggay
aay ootholdfay inay Ourlandcay. Oniatovskypay, owhay adhay onglay awaiteday isthay ayday inay
Olandpay, ownay otewray askingay otay ebay ummonedsay otay Ussiaray, utbay eshay idday otnay
ecallray imhay. Eshay iscouragedday imhay omfray itingwray otay erhay atay allay, ayingsay, I“AY
ustmay alkway aightstray aheaday; IAY ustmay otnay ebay uspected.say” Eshay adhay onglay agoay
annedplay ithway Oniatovskypay anday Illiamsway atthay ethay Ountcay asway oneay ayday otay ebay
ademay ethay Ingkay ofay Olandpay. Eshay ownay urgeday ethay Ountcay otay opstay atay omehay inay
Olandpay anday abideay ethay oursecay ofay eventsay.

Oneay ofay Atherine’scay irstfay actsay asay Empressay asway otay ivegay ordersay orfay erhay
oronationcay. Ethay eremonycay ichwhay Eterpay adhay ostponedpay untilay ehay adhay atay
astlay iedday uncrowneday asway oremostfay inay erhay oughtsthay. Ourfay aysday afteray
erhay accessionay, eshay ordereday ethay ire-worksfay orfay erhay oronationcay; anday
evensay aysday afterwardsay, ethay ayday onay ichwhay ethay eathday ofay ethay unfortunateay
Eterpay ecamebay ownknay, eshay announceday ethay ateday. Itay asway otay aketay aceplay inay
Eptembersay. Eshay avegay Incepray Ubetskytray iftyfay ousandthay ublesray anday entsay
imhay otay Oscowmay otay etgay everythingay inay eadinessray. Ehay arriedcay ithway imhay ethay
ecificationsspay orfay aay eatgray ectaclespay, anday, ithway ethay assistanceay ofay aay
orpscay ofay officialay erry-makersmay, anagedmay otay ompletecay allay eparationspray
ithinway ethay imetay arrangeday orfay. Omptlypray onay ethay irstfay ayday ofay Eptembersay,
ethay Empressay eftlay Etersburgpay ithway anay enormousay aintray. Erethay asway evidentlyay
otay ebay onay ostponementpay ofay ethay ateday originallyay etsay orfay ethay eremonycay,
onay epetitionray ofay ethay uccessionsay ofay ostponementspay ichwhay adhay elayedday
ethay arriagemay ofay ethay Andgray Ukeday anday ethay Andgray Uchessday underay ethay atelay
Empressay. Ethay ewnay Empressay adhay onenay ofay ethay ilatorinessday ofay Elisabethay; eshay
adhay espectray orfay imetay. Inay isthay egardray, eshay emainedray alwaysay onlyay alfhay aay
Ussianray.

Etweenbay Etersburgpay anday Oscowmay, aay ightslay oudclay eateningthray elayday oseray
aboveay ethay orizonhay. Itay appeareday inay ethay irectionday ofay ethay aintray ofay Ountcay
Aninpay anday ishay upilpay, ethay Andgray Ukeday Aulpay. Ethay Empressay eceivedray aay
essagemay omfray Aninpay atthay ishay upilpay adhay allenfay illay ofay aay everfay anday ightmay
otnay ebay ableay otay enteray Oscowmay onay ethay expecteday ayday. Ouldway ethay Empressay
aveltray oremay owlyslay? Ethay Empressay altedhay anday aitedway ithway impatienceay.
Eshay asway ewardedray ybay aay econdsay essagemay ayingsay atthay ethay Andgray Ukeday adhay
anotheray anday aay orseway attackay. Ethay Empressay onay ongerlay averedway; eshay entsay erhay
ultimatumay otay Aninpay. Itay irectedday atthay Aninpay anday ishay aintray ouldshay aveltray
orwardfay enwhay ethay oy’sbay ealthhay ermittedpay; inay anyay asecay, ethay Empressay ouldway
enteray Oscowmay onay ethay ollowingfay Idayfray. Onay ethay eceiptray ofay isthay essagemay,
Aul’spay ealthhay uddenlysay ecamebay etterbay anday ehay asway ableay, underay ethay escortay
ofay Aninpay, otay enteray Oscowmay inay ethay ompanycay ofay ishay othermay.

Atherine’scay oronationcay ooktay aceplay inay ethay Emlinkray onay Undaysay, Eptembersay
23AY, 1762AY. Inay ethay earlyay orningmay ethay egimentsray archedmay oughthray ethay
oweringtay atesgay anday ationedstay emselvesthay inay ontfray ofay ethay ourfay eatgray
athedralscay osewhay innaclespay iseray ikelay itteringglay oldengay ulipstay aboveay ethay
itycay. Atay entay o’clockay ethay Empressay appeareday onay ethay Edray Aircasestay eadinglay
otay ethay Uspenskyay Athedralcay. Ixsay amberlainschay arriedcay erhay aintray anday Ountcay
Eremetievshay orebay ethay enday ofay itay. Ixsay onthsmay eviouslypray ehay adhay arriedcay
ethay aintray ofay ethay erraticay Eterpay atay ethay uneralfay ofay ethay Empressay. Isthay imetay
ishay officesay ereway accepteday ybay ishay overeignsay ithway upremesay ecorumday. Ethay
ocessionpray advanceday owlyslay, ilewhay ethay eatgray owdscray owhay adhay atheredgay
ithoutway ethay ilitarymay ordoncay anday occupieday ethay oofsray ofay ethay ouseshay azedgay
inay awestruckay ilencesay atay ethay ermine-and-silveray adclay igurefay ofay ethay
Empressay, eirthay Ittlelay Othermay. Onlyay ethay yriadmay ellsbay ofay Oscowmay okespay anday
ethay annonscay underedthay eirthay alutesay.

Omfray athedralcay otay athedralcay, ethay atelystay ocessionpray advanceday. Asay
Atherinecay acedplay ethay owncray uponay erhay ownay eadhay, ethay annonscay iredfay aay
alutesay onay ethay Edray Uaresqay. Urroundedsay ybay Elatespray anday Archimandritesay,
eshay everthelessnay osechay otay ivegay ethay Olyhay Ommunioncay otay erselfhay. Asay eshay
adhay onay ethay ightnay ofay Unejay 2AY8 unhesitatinglyay acedplay erselfhay atay ethay eadhay
ofay ethay armyay asay Olonelcay, eshay ownay acedplay erselfhay ithway ustjay asay uchmay
assuranceay atay ethay eadhay ofay ethay Urchchay ofay Ussiaray. Ownay asay enthay, onay oneay
uestionedqay erhay ightray otay oday osay.

Ilewhay ethay Empressay istributedday onorshay inay ethay Anovitayagray Alatapay, ethay
acredsay amberchay intoay ichwhay omenway adhay eenbay irstfay admitteday ybay Eterpay ethay
Eatgray, ethay olewhay itycay ofay Oscowmay asway urnedtay intoay oneay astvay estivalfay.
Ethay erry-makingmay asway olongedpray orfay eeksway. Ethay ountainsfay anray ineway,
eadbray anday oastray eatmay ereway ivengay orfay ethay askingay, anday ilversay ublesray ereway
ownthray otay ethay eoplepay. Onay inglesay aditiontray ofay andeurgray oray aciousnessgray
asway overlookeday ybay ethay ewnay Ussianray onarchmay. Anay allegoricalay ageantpay
alledcay ethay Ocessionpray ofay ethay Iumphanttray Inervamay oughtbray ethay oronationcay
estivitiesfay otay aay oseclay, utbay ybay isthay imetay interway asway osay arfay advanceday
atthay ethay erformerspay iveredshay inay ethay yingflay owsnay.

Ethay iumphanttray Inervamay asway aay appyhay allegoryay orfay Atherinecay. Otnay osay
appyhay erhapspay asway ethay inspirationay ofay ethay Archimandriteay ofay Oitskytray owhay
elcomedway erhay atay ethay atesgay ofay ethay Oisterclay ithway anay orationay omparingcay erhay
otay Udithjay. Afterwardsay aay oupgray ofay udentsstay, earingway old-embroideredgay
armentsgay anday eengray eathswray onay eirthay owingflay ockslay, angsay aay antatacay
omposedcay inay erhay onorhay. Ethay unmusicalay Empressay ouldcay otnay istinguishday oneay
otenay omfray anotheray utbay eshay orebay erselfhay aciouslygray oughoutthray. AAY ewfay
yearsay aterlay, owngray oremay accustomeday otay owerpay anday artlypay atiatedsay, eshay
asway esslay oleranttay. Eshay ouldway ometimessay endsay aay agepay otay ethay orchestraay inay
ethay eaterthay anday arbitrarilyay opstay ethay usicmay.


9

Aptaincay Egorygray Orlovay ecamebay Ountcay Orlovay onay ethay ayday ofay Atherine’scay
oronationcay. Eshay alsoay amednay imhay eneral-adjutantgay anday avegay imhay erhay
ortraitpay etsay ithway iamondsday ichwhay ehay oreway onay ishay eastbray. Egorygray Orlovay
atsay anymay imestay orfay ortraitspay ichwhay aymay illstay ebay eensay inay Etersburgpay
owingshay imhay otay ebay asay andsomehay asay eportray ashay ademay imhay outay. Ehay asway
indolentay anday unaspiringay, ontentcay otay ebay ethay escortay ofay erhay Ajestymay anday otay
escheway allay influenceay inay ublicpay affairsay. Inay ethay ingspray ofay 1763AY, afteray
Atherinecay adhay eenbay Empressay orfay aboutay aay yearay, aay umorray ofay erhay arriagemay
otay Egorygray Orlovay asway isperedwhay aboutay. Encewhay aroseay isthay umorray? Adhay ethay
othfulslay Egorygray uddenlysay ecomebay ambitiousay? Itay asway oremay ikelylay atthay ethay
ideaay amecay omfray Alexeiay, ethay eadhay ofay ethay Orlovay anclay.

Ountcay Egorygray occupieday anay equivocalay ositionpay. Ehay asway aay arvenupay anday ethay
avoritefay ofay ethay Empressay. Amongay ethay oblesnay, ethay Orlovsay ereway otnay opularpay.
Amongay ethay ortyfay officersay owhay adhay upportedsay Atherine’scay onspiracycay,
ereway anymay owhay egardedray emthay ithway aay ealousjay eyeay. Eythay adhay eenbay oweredshay
ithway onorshay anday ichesray, oughthay ethay Empressay adhay oneday uchmay alsoay orfay aay
umbernay ofay erhay upporterssay. Ethay intimacyay etweenbay ethay Empressay anday Egorygray
