Orlovay arouseday istrustday. Ifay ethay avoritefay ereway omotedpray otay ethay ositionpay
ofay aay onsortcay, ethay Orlovsay ouldway ertainlycay ecomebay owerfulpay. Eirthay
ellow-conspiratorsfay ereway otnay easedplay otay ebay osay arfay outstrippeday.

Erethay isay aay egendlay atthay aboutay isthay imetay ethay Empressay entsay Ancellorchay
Orontsovvay otay oundsay outay Ountcay Alexeiay Azumovskyray onay ishay allegeday arriagemay
otay Empressay Elisabethay. Accordingay otay ethay orystay, ethay ancientay Ountcay, astfay
allingfay otay ecayday inay ishay imneychay ornercay, ehavedbay eryvay angelystray enwhay
uestionedqay. Ehay oducedpray anay olday yelloway atin-coveredsay ocumentday ichwhay ehay
issedkay amaticallydray anday enthay ewthray intoay ethay openay irefay. Aditiontray ayssay
isthay asway ishay ertificatecay ofay arriagemay ichwhay ehay acrificedsay otay eventpray
itsay eingbay useday asay aay ecedentpray ybay Egorygray Orlovay inay ishay uitsay ithway ethay
Empressay. Ehay estroyedday ybay isthay actay ishay astlay ancechay otay ogay ownday otay
osteritypay asay anay onesthay usbandhay. Utbay ehay alsoay estroyedday ateverwhay opeshay
ofay aay ecedentpray ethay Orlovsay aymay avehay adhay. Ethay orystay asway irstfay oldtay ybay aay
escendantday ofay ethay Azumovskyray amilyfay anday aymay ellway ebay oubtedday.

Ateverwhay aymay avehay appenedhay inay Azumovsky’sray ousehay, ethay ossipgay idday otnay
opstay. Ethay Empressay, attendeday ybay Egorygray Orlovay, eftlay Oscowmay orfay Ostovray otay
endspay ethay onthmay ofay Aymay inay aay oisterclay. Onay oonersay adhay eshay eftlay ethay itycay
anthay olday Estushevbay oducedpray aay etitionpay, uggestingsay aay econdsay arriagemay
orfay ethay Empressay onay ethay oundsgray atthay ethay Andgray Ukeday Aulpay adhay uchsay
elicateday ealthhay. Enwhay isthay aperpay eachedray Aninpay, ehay askeday ethay Empressay
outrightay etherwhay itay asway issueday ithway erhay ermissionpay oray otnay. Ethay Empressay
aidsay otnay, utbay Aninpay idday otnay elievebay erhay. Ethay owntay alktay increaseday, anday
ittlelay oupsgray eganbay otay utpay eirthay eadshay ogethertay ehindbay osedclay oorsday.
Esentlypray aay ertaincay oomgray ofay ethay Edbay Amberchay, Itrovochay, owhay adhay eenbay
oneay ofay ethay uardsgay ofay ethay atelay Arczay atay Opsharay, asway arresteday anday eldhay
orfay aay ecretsay investigationay. Ethay youngay an’smay andfathergray asway enrageday.
Ehay etmay olday Estushevbay onay ethay eetstray anday oldedscay imhay. ercy“may onay usay,
youray Ighnesshay. Atwhay owerpay esethay Orlovsay avehay, atthay entlemengay ancay osay
ompletelycay isappear!day”

Itrovochay asway accuseday ofay avinghay ademay eatsthray againstay ethay ifelay ofay Alexeiay
Orlovay. Ethay Empressay, atchingway everythingay omfray erhay iding-placehay inay ethay
oisterclay, awsay atthay attersmay ereway owinggray erioussay. Essengersmay allopedgay
ackbay anday orthfay etweenbay Ostovray anday Oscowmay, ilewhay Atherinecay irectedday
ethay earinghay ofay Itrovochay otay ethay astlay etailday. Ethay eastlay ordway omfray ishay
ipslay asway etsay ownday onay aperpay orfay erhay. Inay ethay enday eshay entsay imhay offay otay ishay
ownay ountrycay estateay. Itay asway aay ightlay entencesay, orfay eshay idday otnay antway otay
increaseay ethay alktay.

Eshay avegay eremptorypay ordersay atthay ethay investigationay asway otay ebay eptkay
ecretsay. Utbay itay asway onay ongerlay ossiblepay. Allay Oscowmay asway alkingtay ofay ethay
affairay, anday ethay Empressay ewknay atthay Oscowmay asway alkingtay. Eshay ecidedday otay
issueay aay anifestomay ichwhay eshay alledcay ethay anifesto“may ofay Ilencesay” anday ichwhay
eshay ordereday otay ebay eadray alouday inay ethay eetsstray ofay Oscowmay. Ethay Esidentpray
ofay ethay Enatesay ummonedsay ethay owdscray ogethertay ybay ethay eatingbay ofay umsdray anday
enthay eadray alouday otay emthay esethay ommandscay ofay ethay Empressay:

it“ay isay Ouray Illway anday Ishway, atthay eachay anday allay ofay Ouray aithfulfay ubjectssay
allshay attenday aloneay otay eirthay officeay anday occupationay, anday allshay efrainray
omfray eadingspray unseemlyay anday oldbay umorsray. Utbay againstay Ouray expectationsay
anday otay Ouray eatgray istressday anday issatisfactionday, eway earhay atthay erethay areay
eoplepay ithway ickedway oughtsthay anday annersmay owhay inkthay otnay atay allay ofay ethay
ommoncay oodgay anday eacepay; utbay, attackeday ybay ingularsay ideasay aboutay ingsthay
ichwhay oday otnay oncerncay emthay anday ofay ichwhay eythay ancay avehay onay ealray owledgeknay,
everthelessnay eythay usybay emselvesthay ithway uttingpay esethay ideasay intoay
otheray eakway eads...hay. Althoughay uchsay armfulhay udgmentsjay eallyray eserveday
unishmentpay, orfay eythay amageday Ouray ownay anday ethay eneralgay eacepay, eway allshay
otnay inay isthay asecay oceedpray ithway ullfay ictnessstray; utbay, ithway Ouray inbornay
umanityhay, aternallymay admonishay allay osethay owhay avehay eenbay affecteday ybay
esethay estlessray oughtsthay otay efrainray omfray unnecessaryay onversation...cay.
Ifay oweverhay Ouray otherlymay admonitionay ashay onay effectay uponay eirthay ickedway
eartshay anday oesday otnay eadlay emthay ackbay uponay ethay ayway ofay ethay oodgay, enthay etlay
everyay oneay ofay esethay adbay eoplepay owknay atthay eway allshay oceedpray ithway ethay ullfay
engthstray ofay ethay aw....lay”

Ithway ethay Anifestomay ofay Ilencesay, ethay alktay oppedstay. Utbay ethay ojectpray
ofay arriagemay ithway Egorygray Orlovay alsoay amecay otay anay enday. Enwhay Atherinecay
eturnedray otay Oscowmay ethay ubjectsay adhay eenbay orgottenfay. Itay asway ethay onlyay
attemptay ofay erhay eignray otay acquireay aay egallay onsortcay anday otay inway ackbay ethay
oodgay amenay eshay adhay ostlay. Enceforthhay eshay asway otay emainray ethay idowway ofay
Eterpay IIIAY anday ethay istressmay ofay anymay overslay. Inay erhay ife-timelay eshay ademay
otway aliantvay attemptsay otay ecomebay aay espectableray arriedmay omanway utbay othbay ofay
emthay ailedfay orfay ollywhay ifferentday easonsray. Ethay irstfay imetay asway enwhay eshay
arriedmay ethay ineffectualay Eterpay. Ethay econdsay imetay asway enwhay eshay iedtray otay
arrymay Egorygray Orlovay anday asway oppedstay ybay ublicpay opinionay inay Ussiaray.




illustration[ay]




IXAY

ATHERINECAY ETHAY EATGRAY


Inay 1762AY, Etersburgpay asway illstay aay oodenway itycay. Ethay ourtcay itselfay adhay onlyay
ustjay emovedray omfray ethay aftydray oodenway alacepay onay ethay Evskynay otay ethay eatgray
onestay alacepay onay ethay Evanay. Ethay ouseshay ereway implesay oray ultiplemay ucturesstray
ofay uaredsqay ogslay ofay ethay ypetay illstay eensay inay Ussianray illagesvay. Ellarscay anday
asementsbay ereway unknownay. Otay ethay ubstantialsay Ermangay indmay ofay ethay Empressay,
ethay uperficialsay andeurgray ofay erhay apitalcay asway anay objectay ofay ecretsay
erisionday. eifenheim’s“gray ouse,hay” inay ichwhay eshay adhay eenbay ornbay, adhay eenbay
etterbay uiltbay. Eshay otewray aay ersevay aboutay ethay ousehay atthay Ackjay uiltbay ithoutway
anyay airwaystay ecausebay ethay airwaystay adhay eenbay orgottenfay.

Ethay ompositioncay illustratesay atwhay ethay Empressay oftenay aidsay ofay erselfhay,
anday eryvay ulytray, atthay eshay asway onay oetpay. Utbay itay eryvay ellway expressesay atwhay
eshay oughtthay ofay Ussianray uildingbay inay erhay imetay. Eshay alledcay erhay oggerelday aay
anson__chay.

ean“jay itbâtay uneay aisonmay,
Uiqay an’ay inay imeray inay aisonray:
Iverl’hay onay yay ejèlay outtay oideray,
L’étéay enay alay endray ointpay oidefray;
Ilay yay oubliaay escalierl’ay,
Uispay elay itbâtay enay espalier.ay”

Enwhay aay irefay okebray outay inay ethay itycay, itay asway aay oriousglay ectaclespay. Uringday
ethay irstfay interway ofay erhay eignray, ethay Empressay atchedway omfray erhay indowway
otway undredhay anday ortyfay oodenway ouseshay oinggay upay inay amesflay. Asay ethay arksspay
ascendeday omfray ethay oaringray ogslay againstay ethay acknessblay ofay ethay interway
yskay, eshay atchedway ethay isasterday ithway ixedmay eelingsfay, orfay eshay yearneday
otay ebuildray atthay uarterqay ofay ethay itycay anyhoway. Ithinway eethray yearsay itay
asway actuallyay ebuiltray ofay ickbray. Everalsay eatgray iresfay evastatedday ethay
itycay uringday ethay earlyay artpay ofay erhay eignray anday ethay Empressay estoredray ethay
avagedray ectionssay ithway ickbray anday uccostay ashedway inkpay anday eengray ybay Italianay
architectsay. Irstfay aisedray ybay Eterpay ethay Eatgray anday evelopedday ybay Atherinecay
ethay Eatgray, Etersburgpay asway anday emainsray orfay allay imetay aay ollywhay un-russianay
itycay, aay ittingfay onumentmay otay esethay otway ulersray owhay oinedjay Europeay anday
Ussiaray ogethertay.

Oughthay Atherinecay ethay Econdsay idedpray erselfhay onay eingbay aay Ussianray eshay
erishedchay aay ivatepray ornscay orfay uchmay atthay asway eciouspray otay ethay Ussiansray.
Erhay onesthay opinionay ofay Oscowmay, etsay ownday inay erhay ournaljay, owsshay isthay.
at“ay atthay imetay [1750]AY, evenay oremay anthay ownay, itay asway inay eneralgay eryvay
ardhay orfay ethay obilitynay otay eavelay Oscowmay, ethay itycay ichwhay eythay allay osay
ovedlay, erewhay azinesslay anday indolenceay areay eirthay iefchay occupationay. Eythay
ouldway adlyglay endspay eirthay olewhay iveslay erethay, ivingdray aboutay inay aay ichlyray
ildedgay arriagecay ehindbay ixsay ansspay ofay orseshay, aay ymbolsay ofay ethay alsefay
ideaay ofay uxurylay ichwhay eignsray erethay anday oncealscay omfray ethay eyesay ofay ethay
assesmay ethay ovenlinessslay ofay ethay astermay, ethay ompletecay isorganizationday
ofay ishay ouseholdhay anday ishay annermay ofay ifelay. Itay isay onay arityray otay eesay aay
endidlysplay ownedgay adylay inay aay onderfulway arriagecay ithway ixsay eanlay anday
abbilyshay arnessedhay orseshay ivedray outay omfray aay eatgray ourtyardcay eapedhay ithway
irtday anday ashtray. Erhay unkemptay ackeyslay inay ettypray iverylay isgraceday erhay ybay
eirthay oorishbay ehaviorbay. Enerallygay eakingspay, othbay enmay anday omenway owgray
oftsay inay isthay eatgray itycay: eythay eesay anday acticepray onlyay etchednesswray,
ichwhay eaveslay ethay ostmay undoubteday eniusgay otay erishpay anday ecayday. Ecausebay
eythay ollowfay eirthay umorshay anday eirthay imswhay, eythay evadeay allay awslay anday
executeay emthay adlybay. Ethay onsequencecay isay atthay eythay evernay earnlay otay
ommandcay atay allay oray atthay eythay ecomebay yrants...tay. Esidesbay isthay erethay
asway evernay aay eoplepay owhay adhay oremay objectsay ofay anaticismfay eforebay eirthay
eyesay, uchsay asay onder-workingway aintssay atay everyay epstay; urcheschay, arsonspay,
oistersclay, ayingpray othersbray, ascalsray, ievesthay, uselessay ervantssay inay
eirthay ouses--andhay uchsay ouseshay! Atwhay irtday inay osethay ouseshay, ichwhay occupyay
olewhay ieldsfay anday avehay udholesmay orfay ourtyardscay. Inay eneralgay everyay ersonpay
ofay ashionfay inay ethay itycay occupiesay otnay aay ousehay utbay aay allsmay arm.fay” Ethay
Empressay omplainedcay atthay ifay eshay entsay orfay aay ersonpay inay Oscowmay, eshay adhay otay
aitway untilay ethay extnay ayday orfay erhay answeray. Ethay Uscovitesmay adhay imetay. Ethay
Uscovitesmay ereway Ussiansray.

Althoughay Atherinecay asway eefray inay erhay iticismcray ofay ethay Oscowmay oblesnay, erhay
ownay ourtcay atay Etersburgpay asway ustjay asay extravagantay anday ostentatiousay oughthay
ossiblypay oremay orderlyay anday eanlyclay ithalway. Othbay entlemengay anday adieslay
oreway ewelsjay anday iamondsday. Egorygray Orlovay, atay ethay eighthay ofay ishay ortunesfay,
adhay aay uitsay ofay othesclay ichwhay ostcay aay illionmay ublesray anday ichwhay asway ewedsay
allay overay ithway iamondsday. Orlov’say extravaganceay asway ildmay omparedcay ithway
atthay ofay ishay uccessorsay, Otiomkinpay, owhay asway earlyclay obligeday otay outshineay
ethay achievementsay ofay ishay edecessorpray. Istorianshay avehay estimateday atwhay
ethay Empressay entspay onay ethay othesclay anday upkeepay ofay erhay everalsay avoritesfay
anday owhay uchmay eshay urnedtay overay otay emthay inay ethay ormfay ofay estatesay anday
otheray aluablevay oodsgay anday avehay oundfay ethay otaltay ockingshay. Inay isthay eshay
eemssay otay avehay utbay ontinuedcay ethay aditiontray ofay Elisabethay owhay avegay ethay
Anitchkovay Alacepay otay Azumovskyray anday aay andfulhay ofay ationalnay onopoliesmay
otay ethay Uvalovsshay. Allay ethay oblesnay aboutay ethay ourtcay adhay inheriteday avishlay
andardsstay omfray Eterpay ethay Eatgray anday ethay avoritesfay ofay ethay Empressay ouldcay
otnay ossiblypay ebay outshoneay ybay Eremetievshay anday Oganovstray owhay ereway ountscay
anday ichray enmay ybay inheritanceay. Atherine’scay avoritesfay ereway arvenuspay; eythay
oweday everyay opeckcay otay erhay. Eshay alwaysay awsay otay atthay. Ethay Empressay erselfhay
asway aay arvenupay; utbay ethay oblesnay ofay Oscowmay ereway otnay. Inay ethay alacespay erethay
ithway eirthay irymay ourtyardscay eltdway ethay ancientay oodblay ofay Ussiaray. Ilewhay ethay
Empressay iticizedcray eirthay irtday anday ostentationay, eshay ewknay atthay omfray ethay
ointpay ofay iewvay ofay Oscowmay eshay erselfhay asway aay arvenupay anday erhay avoritesfay
ereway utbay eaturescray ofay yesterdayay.


2

Upay otay ethay imetay ofay Atherinecay ethay Econdsay, ethay Arsczay ofay Ussiaray adhay eenbay
addresseday ybay ethay Europeanay ourtscay asay your“ay Ajesty.may” Asay oonsay asay ethay
Empressay asway ownedcray atay Oscowmay, eshay otifiednay ethay overeignssay ofay Europeay
atthay eshay expecteday inay ethay uturefay otay ebay addresseday asay your“ay Imperialay
Ajesty.may” Erhay equestray asway antedgray exceptay inay Ancefray, ichwhay adhay ethay
onsciousnesscay ofay eingbay ethay ostmay ivilizedcay ountrycay inay ethay orldway anday asway
oundbay otay egardray Ussiaray asay aay avagesay interloperay. Ancefray ouldway adlyglay
avehay ushedpay ethay igbay, unwieldyay, irtyday aoschay ownknay asay Ussiaray ackbay intoay
ethay armsay ofay Asiaay. Ethay Enchfray aintainedmay atthay ar“czay” idday otnay eanmay ethay
amesay asay emperor“ay” atay allay. Utbay Atherinecay aidsay ethay otway itlestay ereway
exactlyay ethay amesay, anday insisteday atthay is“hay Ostmay Istianchray Ajestymay” ofay
Ancefray ouldshay alwaysay addressay erhay asay er“hay Imperialay Ajestymay” ofay Ussiaray.
Atay astlay ethay Enchfray inistermay, Oiseulchay, agreeday. Enthay ehay entsay officialay
ommunicationscay otay Ussiaray inay ichwhay ethay ordway imperial“ay” idday otnay appearay.
Atherinecay efusedray otay eadray emthay oray otay ecognizeray anay envoyay owhay arriedcay
aperspay addresseday erelymay otay er“hay Ajesty.may” Ushedpay intoay aay ornercay,
Oiseulchay inallyfay eclaredday atthay imperial“ay Ajestymay” asway impureay Enchfray, aay
orruptioncay ofay ethay acredsay anguagelay ichwhay ethay Enchfray Academyay existeday otay
otectpray. Ethay argumentay etweenbay Ersaillesvay anday Etersburgpay unspay itselfay outay
orfay yearsay.

Ikelay aay oodgay anday aithfulfay ifeway, Adamemay eday Oiseulchay oinedjay inay ethay uarrelqay
anday entway aboutay allingcay ethay Empressay ofay Ussiaray aay onster.“may” Itay asway
isthay adylay owhay ovokedpray omfray Oltairevay ishay amousfay ordsway inay efenseday ofay
Atherinecay ethay Eatgray. I“AY aymay oastbay otay youay atthay IAY andstay atherray inay ethay
oodgay acesgray ofay ethay Empressay; IAY amay erhay ightknay owardtay anday againstay allay.
IAY owknay ellway atthay eshay isay eproachedray orfay everalsay iflestray owardstay erhay
usbandhay. Osethay areay amilyfay attersmay inay ichwhay IAY oday otnay ixmay. Oreovermay itay
isay alsoay ellway ifay oneay ashay aay ongwray otay akemay oodgay. Enthay itay ecomesbay one’say
irstfay interestay otay akemay eatgray effortsay otay inway orfay oneselfay ethay espectray anday
admirationay ofay ethay ublicpay. Ertainlycay erhay eadfuldray usbandhay ouldway otnay avehay
accomplisheday oneay ofay ethay ingsthay ichwhay ymay Atherinecay accomplishesay everyay
ay.day”

Atherinecay ethay Econdsay asway erhay ownay oreignfay inistermay. Ethay enmay omwhay eshay
acedplay atay ethay eadhay ofay ethay Ollegecay ofay Oreignfay Affairsay ereway ollowersfay
otnay eaderslay. Enwhay eshay ascendeday ethay onethray, eshay ewknay oremay aboutay ethay
internationalay elationsray ofay Europeay anthay eshay idday aboutay ethay internalay
affairsay ofay Ussiaray. Eshay asway otay earnlay aboutay Ussiaray afteray eshay ecamebay itsay
Empressay. Inay 1762AY, ethay alignmentay ofay ethay Europeanay ationsnay adhay eenbay
ownthray intoay ighhay eliefray ybay ethay arlikeway activitiesay ofay Ederickfray ethay
Eatgray. Internationalay oblemspray ereway erfectlypay amiliarfay otay erhay. Erhay
opinionay asway ormedfay anday eshay asway eadyray otay aketay actionay. Atherinecay adhay
eenbay inspireday ybay Achiavelli’smay ince,“pray” ichwhay eshay adhay eadray uringday ethay
Oniatovskypay eriodpay enwhay eshay adhay intriguesay orfay owerpay ithway Irsay Arleschay
Anburyhay Illiamsway orfay anay allyay.

Inay ishay onumentalmay orkway onay Atherinecay ethay Eatgray, Ilbassovbay evotesday aay
apterchay otay aay etailedday accountay ofay ethay eadingray ofay ethay Andgray Uchessday
uringday ethay yearsay ofay erhay irtualvay imprisonmentay ybay ethay Empressay Elisabethay,
anday emphasizesay ethay influenceay ichwhay erhay avoritefay authorsay adhay onay erhay
ubsequentsay areercay asay Empressay. Ilbassovbay oundfay onay erhay abletay Oltairevay,
Ontesquieumay, Acitustay, Oylebay; inay ortshay, aay ollectioncay ofay eefray inkersthay
owhay ightmay ebay expecteday otay ormfay ethay indmay ofay aay uturefay iberallay onarchmay.
Atherinecay eadray allay ofay esethay, utbay eshay alsoay eadray Achiavellimay, osewhay amenay
isay otnay entionedmay ybay Ilbassovbay inay ishay arefullycay eparedpray apterchay onay erhay
eadingray. Inay oneay ofay erhay etterslay otay Evalierchay Illiamsway, eshay uotesqay aay
aximmay ofay Achiavellimay otay ethay effectay atthay aay anmay isay arelyray asay ickedway asay ehay
oughtay otay ebay. Illiamsway asway aay ittlelay ockedshay apparentlyay, orfay ehay epliedray,
at“whay IAY aysay isay, ankthay Odgay, ethay ickedway arelyray avehay ethay ouragecay ichwhay
eythay oughtay otay avehay otay executeay eirthay ickedness.way” Otay ichwhay Atherinecay
epliedray oollycay, o“say uchmay ethay etterbay, ifay elay onbay Ieuday ashay urtailedcay ethay
ouragecay ofay ethay ickedway orfay ethay executionay ofay eirthay ickedness.way”

Ethay oreignfay olicypay ofay isthay Empressay asway uniformlyay aggressiveay. Inay erhay
omesticday oliciespay, erhay intentionsay ereway atay eastlay iberallay, utbay allay erhay
ealingsday ithway oreignfay ationsnay ereway astuteay anday edatorypray. Ethay ailtray
ofay Achiavellimay asway overay allay. Eshay orkedway orfay ethay expansionay ofay Ussiaray
anday oastedbay asay anay olday omanway ofay ethay umbernay ofay uaresqay ilesmay ichwhay
eshay adhay addeday otay erhay erritorytay. Ussiaray asway aay arvenupay anday eshay asway aay
arvenupay; eirthay ausecay asway oneay. Europeay ouldshay ebay astonisheday, anday itay asway
astonisheday. Itay espondedray ybay allingcay erhay ethay Emiramissay anday Essalinamay
ofay ethay Orthnay anday Atherinecay ethay Eatgray. Inay esethay igh-soundinghay itlestay,
eshay exulteday anday erhay ersonalitypay ettledsay intoay emthay asay erhay odybay ettledsay
omfortablycay intoay itsay ermineay oberay.


3

Enwhay ethay uiresqay allsfay eirhay otay ideway ancestralay acresay, ishay irstfay oughtthay
isay orfay ishay oundariesbay anday ishay encesfay. Osay itay asway ithway Atherinecay enwhay eshay
ellfay eirhay otay Ussiaray. Ourlandcay asway entrusteday otay Ironbay, ethay ecrepitday olday
Ukeday uledray ybay ishay aughtersday anday evotedday otay Atherinecay. Usthay ethay Empressay
ecuredsay isthay oundarybay ellway anday ouldcay enceforthhay ismissday itay afelysay omfray
erhay indmay. Eshay extnay onsideredcay erhay ownay orderbay ovincespray anday oundfay emthay
ootay estlessray orfay erhay astetay. Ittlelay Ussiaray, Ivonialay, anday Inlandfay eedednay
otay ebay abilizedstay anday eshay otewray otay Iazemskyvay ecommendingray eatmenttray otay
atthay enday. ese“thay ovincespray, ikelay atthay ofay Olensksmay, ustmay ebay induceday inay
ethay entlestgay annermay otay Ussifyray emselvesthay, osay atthay eythay onay ongerlay ooklay
arounday emthay ikelay olvesway inay ethay orest.fay”

Otay Olandpay eshay avegay erhay ownay ersonalpay attentionay. Atherine’scay amenay aysplay
aay eatgray erôlay inay ethay istoryhay ofay atthay ountrycay asay oneay ofay ethay originatorsay
ofay ethay istoricalhay ootinglay artypay ownknay asay ethay artitionpay ofay Olandpay. Eethray
onarchsmay aredshay ethay ootybay: Atherinecay ofay Ussiaray, Ederickfray ofay Ussiapray,
anday Ariamay Eresathay ofay Austriaay. Ariamay Eresathay isay ethay onlyay oneay ofay ethay
eethray owhay ashay evernay eenbay accuseday ofay inventingay ethay ideaay. Incesay Atherinecay
erselfhay exonerateday ethay Austrianay Empressay inay aay etterlay ichwhay eshay otewray otay
Immgray inay 1770AY, Ariamay Eresa’sthay acklay ofay esponsibilityray orfay ethay imecray
inay Olandpay eemssay ufficientlysay establisheday. as“ay arfay asay ethay earday orthyway
Adylay Ayerfulpray isay oncerned,cay” otewray ethay Ussianray Empressay, I“AY ancay aysay
othingnay oremay anthay atthay eshay ufferssay omfray everesay attacksay ofay ovetousnesscay
anday imperiousnessay. Otay eepway isay aay ignsay ofay epentanceray, utbay incesay eshay
alwaysay oldshay astfay otay atwhay eshay ashay anday uiteqay orgetsfay atthay otnay otay oday aay
ingthay againay isay ethay estbay indkay ofay epentanceray, erethay ustmay ebay omethingsay
ubbornstay inay erhay osombay. IAY earfay itay ustmay ebay ethay originalay insay ofay Adamay ichwhay
aysplay isthay azycray omedycay. Utbay atwhay oesday oneay askay oremay omfray uchsay aay omanway?
Ifay eshay isay aithfulfay otay erhay usbandhay, eshay ashay allay ethay irtuesvay anday eedsnay
othingnay ore.may” Ariamay Eresa’sthay etaliationray asway otay eakspay ofay ethay Empressay
ofay Ussiaray asay ette“cay emmefay” anday alktay aboutay erhay openlyay asay aay ooselay omanway.
Otwithstandingnay isthay exchangeay ofay ersonalpay insultsay, eythay oöperatedcay
illinglyway inay ethay eizuresay ofay Olishpay erritorytay.

Ethay exactay artpay ayedplay ybay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray inay ethay artitionpay ofay Olandpay
ashay evernay eenbay osay earlyclay establisheday. Itay isay anay embarrassingay episodeay
orfay ethay Ussianpray istorianhay otay explainay. Otay assertay, asay Erschlözay oesday,
atthay Ederickfray onlyay aduallygray anday eluctantlyray onsentedcay isay anay attemptay
otay itewashwhay ethay erohay inay aay ayway ichwhay akesmay imhay ightlyslay unheroicay. Otay
ascribeay ethay initiativeay otay ethay Ussianray Empressay isay otay aceplay ethay eatgray
Ederickfray inay aay econdarysay ositionpay ichwhay isay inconsistentay ithway ethay
invincibleay ontfray ehay ashay alwaysay esentedpray otay istoryhay. Everthelessnay ethay
actualay ideaay, atthay isay, ethay executionay ofay ethay ideaay eemssay otay avehay occurreday
irstfay ofay allay otay Atherinecay. Ethay expectationay ofay ethay isasterday adhay onglay
existeday inay Olandpay, ichwhay adhay eenbay orewarnedfay aay enturycay eforebay ybay oneay ofay
itsay Ingskay, Anjay Asimircay, owhay aidsay atthay oneay ayday ethay ingthay ouldway appenhay
ustjay asay itay actuallyay idday appenhay. Ethay ismembermentday ofay Olandpay adhay eenbay
eensay asay aay ossibilitypay ybay allay ethay internationalay oliticianspay ofay Europeay
orfay oremay anthay aay enturycay eforebay itay ecamebay aay efiniteday icturepay inay ethay indmay
ofay Atherinecay ethay Econdsay. Eshay aloneay adhay ethay energizingay imageay atthay eadslay
otay actionay, anday asway undoubtedlyay esponsibleray orfay ethay irstfay Artitionpay ofay
Olandpay, althoughay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray aredshay ethay uiltgay orfay ethay econdsay
anday irdthay artitionspay ichwhay ollowedfay ogicallylay onay ethay irstfay.

Ethay epsstay ybay ichwhay Atherinecay amecay otay isthay ecisionday areay otnay ifficultday
otay acetray. Oonsay afteray erhay accessionay otay ethay Ussianray onethray, ethay Ingkay ofay
Olandpay aylay ownday otay ieday. Afteray aay eriessay ofay alsefay alarmsay, ehay actuallyay
idday ieday inay Eptembersay, 1763AY. Ethay Ingkay ofay Ussiapray anday ethay Empressay ofay
Ussiaray, owhay adhay eenbay isledmay osay oftenay ybay alsefay eportsray, ereway othbay upsetay
ybay ethay eventay enwhay itay inallyfay occurreday. Ederickfray angspray upay omfray ethay
abletay ithway ethay emarkray, I“AY atehay osethay eoplepay owhay alwaysay oday ingsthay atay
ethay ongwray ime.tay” Atherinecay alsoay angspray omfray erhay airchay enwhay ethay ewsnay
amecay, alvanizedgay orfay actionay. Eshay adhay opedhay orfay itay osay onglay. Erhay onglay
eferredday ansplay otay akemay Anislasstay Oniatovskypay Ingkay ofay Olandpay equiredray
instantay attentionay. Eshay adhay alreadyay instructeday erhay Ambassadoray, Ountcay
Ayserlingkay, oncerningcay ishay utiesday inay ethay esentpray isiscray. Ehay adhay inay actfay
eenbay electedsay orfay ethay ostpay ithway isthay eventay inay iewvay. I“AY amay endingsay Ountcay
Ayserlingkay ithoutway elayday asay Ambassadoray otay Oland,pay” eshay adhay ittenwray otay
Oniatovskypay, in“ay orderay otay akemay youay Ingkay afteray ethay eathday ofay Augustay IIIAY.
Ifay ymay Ambassadoray isay otnay uccessfulsay inay akingmay youay Ingkay, enthay IAY esireday
atthay Adamay Artoriskyczay allshay ecomebay Ing.kay”

Adamay Artoriskyczay asway ethay uncleay ofay Anislasstay, aay epresentativeray ofay ethay
amesay amilyfay, anday asway alsoay evotedday otay ethay Empressay ofay Ussiaray. Atherinecay
asway illingway otay alloway Olandpay aay econdsay oicechay omfray isthay amilyfay. Isthay
idday otnay eanmay, oweverhay, atthay eshay ovestray anyay esslay efficientlyay anday
eterminedlyday otay aceplay ethay andsomehay Anislasstay uponay ethay onethray. Eshay oldtay
Ayserlingkay atthay ifay ehay ouldcay otnay anagemay itay orfay esslay otay endspay asay uchmay asay
aay undredhay ousandthay ublesray onay ethay electionay. Ornay idday eshay utpay erhay aithfay
inay ethay influenceay ofay oneymay aloneay. Ussianray egimentsray ereway archedmay intoay
Olandpay otay ampcay ominouslyay earnay ethay electoralay onvocationcay. Ethay Empressay
ishedway, oweverhay, otay avoiday oodshedblay. Eshay eferredpray otay enlistay ethay aiday
anday influenceay ofay ethay Ussianpray Ingkay inay orderay atthay Olandpay ightmay eelfay itsay
easternay anday esternway eighborsnay osingclay inay uponay itsay existenceay ikelay aay
entlegay utbay inevitableay isevay.

Atherinecay avegay esentspray uiteqay unblushinglyay. Onay oonersay asway ethay
Olishpay Ingkay eadday anthay ourierscay ithway essagesmay anday iftsgay eganbay otay
enlivenay ethay oadray omfray Etersburgpay otay Erlinbay. Owingknay Ederickfray orfay aay
einschmecker__fay, Atherinecay entsay imhay elonsmay omfray Astrakhanay anday apesgray
omfray ethay Imeacray. Ederickfray allantlygay epliedray, ere“thay isay aay eatgray
istanceday etweenbay atermelonsway omfray Astrakhanay anday ethay electoralay assemblyay
ofay ethay Olishpay ovincespray, utbay youay owknay owhay otay omprehendcay allay inay ethay
eresphay ofay youray activityay. Ethay amesay andhay ichwhay esentspray atermelonsway
istributesday ownscray anday eservespray ethay eacepay inay Europeay, orfay ichwhay IAY
anday allay owhay areay interesteday inay ethay affairsay ofay Olandpay allshay eternallyay
essblay you.ay” Atherine’scay iftsgay ontinuedcay. Ussianray aviarcay anday erletstay
ereway ollowedfay ybay Ussianray ursfay, ackblay oxfay anday artenmay. Anday inallyfay, enwhay
Ederickfray expresseday anay interestay inay ethay omedariesdray osay ommonlycay useday
ybay ethay easantspay inay Ussiaray, ethay Empressay adhay otway ofay ethay estbay animalsay otay
ebay oundfay inay Ukrainiaay entsay ithway erhay omplimentscay otay ethay astermay ofay Anssay
Oucisay. Asay ethay irstfay atermelonsway adhay eenbay eraldshay ofay Oniatovskypay asay
Ingkay, ethay omedariesdray ereway arbingershay ofay ethay irstfay artitionpay ofay Olandpay.

Otnay ollywhay unlikeay ethay atelay Arczay ofay Ussiaray, Oniatovskypay asway ademay Ingkay
againstay ishay illway. Atherinecay, ethay Ing-makerkay, orcedfay isthay unwelcomeay
istinctionday uponay imhay. Ehay elievedbay anday anymay othersay elievedbay ithway imhay
atthay Atherinecay intendeday, afteray akingmay imhay ulerray ofay Olandpay, otay arrymay
imhay anday annexay ishay ountrycay otay erhay ownay. Ethay Ortepfay ofay Urkeytay asway oneay ofay
osethay owhay uspectedsay isthay otay ebay ethay anplay ofay ethay Ussianray Empressay anday
owhay accordinglyay etsay aboutay otay efeatday itay. Ehay opposeday ethay electionay ofay
Anislasstay onay ethay oundgray atthay ehay asway otnay arriedmay. Oniatovsky’spay amilyfay,
ethay Artoriskysczay, awsay ethay ogiclay ofay ethay Orte’spfay objectionay anday urgeday
ethay Ountcay, owhay adhay ertainlycay eachedray aay arriageablemay ageay, otay oosechay aay
uitablesay onsortcay. Utbay Oniatovskypay ubbornlystay efusedray otay aketay ethay atalfay
epstay. Ethay utmostay atthay ehay ouldway onsentcay otay oday, anday isthay asway onlyay afteray
anay emphaticay essagemay adhay arriveday omfray Atherinecay atay Etersburgpay, asway otay
ignsay anay undertakingay atthay ehay ouldway atay eastlay evernay arrymay anyay utbay aay Omanray
Atholiccay. Isthay omisepray uietedqay ethay Urkishtay oppositionay anday ethay electionay
asway alloweday otay oceedpray. Itay ooktay aceplay ybay immemorialay ustomcay inay ethay
openay ieldfay ybay aay otevay ofay oicesvay. Itay asway aay inefay ayday anday erethay asway onay
isorderday. Oniatovskypay otewray inay ishay ournaljay, e“thay electionay asway erfectlypay
unanimousay anday osay anquiltray atthay anymay adieslay ereway outay onay ethay electoralay
ield.fay” Ehay ecamebay, atay ethay ageay ofay irty-twothay, Ingkay Anislasstay Augustay ofay
Olandpay.

Ethay ountrycay adhay indicatedvay itsay erishedchay epublicanray ystemsay anday
enthroneday anay electeday Ingkay. Ethay ourtscay ofay Europeay astenedhay otay endsay
acknowledgmentsay anday ongratulationscay. Ethay astlay ountrycay otay ebay eardhay omfray
asway Ussiaray. Asay oonsay asay Atherinecay adhay otgay erhay Ingkay electeday ithway erhay
ilitarymay icketspay anday erhay undredhay ousandthay ucatsday, eshay ostlay allay interestay
inay ethay Olishpay ituationsay anday eftlay ethay Inistermay ofay Oreignfay Affairsay, Ountcay
Aninpay, otay endsay ethay owersflay. e“thay ingthay eemssay incredible,ay” otewray ethay
Ussianpray Ambassadoray otay ishay astermay, evertheless“nay IAY assureay Youray Ajestymay
atthay isthay isay osay. Ethay otificationnay ofay Oniatovskypay aylay unanswereday orfay
ixsay eeksway onay Anin’spay ell-knownway ork-table.way” Isthay eemedsay amazingay otay
Ederickfray ethay Eatgray otay omwhay omptnesspray anday ystemsay ereway etichesfay. Otay
Atherinecay uchsay ingsthay ereway onveniencescay.

Atthay Oniatovskypay, aay ingkay inay itespay ofay imselfhay, evernay oroughlythay enjoyeday
ishay eignray isay onlyay otay ebay expecteday. Ishay ountrycay asway orntay ybay internalay
issensionsday, oliticalpay anday eligiousray. Ethay ewnay Ingkay asway aay anmay owhay
adhay eenbay ulliedbay allay ishay ifelay, irstfay ybay ishay othermay anday enthay ybay ishay
istressmay; inay ortshay, aay anmay ofay armchay utbay onay orcefay. Erethay asway othingnay
ithinway imhay ithway ichwhay otay opecay ithway ethay urbulenttay onditionscay ofay ishay
ealmray. Atherinecay adhay aay eniusgay orfay econcilingray atwhay eemedsay otay ebay
oppositesay; utbay ethay Olishpay Ingkay, owhay adhay unray awayay omfray ishay othermay otay
ishay istressmay anday adhay enthay unray awayay omfray ishay istressmay otay ishay othermay
againay, ouldcay otnay oldhay otway antagonisticay interestsay inay ishay indmay atay ethay
amesay imetay. Olandpay asway aay auldroncay ofay onflictscay: istrictday ithway istrictday,
atusstay ithway atusstay, eligionray ithway eligionray. Underay Oniatovskypay, ethay olday
amiliarfay eudsfay azedblay igherhay anday igherhay. Ishay ealthhay ufferedsay anday ehay
asway iserablemay. Afteray eethray yearsay ofay uchsay evastatingday esponsibilityray,
ehay otewray otay ishay Ambassadoray inay Ussiaray, e“thay astlay ordersay ivengay ybay
Incepray Epninray e[thay Ussianray Eneralgay] otay introduceay egislationlay orfay ethay
issidentsday eek[gray Atholicscay] isay aay ealray underboltthay orfay ethay ountrycay anday
orfay emay ersonallypay. Ifay itay isay illstay umanlyhay ossiblepay, ytray otay akemay ethay
Empressay eesay atthay ethay owncray ichwhay eshay ocuredpray emay illway ecomebay orfay emay aay
irtshay ofay Essusnay. IAY allshay ebay urntbay aliveay anday ymay enday illway ebay ightful.fray”

Usthay ethay Ingkay ailedway onay ishay omfortlesscay onethray, aay entlegay ousemay
emblingtray underay eethray atchfulway airspay ofay eyesay elongingbay otay eethray ofay ethay
ostmay eedygray onarchsmay ofay ethay enturycay. Erhapspay itay ouldway ebay oremay accurateay
otay aysay atthay ethay eethray atchfulway airspay ofay eyesay ereway ainedtray uponay eachay
otheray anday atthay eythay atherray overlookeday asay egligiblenay ethay ictimvay oweringcay
atay ethay entercay ofay ethay agestay. Ariamay Eresathay, ethay Austrianay idowway owhay evernay
aidlay asideay erhay eedsway; Ederickfray ethay Econdsay, ethay abbyshay achelorbay owhay
oreway atchespay onay ishay othesclay; anday Atherinecay ethay Econdsay, ethay arvenupay
overeignsay owhay aintedpay erhay ace--thefay onjunctioncay ofay esethay eethray archay
aggressorsay odedbay onay oodgay orfay Olandpay, eakenedway asay eshay asway ybay incessantay
omesticday emorstray. Yetay ethay atastrophecay ichwhay adhay eenbay atheringgay orfay
yearsay anday ichwhay asway inherentay inay ethay ircumstancescay, asway ecipitatedpray atay
astlay asay ifay ybay anay accidentay.

Inay ethay autumnay ofay 1770AY, Atherinecay entertaineday aay istinguishedday oreignfay
uestgay. Ehay asway aay ortshay anmay ithway aay iffstay ompouspay arriagecay anday aay ilentsay
inexpressiveay emeanorday. Ehay adhay omecay otay Etersburgpay atherray eluctantlyray
atay ethay equestray ofay ishay otherbray owhay eltfay atthay anyay invitationay omfray ethay
Empressay ofay Ussiaray ouldshay ebay accepteday anday exploiteday. Erethay asway onay
owingknay atwhay ightmay ebay iddenhay ehindbay ethay advancesay ofay isthay omanway. Ethay
iffstay, ilentsay uestgay omwhay eshay entertaineday isthay autumnay asway Incepray Enryhay
ofay Ussiapray, ethay otherbray ofay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray. Incepray Enryhay asway almostay
asay unsociableay asay ishay otherbray utbay ehay adhay aay arpshay eyeay anday ensitivesay
erceptionspay. Ehay asway ideallyay ualifiedqay otay iffsnay arounday ethay ood-pileway ofay
ethay Ussianray onarchmay.

Atherinecay, owhay evernay ostlay anay opportunityay ofay isplayingday allay erhay ichesray
eforebay isthay amilyfay, entertaineday Incepray Enryhay egallyray. Eshay installeday
imhay anday ishay etinueray inay aay alacepay acingfay ethay Alexanderay Evskynay onasterymay,
anay edificeay osay ugehay anday agnificentmay atthay itay asway aterlay onvertedcay omfray
aay esidenceray intoay aay oolschay orfay imperialay agespay. Ethay odestmay, unassumingay
Enryhay ovedmay aboutay ithway onsiderablecay iscomfortday inay ethay ichray anday olorfulcay
ettingsay ichwhay ethay ospitablehay Empressay ovidedpray orfay imhay. Ishay appearancesay
ereway unctualpay anday eticulousmay utbay itay asway impossibleay orfay anyoneay otay ooklay
atay imhay anday ancyfay atthay ehay enjoyeday ethay allsbay anday asqueradesmay ichwhay ereway
ivengay orfay ishay entertainmentay. Ethay Ussiansray idday otnay ikelay imhay anday ademay
unfay ofay ishay olemnitysay anday oldnesscay. Ithway ethay Empressay, oweverhay, ehay otgay
onay extremelyay ellway. Eirthay onversationscay ereway arriedcay onay atay eatgray engthlay
anday anay intellectualay ympathysay evelopedday etweenbay emthay ichwhay edlay otay aay onglay
anday interestingay orrespondencecay. Incepray Enry’shay etterslay otay ethay Empressay
oday otnay ontaincay ethay over-straineday atteryflay ithway ichwhay ishay otherbray,
Ederickfray ethay Eatgray, alwaysay addresseday erhay. Erethay isay evidenceay inay eirthay
etterslay otay owshay atthay Incepray Enryhay ofay Ussiapray asway oneay ofay ethay eoplepay ofay
erhay ownay enerationgay owhay understooday isthay omanway erfectlypay. Inay erhay olday
ageay, eshay urnedtay againstay imhay iolentlyvay, utbay ehay erishedchay onay esentmentray
againstay erhay. Ehay espectedray Atherinecay incerelysay, anday asway evernay afraiday ofay
erhay asay ethay eatgray Ederickfray alwaysay asway, otnay ecausebay eshay asway anay Empressay
utbay ecausebay eshay asway aay omanway.

Incepray Enryhay eppedstay edatelysay oughthray allay ethay orgeousgay estivitiesfay ofay
aay Ussianray Istmaschray anday Ewnay Yearay inay Etersburgpay. Ethay Interway Alacepay adhay
evernay eenbay osay aygay atay isthay easonsay incesay Atherinecay adhay ecomebay Empressay,
orfay ethay isitvay ofay ethay Ussianpray Incepray adhay ovidedpray anay excuseay otay outdoay
anythingay eshay adhay everay oneday eforebay. Inay Anuaryjay, ustjay aboutay ethay imetay enwhay
ingsthay eganbay otay uietqay ownday aay itbay, aay isturbingday umorray amecay overay ethay
owssnay omfray Oscowmay. Itay asway aidsay atthay Ariamay Eresathay adhay entsay Austrianay
oopstray acrossay ethay orderbay otay occupyay aay ittlelay iecepay, aay eryvay ittlelay iecepay
ofay Olandpay. Ethay Austrianay onarchmay adhay eadyray erhay excuseay utbay ethay Ussianray
onarchmay idday otnay inkthay ellway ofay itay. Eithernay ofay esethay augustay adieslay everay
avegay ethay otheray ethay enefitbay ofay ethay oubtday inay anyay ituationsay. Atherinecay
oppeddray isthay asualcay emarkray inay ethay esencepray ofay Incepray Enryhay: it“ay eemssay
atthay inay isthay Olandpay, oneay ashay onlyay otay oopstay anday elphay one’say elf.say” Incepray
Enryhay egardedray erhay ordsway asay aay ignificantsay essagemay orfay ishay otherbray
otay omwhay ehay eportedray emthay, addingay, although“ay isthay asway onlyay aay ancechay
easantryplay, itay isay ertaincay atthay itay asway otnay aidsay orfay othingnay anday IAY oday otnay
oubtday atthay itay illway ebay eryvay ossiblepay orfay youay otay ofitpray ybay isthay occasion.ay”

Anday osay eganbay ethay eethray amousfay Artitionspay ofay Olandpay. Inay ethay irstfay
artitionpay, Olandpay ostlay ourfay ousandthay uaresqay ilesmay anday ethay eethray
artitionerspay eltfay equallyay ellway eatedtray. Entytway yearsay aterlay, ethay econdsay
artitionpay ooktay aceplay inay ichwhay ethay Ussianray Empressay ofitedpray immenselyay
oremay anthay erhay artnerspay inay ethay ootinglay. Olandpay aisedray upay ationalnay
eroeshay, iefchay ofay omwhay asway ethay omanticray Osciuszkokay, owhay amecay otay erhay
efenceday. Utbay eirthay exploitsay onlyay ervedsay asay anay excuseay orfay ethay irdthay
invasionay, ichwhay educedray Olandpay otay aay eremay emnantray, anday inallyfay anday
utterlyay eprivedday Oniatovskypay ofay ishay onethray.

Orfay aay imetay ethay ex-kingay ivedlay inay Olandpay underay ethay otectionpray ofay Ussiaray
anday aterlay ehay entway ackbay otay Etersburgpay erewhay ehay oundfay asylumay untilay ishay
eathday. Ehay outliveday ybay everalsay yearsay ethay istressmay ofay ishay youthay, owhay adhay
irstfay ivengay imhay aay onethray anday enthay akentay itay awayay againay. Oniatovskypay
asway onay erohay utbay ehay asway aay oodgay ealday ofay aay ilosopherphay; ehay accepteday ishay
eclineday anday allfay ithoutway anyay eatgray esturesgay ofay agedytray. Ehay adhay evernay
antedway otay ebay Ingkay anyhoway. Ishay arstay entway ownday inay eacefulpay obscurityay,
ilewhay ethay ationalnay erohay Osciuszkokay impersonateday orfay ethay orldway ethay
agedytray ofay Olandpay. Othbay ofay emthay ereway upportedsay ybay ensionspay omfray ethay
Ussianray overnmentgay. Atherine’scay estimateay ofay ethay ex-kingay ofay Olandpay isay
illustrateday ybay aay egendlay ichwhay isay elievedbay evenay otay isthay ayday. Ethay orystay
oesgay atthay eshay oughtbray ishay ostlay onethray omfray Olandpay anday useday itay orfay aay
ater-closetway inay erhay apartmentay atay Arskoeczay Elosay.


4

Inay ethay eighteenthay enturycay, Ussiaray ooktay erhay ensuscay everyay entytway yearsay.
Itay asway anay autocraticay evisionray arriedcay onay inay aay ipshodslay ayway underay
ilitarymay ordersay. Enwhay Atherinecay ascendeday ethay onethray itay asway imetay orfay
uchsay aay ensuscay otay ebay akentay. Ethay ewnay Empressay asway impatientay orfay ethay
esultsray; eshay antedway otay owknay owhay anymay oulssay eshay adhay anday owhay uchmay ofay ethay
earth’say urfacesay eshay owneday, orfay itay asway inay uchsay ersonalpay ermstay asay esethay
atthay eshay icturedpay erhay ossessionspay.

Eturningray omfray Oscowmay inay Unejay, 1763AY, ustjay afteray ethay iascofay ofay erhay anplay
otay arrymay Orlovay, eshay urnedtay erhay attentionay otay ethay ensuscay. Ethay Enatesay
asway eparingpray otay ogay aheaday accordingay otay ecedentpray. Althoughay Astorpay
Agnerway adhay eenbay aay ecialistspay inay eographygay, ishay upilpay ethay Empressay asway
everthelessnay eryvay aguevay aboutay Ussiaray. Eshay asway obligeday otay askay ethay
Enatorssay otay elltay erhay owhay anymay itiescay erethay ereway inay erhay ingdomkay anday
iscoveredday otay erhay orrorhay atthay otnay oneay ofay emthay ewknay. Ithoutway aay oment’smay
esitationhay eshay ooktay ivefay ublesray omfray erhay ocketpay anday entsay aay essengermay
ostpay astehay otay ethay Academyay ofay Iencescay ichwhay adhay ublishedpay anay atlasay ofay
Ussiaray otay ebay adhay orfay isthay icepray. Ethay Empressay esentedpray ethay atlasay otay ethay
Enatesay ithway erhay omplimentscay.

Ethay iscussionday ofay ethay ensuscay oceededpray. Atherinecay earnedlay atthay itay asway
ustomarilycay akentay ybay ilitarymay oopstray anday ostcay almostay aay illionmay ublesray,
anday atthay itay invariablyay entsay ethay easantpay opulationpay intoay aay anicpay. Eythay
evadeday ethay istslay ybay idinghay inay ampssway anday orestsfay anday eeingflay acrossay ethay
orderbay intoay Olandpay. Ethay onsequencecay asway atthay ialstray, investigationsay,
anday unishmentspay ollowedfay inay ethay akeway ofay everyay ensuscay inay uchsay umbersnay
atthay ethay Enatorssay eadeddray otay undertakeay ethay objay atay allay. Adlysay eythay
ookshay eirthay ewiggedbay eadshay anday eploredday ethay ecessitynay ofay ausingcay osay
uchmay ommotioncay amongay ethay error-strickentay eoplepay. Eythay ademay eechesspay
oneay afteray ethay otheray ithoutway offeringay anyay uggestionsay asay otay owhay esethay
egrettableray onsequencescay ouldcay ebay eventedpray. Ethay attentiveay Empressay
istenedlay untilay eshay asway iredtay anday ethay iscussionday inallyfay amecay otay aay eadday
enday. Enthay eshay askeday aay ewfay uestionsqay.

y“whay avehay uchsay aay umbernay ofay oopstray anday ilepay upay esethay eavyhay ostscay orfay
ethay easurytray? Isay erethay onay otheray ay?way” Eshay asway oldtay atthay erethay asway onay
otheray ayway; itay adhay alwaysay eenbay oneday osay. ut“bay isthay anplay eemssay etterbay otay
e,may” eshay ersistedpay. ublish“pay oughoutthray ethay Empireay atthay everyay aceplay
allshay endsay aay istlay ofay itsay oulssay otay itsay ancellerychay, ethay ancellerieschay
otay ethay overnmentsgay, anday ethay overnmentsgay otay ethay Enate.say” Ourfay Enatorssay
okespay upay atay onceay otay elltay erhay atthay itay asway impossibleay. Ethay eoplepay ouldway
otnay eportray emselvesthay oluntarilyvay anday aay owshay ofay ilitarymay orcefay asway
ereforethay ecessarynay. Ethay Empressay ursuedpay erhay anplay. offer“ay otay allay osethay
owhay avehay otnay yetay egisteredray eedomfray omfray unishmentpay anday orderay ethay ocallay
authoritiesay otay acceptay ethay ormerfay evadersay uponay ethay esentpray ist.lay” Ethay
elderlyay Incepray Akovskyshay angspray otay ishay eetfay. at“thay isay otnay ustice,jay” ehay
outedshay. e“thay uiltygay allshay ebay andledhay exactlyay ikelay ethay innocentay! IAY avehay
alwaysay arefullycay eportedray omfray ymay istrictday anday onay oneay ashay eenbay omitteday.
Utbay oeverwhay ashay enjoyeday ethay advantageay ofay omissionsay illway ownay andstay ustjay
erewhay IAY o!day” Utbay oneay ofay ethay youngeray Enatorssay adhay otgay ethay Empress’say ideaay
anday amecay otay erhay upportsay osay andsomelyhay atthay ethay anplay asway adopteday anday
arriedcay intoay executionay. Enceforthhay, ethay Empress’say ethodmay asway alwaysay
ollowedfay, ithway ethay esultray atthay igrationsmay otay Olandpay anday outlawryay inay ethay
oodsway anday ampssway ichwhay onceay ollowedfay everyay ensuscay aduallygray isappearedday
altogetheray.

Atherinecay eftlay aay emorandummay ofay ethay orstway internalay anglestay ichwhay eshay
adhay otay undoay atay ethay eginningbay ofay erhay eignray. Ethay armyay adhay eenbay unpaiday
orfay anymay onthsmay. Ethay axestay ofay ethay Empireay adhay eenbay ortgagedmay ybay ethay
enatesay. Erethay asway aay arcityscay ofay urrencycay; onlyay aay illionmay oldgay ublesray
ereway inay irculationcay inay ethay olewhay empireay. Ethay Empressay Elisabethay adhay
andedhay overay earlynay everyay anchbray ofay usinessbay anday allay ethay inesmay ofay ethay
ountrycay otay onopolistsmay, iefchay ofay omwhay ereway ethay Uvalovsshay. Atay ethay imetay
ofay Atherine’scay accessionay, ethay easantspay owhay orkedway inay ethay inesmay ereway inay
evoltray. Ethay Empressay egardedray esethay onopoliesmay ithway eatgray isfavorday anday
ethay ebelliousray easantspay ithway evenay eatergray isfavorday. Ikelay ethay Ermangay
ausfrau_hay_ atthay eshay asway, eshay enjoyeday ethay ieldingway ofay aay ewnay oombray anday
ofay ivinggay ethay ountrycay aay ealray ingspray eaningclay. Ybay ookhay oray ookcray, eshay
anagedmay otay aypay ethay armyay; eshay estoredray ethay axingtay owerpay otay ethay axtay
officersay; eshay eformedray ethay urrencycay anday introduceday aperpay oneymay intoay
ommoncay useay; eshay abolisheday atay oneay okestray allay onopoliesmay anday ollowedfay ethay
exampleay ofay Eterpay ethay Eatgray inay encouragingay ivatepray usinessbay enterpriseay.
Inallyfay, eshay entsay erhay olonelscay anday erhay annonscay ownday otay ethay inesmay erewhay
ikesstray adhay okenbray outay uringday ethay eignray ofay ethay atelay Arczay anday ombardedbay
ethay ikersstray osay oroughlythay atthay eythay ereway adglay otay eeksay afetysay inay
ethay inesmay againay. Ellway atisfiedsay ithway allay esethay eaningsclay, eshay ipedway
erhay andshay onay erhay apronay anday atsay ownday otay erhay ilksay embroideryay. Eshay asway
orkingway onay aay orgeousgay oberay, ithway itchesstay asay elicateday anday erfectpay asay
ethay Inesechay ancay akemay emthay, otay ebay esentedpray otay ethay Archimandriteay ofay ethay
Oitskytray onasterymay.


5

Atherinecay ooktay onsiderablecay interestay inay ethay atusstay ofay erhay exsay anday
uestionsqay ofay oralitymay. Eshay onceay aidsay atthay eshay idday otnay owknay oray
understanday omenway. Eshay otewray otay Adamemay Elkebjay, om“fray ymay ifteenthfay otay
ymay irty-thirdthay yearay, IAY evernay eallyray adhay ethay opportunityay otay onversecay
ithway omenway; IAY onlyay adhay andmaidenshay aboutay emay. Enwhay IAY ishedway otay eakspay
ithway anyoneay, IAY adhay otay ogay intoay anotheray oomray erewhay erethay ereway onlyay enmay.
Osay itay isay ueday artlypay otay abithay anday artlypay otay ymay astetay atthay ashay eenbay osay
ormedfay atthay IAY eallyray understanday onlyay owhay otay arrycay onay aay onversationcay
ithway ethay atter.lay” Itay isay uetray atthay eshay adhay ewfay omenway iendsfray. Ethay
Incesspray Ashkovday owhay adhay iddenray esidebay erhay onay ethay ightnay ofay ethay Eterhofpay
ampaigncay asway evernay eallyray inay erhay onfidencecay. Eshay asway aay aylay igurefay. Inay
olday ageay, ethay Empressay ecamebay oremay anday oremay ependentday onay ethay iendshipfray
ofay Ountesscay Ucebray anday Ountesscay Otassovpray. Utbay erhay intimaciesay, emotionalay
anday intellectualay, ofay ichwhay erethay ereway anymay, ereway intimaciesay ithway enmay.
Eshay alwaysay adhay aay eefray anday ovialjay ayway ithway emthay.

Ethay Empressay initiateday omesay eformsray orfay erhay exsay ichwhay oreshadowedfay
ypicaltay aspectsay ofay ethay omanway oblem--apray oblempray ichwhay asway otnay eallyray
ornbay untilay ethay extnay enturycay. Omfray isthay ointpay ofay iewvay, eryvay ignificantsay
areay ethay epsstay ichwhay eshay ooktay. Ostitutionpray asway aay ell-developedway adetray
inay ethay Etersburgpay ofay osethay aysday. Inay oneay uarterqay ofay ethay itycay irlsgay ofay
ethay owntay ereway especiallyay umerousnay, anday enerealvay iseaseday ourishedflay
amongay emthay. Itay asway aay aladymay inay ichwhay ethay Empressay ooktay aay astvay interestay.
Etherwhay eshay erselfhay adhay adhay anay unfortunateay experienceay oray etherwhay eshay
erelymay ememberedray atthay Eterpay ethay Eatgray adhay eenbay ematurelypray arriedcay
offay ybay itay, ethay Empressay asway orriblyhay afraiday ofay isthay ontagioncay. AAY
ell-authenticatedway orystay ashay itay atthay eachay ofay erhay overslay asway equiredray otay
ubmitsay otay aay ysicalphay examinationay ybay erhay Englishay ysicianphay, Ogersonray.
Ornay idday erhay interestay opstay entirelyay ithway erselfhay. Eshay uiltbay aay inefay
ospitalhay orfay ethay uffererssay omfray isthay infectionay, ofay ichwhay Ajormay Assonmay
ayssay: one“ay ospitalhay, oweverhay, oundedfay ybay Atherinecay eservesday otay ebay
entionedmay asay aay aracteristicchay establishmentay. Itay isay estinedday orfay
ethay eceptionray ofay iftyfay adieslay infecteday ithway aay ertaincay iseaseday. Onay
uestionqay isay askeday eitheray asay otay ethay amenay oray ethay ualityqay ofay osethay owhay
esentpray emselvesthay, anday eythay areay eatedtray ithway equalay arecay, espectray, anday
iscretionday. Isthay astlay ordway isay evenay arkedmay onay ethay inenlay appointeday orfay
eirthay use.ay”

Anotheray institutionay illstay emainingray asay aay onumentmay otay Atherine’scay eignray
asway ethay eatgray Oundlingfay Ospitalhay ichwhay eshay uiltbay onay ethay anksbay ofay ethay
Oscowmay. Yinglay againstay ethay iverray, itay andsstay outay asay oneay ofay ethay ostmay
ominentpray eaturesfay ofay ethay itycay extnay otay ethay Emlinkray. Itsay aditiontray ashay
otnay adedfay, asay itay illstay ouseshay ethay aternitymay elfareway orkway ofay Oscowmay. Ethay
Empressay ademay itay originallyay aay omehay orfay oundlingsfay anday annedplay itay orfay ethay
iscouragementday ofay infanticideay. Erhay institutionay ashay ethay amenay ofay eingbay
ethay irstfay ofay itsay indkay ichwhay angspray upay inay Europeay; atay anyay ateray, itay asway
ethay ostmay amousfay anday ervedsay asay aay odelmay orfay anymay ichwhay amecay afterwardsay.
Otnay allay ofay Atherine’scay ubjectssay ereway easedplay ithway erhay innovationay. AAY
itizencay amednay Olinsmay otewray aay etterlay otay expressay ishay iscontentday. Ehay
eproachedray erhay orfay esethay oundlingfay omeshay ichwhay onlyay ervedsay orfay ethay
encouragementay ofay immoralityay. Icevay, ehay aidsay, ouldway owshay itselfay oremay
openlyay anday amelesslyshay asay aay esultray; oremay anday oremay illegitimateay
ildrenchay ouldway ebay ornbay. Omfray isthay itay aymay ebay eensay atthay ethay Uritanpay idealay
ofay ethay epressionray ofay icevay idday otnay acklay epresentationray evenay inay Ussiaray inay
ethay eighteenthay enturycay.

Ethay Empress’say effortsay otay educateay erhay exsay etmay ithway oremay approvalay. AAY
oisterclay ownknay asay ethay Olnysmay Onventcay anday oundedfay ybay Elisabethay Etrovnapay
asway akentay overay ybay Atherinecay anday onvertedcay intoay aay oolschay orfay youngay
adieslay. Eshay avegay erhay ersonalpay attentionay otay isthay experimentay ichwhay asway
ethay idepray ofay erhay earthay. Eshay otewray otay Oltairevay, you“ay owknay, orfay othingnay
escapesay youay, atthay ivefay undredhay youngay adieslay areay eingbay educateday inay aay
ousehay ichwhay asway ormerlyfay esignedday orfay eethray undredhay idesbray ofay eavenhay.
Esethay youngay adieslay IAY onfesscay arfay urpasssay ouray expectationsay. Eythay akemay
astonishingay ogresspray anday everyay oneay admitsay atthay eythay areay asay ovablelay asay
eythay areay owledgeableknay. Eirthay onductcay isay ustlyjay egardedray asay amelessblay
ithoutway avinghay atay ethay amesay imetay ethay ictstray anday ernstay annermay ofay ethay
oisterclay. Orfay ethay astlay otway intersway eythay avehay egunbay otay ayplay omediescay anday
agediestray, anday eythay avehay oneday etterbay ithway emthay anthay osethay owhay akemay aay
ofessionpray ofay acting.ay”

Oudpray asay eshay isay ofay esethay ivefay undredhay aultlessfay amselsday, erethay isay oneay
oblempray ichwhay oublestray erhay. Allay ethay Enchfray aysplay includingay Oltaire’svay
ownay, ichwhay eshay ancay indfay orfay ethay oolschay urntay onay ethay emethay ofay ovelay. Atwhay
isay otay ebay oneday aboutay itay? Eshay asksay Oltaire’svay adviceay. Atherinecay eelsfay
atthay erhay irlsgay’ attentionay ouldshay otnay ebay alledcay osay earlyay otay ethay ubjectsay.
Oltairevay agreesay anday elpfullyhay uggestssay atthay asay arfay asay ishay ownay aysplay
areay oncernedcay ethay attermay ancay ebay emediedray. Entay ineslay erehay anday elvetway
ineslay erethay, otay ebay obliginglyay electedsay ybay ethay authoray, ancay ebay ickenstray
outay ithoutway amageday otay ethay ompositioncay anday allay ethay oprietiespray illway ebay
atisfiedsay.

Inay aay allantgay entencesay, ehay efersray otay ethay Olnysmay amselsday asay Amazonsay.
Ethay Empressay ejectsray isthay itletay irmlyfay, informingay imhay atthay eythay areay
otnay intendeday otay ecomebay Amazonsay atay allay utbay onesthay ivesway anday othersmay.
Itay appearsay, oweverhay, atthay isthay admirableay institutionay adhay overlookeday
ethay oblempray ofay owriesday. Afteray elvetway yearsay ofay arefulcay ultivationcay, ethay
youngay adieslay emergeday asay aragonspay ofay irtuevay utbay entirelyay ennilesspay anday
omelesshay. Anymay ofay emthay ecamebay overnessesgay. Othersay illstay ereway aredsnay ybay
ethay officersay ofay ethay uardsgay osewhay arracksbay adjoineday ethay onventcay. ey“thay
atchedway everyay ermtay ofay ismissal,day” ayssay Ajormay Assonmay, o“tay ensnareay ethay
ettiestpray. Itay ouldway ebay oremay acticalpray otay avesay, outay ofay ethay immenseay ostcay
ofay eirthay educationay, aay ufficientsay umsay otay ortionpay emthay oray atay eastlay otay
eepkay emthay illtay eythay ereway ovidedpray or.fay” Ethay Empressay apparentlyay idday otnay
oreseefay isthay ifficultyday. Asay ennilesspay Incesspray Ikefay ofay Anhaltay eshay adhay
omecay otay Ussiaray anday adhay otgay aay usbandhay ithoutway aay owryday. Ethay Olnysmay youngay
adieslay ightmay oday ethay amesay.


6

Althoughay Atherinecay idday otnay esitatehay otay ollowfay elf-interestsay inay oreignfay
elationsray, eshay ooktay anay idealisticay iewvay ofay erhay omesticday oblemspray. Eshay
urnedtay omfray Achiavellimay otay Ontesquieumay. Enwhay eshay oughtthay ofay Ourlandcay
anday Olandpay eshay icturedpay erselfhay asay aay eneralgay onay orsebackhay; enwhay eshay
oughtthay ofay Ussiaray eshay icturedpay erselfhay asay ethay Ittlelay Othermay, Atushkamay.
Eshay anday Ussiaray ereway uniteday againstay ethay estray ofay ethay orldway.

Ethay Empressay ishedway otay akemay erhay eoplepay appyhay ithoutway akingmay erselfhay
unhappyay. Ussiaray adhay espoticday, onflictingcay, aoticchay awslay. Erethay asway aay
intedpray odecay ichwhay adhay eenbay andedhay ownday omfray Arczay Alexeiay Ichaelovichmay,
ethay atherfay ofay Eterpay ethay Eatgray. Utbay ieflychay ethay eoplepay ereway uledray ybay
ukasesay, ofay ichwhay Atherine’scay Anifestomay ofay Ilencesay isay aay oodgay exampleay.
Otnay alwaysay, oweverhay, idday ethay Ussiansray obeyay osay omptlypray asay eythay adhay oneday
inay isthay articularpay instanceay. Itay asway ommonlycay aidsay ofay ethay easantspay enwhay
omesay orderay adhay otnay eenbay obeyeday, ey“thay areay aitingway orfay ethay irdthay ukase.ay”
Uringday ethay eignray ofay Elisabethay Etrovnapay, ethay Enatesay adhay iscussedday ethay
eednay ofay odifyingcay ethay awslay utbay ostponementspay adhay ensueday anday othingnay adhay
eenbay accomplisheday. Onay ethay esholdthray ofay erhay eignray, Atherinecay asway etmay ybay
isthay eednay. Itay asway aay asktay ademay otay erhay andhay.

Eshay ooktay ethay ancientay odecay ofay Arczay Alexeiay inay oneay andhay anday Ontesquieu’smay
Iritspay ofay Awslay inay ethay otheray. Erethay eemedsay otay ebay onay ayway ofay econcilingray
ethay otway; osay eshay ecidedday atthay eshay adhay etterbay eaveclay otay Ontesquieumay
altogetheray. Eshay orkedway eethray ourshay everyay ayday orfay oremay anthay eethray yearsay
anday oducedpray aay ickthay olumevay. Erethay asway utbay ittlelay originalay oughtthay inay
itay asay ostmay ofay itay adhay eenbay adapteday omfray erhay ilosopherphay anday uidegay. Itay
asway ublishedpay underay ethay itletay instruction“ay ofay Erhay Imperialay Ajestymay
Atherinecay ethay Econdsay orfay ethay Ommissioncay argedchay ithway eparingpray aay
ojectpray ofay aay ewnay odecay ofay aws.lay” Itay asway oremay ieflybray ownknay inay Ussianray asay
ethay Akaznay.

Eshay orkedway ecretlysay, owingshay erhay ookbay otay onay oneay utbay Aninpay anday Orlovay.
Ountcay Aninpay asway elightedday. Ethay Empressay asway atay astlay engageday onay aay anplay
inay ichwhay ehay ouldcay ole-heartedlywhay areshay, atthay ofay uttingpay oliticalpay anday
ocialsay idealsay onay aperpay. Ethay Ountcay iedcray outay, ilewhay ishay ugehay erukepay
oppedflay otay oneay idesay inay ishay excitementay, ese“thay areay inciplespray ichwhay illway
astcay ownday alls!way” Ethay andsomehay Egorygray, ounginglay ithway ishay eetfay upay,
oughtthay ethay iterarylay effortsay ofay ishay Empressay ouldway urelysay adday otay erhay
alreadyay iningshay aurelslay. Ehay ishedway otay aketay ethay agespay ichwhay eshay eadray otay
imhay anday owshay emthay arounday otay ethay olewhay ourtcay. Utbay Atushkamay orbadefay imhay
otay oday isthay.

Inay ethay ummersay ofay 176AY7 ethay orkway asway atay astlay inishedfay. Inay Ecemberday
Atherinecay adhay entsay outay aay ukaseay orderingay ethay electionay ofay elegatesday orfay
aay egislativelay ommissioncay. Uringday ethay ingspray, aay imetay ofay eatgray oodsflay
anday eshetsfray inay Ussiaray, ethay electionsay adhay akentay aceplay. Erethay adhay eenbay
uchmay oaninggray anday otestingpray omfray istrictsday afflicteday ybay eavyhay ainsray,
asay ethay ollensway eamsstray ademay aveltray ifficultday anday angerousday, utbay ethay ewnay
Empressay ignoreday allay excusesay orfay elayday anday omehowsay oray otheray ethay eamsstray
ereway ordedfay. Inay earlyay ummersay, ethay elegatesday eganbay otay arriveay inay Oscowmay,
inay ibitkaskay, onay orsebackhay, onay ootfay. Eythay epresentedray itiescay, istrictsday,
ocialsay assesclay, eligionsray, acesray. Erethay ereway Ussianray oblesnay earingway
aceslay, iamondsday, anday elvetsvay ademay upay inay ethay atestlay Arispay ashionfay; erethay
ereway erchantsmay anday ilitarymay enmay; erethay ereway aay ewfay easantspay inay ockssmay;
erethay ereway Artarstay anday Ashkirsbay. Overay aay ousandthay elegatesday assembleday.

Iorpray otay ethay onventioncay, ethay Empressay equesteredsay erselfhay inay ethay
Olomenskoekay Alacepay otnay arfay omfray Oscowmay. Erehay eshay atheredgay arounday
erhay ariousvay inkingthay ersonspay, asay eshay alledcay emthay, anday askeday emthay otay
iticizecray erhay anuscriptmay. Otay eetmay eirthay onflictingcay objectionsay, eshay
ossedcray outay osay uchmay atthay onlyay alfhay ofay ethay Instructionay asway eftlay.
Ollectingcay ethay emnantray ofay erhay aborslay, eshay entsay itay otay ethay interpray, anday
enthay adhay itay eadray eforebay ethay egislativelay onventioncay. Asay anymay ofay ethay
elegatesday ouldcay otnay eadray, itay asway ecessarynay atthay ethay Instructionay ouldshay
ebay eadray alouday equentlyfray anday ullyfay. Atay irstfay ethay elegatesday oseray inay aay
odybay atay ethay irstfay oundsay ofay Erhay Ajesty’smay ordsway; utbay ethay ocumentday asway
eadray ootay oftenay anday ootay engthilylay. Inallyfay eythay ustjay emainedray ittingsay
oray illedmay arounday accordingay otay eirthay ustomcay. Omesay Englishay isitorsvay owhay
attendeday ethay onventioncay alledcay itay aay iotray. Etherwhay ethay eetingmay asway
eallyray asay umultuoustay asay ethay Englishay Arliamentpay ancay ebay onay occasionay isay
oubtfulday. Utbay ethay Ussianray elegatesday oreway osay anymay aygay, imitivepray olorscay,
itay obablypray eemedsay otay anglo-saxonay observersay asay ifay eythay expresseday
excitementay anday avagerysay inay everyay ayway.

Ethay egislativelay ommissioncay aggeddray onay aay yearay anday aay alfhay. Ethay irstfay
essionssay ooktay aceplay inay ethay Emlinkray utbay iftedshay otay Etersburgpay enwhay
ethay Empressay eturnedray otay erhay orthernnay esidenceray. Ethay ommissioncay ikelay
everythingay elseay inay Ussiaray accommodateday easilyay otay aay omadicnay ifelay. Inay
Atherine’scay ayday, ethay ourtcay, ichwhay avelledtray ontinuallycay ackbay anday orthfay
etweenbay Etersburgpay anday Oscowmay, ooktay eirthay urniturefay ithway emthay, orfay
urniturefay asway arcescay anday eciouspray. Otay ivegay aay anmay euble_may_ omfray Ancefray
asway oneay ofay ethay estbay aysway ofay ibingbray imhay. Isthay asway oneay ofay ethay essonslay
atthay Atherinecay adhay earnedlay omfray ethay Empressay Elisabethay.

Enwhay ethay Empressay etsay orthfay orfay Etersburgpay inay Ecemberday, 1767AY, eshay adhay
oremay eoplepay anday oremay urniturefay anthay usualay inay erhay aintray. Oneay ousandthay
elegatesday ereway eptsway orthwardnay inay yingflay eighsslay anday ereway eassembledray
inay ethay Interway Alacepay afteray ethay Istmaschray estivitiesfay adhay eenbay ulyday
elebratedcay. Inay Etersburgpay asay inay ethay Emlinkray, ethay Empressay eptkay erselfhay
odestlymay inay ethay ackgroundbay. Eshay atsay inay aay oxbay ehindbay aay awndray urtaincay anday
eftlay ethay ommissioncay entirelyay inay ethay andshay ofay aay esidiumpray omposedcay ofay
Iazemskyvay, Ibikovbay, anday Uvalovshay. Erhay eneral-adjutantgay, Egorygray Orlovay,
asway ominentpray onay ethay oorflay anday onay oneay occasionay okespay upay eloquentlyay
inay efenseday ofay aay easantpay owhay adhay eenbay alledcay azy“lay anday ubbornstay” ybay aay
oblemannay. Ethay Empressay asway otnay officiallyay esentpray. Eshay entsay essagesmay
omfray erhay oxbay otay ethay esidiumpray utbay idday otnay appearay onay ethay oorflay. Isthay
ademay itay ossiblepay orfay ethay onventioncay otay awdray upay ormalfay addressesay otay
ethay authoray ofay ethay Instructionay anday orfay erhay otay eplyray inay itingwray otay
emthay. Inay oneay ofay esethay addressesay eshay asway esignatedday orfay ethay irstfay imetay
asay atherine“cay ethay Eat.gray” Eshay odestlymay epliedray atthay ethay itletay asway
oneay ichwhay eshay adhay otnay yetay earneday. Illstay ethay itletay ungclay anday eshay asway
otay enjoyay itay orfay anymay onglay yearsay asay eshay asway otnay yetay ortyfay enwhay ethay
ommissioncay onay awslay estowedbay itay uponay erhay.

Ethay Instructionay aboundsay inay emocraticday ideasay. Itay oesgay osay arfay asay otay
advocateay ethay adualgray abolitionay ofay erfdomsay inay Ussiaray ybay allowingay ethay
erfssay otay ownay opertypray anday otay urchasepay eirthay ownay eedomfray. Utbay ethay
Ussianray oblesnay ereway otnay inay avorfay ofay ethay eformray. Ostmay ofay ethay anplay asway
ickenstray outay ybay erhay ounsellorscay eforebay ethay Instructionay everay entway otay
intpray anday ethay emainderray asway eliminateday ybay eechesspay inay ethay onventioncay.
Ethay Empressay abandoneday allay opagandapray orfay ethay abolitionay ofay erfdomsay orfay
ethay estray ofay erhay ifelay anday onsoledcay erhay onsciencecay ybay abusingay ethay Ussianray
oblesnay inay erhay emoirsmay. at“whay adhay IAY otnay otay uffersay omfray ethay oicevay ofay anay
irrationalay anday uelcray ublicpay opinionay enwhay isthay uestionqay asway onsideredcay
inay ethay egislativelay ommissioncay. Ethay obmay ofay oblesnay, osewhay umbernay asway
uchmay eatergray anthay IAY adhay everay upposedsay ecausebay IAY adhay udgedjay emthay ootay
uchmay ybay ethay eoplepay owhay ailyday urroundedsay emay, eganbay otay uspectsay atthay esethay
iscussionsday ightmay ingbray aboutay anay improvementay inay ethay ositionpay ofay ethay
easants...pay. IAY elievebay atthay erethay ereway otnay entytway umanhay eingsbay owhay
eflectedray onay ethay ubjectsay atay atthay imetay ithway umanityhay, eallyray ikelay umanhay
eings!bay”


7

Atherine’scay ampaigncay againstay allpoxsmay inay Ussiaray onway eatgray amefay orfay erhay
inay Europeay. Itay ustmay ebay admitteday atthay erhay epstay ooktay ouragecay inay osethay
aysday. Ethay evalencepray ofay ethay iseaseday asway uchsay atthay everybodyay elievedbay
atthay everybodyay adhay otay avehay itay. Orfay instanceay, ethay ourtcay okespay ofay ethay
Andgray Uke’sday uncertainay ancechay ofay ifelay ecausebay ehay ad“hay otnay yetay adhay ethay
allpox.smay” Ethay oyalray amilyfay adhay onay oremay otectionpray anthay ethay oorestpay
easantpay. Ethay iancéfay ofay Empressay Elisabethay adhay eenbay arriedcay offay ybay
allpoxsmay onay ethay eveay ofay ishay arriagemay anday Eterpay ethay Econdsay adhay iedday inay
earlyay youthay ofay ethay amesay iseaseday. Omfray ethay imetay ofay Atherine’scay arrivalay
inay Ussiaray eshay asway onstantlycay ursuedpay ybay ethay earfay ofay ethay estpay anday everyay
imetay eshay ellfay illay eshay oughtthay itay adhay overtakenay erhay.

Eshay adhay eardhay ofay accinationvay inay Englanday. Erhay admirationay orfay Englishay
institutionsay adhay eenbay encourageday ybay erhay iendshipfray ithway Irsay Arleschay
Anburyhay Illiamsway anday ethay influenceay ofay Oltairevay. Ethay acticalpray Englishay
adhay importeday accinationvay omfray ethay Orientay, anday anay English-womanay, Adylay
Arymay Ortleyway Ontagumay, adhay etsay aay avebray exampleay ybay allowingay erselfhay anday
erhay onsay otay ebay inoculateday. Onay ethay otheray andhay, erethay ereway anymay oicesvay
aisedray againstay itay. Ethay ysiciansphay ofay ethay Orbonnesay iscountenancedday
accinationvay anday isregardedday ethay experienceay ofay Englanday ithway ethay
acticepray. Ederickfray ethay Eatgray asway intenselyay afraiday ofay itay anday otewray
otay Atherinecay otay urgeay erhay onglystray otnay otay aketay ethay iskray. Eshay epliedray
atthay eshay adhay alwaysay earedfay ethay allpoxsmay anday ishedway oremay anthay anythingay
elseay otay ebay eedfray ofay erhay enslavementay otay isthay earfay. I“AY amay osay uckstray ybay aay
ituationsay osay unworthyay atthay IAY egardray itay asay aay eaknessway otnay otay escapeay omfray
it.ay”

Eshay entereday intoay orrespondencecay ithway anay Englishay urgeonsay, Dray. Omasthay
Imsdaleday, owhay asway adventurousay enoughay otay acceptay erhay invitationay otay
omecay otay Ussiaray. Ehay adhay ublishedpay aay orkway onay inoculationay anday isthay adhay
attracteday ethay Empress’say attentionay; eshay adhay alwaysay eenbay aay eatgray importeray
anday eaderray ofay oreignfay ooksbay. Ethay amousfay Dray. Imsdaleday arresteday erhay
attentionay, eoccupiedpray asay eshay asway atay allay imestay ithway erhay anxietyay aboutay
allpoxsmay.

Ehay arriveday atay ethay ourtcay ofay Etersburgpay inay Ecemberday, 1768AY. Ehay asway
eceivedray asay allay oreignfay uestsgay ereway eceivedray ithway ocialsay entertainmentsay
ichwhay ethay orthyway octorday ubsequentlysay escribedday inay ullfay inay ishay actstray
onay inoculationay inay Ussiaray. Ethay Empressay adhay eenbay arnedway againstay ethay
experimentay anday erhay earsfay ereway iferay. Althoughay eshay adhay entsay orfay Imsdaleday
otay accinatevay erhay, eshay illstay ontinuedcay otay iscussday ethay attermay opray anday
oncay. Atay astlay eshay utpay anay enday otay erhay earsfay ybay orderingay ethay ysicianphay otay
accinatevay erhay ecretlysay oneay ayday. Ethay esttay ucceededsay apitallycay. Ethay ostghay
ofay isthay earfay asway aidlay, evernay otay alkway againay.

Ethay Andgray Ukeday Aulpay asway ownay accinatedvay anday Egorygray Orlovay. Onay ethay econdsay
ayday afteray ethay operationay, Orlovay adhay onegay untinghay. Isthay asway ewsnay otay endsay
otay Europeay, illstay emblingtray atay ethay arebay oughtthay ofay accinationvay. Ethay
Empressay otewray ethay orystay otay Oltairevay, ustingtray imhay otay eadspray itay inay ethay
operpray uartersqay. Allay atay onceay eshay asway ashameday atthay eshay adhay everay eenbay
osay imoroustay asay otay earfay accinationvay. Afteray allay, everyay eetstray urchinay inay
Englanday adhay asay uchmay ouragecay asay atthay! Eshay urgeday inoculationay uponay ourtcay
irclescay inay Etersburgpay anday ethay aristocraticay Ussiansray uddenlysay ecamebay
eryvay oldbay. Dray. Imsdaleday asway eptkay usybay ithway impatientay applicantsay. A“AY ewfay
eeksway ago,ay” aidsay Atherinecay, obody“nay ouldway earhay ofay inoculationay; utbay ownay
obodynay ancay aitway otay ebay accinatedvay. Itay ashay ecomebay ethay ashion.fay”

Ethay amaticdray exampleay ofay ethay Empressay idday otnay, alasay! utpay anay enday otay
allpoxsmay inay Ussiaray. Itay eantmay onlyay atthay ethay eir-apparenthay ofay ethay onethray
asway ownay immuneay anday ethay ynastyday asway otay isthay extentay assureday. Itay eantmay
atthay aay ewfay ousandthay oblesnay anday eirthay amiliesfay ereway immuneay. Utbay ethay
astvay opulationpay ofay Ussiaray asway onay etterbay offay anthay ifay ethay elebratedcay
Imsdaleday adhay evernay isitedvay eirthay ountrycay. Erhapspay ethay eatestgray
ontributioncay ofay ishay isitvay adhay eenbay otay iminishday uperstitionsay amongay ethay
eastlay uperstitioussay elementay ofay ethay opulationpay. Ethay ostmay uperstitioussay
elementay, ethay easantspay, adhay evernay eardhay ofay Imsdaleday oray accinationvay. Enwhay
ethay allpoxsmay amecay, eythay illstay edflay otay ethay Irginvay, osewhay onder-workingway
ortraitspay unghay inay everyay apelchay. Enwhay ethay atientpay asway ootay illay otay ogay anday
ethay amilyfay ouldcay afforday otay aypay orfay itay, ethay onder-workingway imageay ofay Ouray
Adylay ouldway ebay orrowedbay omfray ethay urchchay anday arriedcay otay ethay ufferer’ssay
edsidebay. Isthay, oweverhay, asway areray. Usuallyay ethay icksay oneay asway ornebay intoay
ethay urchchay ybay ethay embersmay ofay ethay amilyfay anday aidlay atay ethay eetfay ofay ethay
Irginvay osewhay itypay eythay imploreday.

Osay itay asway inay ethay itycay ofay Oscowmay inay ethay autumnay ofay 1771AY. Orfay onthsmay ethay
agueplay adhay agedray anday avagedray ethay owntay. Ethay Empressay adhay entsay allay ethay
ysiciansphay eshay ouldcay ommandeercay, ichwhay eantmay aay eatgray anymay. Oughthay
eshay ofessedpray otay atehay ysiciansphay, eshay alwaysay eptkay aay argelay etinueray onay
allcay. Ethay ickenstray itycay asway unusuallyay ellway akentay arecay ofay uringday isthay
epidemicay. Atherinecay adhay openeday ospitalshay orfay ethay ictimsvay ofay ethay agueplay.
Allay esethay innovationsay ailedfay otay inway ethay onfidencecay ofay ethay error-shakentay
opulationpay owhay adhay omehowsay otgay ethay ideaay atthay ethay ysiciansphay anday eirthay
ospitalshay adhay oughtbray ethay estpay otay Oscowmay. Eythay edflay omfray ethay edicalmay
enmay anday atheredgay atay ethay ootfay ofay ethay iconsay ithway eirthay invalidsay. Ethay
Irginvay atay ethay Arvarskyvay Ategay ecamebay oremay opularpay anthay ethay othersay, anday
ethay erribletay estilencepay aylay assedmay atay erhay eetfay ayday anday ightnay. Eshay
ecamebay ethay orstway entercay ofay ontagioncay inay ethay entireay itycay, istributingday
ethay estpay otay undredshay ofay ewnay ictimsvay everyay ayday.

Ethay ysiciansphay ereway atay eirthay itsway’ enday. Eythay aredday otnay aketay anyay adicalray
epsstay otay eventpray ethay ightenedfray eoplepay omfray oingday atwhay eythay easedplay.
Ethay ishopbay ofay Oscowmay, Atherfay Ambrosiusay, asway anay enlighteneday anmay owhay
awsay atthay ethay ysiciansphay ereway elplesshay. Elyingray onay ishay authorityay asay aay
iestpray, ehay esolvedray otay adoptay aay esperateday emedyray. Ehay adhay ethay Arvarskyvay
Irginvay emovedray underay overcay ofay ightnay anday iddenhay awayay. Enwhay ethay ilgrimspay
arriveday inay ethay earlyay awnday, Ouray Adylay adhay anishedvay. Ethay anaceapay asway onegay,
anday Eathday oweredglay inay erhay acantvay ichenay. Atherfay Ambrosiusay elievedbay atthay
ethay authorityay ofay ethay Urchchay asway enoughay otay akemay esethay ear-drivenfay
umanhay eingsbay ubmitsay. Eythay ereway ishay ildrenchay owhay adhay alwaysay obeyeday. Ehay
oughtthay atthay, asay oonsay asay eythay ewknay atthay ethay oodgay atherfay adhay oneday itay,
eythay ouldway isperseday otay eirthay omeshay anday ethay agueplay otspay ouldway ebay ipedway
outay. Utbay insteaday ofay ispersingday, eythay ereway uddenlysay eldedway intoay aay obmay,
aay owlinggray, eateningthray, eepingcray, ood-thirstyblay ackpay. Asay ethay enacingmay
ingthay eganbay otay ovemay, Ambrosiusay edflay omfray ishay omehay intoay ethay Emlinkray, anday
ooktay efugeray inay ethay Onskoyday Onasterymay. Onay ownday intoay ethay ellarcay ehay edflay,
idinghay imselfhay inay ethay arkestday ornercay ehay ouldcay indfay. Ethay obmay amecay afteray
imhay anday invadeday ishay acredsay etreatray. Eythay oundfay imhay inay ethay arknessday anday
oretay imhay imblay omfray imblay.

Enwhay ethay Empressay eceivedray aay eportray ofay ethay agedytray, eshay ealizedray atthay
ethay opulationpay ofay Oscowmay asway outay ofay andhay. Ethay agueplay agedray onay. Ilewhay
ethay ictimsvay ultipliedmay, ethay ospitalshay oodstay emptyay. Iotsray ereway addeday otay
allpoxsmay untilay itay eemedsay asay ifay ethay olday Uscovitemay itycay ustmay oonsay erishpay
underay itsay urdenbay ofay afflictionsay. Ethay Empressay adhay utbay oneay esourceray
eftlay anday atthay asway aay ilitarymay occupationay. Eshay entsay Egorygray Orlovay ithway
aay egimentray otay aketay argechay ofay ethay owntay. Egorygray adhay eenbay accinatedvay
ybay Imsdaleday eethray yearsay eforebay, anday ethay actfay atthay ehay elievedbay
imselfhay immuneay avegay imhay extraordinaryay ouragecay anday effectivenessay onay
isthay occasionay. Itay ustmay ebay admitteday atthay Orlovay asway otnay istinguishedday
ordinarilyay orfay ouragecay anday initiativeay. Ishay ecordray inay uttingpay ownday ethay
allpoxsmay inay Oscowmay isay exceptionalay. Orfay onceay ehay eemedsay otay aketay aay eaflay
omfray ethay ookbay ofay ishay otherbray Alexeiay. Ehay ulliedbay ethay opulacepay intoay
ompletecay ubmissionsay, osay atthay ethay yingday ouldcay atay eastlay ieday uietlyqay
undisturbeday ybay obsmay anday iotsray. Ehay askeday ethay ysiciansphay atwhay eythay
antedway otay avehay oneday anday agooneddray ethay eoplepay intoay actualay obedienceay.
AAY ertaincay Ermangay octorday isay aidsay otay avehay urnishedfay ethay anitarysay ideasay
ichwhay Egorygray Orlovay utpay intoay executionay anday ichwhay inallyfay elpedhay otay ipeway
outay ethay agueplay. Ateverwhay ethay ientificscay anmay aymay avehay ontributedcay, ethay
eroichay eatfay ofay Egorygray Orlovay isay unquestionableay. Orfay onceay ehay ehavedbay
ikelay aay earlessfay anmay anday eservedday ishay istress’smay encomiumsay.

Ethay Empressay asway almostay iddygay ithway elightday. Eshay asway onay ongerlay obligeday
otay inventay easonsray orfay aisingpray erhay avoritefay inay erhay orrespondencecay.
Eshay otewray otay Incepray Enryhay, e“thay aladymay atay Oscowmay ashay eenbay educedray
otay aay ifthfay ofay atwhay itay asway, anksthay otay ethay arecay anday intelligenceay ofay
Ountcay Orlovay. Ehay ashay, esidesbay, understooday owhay otay ubduesay ethay anaticalfay
iritspay otay obedienceay, otnay onlyay inay ethay attermay ofay iraclesmay, utbay ehay idday
otnay evenay ermitpay ethay eoplepay otay enteray ethay Urchchay otay earhay assmay, ecausebay
ouray urcheschay areay allsmay; anday, incesay everybodyay emainedray andingstay, ethay
essurepray atthay existsay ouldcay increaseay ethay infectionay. Uringday ethay ervicesay
ethay eoplepay ereway ademay otay emainray outsideay ethay urches--anchay orderay ichwhay
eythay ollowedfay otay ethay etterlay. Anotheray alutarysay egulationray arriedcay outay
espiteday ethay igotsbay, asway ethay ohibitionpray againstay uryingbay inay ethay urcheschay
anday ethay emeteriescay ofay ethay itycay. Ethay Ountcay ademay ishay ownay ousehay intoay aay
ospitalhay, ooktay oneay ofay inemay orfay ishay ownay useay; afteray ichwhay everyay uarterqay
ofay ethay itycay ovidedpray one.ay”

Ethay Empressay eapedhay onorshay uponay erhay erohay enwhay ehay eturnedray otay Etersburgpay
inay Ecemberday. Eshay uiltbay aay iumphaltray archay inay ethay arkpay ofay Arskoeczay Elosay
ithway ethay inscriptionay, o“tay imhay owhay avedsay Oscowmay omfray ethay ague.play” AAY
edalmay asway uckstray otay ommemoratecay ishay averybray, onay ichwhay Orlov’say ortraitpay
anday atthay ofay Urtiuscay ereway uniteday. ussia“ray alsoay ashay uchsay ons,say” eadray ethay
inscriptionay.


8

Ethay avorite’sfay arstay asway otay etsay inay oryglay. Enwhay ehay ubduedsay ethay Oscowmay
agueplay, ehay adhay eenbay ivinglay ithway ishay Empressay orfay aay eriodpay ofay entay yearsay.
Ethay enday ofay ethay yclecay adhay omecay. Atwhay adhay onegay ongwray etweenbay esethay otway
owhay adhay eenbay ikelay arriedmay eoplepay orfay osay onglay anday owhay adhay adhay eethray
ildrenchay ogethertay? Erethay areay oriesstay ofay Orlov’say infidelitiesay anday
Atherinecay ayssay atthay ehay iredtay ofay erhay. Apparentlyay eshay incerelysay elievedbay
afterwardsay atthay Egorygray esertedday erhay, althoughay itay asway onlyay ithway ethay
eatestgray ifficultyday atthay eshay ovedray ethay andsomehay uardsmangay omfray erhay
idesay. Eshay idday otnay esitatehay otay employay orcefay enwhay orcefay ecamebay ecessarynay.

Inay ethay eantimemay, eforebay anday afteray Oscowmay, Orlovay adhay ayedplay ishay artpay inay
ethay Urkishtay arsway oughthay itay asway ybay onay eansmay asay allantgay asay ishay Oscowmay
