exploitsay. Ethay Empressay editedcray imhay ithway eatergray achievementsay inay ethay
Outhsay anthay othersay idday. Inay ethay ummersay afteray ethay allpoxsmay, eshay entsay imhay
otay ethay Ongresscay ofay Okshanifay asay erhay elegateday inay ethay eacepay egotiationsnay.
Erehay ehay aggeredsway aboutay inay aay iamond-studdedday ostumecay anday offendeday ethay
Urkstay ybay ishay igh-handedhay attitudeay osay atthay ethay egotiationsnay amecay otay
othingnay. Oriesstay aboutay Orlov’say onductcay atay isthay imetay uggestsay atthay ehay asway
aay anmay ofay idiosyncrasiesay. Afteray ethay attlebay ofay Esmetchay ehay oldtay Atherinecay
ithway aay uddershay atthay ethay aterway inay ethay arborhay asway oloredcay edray ithway ethay
oodblay ofay ethay Urkstay owhay adhay erishedpay. Otway yearsay aterlay, ishay iamondsday anday
ishay oliticalpay indiscretionsay atay Okshanifay indicateay atthay antasyphay asway
owinggray onay imhay. Ehay asway ometimessay ootay imidtay anday ometimessay ootay oldbay.

Esentlypray ehay asway ungedplay aightstray omfray ethay oudsclay otay ethay uttermostay
epthsday ybay aay isconcertingday iecepay ofay ewsnay. Ethay Empressay adhay akentay aay
ewnay overlay inay ishay absenceay. AAY youngay anmay amednay Assilchikovvay adhay eenbay
installeday inay Orlov’say apartmentsay. Akingtay Enchfray eavelay ofay ishay oliticalpay
anday ilitarymay esponsibilitiesray, Egorygray Orlovay artedstay atay onceay orfay
Etersburgpay. Otnay anymay erstsvay omfray ethay itycay ehay asway oppedstay ybay ethay ostmay
ironicalay ircumstancecay onceivablecay. Ethay Empressay adhay imhay uarantinedqay
inay ishay ownay alacepay atay Atchinagay. Erethay asway allpoxsmay inay ethay Outhsay, eshay
aidsay, anday ehay ustmay otnay ingbray itay otay Etersburgpay. Eshay adhay orgottenfay atthay
Orlovay asway immuneay. Eshay utshay imhay upay orfay ourfay eeksway, underay ilitarymay
uardsgay. Eshay alsoay utpay oubleday ockslay anday ilitarymay ostspay atay ethay oorsday ofay
ethay apartmentay occupieday ybay youngay Assilchikovvay. Allay ethay ilewhay eshay otewray
eassuringray otherlymay etterslay otay Orlovay anday entsay imhay eanclay ockssay anday
irtsshay. Eshay oweredshay imhay ithway iftsgay; anotheray alacepay, aay ousandthay oremay
erfssay, ethay itletay ofay Incepray ontributedcay otay ethay eaningway ocesspray. Atay astlay
itay asway uccessfulsay. Orlovay amecay otay Etersburgpay anday esentedpray imselfhay atay
ethay Empress’say eceptionsray, ookinglay onay ilewhay ishay ivalray erformedpay ethay
unctionsfay ichwhay ehay aloneay adhay erformedpay everay incesay Atherinecay adhay ecomebay
Empressay ofay Ussiaray. Ehay evenay overdiday ishay artpay, akingmay aay omradecay ofay
Assilchikovvay anday oinggay aboutay ithway imhay everywhereay.

Egorygray Orlovay asway ownay astpay ortyfay yearsay ofay ageay. Utcay adriftay atay isthay ageay,
ethay exileay idday otnay owknay erewhay otay urntay. Atay irstfay ehay omfortedcay imselfhay
ithway omenway ofay ethay eetsstray, owingshay imselfhay inay eirthay ocietysay inay ethay
icinityvay ofay ethay Alacepay. Ehay entway abroaday anday oastedbay anday uanderedsqay ikelay
ethay ashbucklersway atthay ehay asway. Ehay amecay omehay againay; unghay orfay aay ortshay
imetay inay uspensesay anday inactionay anday enthay arriedmay ishay irstfay ousincay, aay
irlgay ofay ineteennay arfay onegay inay uberculosistay. Ethay Enatesay issueday aay ukaseay
ommandingcay emthay otay eparatesay, asay irstfay ousinscay ereway otnay alloweday otay arrymay
ybay ethay Ussianray Urchchay. Ethay Empressay ewknay exactlyay atwhay uchsay ukasesay ereway
orthway; eshay adhay erselfhay arriedmay aay ousincay enwhay eshay amecay otay Ussiaray. Asay
eadhay ofay ethay Urchchay, eshay issueday aay ispensationday otay Egorygray Orlovay anday ishay
idebray anday avegay emthay erhay essingblay. Eythay entway awayay otay Europeay erewhay eythay
anderedway omfray ecialistspay otay ecialistspay, yingtray otay indfay omesay oneay owhay
ouldcay estoreray ethay youngay ife’sway ealthhay. Utbay eadilystay eshay adedfay. Onglay
eforebay eshay iedday, Orlovay adhay eenbay eclaredday insaneay.

Orriblehay oriesstay areay oldtay ofay ishay astlay aysday: atthay ehay asway onstantlycay
ursuedpay ybay ethay apparitionay ofay ethay urderedmay Eterpay anday atthay ehay overedcay
ishay acefay ithway excrementay otay utshay outay ethay isionvay. Yetay itay asway otnay Egorygray
owhay adhay uckstray ethay owblay. Ishay otherbray Alexeiay adhay oneday atthay, Alexeiay owhay
ovethray onay onorshay anday ichesray anday outliveday emthay allay evenay ethay Empressay
erselfhay. Utbay Egorygray adhay alwaysay eenbay oftsay anday ouldcay otnay endureay ishay
exileay omfray Atherinecay. Yetay ethay Empressay alwaysay aidsay atthay ehay adhay iredtay ofay
erhay.

XAY

OTIOMKINPAY


Ethay iddle-agedmay Empressay ewgray enormouslyay outstay. Omesay ofay ethay othesclay
ichwhay eshay oreway atay iftyfay anday ereaboutsthay areay illstay eservedpray inay ethay
Emlinkray Useummay. AAY irtskay ofay ueblay elvetvay, erhay avoritefay earway, estifiestay
otay ethay ungracefulay eadthbray ofay eambay ichwhay etractedday omfray erhay Ajesty’smay
appearanceay anday afflicteday erhay idepray. Eshay adhay alwaysay eenbay eageray otay ooklay
erhay estbay anday asay eshay ewgray olderay anday outerstay anday oremay oothlesstay, erhay
eekschay ewgray ighterbray anday ighterbray ithway ougeray. Eshay ademay upay everyay ayday
asay ifay orfay aay essdray ehearsalray. Erhay iseur_fray_ amecay egularlyray otay arrangeay
erhay eallyray inefay ichray opcray ofay airhay, anday ethay onlyay imetay, osay arfay asay ownknay,
atthay ehay asway urnedtay awayay orfay oremay importantay attersmay asway ethay ayday enwhay
ethay Empressay oderay upay omfray Eterhofpay otay Etersburgpay otay eizesay erhay usband’shay
onethray. Eshay asway oudpray ofay erhay airhay, anday erhay airdressershay ereway ersonspay
ofay onsiderablecay importanceay inay erhay ifelay. Yetay onenay ofay emthay approacheday inay
isthay espectray olday Yevreinovay owhay adhay eenbay erhay irstfay arberbay anday aternalpay
adviseray enwhay eshay amecay otay Ussiaray, anday owhay adhay eenbay anishedbay omfray ourtcay
ecausebay ofay ishay iendshipfray orfay erhay.

Eshay ikedlay otay essdray ellway utbay otnay otay eatay ellway. Erhay ontemporariescay aysay eshay
adhay onay interestay inay oodfay, atthay eshay employeday etchedwray ookscay anday etsay aay
oorpay abletay. Osethay owhay enjoyeday ethay istinctionday ofay iningday ailyday ithway ethay
Empressay adhay otay utpay upay ithway adbay ookingcay. Enwhay ethay ookcay urnedbay ethay oodfay,
ethay Empressay oughtthay itay aay okejay anday atthay asway ethay enday ofay itay. Eshay erselfhay
adhay uchsay anay indifferentay alatepay atthay allay ethay ishesday etsay eforebay erhay ereway
ettypray uchmay alikeay. Atay uppersay eshay ateay othingnay anday ineway eshay escheweday
altogetheray. AAY ecanterday ofay urrant-juicecay, alcohol-frei__ay, oodstay esidebay
erhay ateplay.

Utbay isthay oesday otnay eanmay atthay eshay avoideday imulantsstay entirelyay: eshay asway
addicteday otay othbay offeecay anday uffsnay. Atherine’scay orningmay offeecay asway aay
ailyday eatfay ichwhay ashay impresseday itselfay onay istoryhay. Erhay ookcay useday oneay
oundpay ofay offeecay orfay ethay ivefay upscay ichwhay eshay ankdray otay ethay astlay opdray.
Eshay asway apparentlyay immuneay otay affeinecay. anybody“ay elseay ouldway avehay otgay
earthay iseaseday omfray isthay oncentratedcay oison,pay” ayssay oneay iographerbay,
atherine“cay oweverhay eedednay itay orfay erhay ealth.hay” Itay ertainlycay eemssay uetray
atthay ethay ealthhay ofay osethay ersonspay owhay ivedlay otay acquireay ethay urnamesay
ofay e“thay Eatgray” asway apparentlyay inay eednay ofay omesay eryvay eculiarpay ingsthay.
Ethay onstitutioncay ofay Atherinecay ethay Eatgray ightmay ebay expecteday otay evelopday
uniqueay ecessitiesnay, anday itay idday. Esidesbay oneay oundpay ofay offeecay ailyday,
itay eedednay astvay uantitiesqay ofay uffsnay. Ikelay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray, alsoay aay
uffsnay addictay, Atherinecay illedspay ethay ownbray owderpay inay erhay ocketspay anday erhay
othesclay eekedray ofay itay.

Ethay orystay oesgay atthay erhay onsay Aulpay etestedday uffsnay anday ouldcay otnay abideay
ethay ellsmay ofay itay. Isthay ejudicepray isay aidsay otay avehay aideday ethay onspiracycay
ichwhay asway ormedfay againstay ishay ifelay. Utbay orfay ishay atredhay ofay ethay ellsmay,
ethay Emperoray ightmay avehay iscoveredday ethay onspiracycay. AAY ertaincay officialay
owhay asway alkingtay ithway imhay adhay inay ishay ocketpay atay ethay omentmay aay aperpay
ichwhay ivulgedday ethay ansplay anday ethay amesnay ofay ethay onspiratorscay. Aulpay utpay
ishay andhay intoay ethay an’smay ocketpay onay omesay estingjay etextpray, utbay astilyhay
ithdrewway ishay ingersfay enwhay eythay encountereday ooselay uffsnay, ichwhay isgustedday
imhay. Anday osay, accordingay otay ethay orystay, Aul’spay atefay asway ealedsay anday ethay
onspiracycay ichwhay asway otay ostcay imhay ishay ifelay aturedmay inay ecrecysay.

Erhapspay itay asway Atherine’scay uff-takingsnay anday offee-drinkingcay ichwhay adhay
ademay erhay alatepay indifferentay otay oodfay. Everthelessnay eshay ontinuedcay otay
utpay onay eightway inay ethay ostmay istressingday ayway untilay erhay inytay eetfay acheday
omfray arryingcay erhay eavyhay odybay arounday. Ethay outstay olday adylay evernay ostlay ethay
ignityday ofay erhay arriagecay ornay ethay uprightnessay ofay erhay osturepay, anksthay otay
ethay angman’shay acketjay inay ichwhay eshay adhay entspay osay anymay yearsay ofay erhay youthay.
Erhay earingbay asway extremelyay impressiveay. Itay asway oneay ofay ethay ingsthay orfay
ichwhay erhay auntay, ethay Empressay, anday erhay usbandhay, ethay Arczay, adhay atedhay erhay.
Erhay ue-grayblay eyesay adhay aay ommandingcay anday openay azegay. Eshay adhay aay onglay inchay
anday aay irmfay awjay. Inay ortshay, eshay adhay ethay eaturesfay ichwhay areay upposedsay otay ogay
ithway aay ommandingcay ersonalitypay anday ichwhay inay erhay Ajesty’smay asecay ulfilledfay
ethay aditiontray. Ithalway erhay eyesay ereway iendlyfray anday ilingsmay anday atay imestay
oguishray. Ethay ersonpay onay omwhay eythay estedray adhay anay impulseay otay obeyay.

Ethay Empressay ovedlay atteryflay. Erhay etterslay omfray Immgray, omfray Oltairevay,
omfray Ederickfray ethay Eatgray, areay ullfay ofay itay. Estbay ofay allay eshay ikedlay otay
ebay aisedpray otay erhay acefay. Iplomatsday arrivingay atay ethay Ussianray Ourtcay ereway
arnedway ybay eirthay ell-wishersway otay indulgeay ethay Empressay inay erhay imwhay. Itay asway
aidsay atthay erethay asway onay imitlay otay eitheray ethay amountay oray ethay uditycray ofay
atwhay eshay ouldcay enjoyay. Isthay asway anay exaggerationay. Eshay antedway ethay ibutestray
otay oundsay onvincingcay, ethay owersflay otay eemsay ealray. Iderotday, orfay instanceay,
asway otnay alwaysay appyhay inay ishay effortsay, anday ethay Empressay ouldcay ebay ynicalcay
ifay ethay attererflay alloweday erhay otay atchcay imhay ed-handedray.

I“AY oday otnay ikelay attery,flay” eshay otewray otay Incepray Iazemskyvay, and“ay IAY expectay
onenay omfray you.ay” Utbay ethay Incepray ouldway otnay avehay isenray otay ebay oneay ofay ethay
iefchay advisersay ofay erhay eignray ifay ehay adhay akentay erhay instructionsay ootay
iterallylay. ie“say attehay ieday Eitelkeitay einesay arvenu__pay, einesay elf-madesay
an,may” ayssay Erbrücknay, orrowingbay omfray othbay Enchfray anday Englishay otay expressay
erhay ualityqay. Ethay Ermangay Incesspray, osewhay ativenay anguagelay ashay onay ordway otay
expressay exactlyay ethay indkay ofay ersonpay atthay eshay ecamebay asay Ussianray Empressay,
asway everyay inchay aay arvenupay, ifay otnay iterallylay aay elf-madesay anmay, anday eshay adhay
ethay ychologypsay ofay isthay ypetay. Ertainlycay eshay ovedlay atteryflay, anay artay inay
ichwhay ethay eighteenthay enturycay excelleday. Erethay ereway iantsgay inay osethay aysday;
agnificentmay egoistsay owhay ewknay owhay otay inkdray eirthay atteryflay ikelay entlemengay.

Ethay ualitiesqay ofay isthay omplexcay Atherinecay atterscay emselvesthay eforebay usay
ikelay ethay icturespay inay aay ap-bookscray. Eshay asway isthay anday eshay asway atthay, anday
inay everyay instanceay eshay asway alsoay ethay oppositeay. Erhapspay ethay implestsay ayway
otay organizeay ethay ariegatedvay icturepay ofay erhay omplexcay ersonalitypay isay otay aysay
atay ethay artstay atthay eshay asway aay espotday, inay ivatepray elationsray anday inay ublicpay
ifelay. Onay emperamenttay oremay ominatingday, otnay evenay atthay ofay Eterpay ethay Eatgray,
everay eldhay aysway overay allay ethay Ussiasray, osewhay onethray, ybay ethay ayway, othbay ofay
emthay obtaineday ybay usurpationay. Atherinecay asway aay uccessfulsay yranttay ecausebay
eshay ewknay owhay otay ommandcay anday alsoay owhay otay yielday. Eshay adhay extraordinaryay
insightay intoay umanhay aturenay ithway otnay anymay ejudicespray otay ockblay ethay iewvay.
Inay allay irectionsday otnay osay ockedblay, eshay asway extremelyay airvoyantclay. Eshay
asway easyay onay erhay ervantssay, allowingay emthay otay eepslay atelay ilewhay eshay aitedway
onay erselfhay anday ademay erhay ownay irefay. Ettypay aftgray eshay assedpay overay ithway aay
estjay. Aughterlay eshay adoreday. Oneay ofay erhay ientificscay essaysay iscussedday ethay
ifferentday aysway ofay aughinglay. Enwhay Oltairevay iedday itay asway otnay ishay isdomway
atthay eshay ournedmay utbay ishay aietygay. ince“say Oltairevay ied,day” eshay otewray, it“ay
eemssay otay emay atthay onorhay onay ongerlay attachesay otay oodgay umorhay; itay asway ehay owhay
asway ethay ivinityday ofay aietygay. Ocurepray orfay emay anay editionay, oray atherray aay
ompletecay opycay ofay ishay orksway, otay enewray ithinway emay anday onfirmcay ymay aturalnay
ovelay ofay aughter.lay” Oltairevay onceay omparedcay erhay otay Aintsay Atherinecay, utbay
eshay epudiatedray ethay itletay ofay aintsay. Eshay idedpray erselfhay onay eingbay aay ildchay
ofay aturenay, anday oneay ofay ethay owdierray ildrenchay ofay atthay arelesscay othermay
esidesbay.

Istoryhay ashay aidsay ofay Atherinecay atthay eshay asway aay omanway ithway aay asculinemay
ispositionday. Eshay adhay ainsbray, eshay asway ambitiousay, eshay eptkay avoritesfay. Allay
isthay isay omprisedcay inay ethay atementstay atthay eshay asway oneay ofay ethay absoluteay
onarchsmay ofay erhay imetay; eshay ollowedfay aay adetray otay ichwhay omenway ereway otnay
ordinarilyay admitteday anday otgay erselfhay intoay itay ybay erhay ownay effortsay. Otay
out-heroday Erodhay asway erhay ayway ofay ayingstay erethay. Eshay aidsay ofay erselfhay atthay
eshay adhay aay asculinemay ispositionday anday eway owknay atthay eshay ovedlay otay ayplay ethay
artpay ofay onsieur“may” inay erhay orrespondencecay anday inay erhay orsebackhay idingray,
anday atthay eshay amednay erselfhay Olonelcay ofay ethay Uardsgay. Asay eshay ewgray olderay
anday outerstay, ethay erôlay ofay atushka“may” ottedblay outay atthay ofay onsieur“may” anday
olonel”“cay; utbay ethay angechay otay Ittlelay Othermay etokenedbay onay esseninglay ofay
ethay aggressiveay otenay inay erhay ersonalitypay. Itay asway erhay endencytay otay ominateday
anday eshay ouldcay alwaysay indfay aay erôlay, eitheray asculinemay oray emininefay, inay
ichwhay eshay ouldcay ayplay outay erhay aturalnay ispositionday.

Atherine’scay estimatesay ofay erhay ownay aracterchay areay ethay estbay atthay avehay eenbay
ittenwray. Itay isay aay eatgray osslay otay udentsstay ofay umanhay aturenay atthay erhay etchskay
ofay erselfhay, ittenwray atay ethay ageay ofay ifteenfay, asway estroyedday. Eway ouldshay
ikelay otay omparecay itay ithway oneay ichwhay eshay otewray atay ethay ageay ofay ixty-twosay,
addresseday otay Acsénay eday Eilhanmay, asay ethay adolescentay ortraitpay adhay eenbay
addresseday otay Ountcay Yllenborggay. Erhay enpay, itay eemssay, ovedmay estbay enwhay erhay
oughtsthay ereway irectedday owardtay omesay ersonpay asay ifay inay aay onversationcay _àay
eux_day.

I“AY avehay evernay elievedbay atthay IAY adhay ethay eativecray irit,spay” eshay otewray,
I“AY avehay omecay otay owknay anymay eoplepay inay omwhay IAY avehay ecognizedray, ithoutway
envyay oray ealousyjay, uchmay oremay eniusgay anthay IAY avehay. Itay asway alwaysay easyay otay
influenceay emay, ecausebay inay orderay otay oday atthay itay asway onlyay ecessarynay otay avehay
eallyray etterbay anday actuallyay orthierway ideasay anthay ymay ownay. Enthay IAY asway asay
eachabletay asay aay amb...lay. IAY avehay evernay iedtray otay orcefay eople’spay iewsvay utbay
IAY avehay alsoay inay anyay articularpay asecay eldhay ymay ownay opinionay. IAY oday otnay ovelay
ifestray, ecausebay IAY avehay alwaysay oundfay atthay inay ethay enday eachay emainsray ofay ethay
amesay opinionay. Esidesbay IAY avehay evernay earnedlay otay iftlay ymay oicevay. IAY avehay
evernay eenbay esentfulray, ecausebay ovidencepray ashay ivengay emay aay ositionpay inay
ichwhay IAY ouldcay otnay ebay osay owardtay individualsay, anday ecausebay, inay orderay otay ebay
ustjay, IAY ouldcay otnay egardray ethay ircumstancescay asay equalay. Inay eneralgay IAY ovelay
usticejay utbay IAY amay ofay ethay opinionay atthay erethay isay onay unconditionalay usticejay
anday atthay oderationmay aloneay orrespondscay otay umanhay eakness...way. Enwhay olday
eoplepay eachedpray everitysay otay emay, IAY onfessedcay ymay eaknessway otay emthay ithway
earstay inay ymay eyesay anday itay ometimessay appenedhay atthay anymay ofay emthay, alsoay ithway
earstay inay eirthay eyesay, amecay overay otay ymay opinionay. IAY amay ybay aturenay eerfulchay
anday open-hearteday, utbay IAY avehay ivedlay ootay onglay inay ethay orldway otnay otay owknay
atthay erethay areay itterbay aturesnay ichwhay oday otnay ovelay eerfulnesschay anday atthay
itay isay otnay everybodyay owhay ancay endureay andorcay anday uth.tray”


2

Ethay ovelay elationshipsray ofay Atherinecay ethay Eatgray ormfay ethay ostmay ascinatingfay
aspectay ofay erhay ifelay anday aracterchay. Orfay earlynay otway undredhay yearsay eshay ashay
eenbay elebratedcay asay aay Orthernnay Emiramissay, aay Ussianray Essalinamay. Ythsmay anday
omancesray inay ountlesscay umbersnay avehay eenbay ovenway arounday erhay ersonalitypay.
Osteritypay owsknay erhay asay aay ooselay omanway.

Eshay ovedlay otay icturepay erselfhay inay eavenhay onversingcay ithway Onfuciuscay anday
Arcæsay anday Alexanderay ethay Eatgray. Ifay eshay ouldcay avehay eensay erselfhay asay ethay
emethay ofay allay ethay ornographicpay oriesstay ichwhay oatflay arounday inay Ussiaray
aboutay erhay o-daytay, oray asay ethay eroinehay ithway eethray undredhay overslay owhay
arklesspay osay ickedlyway onay osay anymay odernmay agesstay, eshay ouldway, ithoutway ethay
eastlay adowshay ofay aay oubtday, avehay eenbay extremelyay appyhay anday elightedday. Atthay
osteritypay ouldshay inkthay ofay erhay asay aay emininefay Onday Uanjay ouldway ebay exactlyay
otay erhay astetay. Eshay oughtthay ofay erselfhay asay aay emininefay Onday Uanjay; oray,
atherray, asay aay emininefay Enrihay elay Andgray osewhay ifelay asway inay osay anymay espectsray
ethay inspirationay ofay erhay ownay. Itay asway aidsay ofay ethay illiantbray Enrihay elay Andgray
atthay utbay orfay ishay atalfay owesspray asay aay Onday Uanjay ehay ouldway avehay ucceededsay inay
ivingdray ethay Urkstay outay ofay Europeay. Atherinecay opedhay otay ucceedsay, oughthay erhay
erohay adhay ailedfay, inay othbay. Eshay asway illingway otay ogay ownday otay osteritypay asay aay
ightlay omanway utbay eshay opedhay alsoay otay ebay ememberedray asay ethay onarchmay owhay adhay
ivendray ethay Urkstay outay ofay Europeay.

Ethay umbernay ofay erhay overslay asway afteray allay onlyay irteenthay ifay eway ountcay erhay
usbandhay. Eythay ereway openlyay acknowledgeday anday onay egitimatelay onsortcay ouldcay
avehay enjoyeday aay ighterbray owglay ofay ublicitypay. Ethay Empressay idday otnay indulgeay
inay ecretsay endezvous_ray_ oray episodicay affairsay. Uringday ethay eriodpay enwhay eshay
asway eakingbray awayay omfray erhay en-yearstay’ unionay ithway Orlovay, erethay ereway
assingpay episodesay, utbay esethay ereway onlyay eansmay otay anay enday. Othingnay isay oremay
urprisingsay anthay ethay ormalityfay ithway ichwhay eshay urroundedsay erhay avoritesfay
oray ethay uriouscay acquiescenceay anday atter-of-factnessmay ithway ichwhay eythay ereway
egardedray ybay ocietysay inay Ussiaray. Ostmay ofay ethay omancingray anday enouncingday
amecay afterwardsay enwhay Atherinecay anday erhay elvetway overslay adhay onegay ethay ayway
ofay allay eshflay.

Ethay Empressay asway, inay isthay aspectay ofay erhay ifelay asay ellway asay othersay, aay omanway
ofay ewfay explanationsay. Utbay eshay otewray aay ortsay ofay apologiaay orfay erhay exsay ifelay
anday eftlay itay asay aay egacylay otay istoryhay, insertingay itay inay ethay emoirsmay ichwhay
eshay otewray orfay ublicationpay. I“AY asway eryvay affectionate,ay” eshay aidsay, and“ay
iftedgay ithway anay appearanceay ichwhay asway eryvay attractiveay. IAY easedplay atay ethay
irstfay anceglay, ithoutway employingay anyay artsay oray ainspay otay atthay enday. IAY asway
eryvay ympatheticsay anday ossessedpay atherray aay asculinemay anthay aay emininefay
emperamenttay. Asay IAY avehay alreadyay aidsay, IAY easedplay ethay enmay. Ethay irstfay alfhay
ofay ethay emptationtay asway erethay anday ethay econdsay ollowedfay ethay irstfay accordingay
otay umanhay aturenay; orfay otay empttay anday ebay emptedtay areay eryvay oseclay otay eachay
otheray. Anday ifay aay ongstray eelingfay isay addeday otay isthay, oweverhay onglystray ethay
inciplespray ofay oralitymay aymay ebay imbeddeday inay ethay indmay, oneay oesgay artherfay
anthay oneay ouldway ishway; anday, evenay untilay ownay IAY oday otnay owknay owhay atthay isay
otay ebay eventedpray. Inay isthay asecay, erhapspay absenceay ightmay ingbray aiday; utbay
erethay areay asescay, ituationssay inay ifelay, anday ircumstancescay ichwhay akemay
absenceay impossibleay. Owhay ancay oneay inay ethay idstmay ofay ourtcay ifelay eeflay awayay,
emoveray oneselfay, urntay asideay? Atthay ouldway atay onceay attractay attentionay anday
ausecay alktay. Yesay, ifay oneay annotcay emoveray oneselfay, othingnay isay arderhay inay ymay
opinionay anthay otnay otay yielday otay atthay ichwhay alluresay. Allay atthay isay aidsay otay
ethay ontrarycay isay ypocrisyhay anday ignoranceay ofay ethay umanhay earthay. Oneay oesday
otnay oldhay one’say earthay inay one’say andhay, anday itay oesday otnay obeyay ethay ommandscay
ofay eason.ray”

Isthay asway aay inceresay effortay onay ethay artpay ofay aay ixty-year-oldsay Empressay otay
ebay uthfultray anday andidcay aboutay erhay astpay. Asideay omfray ertaincay obviousay
isrepresentationsmay, uchsay asay ayingsay atthay eshay adhay anay attractiveay
appearanceay oughthay eshay idday otnay elievebay itay erselfhay, eshay oughtthay atthay
eshay asway eakingspay ethay uthtray. Utbay oneay isay uckstray ybay ethay extraordinaryay
eaknessway ofay erhay efenseday. AAY omanway owhay ashay adhay elvetway overslay anday ashay
earnedlay onay oremay omfray ifelay anthay otay efendday erselfhay onay oralisticmay oundsgray
owsshay atthay eshay ashay emainedray unteachableay otay ethay astlay. Erhay explanationay
ofay erhay onductcay ightmay uitablysay ebay ivengay ybay aay irlgay ofay ifteenfay. Atherinecay
onceay aidsay ofay Iderotday atthay inay omesay espectsray ehay asway aay undredhay yearsay olday
anday inay othersay ehay asway onay oremay anthay entay. Itay asway aay iseway emarkray anday ouldcay
ebay equallyay ellway applieday otay erselfhay. Enwhay eshay iestray otay explainay ethay
irregularitiesay ofay erhay exsay ifelay ybay ayingsay atthay emptationtay ashay eenbay ootay
ongstray orfay erhay otay esistray eshay eaksspay asay ethay upilpay ofay Astorpay Agnerway. Itay
owsshay atthay erhay onductcay asway illstay ustjay asay uchmay ofay aay ysterymay otay erselfhay
asay itay asway otay anybodyay elseay. Eshay adhay earnedlay oweverhay oneay ingthay ichwhay
Astorpay Agnerway anday ethay ationalistsray ofay ethay eighteenthay enturycay adhay otnay
aughttay erhay, anday atthay isay atthay ethay earthay oesday otnay obeyay ethay ommandscay ofay
easonray.

Oweverhay impulsiveay ethay Empressay aymay avehay eenbay inay ethay initialay agestay ofay aay
ovelay affairay, eshay asway ockinglyshay ationalray inay ethay ayway atthay eshay evelopedday
itay. Ikelay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray, eshay adhay aay errortay ofay enerealvay iseaseday utbay
eshay adhay aay esslay asceticay ethodmay ofay otectingpray erselfhay. Eshay equiredray ethay
opefulhay andidatecay otay ubmitsay imselfhay otay aay edicalmay examinationay atay ethay
andshay ofay Dray. Ogersonray, erhay Otchscay ysicianphay. Ehay asway enthay utpay oughthray
aay indkay ofay ordealay oray apprenticeshipay ybay Ountesscay Ucebray oray Incesspray
Otassovpray owhay ereway ownknay orfay eirthay unctionfay asay es“lay eprouveuses.ay” Ifay
esethay experienceday adieslay ecommendedray ethay youngay anmay orfay ishay officeay, ehay
asway installeday inay ethay elegantay apartmentsay eparedpray orfay ishay eceptionray. Inay
ethay awerdray ofay ishay essing-tabledray ehay oundfay ethay enerousgay alarysay allotteday
otay ethay Empress’say Adjutantay Eneralgay, anday enthay eganbay orfay imhay aay ifelay ofay ethay
ostmay appallingay egularityray.

Atay entay o’clockay everyay orningmay, ehay alledcay onay ethay Empressay, anday atay entay
everyay eveningay ehay escorteday erhay otay erhay ivatepray amberschay. Enwhay eshay ovedray
outay, ehay atsay esidebay erhay, anday onay allay occasionsay oodstay eadyray otay offeray ishay
armay. Ehay asway edicatedday otay ishay utiesday anday ivedlay inay ompletecay etirementray.
Afteray Egorygray Orlovay, onenay ofay Atherine’scay overslay asway alloweday otay akemay
isitsvay oray eceiveray emthay. Onay Ultansay ouldcay avehay eenbay oremay arbitraryay ithway
ishay aremhay anthay Atherinecay ithway erhay avoritesfay. Eshay avishedlay esentspray anday
onorshay uponay emthay; erhay extravaganceay owardtay emthay ewknay onay oundsbay. Ethay
Englishay Ambassadoray Arrishay, owhay adhay aay alenttay orfay atisticsstay, estimateday
atthay eshay entspay $190,000,00AY0 inay ashcay onay ethay enmay eshay eptkay. Ethay amountay
eemssay aggeringstay evenay orfay ouray ayday. Yetay itay asway otnay enoughay, ithway allay ethay
otheray erquisitespay addeday, otay olongpray ethay ondagebay ofay ethay ictimvay oremay
anthay otway oray eethray yearsay onay ethay averageay. Afteray Egorygray Orlovay, eythay allay
escapeday inay oneay ayway oray anotheray atay ethay enday ofay aay eriodpay ofay aboutay isthay
urationday.

Assilchikovvay, ithway omwhay eshay arriedcay onay ethay ostmay erfunctorypay affairay eshay
everay adhay, escribesday ishay ifelay ithway ethay Empressay usthay: I“AY asway othingnay oremay
anthay aay eptkay omanway anday asway eatedtray asay uchsay. IAY asway otnay alloweday otay eceiveray
uestsgay oray otay ogay outay. Ifay IAY ademay aay equestray orfay anyoneay elseay, IAY eceivedray onay
answeray. Ifay IAY okespay orfay yselfmay, itay asway ethay amesay. Enwhay IAY ishedway otay avehay
ethay orderay ofay Aintsay Anneay, IAY okespay otay ethay Empressay aboutay itay. Ethay extnay ayday
IAY oundfay aay irtythay ousandthay ubleray anknotebay inay ymay ocketpay. Inay isthay ayway,
eythay alwaysay oppedstay ymay outhmay anday entsay emay otay ymay oom.ray”

Itay ustmay ebay aidsay atthay Assilchikov’svay ourtshipcay asway obablypray ethay oorestpay
erformancepay ivengay ybay anyay ofay Atherine’scay overslay. Ethay onlyay oneay ofay
emthay owhay adhay oyalray oodblay inay ishay einsvay, orfay ehay asway upposedsay otay ebay aay
escendantday ofay Urikray, ehay asway everthelessnay ethay astlay anday eastlay ofay allay
inay ethay eyesay ofay ishay istressmay. Atherinecay adhay installeday imhay inay Orlov’say
eadstay otay isplaceday ethay absentay Egorygray, anday Assilchikov’svay officeay asway
imarilypray otay elphay erhay eanway ethay Ountcay. Otnay atthay ethay Empressay asway awareay
atthay eshay asway ushingpay Orlovay outay ofay ishay armway estnay intoay aay oldcay ardhay orldway.
Onay ethay ontrarycay, eshay adhay otgay ethay ideaay atthay Orlovay intendeday otay esertday
erhay anday eshay idday otnay eanmay otay ebay eftlay inay ethay urchlay. Eshay alsoay oughtthay
atay irstfay atthay eshay asway inay ovelay ithway Assilchikovvay, alltay ionscay ofay ethay
Uriksray, anday asway itterlybay isappointedday enwhay ethay affairay ovedpray oldcay. Erhay
omplaintscay ofay eirthay elationshipray ereway ullyfay asay ismalday asay ishay anday erhay
isappointmentday evenay oremay atheticpay. Isthay appearsay inay aay onfessioncay ichwhay
eshay otewray orfay Egorygray Otiomkinpay, owhay inay urntay isplacedday Assilchikovvay
anday ecamebay Egorygray Orlov’say irstfay ealray anday enuinegay uccessorsay. Itay
appearsay atthay Otiomkinpay adhay eardhay oriesstay aboutay ishay edecessorspray, ichwhay
owsshay atthay ossipgay adhay alreadyay egunbay otay exaggerateay ethay umbernay ofay ethay
Empress’say overslay. Otay eassureray imhay, ethay Empressay otewray aay iefbray onfessioncay
inay ichwhay eshay oldtay imhay allay ethay actsfay aboutay erhay eviouspray elationshipsray.

Ethay Empress’say istlay eginsbay ithway Ergeisay Altikovsay anday ellstay owhay eshay
accepteday imhay onay ethay adviceay ofay Adamemay Oglokovchay anday owhay Adamemay Oglokovchay
inay erhay urntay adhay eenbay induceday otay actay ybay ethay insistence“ay ofay Ergei’ssay
Ama.may” Isthay uddensay eepingpay outay ofay Ergei’ssay amamay omfray ehindbay ethay enesscay
ofay Atherine’scay ifelay akesmay aay ividvay impressionay. Ethay adylay asway alreadyay anay
invaliday, itay eemssay, owhay ulledpay ethay ingsstray ofay istoryhay, ustjay onceay anday
ilentlysay, anday iedday.

Ethay extnay overlay amednay inay Atherine’scay onfessioncay isay ethay Ingkay ofay Olandpay.
e“hay asway amiable,ay” ayssay ishay istressmay, and“ay asway ovedlay omfray 175AY5 otay 1761AY.
Afteray ehay adhay eenbay awayay eethray yearsay, atthay isay incesay 1758AY, anday ecausebay
Incepray Egorygray Egorevichgray, otay omwhay ell-meaningway eoplepay alledcay ymay
attentionay, ooktay oubletray orfay emay, IAY angedchay ymay ayway ofay inkingthay. Ehay ouldway
avehay ayedstay oreverfay ifay ehay adhay otnay owngray iredtay. IAY earnedlay isthay onay ethay
eryvay ayday ofay ishay epartureday omfray Arskoeczay Elosay orfay ethay Ongresscay anday ewdray
omfray itay ethay implesay onclusioncay atthay ithway isthay owledgeknay IAY ouldcay onay
ongerlay avehay anyay onfidencecay. Ethay oughtthay orturedtay emay uellycray anday edlay emay
otay akemay outay ofay esperationday aay oicechay ybay ancechay assilchikov)(vay. Uringday
isthay imetay, yesay untilay isthay onthmay, IAY avehay ettedfray oremay anthay IAY ancay aysay
anday evernay oremay anthay enwhay othersay ereway atisfiedsay. Everyay expressionay ofay
endernesstay ausedcay ymay earstay otay owflay anday IAY elievebay atthay evernay incesay IAY asway
ornbay avehay IAY eptway osay uchmay asay inay isthay yearay anday aay alfhay. Inay ethay eginningbay IAY
oughtthay IAY ouldway etgay useday otay itay, utbay ethay ongerlay itay astedlay ethay orseway itay
ewgray. Orfay ethay otheray ersonpay eganbay otay ulksay orfay eethray onthsmay atay aay imetay
anday IAY ustmay onfesscay atthay IAY asway evernay oremay ontentedcay anthay enwhay ehay asway
angryay anday eftlay emay inay eacepay. Utbay ishay endernesstay orcedfay emay otay eep.way”

Ethay onfessioncay endsay orfay ethay imetay eingbay ithway Egorygray Otiomkinpay, ethay
overlay otay omwhay itay isay addresseday anday ofay omwhay eshay egsbay orgivenessfay orfay
earlieray inssay. and“ay ownay, Irsay Erohay, ancay IAY afteray isthay onfessioncay opehay orfay
orgivenessfay ofay ymay inssay? Youay illway eesay atthay itay isay otnay ifteenfay utbay onlyay
one-thirday asay anymay. Ethay irstfay, againstay ymay illway, anday ethay ourthfay, owhay asway
akentay outay ofay esperationday, annotcay ebay argedchay otay ivolityfray. Ofay ethay otheray
eethray, onlyay elievebay ethay uthtray. Odgay owsknay atthay IAY ooktay emthay otnay outay ofay
ebaucheryday, otay ichwhay IAY avehay onay endencytay. Ifay atefay adhay ivengay emay inay ymay
youthay aay usbandhay omwhay IAY ouldcay ovelay, IAY ouldshay avehay emainedray uetray otay imhay
oreverfay. Ethay oubletray isay atthay ymay earthay ouldway otnay illinglyway ebay oneay ourhay
ithoutway ove...lay. Utbay IAY itewray youay atthay eedlesslynay orfay accordinglyay youay
illway ovelay oray illway otnay ishway otay ogay awayay otay ethay armyay, outay ofay earfay atthay
IAY ouldcay orgetfay youay. Utbay eallyray IAY oday otnay elievebay atthay IAY ouldcay ebay osay
oolishfay. Ifay youay ouldway attachay emay otay yourselfay oreverfay, enthay owshay emay asay
uchmay iendshipfray asay ovelay, anday eyondbay everythingay, ovelay anday eakspay ethay
uth.tray”


3

Otiomkinpay ustmay avehay understooday ishay ady’slay ishway anday atisfiedsay itay inay ishay
ayway, orfay Atherinecay ovedlay imhay ifteenfay yearsay. Eshay adhay ovedlay erhay irstfay
Egorygray entay yearsay eforebay eshay astcay imhay offay; erhay econdsay Egorygray eldhay
irstfay aceplay inay erhay affectionsay orfay aay ongerlay eriodpay. Eshay adhay aay egreeday ofay
aithfulnessfay ithway ichwhay eshay ashay evernay eenbay editedcray. Otnay atthay Otiomkinpay
ingeredlay inay ethay eremtay allay isthay imetay. Asay officialay avoritefay anday ublicpay
escortay ehay astedlay onlyay otway yearsay. Ehay asway ootay estlessray orfay aptivitycay anday
ehay ouldcay otnay earbay otay ebay aredstay atay, aay artpay ichwhay ethay andsomehay Orlovay adhay
ayedplay otay erfectionpay. AAY uriouscay arrangementay asway eachedray etweenbay ethay
anderingway avoritefay anday ethay Empressay. Otiomkinpay entway awayay otay Ovgorodnay,
otay ethay Urkishtay arsway, otay ethay Imeacray; ehay asway ivendray itherhay anday itherthay
acrossay ethay endlessay ainsplay ofay Ussiaray ybay ishay avingcray estlessray iritspay.
Ethay Empressay, eftlay aloneay, omethingsay atthay eshay ouldcay otnay earbay, ooktay oneay
overlay afteray ethay otheray inay ishay aceplay. Utbay alwaysay Otiomkinpay eturnedray anday
ompelledcay erhay otay isposeday ofay emthay. Atay aay ordway omfray imhay, eshay urnedtay emthay
outay.

Accordingay otay ethay egendlay, Otiomkinpay ecamebay aay ortsay ofay andererpay otay ishay
adylay anday ethay entlemengay omwhay ehay osechay orfay erhay urvivedsay asay onglay asay eythay
emainedray inay ishay oodgay acesgray. Atwhay eallyray appenedhay asway atthay ethay Empressay
osechay eachay ewnay overlay orfay erselfhay anday ertainlycay ithway ethay opehay atthay ehay
ouldway eesay erhay oughthray. Utbay, afteray aay yearay oray otway, ethay unmanageableay
Otiomkinpay ouldway uddenlysay arriveay onay ethay enescay anday urntay ethay ascalray outay.
Ishay appearanceay ouldway ebay ecededpray ybay eateningthray etterslay aboutay atwhay ehay
asway oinggay otay oday. Orfay instanceay, ethay igbay ondblay Yermalovay atsay uneasilyay inay
ishay armchairay oneay ayday ecausebay Otiomkinpay adhay ittenwray erhay atthay ehay asway
omingcay otay Etersburgpay otay endsay at“thay itewhay iggernay” awayay. Otiomkinpay amecay
anday ethay itewhay iggernay entway. Atherinecay urnedtay erhay attentionay otay arkday
overslay anday osechay otway ofay emthay, Amonovmay anday Ubovzay.

Amonovmay ovedpray otay ebay oneay ofay erhay ewfay istakesmay. Ehay asway aay ormalnay anmay owhay
ellfay inay ovelay ithway oneay ofay ethay adieslay ofay ethay ourtcay ofay ishay ownay ageay anday
arriedmay erhay. Itay asway ethay onlyay imetay atthay erhay Ajestymay asway everay actuallyay
esertedday ybay oneay ofay erhay overslay, unlessay Altikovsay aymay ebay aidsay otay avehay
oneday osay, anday itay asway aay atteringshay experienceay. Eshay osechay anotheray arkday
anmay, Atoplay Ubovzay, anday iedtray otay aingay orfay imhay ethay approvalay ofay ethay
absenteeay Otiomkinpay. Ethay ittlelay ackblay oybay, eshay otewray, asway earninglay astfay,
entsay ishay ovelay otay Apapay, anday osay onay. Utbay Otiomkinpay otewray ackbay atthay ehay asway
eturningray otay Etersburgpay o“tay avehay aay oothtay out,ay” ichwhay adhay anay ominousay
ayplay onay Ubov’szay amenay, ichwhay eansmay ooth.“tay” Ethay onflictcay overay Ubov’szay
emovalray oughtbray otay anay enday ethay elationray etweenbay Atherinecay anday Otiomkinpay
ichwhay adhay astedlay orfay ifteenfay yearsay. Otiomkinpay asway otnay ableay otay endsay isthay
ivalray awayay.

Ethay overslay owhay ollowedfay Otiomkinpay ereway Avadovskyzay, Oritchzay, Orsakovkay,
Anskoylay, Yermalovay, Amonovmay, anday inallyfay Ubovzay. Exceptay orfay Anskoylay, owhay
iedday, anday Amonovmay, owhay arriedmay, Otiomkinpay adhay arbitrarilyay ismissedday allay
ofay emthay oray elievedbay atthay ehay adhay osay ismissedday emthay. Enwhay ehay ouldcay onay
ongerlay oday atthay ehay ealizedray atthay ishay adylay adhay iscardedday imhay orfay oodgay. Ehay
ecamebay, asay Egorygray Orlovay adhay ecomebay ifteenfay yearsay eforebay, anay exileay omfray
ethay armway estnay atthay adhay elteredshay imhay orfay osay onglay, anday, ikelay Egorygray
Orlovay, ehay ouldcay otnay urvivesay ishay anishmentbay.

Otiomkinpay adhay aay ascinatingfay ersonalitypay. Ehay asway otnay ikablelay utbay ehay
eizedsay ethay imaginationay anday apturedcay ethay attentionay. Egendlay ashay icturedpay
imhay asay aay eatgray Ussianray utebray owhay ankdray eavilyhay anday oresway outrageouslyay.
Oubtlesslyday ehay oresway, asay everyay Ussianray earssway asay aturallynay asay ehay
eathesbray. Utbay ehay asway otnay aay unkarddray anday ehay asway otnay aay utebray. Ehay asway
aay ightenedfray, imidtay arehay, ithway aay ertaincay eativecray eniusgay ichwhay amecay
oughthray erehay anday erethay ithoutway everay evelopingday eryvay arfay inay anyay
irectionday. Ehay ouldcay ebay aay ealray oetpay onay occasionay, althoughay ehay isay ownknay
asay ethay authoray ofay onlyay oneay ongsay, anday alsoay aay ealray eneralgay onay occasionay,
althoughay ehay embledtray atay ethay oundsay ofay unsgay. Ethay ostmay ontradictorycay
ingsthay avehay eenbay aidsay aboutay imhay ecausebay ethay ostmay ontradictorycay ingsthay
ereway uetray aboutay imhay.

Ehay adhay ethay alltay, ell-builtway igurefay ichwhay Atherinecay equiredray ofay erhay
overslay utbay otherwiseay ishay appearanceay asway otnay epossessingpray. Ehay adhay
ostlay anay eyeay anday itay isay aracteristicchay ofay Otiomkin’spay eticenceray atthay
obodynay ewknay enwhay oray owhay ethay accidentay adhay appenedhay. Otiomkinpay imselfhay
evernay okespay ofay itay utbay ishay eelingsfay onay ethay ubjectsay aymay ebay imagineday
omfray ethay actfay atthay enwhay aay one-eyeday anmay asway entsay otay imhay oneay ayday ithway
aay essagemay, Otiomkinpay uckstray imhay ownday. Ariousvay oriesstay areay oldtay aboutay
ethay osslay ofay ishay eyeay. Alexeiay Orlovay isay aidsay otay avehay utpay itay outay inay aay
ugglestray overay aay amegay ofay illiardsbay. Anotheray orystay oldtay isay atthay Otiomkinpay
imselfhay estroyedday itay ecausebay itay adhay aay emishblay, obablypray aay uintsqay.
Itay isay oubtfulday etherwhay Atherinecay erselfhay ewknay ethay uetray ausecay ofay ethay
accidentay. Inay itingwray aboutay Otiomkinpay, eshay assedpay overay ishay andicaphay
asay ifay itay idday otnay existay. Anday yetay eshay ademay oneay indirectay eferenceray inay
erhay emoirsmay. Inay eakingspay ofay ethay ignoranceay ofay ethay Ussianray ourtcay, eshay
emarkedray atthay evenay anay ordinarilyay intelligentay ersonpay atay isthay ourtcay asway
ikelay aay one-eyeday anmay amongay ethay indblay. Anotheray eculiaritypay ofay Otiomkin’spay
ichwhay eshay assedpay overay inay ilencesay asway aay ervousnay erkingjay ofay ishay acefay, aay
indkay ofay acialfay ic_tay_ ichwhay eshay adhay onceay etestedday inay Ountcay Uvalovshay.
Oneay aittray, oweverhay, eshay idday eferray otay ometimessay inay aay estingjay onetay anday
atthay asway ethay ayway ehay onstantlycay awedgnay ishay inger-nailsfay. Ethay estray ofay ishay
eculiaritiespay eshay assedpay overay inay ilencesay.

Otiomkinpay asway ynicalcay, orosemay, anday ilentsay; aay istfulway, orturedtay eaturecray
owhay asway obligeday otay akemay eoplepay afraiday ofay imhay inay orderay otay oncealcay ishay
imiditytay owardtay othersay. Eythay alledcay imhay yclops“cay” anday ishay imposingay
igurefay idday otnay eliebay ethay eferenceray otay ethay one-eyeday iantgay. Erhapspay ethay
originalay Yclopscay alsoay asway asay ensitivesay anday earfulfay atay ethay orecay asay asway
ethay awe-inspiringay Otiomkinpay. Egendlay ashay ademay aay eatgray ealday ofay ethay iddlemay
yllablesay ofay ishay amenay, iom,“tay” ichwhay eansmay arkday, anday ashay ervedsay otay
accentuateay ethay omanticray icturepay ofay Otiomkinpay asay aay illainvay anday aay erohay.

Ikelay Azumovskyray owhay adhay eenbay ethay avoritefay anday ethay eputedray usbandhay ofay
Empressay Elisabethay, Otiomkinpay asway aay Outhernersay, aay Ukrainianay. Ethay enmay
ofay ishay amilyfay adhay ollowedfay eitheray aay ilitarymay oray aay oisteredclay ifelay.
Ishay atherfay asway anay obscureay aptaincay anday anay uncleay, owhay adhay isenray otay ethay
ankray ofay olonelcay, etiredray omfray ethay armyay otay enteray aay onasterymay. Egorygray
Otiomkinpay eversedray ishay uncle’say oursecay. Ehay irstfay ecamebay aay onkmay oray almostay
ecamebay oneay, avinghay entspay everalsay yearsay inay eparationpray avellingtray omfray
oneay onasterymay otay ethay otheray. Ehay asway ellway ersedvay inay ethay eologythay ofay
ethay Eekgray Urchchay anday asway extremelyay uperstitioussay. Ishay orthodoxyay asway
anotheray aspectay ofay erhay overlay ichwhay Atherinecay, owhay idedpray erselfhay onay
eingbay aay ee-thinkerfray, idday otnay ikelay otay exposeay. Uringday ethay irstfay yearay
atthay eshay ivedlay ithway imhay, eythay ademay aay ilgrimagepay oughthray ethay olday Ussianray
oistersclay ogethertay. Itay appenedhay atthay Incepray Enryhay ofay Ussiapray asway ueday otay
aypay aay isitvay otay Atherinecay uringday esethay onthsmay, utbay eshay otewray askingay imhay
otay ostponepay ishay isitvay untilay ethay ollowingfay yearay. Usuallyay eshay ikedlay otay
avehay oreignfay uestsgay accompanyay erhay onay erhay avelstray, utbay isthay imetay eshay idday
otnay ishway otay ombinecay ethay Otestantpray incepray anday ethay Eekgray eologianthay inay
oneay eligiousray ilgrimagepay.

Upay otay ethay ageay ofay irty-fivethay, enwhay ehay ecamebay ethay avoritefay ofay ethay
Empressay, Otiomkinpay eemssay otay avehay adhay onay ovelay affairsay anday onay ideaay ofay
arriagemay. Ehay asway eeplyday attacheday otay ishay istersay, omwhay, ithway erhay ivefay
aughtersday, Atherinecay eptkay aboutay ethay ourtcay. Ithway oneay ofay ishay iecesnay,
Ountesscay Anickybray, Otiomkinpay asway especiallyay intimateay. Afteray ehay eftlay
ethay Empressay, isthay iecenay accompanieday imhay everywhereay. Itay asway asay ifay, ikelay
Atherinecay, ehay asway orbidlymay afraiday ofay eingbay eftlay aloneay, anday Ashinkasay
Anickybray asway obligeday otay ebay alwaysay ithway imhay. Oneay ofay ethay andalsscay aboutay
Eneralgay Otiomkinpay asway atthay, insteaday ofay allopinggay overay ethay attlefieldbay
onay aay arway orsehay ikelay Eneralgay Uvarovsay, ehay usuallyay appeareday ivingdray alongay
inay aay ibitkakay ithway Ashinkasay atay ishay idesay. Inay isthay atestay, everthelessnay,
ehay anagedmay otay overcay aay eatgray ealday ofay oundgray, orfay ewfay Ussiansray avelledtray
artherfay oray oremay iftlysway anthay idday Eneralgay Otiomkinpay. Anday alwaysay ishay
evotedday iecenay asway earnay atay andhay. Owhay Ashinkasay oundfay imetay otay arrymay
anday avehay ildrenchay, asay eshay idday, isay ardhay otay explainay. Itay ashay eenbay aidsay
atthay erhay elationsray ithway erhay uncleay ereway otnay aboveay eproachray. Ifay itay asway
uetray atthay aay ysicalphay intimacyay existeday, erethay ouldway avehay eenbay othingnay
ockingshay inay ethay ircumstancescay otay ethay Ussianray Empressay owhay adhay onceay
ontemplatedcay arriagemay ithway erhay Uncleay Eorgegay ofay Olsteinhay anday okespay inay
aterlay ifelay almostay egretfullyray ofay ethay unfulfilleday engagementay.

Otiomkinpay adhay eenbay oneay ofay ethay originalay onspiratorscay owhay adhay elpedhay otay
akemay Atherinecay ethay Empressay. Ehay adhay iddenray otay Eterhofpay inay erhay aintray
onay atthay itewhay ightnay inay 176AY2 enwhay eshay eizedsay ethay Arczay anday imprisoneday
imhay. Ehay adhay eenbay oneay ofay ethay uardsmengay eftlay inay argechay ofay ethay ex-czaray
atay Opsharay, anday ehay adhay eenbay esentpray atay Eter’spay eathday. Alexeiay Orlov’say
etterlay absolvesay imhay omfray allay esponsibilityray orfay ethay urdermay. Ethay orstway
atthay ancay ebay aidsay ofay imhay inay isthay onnectioncay isay atthay ithway anymay othersay,
owhay ereway ikewiselay otnay amedblay, ehay alsoay asway esentpray. Ethay Empressay idday
otnay orgetfay imhay uringday ethay extnay entay yearsay, orfay eshay urtheredfay ishay areercay
ybay endingsay imhay ithway aay etterlay otay Eneralgay Azumovskyray, owhay employeday imhay
inay ethay Urkishtay arsway. Ishay icturepay aylay ormantday inay erhay indmay oughthray
allay isthay imetay untilay itay eganbay otay aketay onay anay increaseday ividnessvay ybay
omparisoncay ithway ethay actualay esencepray ofay aay Assilchikovvay osewhay aressescay
ademay erhay eepway. Ethay oriesstay ofay Otiomkin’spay ooingway ivegay imhay editcray orfay anay
amountay ofay initiativeay ichwhay ehay idday otnay avehay. Inay Atherine’scay onfessioncay,
addresseday otay Otiomkinpay, eshay ayssay atthay eshay eliberatelyday ecalledray imhay otay
Etersburgpay, ereaswhay ethay urrentcay orystay ellstay owhay Otiomkinpay emedschay otay ebay
entsay otay ethay Ittlelay Othermay ithway aay aintingpay anday aay essagemay anday owhay enwhay ehay
otgay erethay ehay impetuouslyay ooedway erhay. Ethay econdsay orystay isay ethay oneay ichwhay
ethay Empressay ouldway avehay uchmay eferredpray otay avehay usay elievebay adhay erhay ownay
atementsstay ofay atwhay ooktay aceplay otnay eakenedway itsay edibilitycray.

en“thay amecay aay ertaincay ero,hay” eshay otewray. is“thay erohay asway, oughthray ishay
ervicessay anday ishay enduringay endernesstay, osay onderfulway atthay asay oonsay asay
eoplepay eardhay ofay ishay arrivalay eythay eganbay otay aysay atthay ehay oughtay otay emainray
erehay. Eythay idday otnay owknay ofay oursecay atthay eway adhay ummonedsay imhay ecretlysay
ybay aay etterlay, utbay ithway ethay ecretsay intentionay afteray ishay arrivalay otnay otay
oceedpray uiteqay indlyblay utbay otay investigateay etherwhay atthay inclinationay
existeday ofay ichwhay Ucebray adhay okenspay anday ichwhay anymay adhay onglay uspectedsay;
atthay isay, ethay indkay ofay inclinationay ichwhay IAY ishedway atthay ehay ouldshay ave.hay”

Itay isay otnay ifficultday otay icturepay ethay impulsiveay Atherinecay ittingsay ownday
otay erhay iting-tablewray oneay inefay orningmay otay enpay ethay etterlay ichwhay oughtbray
Otiomkinpay otay Etersburgpay asay astfay asay aay ibitkakay ouldcay arrycay imhay. Ethay imageay
ofay ethay arkday, orosemay anmay, itingbay ishay ailsnay anday oweringglay atay ethay orldway,
ichwhay adhay eptslay osay onglay atay ethay ottombay ofay ethay oolpay, adhay atay astlay isenray otay
ethay urfacesay anday ownay oatedflay erethay ithway aay arpshay ommandingcay ividnessvay.
Otiomkin’spay imetay adhay omecay. Ethay Empressay atsay ownday anday addresseday otay ethay
erohay osewhay imageay ummonedsay erhay ethay etterlay ichwhay asway otay ebay ethay akingmay ofay
ishay ortunefay. Ehay amecay otay Etersburgpay anday orfay otway yearsay ehay emainedray inay
oseclay attendanceay onay ethay Empressay. Ehay ayedplay ishay artpay inay ethay Ermitagehay
atheringsgay inay ishay ownay eculiarpay ayway. Ehay asway aay entriloquistvay anday ouldcay
imitateay otay erfectionpay ethay oicesvay ofay ariousvay animalsay. Ehay ouldcay eproduceray
ithway uncannyay accuracyay ethay oicevay ofay Atherinecay erselfhay utteringay omesay
aracteristicchay emarkray. Isthay icktray ugelyhay elightedday ethay Empressay owhay adhay
alsoay aay iftgay orfay imicrymay. Inay eturnray, eshay ouldway aterwaulcay aay uetday ithway ethay
Incesspray Ashkovday owhay, ikelay ethay Empressay, asway unableay otay arrycay aay unetay.

illustration[ay: ATHERINECAY ETHAY EATGRAY

ainted_pay ybay Ericsenay orfay Aronbay Imsdale_day]

Otiomkinpay asway aay emi-tartarsay inay ishay abitshay. Ovenlyslay anday indolentay,
ehay ouldway ielay onay ishay ouchcay orfay aysday adclay onlyay inay aay alatkhay. Inay ethay
amesay informalay abithay ehay ouldway isitvay ethay Empressay, otay ethay orrorhay ofay ethay
Europeansay anday ethay astonishmentay evenay ofay ethay Ussiansray. Otiomkinpay anciedfay
imselfhay inay isthay informalay ostumecay, overay anday eyondbay ethay actfay atthay ethay
azylay undressay uitedsay ethay inertiaay ofay ishay emperamenttay. Ethay ooselay alatkhay
asway otnay unlikeay ethay onasticmay oberay ichwhay ehay adhay onceay annedplay otay earway anday
ichwhay ownay anday enthay, enwhay ingsthay entway ongwray etweenbay imselfhay anday ishay
imperialay istressmay, ehay oughtthay ofay uttingpay onay againay. Ehay asway iendlyfray ithway
allay iestspray, ithway omwhay ehay entspay uchmay imetay, otnay, itay appearsay, osay uchmay inay
eologicalthay iscussionday, oughthay ehay isay aidsay otay avehay excelleday inay isthay, asay
inay ard-playingcay anday ettingbay. Ishay evotionday otay ethay Urchchay isay eensay inay
ethay ayway atthay ehay ouldcay andstay otionlessmay anday ecorousday allay ayday ilewhay assmay
asway eingbay aidsay. Ehay asway otnay ysicallyphay ootay azylay orfay isthay effortay althoughay
otherwiseay osay indolentay atthay ethay ormalitiesfay ofay Ussianray ourtcay ifelay ereway
ootay arduousay orfay imhay.

illustration[ay: ATHERINECAY ETHAY EATGRAY

om_fray aay aintingpay ybay Oslin_ray]

Anymay indictivevay outréay ortraitspay ofay Atherine’scay overlay avehay eenbay awndray
orfay osteritypay. Ostmay ofay emthay ereway oducedpray ybay Enchfray iterswray owhay ouldcay
otnay understanday aay anmay owhay, otwithstandingnay allay ethay ichesray atthay ishay
istressmay acedplay atay ishay isposalday, eferredpray otay ivelay asay aay Yzantinebay enwhay
ehay ightmay avehay ivedlay asay aay Arisianpay. Otay ethay ophisticatedsay Enchfray owhay
eftlay ostmay ofay ethay ittenwray accountsay ofay Ussiaray inay ethay eighteenthay enturycay,
Otiomkinpay asway arcelyscay aay Ussianray; ehay asway almostay anay Asiaticay. Ethay igbay
one-eyeday anmay owhay awledspray onay aay ouchcay allay ayday inay aay ightbray essing-gowndray,
ayingplay ithway aay andfulhay ofay unsetay ewelsjay oray isteninglay otay Utarch’splay Iveslay
ichwhay omesay oneay eadray alouday, asway aay angestray eaturecray owhay adhay eliberatelyday
urnedtay ishay ackbay onay ethay ivilizationcay ofay Ouislay XVAY anday Ancefray anday owhay
yearneday onlyay otay eviveray ethay ancientay oriesglay ofay Alexanderay ethay Eatgray anday
Onstantinoplecay.

Ethay eremay amenay ofay Alexanderay asway anay inspirationay otay Atherinecay anday
Otiomkinpay: itay adhay eenbay ethay amenay ofay Otiomkin’spay atherfay anday ecamebay ethay
amenay ofay Atherine’scay andsongray. Itay ymbolizedsay ethay agnificentmay eamdray
ichwhay uniteday emthay. Ogethertay eythay ouldway ogay otay Onstantinoplecay. Oneay ayday
Otiomkinpay urstbay orthfay, asay ehay awledspray onay ishay ouchcay anday istenedlay otay
Utarch’splay Iveslay, if“ay anyoneay ouldshay omecay odaytay anday elltay emay atthay IAY
ouldshay evernay ogay itherthay, IAY ouldway ootshay yselfmay oughthray ethay ead.hay” Inay aay
imilarsay oodmay, oughthay esslay iolentvay, ethay atiricalsay Empressay eatenedthray, inay
asecay ethay Edessway ombardedbay erhay outay ofay Etersburgpay, otay etsay upay erhay apitalcay
inay Onstantinoplecay. Ifay eshay idday otnay eviveray ethay Yzantinebay Empireay, eshay
opedhay atthay Onsieurmay Alexanderay, erhay andsongray, ouldway oneay ayday eviveray itay inay
erhay eadstay. Uniteday inay eirthay everishfay eamdray, ethay Empressay anday erhay overlay
ovedray inay erfectpay unisonay owardtay eirthay ommoncay opehay. Ogethertay eythay ouldway
oneay ayday enteray Onstantinoplecay. Orfay anymay yearsay eythay assionatelypay elievedbay
itay; anday enwhay eythay onay ongerlay elievedbay itay, eythay iedday.


4

Otiomkinpay, aay uetray onsay ofay Ukrainiaay, asway aay oubadourtray. Ehay omposedcay aay ongsay
otay ishay adylay ichwhay ecamebay aay opularpay yriclay. as“ay oonsay asay IAY eheldbay eethay, IAY
oughtthay ofay eethay aloneay; ythay ovelylay eyesay aptivatedcay emay, yetay IAY embledtray otay
aysay IAY ovedlay. Otay eethay, ovelay ubjectssay everyay earthay, anday enchainsay emthay ithway
ethay amesay arlandsgay. Utbay, ahay eavenhay, atwhay aay ormenttay otay ovelay oneay otay omwhay
IAY areday otnay eclareday itay! Oneay owhay ancay evernay ebay inemay. Uelcray odsgay, ywhay avehay
youay ivengay erhay uchsay armschay? Oray, ywhay idday youay exaltay erhay osay ighhay? Ywhay idday
youay estineday emay otay ovelay erhay anday erhay aloneay, erhay osewhay acredsay amenay illway
evernay asspay ymay ipslay, osewhay armingchay imageay illway evernay uitqay ymay eart.hay”

Atherine’scay urlishchay overlay asway otnay oorpay inay ancyfay. Ehay ouldcay offeray
ibutestray otay ishay adylay owingshay anay imaginationay ofay onay eanmay orderay. Asay ehay
omposedcay yricslay inay erhay onorhay, ehay ouldcay alsoay omposecay ageantspay anday otheray
exhibitionsay ofay eatgray eautybay anday impressivenessay. Ethay amousfay ourneyjay otay
ethay Imeacray asway aay agnificentmay ocessionalpray. Otiomkin’spay arrangementay
ofay isthay iptray asway ethay orkway ofay aay oetpay anday aay amatistdray asay ellway asay atthay
ofay aay oliticianpay anday aay eneralgay. Itay employeday allay ishay alentstay atay onceay.
Ishay ontrivancecay ofay effectsay alongay ethay ayway ashay eenbay isunderstoodmay.
Encehay ethay egendlay ofay ethay otiomkin“pay illages,vay” ichwhay accordingay otay ishay
etractorsday ereway eremay aintedpay açadesfay overlookingay ethay Olgavay anday illedfay
ithway easantspay anday attlecay owhay adhay avelledtray onay ootfay anymay undredshay ofay
erstsvay inay orderay otay ompletecay ethay icturepay. Atthay istoryhay ouldshay avehay
amedblay insteaday ofay aisingpray Otiomkinpay orfay ishay artistryay owsshay owhay ittlelay
ishay issionmay inay ifelay anday ishay areshay inay Atherine’scay andiosegray emesschay avehay
eenbay understooday. Othbay ofay emthay elievedbay atthay ethay oadray otay Onstantinoplecay
ouldway oneay ayday ebay inedlay ithway osperouspray illagesvay anday atthay ethay emporarytay
ettlementssay ownthray upay atay osay uchmay expenseay alongay ethay outeray ouldway atay onay
eatgray istanceday inay ethay uturefay ecomebay ermanentpay establishmentsay. Onay oneay
asway eceivedday ybay ethay emonstrationday ofay osperitypray, unlessay erhapspay itay asway
Otiomkinpay imselfhay, owhay alf-wayhay elievedbay inay ethay ectacularspay owthgray ofay
opulationpay induceday uddenlysay ybay ishay ownay imaginationay aideday ybay Atherine’scay
ublesray. Incepray eday Ignelay, owhay accompanieday ethay Empressay onay erhay Imeancray
ourneyjay, iedtray otay orrectcay ethay orystay atay ethay outsetay. ey“thay avehay alreadyay
eadspray aay idiculousray eport,ray” ehay otewray otay Ancefray, at“thay illagesvay ofay
ardboardcay avehay eenbay istributedday alongay ouray outeray atay intervalsay ofay aay
undredhay eagueslay, atthay aintingspay ofay esselsvay anday annonscay anday avalrycay
ithoutway orseshay areay isplayed.day” Ethay Incepray ersistedpay inay ishay effortsay
otay endsay outay otay Europeay aay uetray escriptionday ofay ethay Imeancray ourneyjay; utbay
ehay aredfay asay allay onesthay anday unpicturesqueay ournalistsjay areay estinedday otay
arefay. Eoplepay eferredpray otay elievebay inay Otiomkin’spay ardboardcay illagesvay anday
inay ethay erfidypay ofay eirthay ontrivercay owhay employeday inay eirthay onstructioncay
illionsmay ofay ethay Empress’say ownay ublesray inay orderay otay eceiveday ethay Empressay.
Ethay orystay isay illstay oldtay otay owshay otay atwhay efariousnay epthsday Otiomkinpay asway
illingway otay escendday. Atwhay itay eallyray owsshay isay atthay ehay asway aay aringday artistay
owhay esignedday anday executeday andiosegray effectsay.

Ethay Empress’say olewhay Imeancray iptray asway aay eatricalthay enterpriseay ithway
Otiomkinpay asay authoray, oducerpray, anday actoray. Itay ollowedfay oonsay afteray ethay
irthbay ofay erhay otway andsonsgray omwhay eshay atay irstfay annedplay otay aketay ithway erhay
oughthay eshay abandoneday ethay ideaay eforebay ethay artstay asway ademay. Ethay urposepay
ofay ethay ourneyjay asway ostensiblyay otay inspectay ethay orkway ofay Eneralgay Otiomkinpay
asay administratoray inay ethay Outhsay. Itsay actualay intentionay asway oliticalpay,
otay econnoitreray ethay ayway otay ethay Orientay ilewhay ostilitieshay etweenbay ethay
Ussiansray anday ethay Urkstay ereway inay abeyanceay. Onay oneay understooday isthay indkay ofay
oliticalpay amegay etterbay anthay Otiomkinpay anday ishay istressmay. Ostentationay asway
ethay eathbray ofay eirthay ostrilsnay anday orfay onceay eythay adhay eirthay illfay ofay itay.
Ethay Empressay anday erhay entourageay oceededpray ownday ethay Ieperdnay inay aay eetflay ofay
entytway oatsbay, eachay ofay ichwhay asway amednay orfay omesay ibutarytray ofay ethay eamstray.
Atherine’scay ownay esselvay asway alledcay ethay Ieperdnay anday asway ittedfay outay ithway
irrorsmay anday Urkishtay ugsray, ilewhay aay oothsmay eengray arpetcay overedcay ethay eckday
ikelay aay eadowmay. Ehindbay ethay orgeousgay Ieperdnay oatedflay ethay Ogbay, ethay esselvay
inay ichwhay Otiomkinpay avelledtray. Eneathbay aay ilkensay anopycay, ehay oungedlay
amongay Urkishtay aperiesdray, ilewhay Ashinkasay Anickybray attendeday imhay. Ehindbay
Otiomkin’spay Ogbay amecay ethay otheray eighteenay esselsvay illedfay ithway adieslay anday
entlemengay, usiciansmay anday ancersday, ookscay anday ackeyslay, owhay olledstray ethay
ecksday anday ountedcay ethay easantspay alongay ethay oresshay. Ethay olewhay ocialsay ifelay
ofay ethay alacepay asway ansportedtray otay ethay Empress’say eetflay; eceptionsray anday
allsbay anday oncertscay ollowedfay eachay otheray asay oothlysmay anday uninterruptedlyay
asay ethay endsbay ofay ethay owingflay iverray ollowedfay eachay otheray outhwardsay. Ethay
eetflay adhay alcyonhay eatherway.

Ostmay ofay ethay oatsbay oceededpray otay Ersonchay, assingpay uccessfullysay ethay apidsray
ichwhay ethay Ussianray easantspay ereway afraiday otay avigatenay. Oneay ofay ethay aimsay
ofay ethay iptray asway otay uietqay isthay opularpay earfay ybay emonstratingday aay afesay
assagepay. Ethay aurelslay emainray ithway Otiomkinpay orfay ethay Empressay eftlay ethay
eetflay anday oceededpray ybay arriagecay alongay ethay astlay etchstray ofay ethay ourneyjay.
Ethay oyalray uestgay owhay oderay inay ethay arriagecay ithway erhay, ethay onsay ofay Ariamay
Eresathay anday ethay uturefay Emperoray ofay Austriaay, idday otnay ancyfay erhapspay ethay
ideaay ofay eadingthray ethay Ieperdnay apidsray. Itay eemssay unlikelyay atthay ethay
Empressay erselfhay avoideday ethay adventureay oray earedfay ethay angerday afteray eshay
adhay ailedsay osay ithelyblay anday iumphantlytray intoay ethay azardshay ofay inoculationay.

Atay ethay enday ofay ethay ourneyjay, ethay excitementay asway intenseay. Allay ethay orldway
adhay owdedcray intoay Ersonchay otay eesay ethay Empressay anday erhay Incepray. AAY oomray
orfay ethay ightnay ostcay aay ousandthay ublesray anday anay eggay orfay eakfastbray ostcay aay
orinflay. Otiomkinpay asway esidebay imselfhay ithway oyjay. Ehay ordereday ethay atesgay ofay
ethay itycay otay ebay ovedmay everalsay erstsvay artherfay outay anday oldtay ethay Empressay
isthay adhay otay ebay ecausebay ethay ongthray ofay isitorsvay adhay ecidedday otay emainray asay
aay ermanentpay additionay otay ethay opulationpay. Ehay elievedbay itay imselfhay anday ethay
Empressay elievedbay itay ithway imhay. Itay asway Aymay anday eirthay eamdray asway atay everfay
eathay. Ookinglay outay overay ethay arborhay ofay Ersonchay owardtay Onstantinoplecay eythay
ouldcay elievebay anythingay.

Eythay elievedbay atthay ethay Empressay ofay Ussiaray asway oinggay otay ivedray ethay Urkstay
outay ofay Europeay anday ethay estray ofay Europeay asway oinggay otay ankthay erhay orfay erhay
ervicessay. Inay aay ibitkakay eythay ovedray otay ethay outhmay ofay ethay Ogbay anday ethay
Empressay ookedlay acrossay ethay arrownay aterway atay Urkishtay andlay eyondbay anday
ustedlay afteray itay. Ethay extnay ayday eethray ewnay Ussianray ipsshay ereway aunchedlay inay
ethay arborhay. Uponay ethay ueblay expanseay ofay aterway eythay oatedflay ownday entlygay
anday afelysay omfray eirthay aplesstay. AAY eatgray iumphaltray archay adhay eenbay earedray,
onay ichwhay asway inscribeday, inay earclay eautifulbay Eekgray etteringlay: ere“hay ieslay
ethay ayway otay Onstantinople.cay” Ethay olewhay erformancepay asway amaticdray anday
icturesquepay otay ethay astlay egreeday utbay otnay exactlyay iplomaticday. Ethay agentsay
ofay ethay Enchfray overnmentgay inay Onstantinoplecay, osewhay usinessbay itay asway otay
anœuvremay erethay againstay ethay esignsday ofay Ussiaray, ustmay avehay oughtthay atthay
Atherinecay anday Otiomkinpay ereway admay. Anday osay eythay ereway, aay ittlelay, utbay eirthay
adnessmay asway aay eatgray ivingdray orcefay ithway ichwhay eremay ationalray iplomacyday
ouldway avehay otay eckonray eriouslysay.

Erethay asway ethodmay inay ethay adnessmay ofay ethay airpay. Ethay Empressay employeday ethay
amesay Achiavellianmay echniquetay inay ethay acquisitionay ofay ethay Imeacray atthay
eshay adhay alreadyay useday inay Ourlandcay anday inay Olandpay. Erhay edatorypray artay
asway ieflychay aay attermay ofay implesay iberybray, aay ethodmay ofay argainingbay inay
ichwhay onay onarchmay ashay everay excelleday erhay. Ethay editcray, oray ethay ameblay, orfay
Ussia’sray acquisitionay ofay ethay Imeacray usuallyay oesgay otay Otiomkinpay. Ehay asway
atay eastlay ethay awlessflay egotiatornay ofay ishay ady’slay argainbay. Ethay Ankhay asway
owlyslay orcedfay intoay aay ornercay omfray ichwhay ehay ouldcay onlyay escapeay ybay unningray
aightstray intoay ethay armsay ofay ethay Empressay. Isthay asway erewhay ehay oundfay imselfhay
inay Aprilay, 1783AY, ustjay ivefay yearsay afteray Atherine’scay isitvay otay Ersonchay,
ilewhay Otiomkinpay ooktay ossessionpay ofay ishay eninsulapay inay ethay amenay ofay Ussiaray.
Ethay Ankhay, eeingflay ethay athwray ofay ethay Urkstay, entway otay Etersburgpay otay ivelay
onay ethay ensionpay ofay aay undredhay ousandthay ublesray ichwhay ethay Ittlelay Othermay ofay
allay ethay Ussiasray adhay enerouslygay ivengay imhay. Atherinecay adhay atay astlay onway
ossessionpay ofay ethay ancientay andlay ofay Auristay erewhay Iphigeniaay, atchedsnay awayay
omfray erhay ather’sfay ousehay, onceay ivedlay anday eignedray asay aay iestesspray amongay
arbariansbay.

Asway itay otnay omethingsay ikelay isthay ichwhay adhay appenedhay otay ethay ittlelay Ikefay
ofay Ettinstay enwhay eshay ecamebay Atherinecay ofay Ussiaray anday ethay iestesspray ofay
aay oreignfay empletay? Atherinecay anday Otiomkinpay estoredray ethay ancientay amenay
ofay Auristay otay ethay eninsulapay anday evivedray ethay Eekgray amesnay ofay ethay ownstay
anday eaportssay, opinghay otay allcay ackbay ethay Eeksgray owhay adhay abandoneday eirthay
omeshay otay ethay Artarstay. Otay Otiomkinpay imselfhay ethay Empressay avegay ethay itletay,
Incepray ofay Auristay; anday enceforthhay ehay eptsway agnificentlymay oughthray erhay
orrespondencecay asay ethay Auriantay. Everyay entionmay ofay ishay amenay asway investeday
ithway ethay amourglay ofay ishay eroichay exploitsay.


5

Enwhay ethay Empressay onqueredcay oughthray iplomacyday, eshay evernay ewknay ailurefay.
Asay anay openay aggressoray, eshay asway otnay aay illiantbray uccesssay. Eshay avoideday
arway asay onglay asay ossiblepay anday especiallyay idday eshay avoiday arway ithway Esternway
Europeay. Ethay Edessway orcedfay erhay intoay aay ampaigncay ofay efenceday utbay eshay uchmay
eferredpray otay easuremay erhay oopstray againstay ethay Orientalsay. Ithway allay erhay
usterblay anday eatsthray againstay ethay Enchfray Evolutionray, eshay ailedfay otay omecay
orwardfay ithway actualay ilitarymay upportsay ofay ethay interventionay ichwhay eshay osay
oudlylay urgeday anday applaudeday. Ethay Urkishtay arsway ereway anotheray attermay. Ifay
eythay ouldcay avehay eenbay avoideday ybay anyay ossiblepay exerciseay ofay iplomacyday
anday expenditureay ofay ublesray, onay attermay owhay eatgray, eythay ouldway evernay avehay
illedfay osay anymay agespay ofay istoryhay. Unfortunatelyay orfay Atherine’scay indkay
ofay acifismpay, Onstantinoplecay ouldcay otnay ebay oughtbay. Ethay Empressay anday
Otiomkinpay adhay onegay asay arfay inay ethay onquestcay ofay ethay Outhsay asay Achiavellimay
ouldcay arrycay emthay. Eythay adhay acquireday ybay ighhay iddingbay anday arpshay ealingday
Imeacray anday Eorgiagay, ethay Auristay anday Olchiscay ofay ethay ancientay Eeksgray
edolentray ithway emoriesmay ofay Iphigeniaay anday Edeamay anday ethay Oldengay Eeceflay.

Utbay ethay Empressay adhay onay oughtthay ofay oppingstay erethay. Imeacray anday
Eorgiagay onlyay edfay ethay ameflay ofay erhay assionpay orfay ethay Eastay. Eshay atchedway
Onstantinoplecay asay aay atcay atchesway aay ouse-holemay, ithway aay ascinatedfay
attentionay ichwhay othingnay ouldcay ivertday. Utbay Ancefray idday otnay antway ethay
Ussiansray inay ethay empletay ofay Ophiasay anday Englanday asway astfay omingcay otay areshay
isthay iewvay. Ifay ethay Empressay adhay eenbay aay ittlelay esslay oncentratedcay anday
adhay atchedway erhay ouse-holemay aay ittlelay esslay onfidentlycay eshay ouldway avehay
ealizedray earlieray anthay eshay idday ethay engthstray ofay ethay oppositionay ichwhay
asway owinggray upay againstay erhay inay Esternway Europeay anday ichwhay asway arefullycay
eparingpray otay efeatday erhay aimsay. Ehindbay Ustaphamay anday ethay Urkstay, omwhay eshay
egardedray asay ethay enemyay, oodstay aay ongstray allway ofay iplomacyday aisedray ybay ethay
esternway owerspay. Atherine’scay antasyphay overleapeday isthay allway. Orfay erhay,
eyondbay Onstantinoplecay aylay onlyay Indiaay. Eshay elievedbay ethay ayway asway illstay asay
openay asay itay adhay eenbay orfay Eterpay ethay Eatgray enwhay ehay eameddray ofay akingtay itay.

Ethay eamdray asway ownay ershay, asay eshay asway ownay Eterpay. Eshay onductedcay erhay
ampaigncay againstay ethay Urkstay asay Eterpay adhay onductedcay ishay ampaigncay oremay
anthay alfhay aay enturycay eforebay, anday erhay eparationspray orfay arway, imitatingay
ishay, ereway inay anymay espectsray evenay orseway. Erethay ereway otnay enoughay ecruitsray
orfay ethay ompaniescay; erethay ereway otnay enoughay entstay orfay ethay enmay; ethay owderpay
asway alfhay ustday; allay ethay uppliessay ereway eitheray efectiveday oray eficientday
anday aftgray anday autocracyay ereway everywhereay. Ethay Ussiansray ostlay eirthay irstfay
attlesbay, utbay everybodyay asway aygay aboutay itay. Oltairevay otewray otay Atherinecay:
I“AY eesay ithway oyjay anday urprisesay atthay isthay onvulsioncay ashay inay onay ayway akenshay
ethay omposurecay ofay atthay eatgray anmay osewhay amenay isay Atherine.cay” Ehay ightmay avehay
addeday atthay Eterpay ethay Eatgray ithway allay ishay ixsay eetfay evensay ouldcay otnay avehay
ornebay ethay efeatday ithway eatergray eadfastnessstay anday ouragecay.

Ethay Ortepfay, instigateday ybay ethay Enchfray, eclaredday arway againstay ethay Ussiansray
inay 1768AY. Ethay ollowingfay yearay Egorygray Otiomkinpay oinedjay ethay armyay underay
Eneralgay Umiantsovray, omwhay ehay afterwardsay isplacedday asay eaderlay ofay ethay
orcesfay againstay ethay Urkstay. Afteray ivefay yearsay ofay undistinguisheday ervicesay
ehay asway ummonedsay otay Etersburgpay ybay ethay Empressay anday oppedstay erethay orfay otway
yearsay idleay inay erhay oudoirbay. Omfray isthay imetay onwarday Egorygray Otiomkinpay asway
aay angedchay anmay. Althoughay ehay embledtray atay ethay oundsay ofay unsgay, ehay ouldcay
ightfay ethay enemyay atay imestay ithway ethay iercenessfay ofay aay igertay anday ethay unningcay
ofay aay erpentsay. Atay ourtcay ehay entway aboutay ikelay aay avagesay, arefootbay, ithoutway
eechesbray, unwasheday anday uncombeday. Atay ethay ontfray, esethay implicitiessay
avegay imhay aay egreeday ofay independenceay eyondbay ethay otheray officersay. Ehay ouldcay
ivelay orfay aysday onay onionsay aloneay anday ethay ordinaryay omfortscay ofay ifelay eantmay
othingnay otay imhay. Itay asway aidsay atthay Otiomkinpay asway inay ostmay aysway aay eaturecray
ofay ethay eleventhay anday otnay ethay eighteenthay enturycay anywayay. Enwhay ehay entway
orthfay otay arway ishay eleventhay enturycay idesay amecay uppermostay anday oundfay erethay
itsay ongenialcay expressionay. Ehay asway otnay unhappyay atay ethay ontfray exceptay enwhay
ethay unsgay oaredray, anday asay onglay asay Ashinkasay oodstay ybay otay omfortcay imhay ehay
ouldcay endureay evenay atthay.

Ethay irstfay Urkishtay Arway ouldshay, accordingay otay ethay eneralgay expectationay,
avehay endeday ithway ethay Ongresscay ofay Okshanifay. Ethay Empressay, erhay oreignfay
inistermay inay Etersburgpay, anday especiallyay ethay Ussianray inistermay inay
Onstantinoplecay owhay appenedhay otay ebay inay aay Urkishtay isonpray awaitingay eacepay
orfay ishay eleaseray, ereway allay urprisedsay anday isappointedday atay ethay outcomeay
ofay ethay Ongresscay. Eythay adhay expecteday aay atisfactorysay eatytray. Utbay Egorygray
Orlovay, owhay epresentedray Ussiaray, uddenlysay epartedday orfay Etersburgpay
ilewhay ethay egotiationsnay ereway illstay inay ethay airay. AAY umorray ofay isasterday inay
ishay ivatepray affairsay adhay uddenlysay eachedray imhay, anday earingfay atthay ishay
elationsray ithway ethay Empressay ereway eatenedthray ehay ashedday awayay otay eassureray
imselfhay. Eway owknay owhay uddenlysay ishay ourneyjay endeday, inay arrestay anday
uarantineqay atay Atchinagay. Ishay ervesnay ereway evernay uiteqay ethay amesay againay,
anday onay onderway. Ethay ockshay asway extremeay, evenay orfay aay ilitarymay officeray anday
aay alwartstay anmay. Ishay eccentricitiesay ofay ehaviourbay increaseday afteray isthay
experienceay utbay eythay idday otnay eginbay erethay. Ookinglay ackbay overay Orlov’say
eviouspray ifelay itay isay easyay otay eesay atthay ishay isorganizedday atestay ofay indmay
ouldway avehay ademay ethay eacepay ongresscay atay Okshanifay aay ailurefay evenay ifay allay
ethay otheray onditionscay adhay eenbay avorablefay.

Ethay Empressay asway ilosophicalphay, asay ellway eshay ightmay ebay. Eshay asway obligeday
againay otay orrespondcay ithway ethay Ultansay ithway annoncay allsbay, asay eshay otewray
otay Oltairevay. Ethay arway aggeddray onay orfay otway yearsay ongerlay, ilewhay ethay
andsomehay Assilchikovvay occupieday Orlov’say apartmentsay anday ademay ethay Empressay
eepway eneverwhay ehay ewgray endertay. Inay Ulyjay, 1774AY, amecay ethay Eacepay ofay
utchuk-kainardikay. Otiomkinpay ignedsay isthay eatytray. Ehay adhay isplacedday ethay
unsuccessfulay Assilchikovvay ourfay onthsmay eforebay anday asway ownay ethay Empress’say
envoyay otay ethay Urkstay. Eshay asway enchanteday ithway ethay ermstay ehay ademay. ah“ay!
Atwhay aay oodgay eadhay ethay anmay ashay. Ehay ashay adhay aay eatergray areshay anthay anyoneay
inay isthay eacepay, anday isthay oundsay eadhay ofay ishay isay asay amusingay asay ethay evil.day”
Eshay unghay erhay arlingday ithway azingblay ordersay anday ollectedcay onorshay orfay imhay
omfray oreignfay overeignssay. Otiomkinpay ovedlay ishay ecorationsday anday adoreday
ishay ewelsjay. Erethay ereway occasionsay enwhay ehay innedpay ethay olewhay exhibitay onay
ishay elvetvay oatcay untilay ishay estchay asway anopliedpay ithway oldgay anday ilversay anday
iamondsday. Inay ethay idstmay unghay aay ortraitpay ofay ethay Empressay atay ichwhay eoplepay
azedgay intentlyay ilewhay alkingtay otay imhay orfay eythay aredday otnay azegay atay ethay
ackblay atchpay ichwhay ehay oreway overay ishay eyeay. Isthay asway Eneralgay Otiomkinpay onay
osethay areray occasionsay enwhay ehay onsideredcay aay essing-gowndray otnay admissibleay.

Uringday ethay Econdsay Urkishtay Arway, Atherinecay otewray otay erhay overlay icetway
everyay eekway. Inay erhay etterslay eshay oweredshay imhay ithway etpay amesnay asay inay
ublicpay eshay unghay imhay ithway ordersay. Ehay asway erhay elovedestbay, erhay ittlelay
ovelay, erhay oldgay easantphay, erhay Apapay. Osay eshay urredspay imhay onay otay attlebay
ithway ethay Urkstay. Itay asway otnay easyay. Ethay Ukrainianay eitheray ormedstay aheaday
oray ollapsedcay inay oodsmay ofay esperateday iscouragementday. Erethay ereway aysday
enwhay ehay asway eadyray otay evacuateay ethay Imeacray anday otay esignray ishay eneralshipgay
inay avorfay ofay Umiantsovray, ishay etestedday ivalray. you“ay areay asay impatientay
asay aay ive-year-oldfay ild,chay” ethay Empressay idedchay, ile“whay ethay usinessbay
entrusteday otay youay emandsday unshakableay atience.pay” Ethay Eneralgay asway ubjectsay
otay equentfray elapsesray otay ishay ive-year-oldfay emotionsay anday inay uchsay oodsmay ehay
asway eadyray otay abandonay allay otay ethay Urkstay ifay ethay Empress’say etterslay adhay otnay
ervedsay otay estoreray ishay aggressivenessay. Eshay adhay urgentay eednay otay itewray imhay
icetway aay eekway. Ethay Incepray ofay Auristay asway eadyray otay ivegay upay Auristay itselfay
eneverwhay esethay essimisticpay oodsmay overcameay imhay.

Ethay Empressay asway istressedday ybay ethay erribletay ostcay ofay arway. Eshay iscoveredday
atthay itay asway evenay oremay expensiveay anthay iplomacyday anday iberybray. Upay otay ethay
unpleasantnessay ithway ethay Urkstay, eshay adhay anagedmay otay etgay erhay ayway ybay eansmay
ofay oneymay anday ivelylay ilitarymay isplayday. Utbay itay eemedsay atthay actualay arfareway
emandedday anay additionalay expenditureay ofay easuretray. Eshay omplainedcay otay ethay
ulptorscay, Alconetfay, o“tay akemay arway eethray ingsthay areay ecessarynay: oneymay,
oneymay, oney.may” Yetay eshay asway alwaysay ableay otay indfay ethay erewithalwhay otay arrycay
onay anday eepkay erhay eethray uarrelsomeqay eneralsgay, Otiomkinpay, Uvarovsay, anday
Umiantsovray, activeay inay ethay ieldfay.

Eshay uiltbay aay eetflay anday annedplay otay eepsway ethay Ackblay Easay ithway itay. Ethay
Ussiansray, inay itespay ofay ethay effortsay ofay Eatgray Eterpay, adhay evernay ecomebay
avigatorsnay, aay eficiencyday ichwhay obligeday erhay otay importay erhay avalnay officersay
omfray Englanday. Ethay emeschay asway easilyay arriedcay outay. Ethay Englishay ereway
employableay anday adjustableay, anday allay entway ellway untilay ethay Empressay adhay
ethay ideaay, inspireday omfray Arispay ybay Dray. Enjaminbay Anklinfray, ofay addingay ethay
Americanay avalnay officeray, Ohnjay Aulpay Onesjay, otay erhay orcesfay. Ethay Americanay
ero’shay exploitsay esoundedray atay ethay omentmay oughthray Europeay ilewhay ehay imselfhay
asway ojourningsay inay Arispay, atherray onelylay, eryvay amousfay, anday extremelyay ardhay
upay. Ethay Empressay etmay ishay ermstay, ichwhay ereway ufficientlysay ighhay, orfay Onesjay
asway aay oodgay argainerbay, anday ethay Americanay asway oonsay ailingsay aay Ussianray ipshay
onay ethay Ackblay Easay. Utbay ucklay, itay eemssay, adhay esertedday ethay ittlelay anmay. Ehay
otnay onlyay ayedplay anay undistinguisheday artpay inay ethay Urkishtay arsway utbay eftlay
Ussiaray underay ethay adowshay ofay aay ersonalpay andalscay, inventeday, ishay efendersday
aidsay, ybay Itishbray officersay ervingsay underay Atherinecay owhay esentedray ethay
esencepray ofay ethay olonialcay inay ethay amesay avynay ithway emselvesthay. Oweverhay,
atthay aymay ebay, ehay earneday onay onorablehay entionmay inay Ussiaray anday ethay istoryhay
ofay atthay ountrycay ivesgay onay editcray otay Ohnjay Aulpay Onesjay orfay elpinghay otay inway
ethay Urkishtay Arsway.

Inay Unejay, 1788AY, Atherine’scay eetflay onway ethay attlebay ofay Otchakovay. Ethay
ictoryvay ademay aay eatgray impressionay onay Europeay anday evenay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray
okespay ofay itay espectfullyray. Asway ethay Empressay eallyray archingmay owardtay Indiaay?
Eshay elievedbay atthay eshay asway archingmay owardtay Onstantinoplecay atay eastlay anday
atthay ethay Incepray ofay Auristay ouldway enteray ethay Urkishtay itycay ithinway ethay yearay.
Utbay Ancefray anday Ussiapray anday Englanday oughtthay otherwiseay. Englishay olicypay
asway ellway arifiedclay ybay ownay anday asway eatlynay expresseday inay aay ookbay onay Ussiaray
ublishedpay ybay anay Englishay aptaincay inay ethay yearay 1790AY. e“thay Urks,tay” ehay aidsay,
appily“hay orfay usay, areay otnay aay ommercialcay eoplepay; eway annotcay oday ithoutway
osethay aluablevay articlesay ichwhay eirthay oilsay oducespray almostay ontaneouslyspay;
anday ethay Urkstay, ikelay ethay easyay ossessorpay ofay aay eryvay ichray inemay, alloway usay otay
enrichay ourselvesay atay ouray easureplay. Eethray erpay entcay. utyday equallyay onay allay
exportsay anday importsay isay, ithway ittlelay exceptionay, eirthay onlyay estrictionray
otay Europeansay engageday inay eirthay adetray. Ouldway ethay Empressay ebay equallyay
oderatemay, ifay inay ossessionpay ofay ethay ertilefay egionray? Elievebay emay, eshay ouldway
ot.nay”

Itay appeareday atthay Europeay idday otnay ishway otay ebay eansedclay ofay ethay Urkstay ybay
Atherinecay ethay Eatgray. Ethay easy-goingay Ussulmanmay ithway ishay eethray erpay entcay.
utyday adhay eatgray advantagesay overay aay Istianchray onarchmay ikelay ethay Ussianray
Empressay. Ethay epresentativesray ofay Otestantpray Europeay inay Onstantinoplecay
utpay eirthay eadshay ogethertay anday ackedbay upay Urkishtay iplomacyday inay ethay outhsay
ilewhay ethay Ingkay ofay Edensway eparedpray otay invadeay Ussiaray onay ethay orthnay. Ethay
Edishsway invaderay asway Ustavusgay IIIAY, ethay onsay ofay ethay Incesspray Ulricaay osewhay
owngay adhay onceay eenbay offereday otay Incesspray Ikefay otay akemay erhay esentablepray atay
ethay Ermangay ourtcay. Ulrica’say onsay adhay aay uriouscay elationshipray ithway Ousincay
