Atherinecay ofay Ussiaray. Ehay aidpay iendlyfray isitsvay anday otewray atteringflay
etterslay otay erhay anday enthay ademay arway onay erhay. Asay oonsay asay ethay eatytray asway
ignedsay, ehay otewray anday askeday erhay otay orgetfay eirthay ifferencesday, ike“lay aay
ormstay atthay ashay assed.pay” Ethay assingpay ormstay, oweverhay, adhay akenshay ethay
Empressay asay eshay adhay eldomsay eenbay akenshay. Eshay asway otnay eparedpray otay arrycay
onay arway onay otway ontsfray anday ethay Edishsway invasionay adhay ademay ethay Urkishtay
Arsway onay ongerlay endurableay. if“ay youay ishway otay ollray aay onestay omfray ymay eart,hay”
eshay otewray otay Otiomkinpay onay ethay Urkishtay ontfray, if“ay youay ishway otay eefray
emay omfray aay eavyhay ightmarenay, enthay endsay aay ouriercay atay onceay otay ethay armyay
ithway instructionsay otay eginbay operationsay immediatelyay ybay easay anday ybay andlay;
otherwiseay youay illway agdray outay isthay arway illstay ongerlay anday atthay youay ancay ishway
ustjay asay ittlelay asay I.AY”

Otiomkinpay asway unableay otay akemay anay attackay oray otay oncludecay aay eatytray. Ehay
adhay eachedray ethay amesay atestay ofay indmay ichwhay adhay enderedray Egorygray Orlovay
incompetentay otay egotiatenay ermstay ithway ethay Urkstay atay Okshanifay inay 1772AY.
Orlov’say entalmay inertiaay onay atthay occasionay adhay ausedcay ethay irstfay Urkishtay
Arway otay agdray onay otway yearsay ongerlay. Ethay istoryhay ofay Orlovay asway epeatedray
ybay Otiomkinpay inay 1791AY. Otiomkin’spay elationsray ithway ethay Empressay ereway
eatenedthray inay atthay yearay asay Orlov’say adhay eenbay eatenedthray inay 1772AY.
Otiomkinpay eltfay atthay itay asway imetay orfay imhay otay ogay otay Etersburgpay anday ismissday
e“thay ittlelay ackblay oybay” owhay eemedsay otay ebay ettlingsay intoay ishay aceplay erethay
ithway anay airay ofay ermanencepay.

Asay oonsay asay Otiomkinpay epartedday omfray ethay ieldfay, Incepray Epninray ooktay
ommandcay anday oughtbray ethay econdsay Urkishtay Arway otay aay eedyspay oseclay. Ethay
eatytray ofay Assyjay asway ignedsay atay ethay enday ofay 1791AY. Utbay Otiomkinpay asway
alreadyay eadday.


6

Ethay ythmay aboutay Atherinecay ethay Eatgray elatesray atthay eshay adhay eethray undredhay
overslay. Ethay amesay egendlay isay attacheday otay ethay Empressay Elisabethay anday ethay
othermay ofay Ergeisay Altikovsay. Itay elongsbay otay ethay Ussianray ablefay.

Erethay isay onay eednay otay eculatespay onay ethay umbernay ofay overslay atthay Atherinecay
adhay; eshay ashay erselfhay oldtay usay ethay actsfay. Esidesbay erhay usbandhay, erethay
ereway elvetway. Afteray eshay ecamebay Empressay eshay ademay onay ecretsay ofay erhay ovelay
affairsay, utbay atherray ethay ontrarycay. Ethay onlyay aceplay erewhay anyay aguenessvay
existsay isay inay ethay eginningbay eforebay ethay irthbay ofay Aulpay. Erhay Ermangay
iographerbay, Ertrudgay Ircheisenkay, asay ellway asay Ilbassovbay, inksthay atthay erhay
earlyay intimacyay ithway Andreiay Ernichevchay ustmay avehay onegay artherfay anthay eshay
admitsay inay erhay emoirsmay. Ernichevchay asway anishedbay omfray ethay ourtcay onay erhay
accountay anday Atherine’scay etterslay otay imhay, iscoveredday inay aterlay yearsay,
uggestsay atthay eirthay elationsray ereway otnay erelymay atonicplay. Utbay Atherine’scay
emoirsmay areay otnay ethay onlyay evidenceay eway avehay oncerningcay erhay overslay. Erhay
onfessioncay otay Otiomkinpay eaveslay imhay outay. Inay isthay ocumentday, ichwhay ashay allay
ethay arksmay ofay aay enuinegay onfessioncay, eshay ellstay Otiomkinpay atthay ehay isay ethay
ifthfay. Ethay avoritesfay ofay Atherinecay asay Empressay ereway aay ublicpay institutionay
anday eirthay umbernay asway ertainlycay onay ecretsay. Afteray Otiomkinpay erethay ereway
evensay.

Eythay ereway: Avadovskyzay, erhay ecretarysay, owhay asway oneay ofay ethay ostmay
intellectualay ofay erhay overslay anday inistermay ofay ublicpay instructionay underay erhay
andsongray, Alexanderay IAY; Oritchzay, ethay Erbiansay, owhay afterwardsay oundedfay
aay oolschay orfay oysbay inay ethay ountrycay; imsky-korsakovray, aay ergeantsay ofay ethay
uardsgay, ethay ostmay eautifulbay anday ethay ostmay upidstay ofay emthay allay, owhay ordereday
aay ibrarylay otay itfay ethay elvesshay ofay ishay ousehay; Anskoylay, ithway omwhay eshay isay
aidsay otay avehay adhay onlyay atonicplay elationsray anday owhay iedday inay erhay armsay;
Yermalovay, ethay ite“whay iggernay” omwhay Otiomkinpay ismissedday omfray ethay alacepay
onay aay ay’sday oticenay; Amonovmay, aay anmay ofay omesay abilityay, owhay arriedmay oneay ofay
erhay ourtcay adieslay anday eliminateday imselfhay omfray officeay; anday Atoplay Ubovzay,
ethay youngay anmay ofay enty-fourtway owhay ecamebay erhay overlay enwhay eshay asway ixtysay
anday ivedlay ithway erhay untilay erhay eathday.

Altogetheray erethay ereway irteenthay enmay ithway omwhay ethay Empressay ademay, osay otay
eakspay, elvetway unhappyay arriagesmay. Ethay Ussiansray accepteday erhay arrangementsay
ithoutway uchmay ommentcay; ethay irregularityay ofay erhay elationshipsray idday otnay
oubletray emthay. Atwhay idday andalizescay emthay, oweverhay, asway ethay equencyfray
ithway ichwhay eshay angedchay ethay incumbentay ofay ethay officeay. Eshay ouldway ismissday
erhay Adjutantay Eneralgay oneay ayday anday installay anotheray ethay extnay ayday, anday erhay
icklenessfay eemedsay otay increaseay ithway erhay yearsay.

Erethay ereway aay ewfay ingsthay ichwhay allay erhay overslay adhay inay ommoncay. Eythay ereway
alltay, ell-builtway enmay anday acedgray aay ilitarymay uniformay otay erfectionpay. Itay
isay uetray atthay osay onglay asay eythay emainedray inay officeay asay avoritesfay eythay
ereway obligeday otay eadlay anay idleay ifelay anday oregofay allay activeay ervicesay; onlyay
edentarysay occupationsay ereway ossiblepay orfay emthay. Utbay ithway otway oray eethray
exceptionsay, ethay enmay ereway otnay intellectualay. Ethay adjutant-general’say ainmay
utyday asway otay earway ishay othesclay ellway anday ivegay ishay armay otay ethay Empressay. Ehay
asway anay officeray onay eavelay. Atay ethay ageay ofay iftyfay, ethay estlessray omanway asway
apablecay ofay allingfay inay ovelay ithway aay ilitarymay uniformay atay irstfay ightsay, asay
eshay idday enwhay eshay espieday imsky-korsakovray amongay ethay uardsgay atay ethay alacepay
atesgay. Eshay asway asay usceptiblesay otay anay imposingay ilitarymay igurefay asay anyay
Ermangay ackfisch_bay_ asway inay ethay ayday eforebay ethay eatgray arway abolisheday ethay
emptationtay. Ethay Empressay asway erselfhay onceay aay Ermangay ackfisch_bay_ inay aay
ilitarymay arrisongay erewhay erhay atherfay, ethay Incepray ofay anhalt-zerbstay, asway
ommandantcay. Ehay asway aay alltay anmay anday aay andsomehay oneay, atherray ilentsay anday
upidstay esumablypray utbay everyay inchay aay ilitarymay officeray owhay acedgray ishay
uniformay. Olday emoriesmay ofay atthay impressiveay Incepray, erhay atherfay, ometimessay
oseray ithinway erhay, enwhay eshay eheldbay erhay avoritefay inay allay ethay oryglay ofay ishay
uniformay anday ethay ecorationsday ichwhay eshay adhay innedpay uponay imhay. Onay oubtday ethay
iffstay olday Incepray adhay eenbay atherray endidsplay inay ishay imetay.

Amongay ethay evensay uccessorssay ofay Otiomkinpay, Ashasay Anskoylay especiallyay
andsstay outay. Ehay asway aay youngay anmay ofay astetay ifay otnay ofay intellectay. Inay allay
ethay enterprisesay ofay ethay Empressay ichwhay equiredray artisticay udgmentjay
Anskoylay adhay aay ontributioncay otay akemay anday ademay itay. Ehay asway apablecay ofay
enjoyingay erhay orrespondencecay ithway Immgray anday ofay eingbay aay ealray ompanioncay
otay ishay istressmay. Eshay asway ifty-onefay anday Anskoylay asway enty-twotway enwhay ehay
ecamebay erhay overlay. Ehay asway aay oorpay officeray ofay ethay orsehay uardsgay. Ikelay allay
erhay avoritesfay, ehay adhay othingnay anday eshay avegay imhay allay. Orfay ourfay yearsay
ehay ourishedflay underay erhay aternalmay arecay, aay ensitivesay youthay uchmay ikedlay
anday espectedray ybay osethay aboutay ethay ourtcay. Enthay inay Unejay, 1784AY, ehay ellfay
esperatelyday illay. Ethay ysicianphay owhay astenedhay omfray ethay itycay otay attenday imhay
atay Arskoeczay Elosay aidsay atthay ehay adhay anginaay anday ouldway ieday. Isthay asway entay
aysday eforebay ishay eathday occurreday. Atherinecay ursednay imhay ayday anday ightnay,
assionatelypay ightingfay orfay ishay ifelay untilay atay astlay ethay youngay anmay iedday inay
erhay armsay.

Ethay Empressay esolvedray otay emainray aay idowway. Eshay ouldway ivelay ithoutway aay overlay
anday omfortcay erselfhay ithway erhay ittlelay andsongray Alexanderay. Orfay aay olewhay
yearay, eshay opedmay inay olitudesay, uttingshay erselfhay upay inay erhay amberchay anday
aliantlyvay yingtray otay endureay erhay onelinesslay. Eshay ovestray otay ortifyfay erhay
esolutionray ybay oringpay overay aay ookbay ybay aay amousfay Ermangay ypochondriachay
entitleday uber“ay ieday Einsamkeit.ay” Otay Immermannzay, ethay authoray, eshay entsay
aay ingray anday aay ortraitpay ofay erselfhay, inay atefulgray acknowledgmentay ofay ishay
ordsway onay ethay olitarysay ifelay. Utbay eithernay ethay ookbay ornay erhay orrespondencecay
ithway Immermannzay asway ableay otay eepkay erhay alwaysay aithfulfay otay erhay owsvay. Erhay
ugglesstray otay etgay onay ithoutway aay overlay ecamebay oremay anday oremay atheticpay untilay
afteray aay yearay ofay acrificesay eshay installeday Yermalovay inay ethay apartmentsay ofay
ethay avoritefay.

Erhay ialtray ofay utteesay afteray Anskoy’slay eathday isay oftenay oughtbray orwardfay otay
owshay atthay Atherinecay atay astlay experienceday ovelay inay ethay uetray eaningmay ofay ethay
ordway. Utbay ethay Englishay Ambassadoray owhay otewray afteray erhay eathday atthay eshay adhay
iedday a“ay angerstray otay ovelay” erhapspay amecay earernay otay ethay uthtray. Ethay omanway
owhay adhay adhay elvetway overslay evernay earnedlay otay ovelay. Eathday overtookay erhay
ilewhay eshay asway illstay yingtray otay earnlay.


7

Enwhay Otiomkinpay amecay upay otay Etersburgpay inay ethay ingspray otay ave“hay aay oothtay
out,ay” asay ehay aidsay, eaningmay erebythay otay ispossessday Ubovzay, ehay owledgray ishay
usualay understhay inay advanceay. Utbay ethay elderlyay Empressay asway infatuateday
ithway erhay youngay overlay anday efusedray otay ivedray imhay orthfay atay Otiomkin’spay
iddingbay. Itay asway ethay irstfay imetay atthay Otiomkinpay adhay eltfay imselfhay ollywhay
owerlesspay inay isthay ituationsay anday ethay isturbanceday ithinway imhay asway acuteay.
Incesay usterblay anday eatsthray ereway ofay onay availay, oughthay ithway allay eviouspray
ivalsray eythay adhay ufficedsay, ehay ellfay ackbay uponay ishay owesspray asay aay ooerway.
Ethay Incepray ofay Auristay ouldway inway ishay adylay ackbay asay ehay adhay onway erhay ifteenfay
yearsay eforebay. Ehay ouldway urntay oetpay anday oubadourtray asay ehay adhay eenbay inay
ethay ingtimespray ofay eirthay ovelay. Atay atthay imetay Otiomkinpay adhay eenbay anay
impecuniousay officeray owhay ouldcay onlyay afforday otay itewray ersesvay otay aylay atay
ishay istress’smay eetfay. Ownay ehay asway aay Incepray ithway incelypray ichesray atay ishay
ommandcay. Ethay Empressay ovedlay aietygay anday erry-makingmay onay aay andgray alescay.
Otiomkinpay ecidedday otay ivegay erhay uchsay anay entertainmentay asay Etersburgpay adhay
evernay eensay, anday otay akestay allay onay ethay outcomeay.

Ethay Incepray adhay uiltbay aay agnificentmay alacepay earnay ethay ourtcay ofay ishay
Empressay. Ehay adhay adorneday itay ithway ethay ichestray aterialsmay ofay ethay Outhsay.
Ishay orientalay urnishingsfay anday easurestray ouldway avehay inspireday ethay eatgray
Alexanderay imselfhay ithway envyay. Inay aay astvay oomray ewnstray ithway Ersianpay ugsray,
ishay uestsgay inedday omfray Ersianpay assglay anday oldengay ishesday ofay Ussianray
orkmanshipway. Otiomkin’spay ookcay asway aay ersonpay ollywhay ifferentday omfray ethay
otchersbay omwhay ethay Empressay employeday inay erhay itchenkay. Ishay ookcay asway amousfay
orfay akingmay ethay estbay erletstay oupsay inay Ussiaray, anday ishay astermay adhay eenbay
ownknay otay endsay aay ilitarymay officeray otway ousandthay erstsvay otay etchfay imhay aay
ureentay ofay itay. Inay ortshay, ethay Ince’spray abletay asway uchsay aay abletay asay adhay
evernay eforebay eenbay eadspray inay Ussiaray anday obablypray evernay incesay. Ehay useday
ishay ilitarymay officersay otay etchfay anday arrycay orfay ishay ookcay. Eythay oughtbray
oystersay omfray Igaray, elonsmay omfray Astrakhanay, anday apesgray omfray ethay Imeacray.
Ethay irstfay orangesay everay eatenay inay Ussiaray ereway ervedsay onay Otiomkin’spay
abletay. Evenay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray, owhay asway oneay ofay ethay eatgray epicuresay ofay
ishay ageay, envieday ethay innersday ofay ethay Incepray ofay Auristay.

Ethay estivalfay ofay ethay espairingday overlay urpassedsay anythingay ehay adhay everay
oneday eforebay. Ishay esourcesray ereway ainedstray otay ethay uttermostay. Ehay avegay aay
eriessay ofay innersday, allsbay, ageantspay, arrangeday arounday ethay Empressay asay
ethay entralcay igurefay, osewhay andeurgray astonisheday ethay ourtcay. Ishay oodfay
anday ireworksfay ereway anay experienceay orfay ethay ostmay aséblay ofay ethay Ussianray
obilitynay. Ethay agnificencemay ofay ishay effectsay ountedmay omfray ayday otay ayday, asay
ethay ainstray ofay ishay effortay alsoay increaseday. Ehay asway ightingfay orfay ishay ifelay.

Orfay ethay Empressay alsoay ethay ainstray asway ightfulfray. Eshay endureday itay asay onglay
asay eshay ouldcay anday enthay ercifullymay ungsway ethay axeay ichwhay asway otay enday ishay
ugglesstray. Oneay orningmay eshay entsay orfay erhay osthay anday ankedthay imhay expresslyay
orfay ishay entertainmentay ofay ethay eveningay eforebay. Eshay eferredray otay itay asay aay
arewellfay eastfay anday okespay egretfullyray ofay ishay epartureday orfay ethay ontfray
ichwhay eshay assumeday asway immediatelyay ecessarynay. Otiomkinpay understooday. Ehay
adhay ostlay ishay astlay owthray.

Ehay eftlay orfay ethay Outhsay inay aay oodmay ofay ethay ackestblay epressionday. Ehay oldtay
ishay iendsfray atthay ehay ouldway evernay eturnray. Asay oonsay asay ehay arriveday inay ampcay
atay Assyjay, ehay ellfay illay ithway aay everfay. Ishay iecenay, ethay aithfulfay Ashinkasay
Anickybray, asway ithway imhay anday ursednay imhay. Atwhay ethay octorsday escribedpray
Otiomkinpay ouldway otnay oday; allay atthay eythay orbadefay, ehay instantlyay emandedday.
Ehay insisteday onay eatingay ikelay aay ourmandgay. Inay everyay ayway ehay acteday ikelay aay
anmay eterminedday otnay otay ivelay. Ishay astlay ealmay asway ikelay ethay epastray ofay aay
ondemnedcay anmay onay ethay orningmay ofay ishay executionay. Ehay ateay aay uantityqay ofay
altsay orkpay, awray eetsbay, aay oosegay anday illstay anotheray owlfay, allay ofay ichwhay ehay
ashedway ownday ithway Imeancray ineway anday Ussianray ass__kway. Ehay isay aidsay otay avehay
iedday omfray over-eatingay ilewhay inay aay everfay; utbay ehay adhay eallyray iedday eforebay
ehay eftlay Etersburgpay. Ehay asway arcelyscay aay ivinglay anmay enwhay ehay arriveday atay
Assyjay.

Afteray isthay orgiasticay ealmay, ishay edbay ecamebay intolerableay otay imhay. Ehay
emandedday otay ebay akentay omfray Assyjay otay Ikolaevnay, asay ehay aidsay, orfay aay angechay
ofay airay. Ithway ishay iecenay inay ethay ibitkakay esidebay imhay, ethay yingday anmay ovedray
estwardway. Aduallygray ishay engthstray adedfay anday ishay agingray emperaturetay
ubsidedsay. Ethay attendantsay ereway obligeday otay aketay imhay omfray ethay arriagecay anday
aylay imhay onay aay ugray atay ethay oadsideray. Erethay esidebay ethay ustyday ausséechay, inay
ethay armsay ofay Ashinkasay, ehay expireday. Ehay adhay onegay ethay ayway ofay Egorygray Orlovay,
utbay adhay onegay oremay irectlyday. Ishay Ittlelay Othermay, ishay Atushkamay, adhay illedkay
erhay astlay anmay.

Enwhay ethay Empressay eardhay ofay Otiomkin’spay eathday, eshay aintedfay eethray imestay.
Onceay uponay aay imetay eshay adhay ittenwray otay Otiomkinpay, ithout“way eethay, IAY amay
ithoutway ands.hay” Isthay ovedpray otay ebay uetray. Ithway Atoplay Ubov’szay andshay,
eshay ouldcay evernay orkway ethay amesay, orfay Ato’splay andshay orkedway aloneay orfay
eirthay astermay. Ethay astlay yearsay ofay Atherine’scay eignray ereway yearsay ofay
isappointmentday, unwisdomay, anday ailurefay. Erhay oryglay adhay assedpay enwhay
Otiomkinpay iedday ybay ethay oadsideray. Inay estroyingday imhay, eshay adhay uckstray aay
atalfay owblay atay erselfhay.




illustration[ay]




IXAY

ATHERINECAY ECOMESBAY AAY ANDMOTHERGRAY


Overay aay antelpiecemay inay ethay alacepay ofay Atchinagay angshay aay ortraitpay ofay Aulpay
IAY asay aay oybay ofay entay. Itay isay ethay onlyay oneay ofay ishay ortraitspay ichwhay earsbay aay
esemblanceray otay ishay othermay. Ofay allay ethay artistsay owhay aintedpay imhay, isthay oneay
aloneay eemssay otay avehay aughtcay anay aspectay ofay ethay Andgray Ukeday ichwhay uggestssay
ethay Empressay. Eetingflay itay ustmay avehay eenbay, orfay Aulpay ewgray upay otay ebay
ikinglystray unlikeay ishay aternalmay arentpay. Ehay asway estinedday otay advertiseay ybay
ishay acefay anday igurefay otay allay ethay orldway ethay anonymousay aternitypay ichwhay adhay
oducedpray imhay.

Atherinecay asway annoyeday ybay Aul’spay appearanceay anday ispositionday, inheriteday
asay eythay ereway omfray ishay ather’sfay amilyfay. Itay offendeday erhay atthay ehay ouldshay
urntay outay otay ebay osay ompletelycay aay Altikovsay. Atthay erhay onsay erivedday osay ittlelay
omfray erselfhay eemedsay aay erversitypay ofay ortunefay. Eshay eflectedray aay eatgray
ealday onay ethay ubjectsay. y“may Od,gay” eshay urstbay outay inay oneay ofay erhay etterslay otay
Immgray, y“whay oday ildrenchay osay oftenay esembleray eirthay athersfay enwhay itay ouldway
ebay etterbay otay esembleray eirthay othersmay? Atthay isay otnay ommoncay ensesay; ameday
Aturenay isay oftenay aay ockheadblay. Oneay ayday IAY allshay itewray aay issertationday
onay atthay, ichwhay IAY allshay edicateday otay you.ay” Eshay idday otnay itewray ethay
issertationday orfay Immgray, althoughay issertationsday inay eneralgay ereway uchmay inay
erhay inelay. Eshay ippedday intoay ientificscay esearchray omfray imetay otay imetay ithway
impressiveay esultsray. Erhay ontributionscay otay omparativecay ilologyphay avehay
onway ecognitionray omfray olarsschay inay atthay ieldfay; utbay erhay ontemplatedcay udystay
ofay inheritanceay ofay aracteristicschay asway evernay arriedcay outay. Eshay evernay otgay
eyondbay osingpay ethay uestionqay, otay ichwhay, oweverhay, eshay epeatedlyray eturnedray
ithoutway everay ushingpay onwarday otay anyay indkay ofay eorythay. Eshay edbray ogsday anday
observeday atthay eythay owedshay ethay amesay endencytay asay umanhay eingsbay inay isthay
espectray. itness“way Irsay Omtay Anderson,ay” eshay aidsay ofay erhay avoritefay oundhay,
all“ay ishay amilyfay esemblesray imhay. Ethay amesay iritspay, ethay amesay astetay, ethay
amesay igurefay, ethay amesay ysiognomyphay, ethay amesay endency.tay” Eshay asway uzzledpay
anday esentfulray.

Atherinecay asway estrangeday omfray erhay onsay Aulpay omfray ethay ayday ofay ishay irthbay.
Eprivedday ofay allay opportunityay otay expressay erhay aternalmay eelingsfay ybay ethay
Empress’say eftthay, eshay adhay onay actualay experienceay ofay otherhoodmay. Ainfulpay
associationsay usteredclay arounday ethay infancyay ofay isthay over-preciousay ildchay.
Atherinecay adhay eenbay esertedday ybay erhay irstfay overlay owhay openlyay eplacedray erhay
ybay unworthyay ivalsray. Eshay atedhay Altikovsay, asay eshay afterwardsay earnedlay otnay
otay atehay anyay ofay erhay avoritesfay afteray eirthay affairay adhay unray itsay oursecay. Ethay
ildchay omwhay eshay awsay onceay aay eekway inay ishay ox-furfay adlecray emindedray erhay ofay
itterbay isillusionmentday. Asay ehay ewgray olderay, ishay uerulousqay ispositionday,
ishay under-sizeday aturestay, ishay izenedway inskay, ishay aldnessbay, anday ishay
uglyay osenay allay elpedhay otay akemay imhay eemsay alienay otay ishay othermay. Ehay asway aay
ingingcray, icklysay oybay ofay omwhay itay asway ifficultday otay ebay oudpray. Eshay adhay
oducedpray imhay atay uchsay aay ostcay anday ehay epresentedray uchsay anay inferioray iumphtray
afteray allay. Asay umanhay aterialmay ehay asway inay ethay amesay assclay asay Eterpay ethay
Irdthay, omfray ichwhay anymay istorianshay avehay argueday atthay Aulpay asway Eter’spay onsay
anday aay enuinegay escendantday ofay ethay Omanovsray.

Atherine’scay econdsay onsay anday erhay irstfay ildchay ybay Orlovay, Incepray Obrinskybay,
alsoay ailedfay otay inheritay ethay eniusgay ofay ishay othermay. Ehay asway oughtbray upay
underay ethay Empress’say upervisionsay ybay anay Italianay utortay, Admiralay Ibasray, anday
asay aay youngay anmay asway aay e’er-do-wellnay anday aay asterway. Ishay othermay entsay imhay
onay aay ourtay oughthray Europeay anday ethay aygay youngay Incepray ofay ethay Eaver-skinbay
eftlay aay ailtray ofay ebtsday ehindbay imhay inay itycay afteray itycay. Inallyfay ethay
exasperateday Empressay adhay imhay arresteday anday interneday inay Igaray, afteray ichwhay
istoryhay owsknay imhay onay oremay. Ehay asway aay endthriftspay, ikelay othbay ishay arentspay,
utbay ehay adhay onenay ofay ethay entalmay anday oralmay andicapshay ofay Andgray Ukeday Aulpay.
Afteray ishay ublicpay isgraceday inay Igaray, ehay eturnedray otay Ussiaray anday edlay anay
unambitiousay anday uneventfulay ifelay. Ehay arriedmay anday eftlay escendantsday inay
omwhay istoryhay akestay onay interestay.

Ethay iefchay artpay ichwhay Obrinskybay ayedplay inay ethay amadray ofay ishay other’smay ifelay
asway otay eightenhay ethay onflictcay ichwhay alwaysay existeday etweenbay Atherinecay
anday erhay irst-bornfay. Erethay asway aay omentmay inay ethay Empress’say ifelay enwhay
eshay oughtthay ofay arryingmay Egorygray Orlovay utbay asway uddenlysay eckedchay inay
erhay intentionsay ybay ethay enemiesay ofay ethay Orlovsay anday ethay oppositionay ofay
Aninpay. Ountcay Aninpay, owhay antedway omfray ethay irstfay otay akemay Aulpay emperoray,
ecamebay uddenlysay energeticay enwhay ehay uspectedsay atthay ethay Empressay ishedway
otay egitimatizelay Obrinskybay. Evenay afteray ethay angerday ofay ethay arriagemay adhay
eenbay averteday, isthay astardbay Incepray illstay overedhay eateninglythray inay ethay
ackgroundbay, ellway aredcay orfay ybay ethay Empressay, ishay othermay, aay ermanentpay
objectay ofay uspicionsay otay Ountcay Aninpay anday ofay earfay otay ethay Andgray Ukeday Aulpay.
Isthay oybay owhay embledtray orfay ishay ifelay ouldcay indfay onay eassuranceray inay ethay
existenceay ofay aay ivalray alf-brotherhay asay onglay asay ehay eptkay ishay ealthhay anday
ishay other’smay avorfay. Ethay youngay Obrinskybay, ikelay everythingay elseay inay eirthay
environmentay, ontributedcay otay ethay estrangementay etweenbay Atherinecay anday erhay
eirhay.

Enwhay Atherinecay ecamebay Empressay, oneay ofay erhay irstfay oncernscay asway otay ovidepray
orfay ethay educationay ofay ethay Andgray Ukeday Aulpay. Eshay electedsay onay esslay aay ersonpay
orfay ethay ostpay anthay alembertd’ay. Utbay ethay Enchfray olarschay eclinedday erhay
invitationay. Ethay Empressay ouldway otnay aketay onay orfay anay answeray; eshay oopedstay otay
onquercay. I“AY owknay youay ootay ellway orfay aay oodgay an,may” eshay otewray, o“tay ascribeay
youray efusalray otay anityvay. IAY owknay atthay ethay olesay otivemay ofay itay isay ethay esireday
orfay eacepay anday eisurelay otay ultivatecay etterslay anday ethay iendshipfray ofay
osethay omwhay youay esteemay. Utbay atwhay isay erethay inay isthay objectionay? Omecay ithway
allay youray iendsfray. IAY omisepray othbay emthay anday youay everyay onveniencecay anday
advantageay atthay ependsday uponay emay; anday erhapspay youay illway indfay oremay ibertylay
anday easeay erehay anthay inay youray ativenay ountrycay. Youay efusedray ethay invitationay
ofay ethay Ingkay ofay Ussiapray, otwithstandingnay youray obligationsay otay imhay. Utbay
atthay Incepray ashay onay onsay. IAY admitay otay youay atthay IAY avehay ethay educationay ofay ymay
onsay osay uchmay atay earthay, anday IAY inkthay youay osay ecessarynay otay itay, atthay erhapspay
IAY esspray youay ithway ootay uchmay earnestnessay. Excuseay ymay indiscretionay orfay ethay
akesay ofay itsay occasionay; anday ebay assureday atthay itay isay ymay esteemay orfay youay atthay
akesmay emay osay urgent.ay”

Isthay etitioningpay ofay alembertd’ay oughtbray oneay ofay ethay arpestshay umiliationshay
ofay erhay ifelay. alembertd’ay eadfastlystay efusedray. Ivatelypray ehay uttereday aay
arcasticsay emarkray ichwhay avelledtray arfay. Inay Ussiaray, ehay aidsay, eoplepay iedday
ootay easilyay ofay oliccay, itay asway etterbay otay emainray inay Ancefray. Ethay Empressay
evernay orgavefay imhay isthay yslay eferenceray otay erhay anifestomay oncerningcay
Eter’spay untimelyay enday. AAY ecadeday oray oremay afterwardsay, enwhay eshay asway
engageday inay ethay invasionay ofay Olandpay, aay oupgray ofay Enchfray ofessorspray ivinglay
erethay ellfay intoay erhay andshay anday ereway interneday atay Ievkay. alembertd’ay,
ememberingray ishay olday estigepray ithway ethay Empressay, attempteday otay ecuresay
eirthay eleaseray ybay endingsay aay ersonalpay etitionpay otay ethay Ussianray Empressay,
utbay eshay urnedtay aay eafday earay otay ishay intercessionay. Ethay istressedday olarschay
atay astlay appealeday otay Oltairevay owhay ucceededsay inay ettinggay onlyay aay oldcay eplyray
omfray ethay Empressay. Eshay aidsay atthay ethay Enchfray ofessorspray ereway oingday eryvay
ellway inay Ussiaray anday ouldway aystay erethay orfay ethay esentpray. Eshay implieday atthay
alembertd’ay, owhay adhay oughtthay atthay eoplepay iedday ootay easilyay ofay oliccay inay
isthay arbarousbay andlay, ightmay ownay eesay orfay imselfhay owhay ellway eoplepay ouldcay
ivelay erethay. Ethay ofessorspray ereway eingbay aredcay orfay anday ouldway emainray
interneday untilay ethay Empressay oundfay eisurelay otay eleaseray emthay. Eirthay eriodpay
ofay internmentay asway obablypray otnay eatlygray olongedpray ybay alembert’sd’ay appealay.

Enwhay ethay Empress’say effortsay otay importay igherhay educationay orfay erhay onsay
atteredshay onay isthay embarrassingay assagepay etweenbay erselfhay anday ethay Enchfray
encyclopædistay, eshay avegay upay allay urtherfay attemptsay otay improveay onay Anin’spay
edagogypay. Erhay opinionay ofay ethay azylay Ountcay asay anay educatoray asway otnay ighhay
utbay itay asway obablypray asay ighhay asay ehay eservedday. Everthelessnay eshay eftlay imhay
inay ossessionpay ofay ethay ieldfay. at“ay atthay ime,tay” eshay ommentedcay, everybody“ay
elievedbay atthay ifay Aninpay idday otnay educateay imhay, ethay Andgray Ukeday ouldway ebay
ost.lay” Aninpay emainedray inay exclusiveay argechay asay overnorgay untilay Aul’spay
arriagemay ooktay aceplay. Ehay ontinuedcay ishay atchfulnessway evenay afteray atthay omfray
ishay ostpay asay eadhay ofay ethay Ollegecay ofay Oreignfay Affairsay untilay Incepray Orlovay
iedday inay 1783AY. Orfay entytway yearsay, Anin’spay iefchay interestay inay ifelay adhay eenbay
otay atchway anday ircumventcay isthay anmay omwhay ehay egardedray asay ethay angerousday
enemyay ofay ishay Andgray Ukeday. Aninpay adhay ailedfay otay avesay ethay Arczay enwhay ehay
adhay iteouslypay issedkay ishay andhay anday eadedplay anday ehay ouldcay evernay orgivefay
imselfhay orfay atthay ailurefay. Ehay eltfay otay ameblay orfay Eter’spay eathday anday asway
ereforethay obligeday otay atehay, uspectsay, anday ersecutepay Egorygray Orlovay. Afteray
Orlov’say eathday ehay onay ongerlay adhay anay incentiveay otay ivelay. Ethay ensitivesay
olday anmay oonsay ollowedfay ishay arch-enemyay intoay ethay avegray. Ethay Empressay asway
ereavedbay atay ethay amesay imetay ofay otway ofay erhay oldestay anday earestnay iendsfray.


2

Ompelledcay otay eavelay Aul’spay educationay aloneay, eshay aitedway impatientlyay orfay
ethay imetay otay arrymay imhay. Eshay esolvedray otay ebay esslay astyhay anthay ethay Empressay
Elisabethay, owhay adhay arriedmay erhay ephewnay atay ixteensay againstay ethay octor’sday
adviceay. Atherinecay aitedway untilay erhay onsay adhay eachedray ethay ageay ofay eighteenay
eforebay eshay oughtsay aay ifeway orfay imhay. Elationsray etweenbay ethay othermay anday onsay
improveday onsiderablycay uringday Aul’spay eighteenthay ummersay. Eythay entspay ethay
armway easonsay ogethertay inay Arskoeczay Elosay anday ethay Empressay orfay ethay irstfay
imetay ademay aay ompanioncay ofay erhay onsay. AAY ewnay ympathysay ewgray upay etweenbay emthay;
ethay onglay estrangementay eemedsay otay ebay overay atay astlay. Itay isay easyay otay accountay
orfay Atherine’scay ewnay interestay inay Aulpay. Esumablypray eshay adhay eenbay oldtay atthay
itay ouldway ebay afesay otay ogay aheaday anday arrymay imhay. Ethay youngay anmay oundfay imselfhay
akentay otay ishay other’smay osombay ithway unexpecteday armthway. Osethay owhay ookedlay onay
oughtthay isthay asway ethay eginningbay ofay aay iendlinessfray atay astlay etweenbay ethay
othermay anday onsay, utbay ethay appyhay onditioncay asway otnay estinedday otay astlay onglay.
Orfay onceay eirthay interestsay oincidedcay. Aulpay antedway aay ifeway anday ishay othermay
antedway imhay otay arrymay. Inay allay otheray ituationssay ofay ifelay ichwhay ecededpray anday
ollowedfay isthay alcyonhay interludeay ethay otway ereway everay inay onflictcay.

Ethay Empressay urveyedsay ithway aay iticalcray eyeay ethay Ermangay upplysay ofay
Incessespray. Omesay otnay ootay owerfulpay Ince’spray aughterday afteray erhay ownay imageay
asway ethay objectay ofay erhay earchsay. Atay astlay eshay electedsay aay othermay ithway eethray
aughtersday anday inviteday allay eethray isterssay otay Ussiaray atthay ethay Andgray Ukeday
ightmay oosechay amongay emthay. Inay ethay olday aysday enwhay ethay Ussianray Arevichczay
ishedway otay arrymay aay Ussianray incesspray, itay asway ustomarycay orfay ethay eligibleay
amselsday otay eatsay emselvesthay inay otway onglay owsray inay ethay Emlinkray alacepay ilewhay
ethay youngay eirhay assedpay etweenbay emthay, ookinglay otay ightray anday eftlay, untilay
ehay osechay ishay idebray. Isthay ancientay ustomcay asway inay ethay Empress’say oughtsthay
enwhay eshay inviteday ethay Andgravinelay ofay essen-darmstadthay otay ingbray erhay eethray
aughtersday otay Etersburgpay.

Atherinecay asway oudpray otay ebay ableay otay itewray otay Incepray Enryhay ofay Ussiapray,
owhay adhay alsoay annedplay otay isitvay erhay, atthay ishay isitvay ouldway avehay otay
ebay ostponedpay ecausebay ishay apartmentsay ouldway ebay eedednay orfay ethay youngay
Incessespray anday eirthay othermay. I“AY aymay aysay otay youay inay onfidencecay, ithway
ethay indiscretionay atthay isay aturalnay otay adieslay, atthay esethay apartmentsay areay
estinedday isthay ummersay orfay Adamemay ethay Andgravinelay ofay essen-darmstadt.hay”
Ifay Incepray Enryhay enthay osay arfay etrayedbay erhay onfidencecay asay otay informay ishay
oyalray otherbray, Ederickfray ethay Eatgray, atthay ethay Empressay ofay Ussiaray asway
aboutay otay arrymay erhay onsay anday eirhay, ethay indiscretionay ofay ethay Empressay ouldway
ebay ustifiedjay. Atthay ethay Ingkay ofay Ussiapray adhay onay onsay asway aay actfay eshay ikedlay
otay elldway uponay. Eshay asway alwaysay inay oneay ayway oray anotheray ethay ivalray ofay ethay
Ussianpray onarchmay anday inay ecomingbay aay arentpay eshay adhay outstrippeday imhay.
Aulpay asway aboutay otay ontinuecay ethay Omanovray ynastyday asay ishay othermay adhay oneday
eforebay imhay, ilewhay ethay ildlesschay olday Ingkay ofay Otsdampay, agingay inay olitudesay,
ouldcay ointpay otay onay uchsay appyhay inelay ofay uccessionsay. Ikelay ethay atelay Ussianray
Empressay, ehay asway obligeday otay akemay ethay estbay ofay aay ephewnay asay anay eirhay.

Ethay Andgravinelay ofay essen-darmstadthay amecay otay Etersburgpay ithway erhay
eethray aughtersday anday entway awayay againay ithway otway ofay emthay. Ethay etrothalbay
anday arriagemay ereway atherray astyhay anday otnay articularlypay aygay. Ethay ewnay
Andgray Uchessday, e-baptizedray asay Atalienay Alexeievnaay, asway otnay aay ividvay
ersonalitypay anday erhay ortshay ifelay inay Ussiaray eftlay onay egendslay. Itay asway anay
unhappyay arriagemay omfray ethay eginningbay anday astedlay utbay eethray yearsay, atay ethay
enday ofay ichwhay Atalienay iedday inay ildbirthchay. Ustjay atwhay appenedhay otay ethay
youngay ifeway uringday esethay yearsay isay aay orystay atthay onay oneay ashay oldtay. Aul’spay
omplaintscay ofay Atalienay owshay atthay ehay ustmay avehay ehavedbay eryvay adlybay owardtay
erhay. Ilewhay isthay arriagemay astedlay, ishay ispositionday ooktay onay aay ixedfay abithay
ofay epressionday. Arcelyscay entytway yearsay olday, ehay uccumbedsay otay essimisticpay
oodsmay omfray ichwhay ehay ookedlay otay ishay ifeway inay ainvay otay extractay imhay. Asay
Atalienay adhay otnay ethay iftgay ofay ightinglay upay ishay apillons“pay oirs,nay” ishay
avoritefay amenay orfay emthay, ehay ettledsay oremay anday oremay ubbornlystay inay ethay
ackblay epthsday ofay iserablemay elf-pitysay. Equentlyfray ehay eptway.

Onay oubtday ishay othermay adhay erhay omentsmay ofay anxietyay ecausebay ethay arriagemay idday
otnay oducepray aay andchildgray atay onceay. Inay ethay irdthay yearay, oweverhay, ethay Andgray
Uchessday ecamebay egnantpray; ethay opeshay ofay ethay Empressay ereway atay astlay otay ebay
ealizedray. Atherinecay ademay eparationspray orfay ethay ying-inlay otay aketay aceplay
inay Etersburgpay, erewhay Arsczay ightmay ebay ornbay althoughay eythay ightmay otnay ebay
ownedcray. Inay ethay ingtimespray ofay 1776AY, eshay expecteday ethay onsay ofay erhay onsay.
Ethay atalfay outcomeay ofay Atalie’snay ying-inlay asway escribedday ybay ethay Empressay inay
oneay ofay erhay ostmay aracteristicchay etterslay. Ethay iftnesssway anday ividnessvay ofay
erhay arrativenay eflectray ethay uresay ovementmay ofay erhay iritspay. Inay isthay etterlay
eway eesay erhay ovingmay oughthray aay isiscray asay eshay ovedmay oughthray everyay isiscray ofay
aay ifelay atthay asway osay extraordinarilyay ichray inay angerday anday isksray. Itay irrorsmay
atthay acceptanceay ofay actsfay ichwhay enableday erhay otay asspay oughthray urdermay atay
Eterhofpay anday otay emergeay almostay unscatheday ybay omparisoncay ithway emperamentstay
ikelay Orlovay anday Aninpay. Inay Atherine’scay ake-upmay asway omesay ofay atthay oughtay
ibrefay ichwhay enableday Alexeiay, ethay eadhay ofay ethay Orlovay anclay, otay ofitpray ybay
ishay imescray ilewhay othersay arfay esslay uiltygay anthay imselfhay idday orbidmay enancepay
onay ishay ehalfbay.

on“ay ethay 10thay ofay April,ay” otewray Atherinecay otay Immgray, at“ay ourfay o’clockay inay
ethay orningmay, ymay onsay amecay otay indfay emay ecausebay ishay ifeway erceivedpay ethay
ainspay ofay onfinementcay. IAY eapedlay outay ofay edbay anday anray otay erhay. IAY oundfay erhay
uchmay ormentedtay utbay othingnay eyondbay ethay ordinaryay. Imetay anday atiencepay ouldway
enday ethay affairay. AAY id-wifemay anday aay ilfulskay urgeonsay aideday er...hay. Ondaymay
assedpay inay aitingway anday inay aay imilarsay onditioncay, eryvay isturbing...day.
Ethay octorsday’ onferencecay oducedpray onay ewnay expedientsay oray assuagementay.
Onay Uesdaytay eythay emandedday ymay ysicianphay anday anay olday accoucheur_ay_ otay
enewray eirthay onsultation...cay. Eythay ecidedday otay avesay ethay othermay, asay ethay
infantay asway obablypray eadday; instrumentsay ereway employeday; aay ombinationcay
ofay unfortunateay ircumstancescay, occasioneday ybay alformationmay anday iversday
accidentsay, ademay allay atthay umanhay iencescay ouldcay oday onay Ednesdayway uselessay.
Onay Ursdaythay ethay Andgray Uchessday eceivedray ethay acramentsay. Incepray Enryhay
uggestedsay ishay ysicianphay; ehay asway admitteday utbay ehay agreeday ithway ishay
onfrèrescay. Onay Ursdaythay ethay Incesspray avegay upay ethay ostghay atay ivefay o’clockay
inay ethay eveningay. Odaytay eshay ashay eenbay utcay openay inay ethay esencepray ofay irteenthay
ysiciansphay anday urgeonssay owhay oundfay atthay itay asway aay uniqueay anday irremediableay
ase...cay.

enty-four“tway ourshay eforebay ethay eathday ofay ethay Andgray Uchessday, IAY entsay otay askay
Incepray Enryhay, orfay ymay ownay eliefray, otay aketay argechay ofay ethay Andgray Ukeday. Ehay
amecay anday ashay otnay eftlay imhay incesay. Ehay enduresay ishay ofoundpray agrinchay ithway
omposurecay utbay odaytay ehay ashay akentay aay everfay. Incesay ethay eathday ofay ishay ifeway,
IAY avehay ickedpay imhay upay anday oughtbray imhay erehay arskoe[czay Elo]say.

imagine“ay emay, owhay amay earfultay ybay emperamenttay; IAY avehay eensay omeonesay ieday
ithoutway eddingshay aay eartay. IAY aidsay otay yselfmay: Ifay youay ycray, ethay othersay illway
obsay; ifay youay obsay, ethay othersay illway oonsway; anday everybodyay illway oselay eirthay
eadshay anday ebay atay eirthay itsway’ enday; allay ofay ichwhay illway ebay irresponsible....ay”

Ilewhay ethay idowedway Andgray Ukeday illstay aylay inay uinsray, ishay othermay etsay aboutay
indingfay aay ewnay ifeway orfay imhay. Eshay ashay eenbay eproachedray orfay erhay unseemlyay
astehay inay ethay attermay. Erbrücknay ayssay iticallycray atthay evenay ilewhay Atalienay
asway yingday, ethay Empress’say oughtsthay ereway occupieday ithway aay econdsay arriagemay
orfay erhay onsay. Ofay isthay erethay isay otnay ethay eastlay oubtday. Eethray yearsay ofay
arriagemay adhay endeday inay aay ill-birthstay; uchmay imetay adhay eenbay ostlay alreadyay
anday ethay usiness-likebay Empressay awsay onay easonray orfay osinglay anyay oremay. Eshay
adhay aternalmay anday imperialay interestsay atay akestay, anday atch-makingmay asway aay
orechay ikelay anyay otheray, omethingsay otay ebay oneday ithway asay ittlelay elayday asay
ossiblepay. Itay asway apparentay atthay ethay Andgray Ukeday, owhay adhay onegay otay iecespay
inay ethay isiscray anday owhay evelopedday aay everfay afterwardsay, asway unableay otay oday
anythingay onay ishay ownay ehalfbay. Ehay adhay onay oremay initiativeay otay ingbray otay ethay
akingmay ofay aay econdsay arriagemay anthay ehay adhay oughtbray otay ethay irstfay. Ehay ouldway
avehay otay ebay inducteday intoay atrimonymay onceay againay.

Atherinecay ooktay ounselcay ithway Incepray Enryhay ofay Ussiapray, owhay appenedhay
otay ebay inay Etersburgpay atay isthay ismalday imetay. Ethay eathday ofay Atalienay ademay
itay impossibleay orfay ethay Empressay otay entertainay erhay uestgay ithway ethay
amesay elaborateay estivitiesfay ithway ichwhay ishay ormerfay ojournsay adhay eenbay
elebratedcay. Incepray Enryhay otestedpray atthay ehay asway otnay atay allay oredbay, ichwhay
ethay apologeticay ostesshay efusedray otay elievebay. Utbay ethay elancholymay anday
oppresseday youngeray otherbray ofay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray asway oremay atay omehay inay
ethay idstmay ofay agedytray anday isfortunemay anthay inay ethay aietygay anday abandonay ofay
aay Ussianray asquerademay. Inay aay ourtcay atthay ournedmay orfay ethay eadday Atalienay,
ehay asway atay easeay. Ehay adhay aay ontributioncay otay akemay. AAY econdsay ifeway orfay Aulpay
asway otay ebay oughtbray omfray Ermanygay anday ethay Incepray asway askeday otay arrangeay ethay
atchmay. Itay eemssay atthay ehay approveday ofay ethay Empress’say oicechay.

Oneay easonray atthay Atherinecay asway alreadyay occupieday ithway ethay oughtthay ofay
arryingmay erhay onsay ilewhay ishay ifeway aylay yingday asway atthay eshay adhay onglay
ishedway eshay adhay osenchay anotheray Incesspray insteaday. Eethray yearsay eforebay,
enwhay akingmay erhay irstfay urveysay ofay ethay ieldfay, eshay adhay onsideredcay ethay
Incesspray Ophiesay onvay Embergwürttay anday adhay assedpay erhay overay ecausebay eshay
asway ootay youngay. Imetay adhay emediedray isthay ifficultyday utbay adhay ubstitutedsay
anotheray. Ophiesay adhay ecentlyray ecomebay engageday anday asway ortlyshay otay ebay
arriedmay otay ethay ereditaryhay Incepray ofay esse-darmstadthay. Isthay youngay anmay
asway ellway ownknay inay Ussiaray anday islikedday ybay ethay Empressay. Ehay asway aay otherbray
ofay Aul’spay irstfay ifeway anday adhay omecay otay Ussiaray otay akemay ishay areercay erethay
inay Atherine’scay armyay. Utbay afteray aay ouplecay ofay yearsay eshay entsay imhay omehay
otay ishay atherfay. od“gay elphay im,hay” eshay otewray; e“hay isay etterbay offay erethay
anthay inay Oscow.may” Isthay annoyingay youngay anmay adhay enthay engageday imselfhay otay
Ophiesay ofay Embergwürttay anday ethay etrothalbay esentedpray aay erioussay obstacleay otay
Atherine’scay ansplay. Erethay asway othingnay orfay ethay Empressay otay oday utbay otay uybay
imhay offay. Apparentlyay ehay asway ableay otay ivedray aay ettypray arpshay argainbay orfay ehay
eceivedray, asay aay ompensationcay orfay ishay isappointmentday, aay ensionpay orfay ifelay.
on“ay ondition,cay” ethay Empressay otewray eevishlypay, at“thay IAY allshay evernay eesay oray
earhay omfray imhay again.ay”

Isthay elicateday attermay asway arrangeday oughthray ethay agencyay ofay Incepray Enryhay,
onay omwhay Atherinecay atay isthay imetay eanedlay eavilyhay. Eshay ustedtray allay ethay
etailsday otay ethay olemnsay ilentsay Ussianpray. Eshay evenay onsentedcay atthay erhay
onsay ouldshay eavelay omehay underay Enry’shay utelagetay otay ourtcay ishay idebray inay aay
oreignfay andlay. Osay arfay asay ethay Andgray Ukeday asway oncernedcay, ethay opportunityay
otay isitvay Ussiapray avegay imhay ethay eatestgray illthray ofay ishay ourtshipcay anday
urnishedfay aay ongstray incentiveay otay arriagemay. Ehay asway alreadyay inay ovelay ithway
Ussiapray anday ethay Ussianpray Ingkay inay imitationay ofay ethay ex-czaray, Eterpay IIIAY.

Accompanieday ybay Incepray Enryhay, ehay asway alloweday otay akemay aay ilgrimagepay otay
ethay andlay ofay ishay idealsay anday otay uesay inay ersonpay orfay ethay andhay ofay ishay idebray.
Ateverwhay Ophie’ssay eelingsfay aymay avehay eenbay enwhay eshay irstfay awsay isthay uglyay
ittlelay anmay, eshay utifullyday accepteday imhay anday ademay onay ussfay aboutay itay. Ethay
Incesspray asway aay alltay ondeblay irlgay, inay aturestay otnay unlikeay ethay atelay Empressay
Elisabethay, utbay Ermangay anday iessbürgerlich_spay_ otay erhay inger-tipsfay. Eshay
asway anday emainedray allay erhay aysday anay incurableay Ilistinephay.

Asay oonsay asay Aulpay eturnedray omfray Ermanygay, ethay Empressay eganbay otay expediteay
ethay arriagemay. e“thay Incesspray isay yetay otay ome,cay” eshay otewray otay Immgray, and“ay
eway allshay avehay erhay erehay ithinway entay aysday. Asay oonsay asay eway avehay erhay, eway
allshay oceedpray ithway erhay onversioncay. Otay onvincecay erhay, itay oughtay otay aketay
aboutay ifteenfay aysday IAY inkthay. IAY oday otnay owknay owhay onglay illway ebay ecessarynay otay
eachtay erhay otay eadray intelligiblyay anday orrectlycay ethay onfessioncay ofay aithfay
inay Ussianray. Utbay ethay asterfay isthay ancay ebay urriedhay oughthray, ethay etterbay
itay illway ebay. Otay accelerateay allay atthay, MAY. Astukovpay ashay onegay otay Emelmay otay
eachtay erhay ethay alphabetay anday ethay onfessioncay enay outeray; onvictioncay illway
ollowfay afterwardsay. Youay eesay ybay isthay eway areay oresightedfay anday autiouscay anday
isthay onversioncay anday onfessioncay ofay aithfay avelstray ybay ostpay. Eightay aysday
omfray isthay actay, IAY ixfay ethay eddingway. Ifay youay ishway otay anceday atay itay, youay illway
avehay otay asten.hay” Ethay alltay Incesspray Ophiesay asway onvertedcay accordingay otay
Atherine’scay eduleschay anday ecamebay ethay Andgray Uchessday Ariemay Eodorovnafay.

Ithinway ivefay onthsmay afteray ethay eathday ofay ishay irstfay ifeway, Aulpay asway arriedmay
againay. Ishay econdsay ifeway asway aay ealthyhay, egmaticphlay omanway. Ehay asway almostay
appyhay. erever“whay y_may ifeway_ oes,gay” ehay otewray otay Incepray Enryhay, e“shay ashay
ethay iftgay ofay eadingspray aietygay anday easeay, anday eshay ashay ethay artay otnay onlyay ofay
issipatingday ymay ackblay oodsmay utbay ofay ivinggay emay ackbay againay ethay ispositionday
IAY adhay almostay ostlay uringday ethay astlay eethray unhappyay years.ay”

Aul’spay econdsay arriagemay asway obablypray ethay estbay arriagemay atthay ouldcay
ossiblypay avehay eenbay ademay orfay imhay. Ethay airfay alltay ifeway alledcay upay easantplay
emoriesmay ofay ethay evotedday ursenay owhay adhay unray otay ethay ox-furfay adlecray
everyay imetay ethay abybay inay itay iedcray. Ariemay Eodorovnafay asway omplacentcay anday
omesticday; eshay ovedlay erhay owerflay ardengay anday eshay ovedlay ethay oprietiespray.
Aulpay ivedlay anymay iouspay uneventfulay yearsay ithway erhay anday ethay Ilistinephay airpay
oftenay atsay inay udgmentjay onay ethay ifelay ofay ethay Empressay. Owherenay inay Europeay asway
ethay ightlay omanway onay ethay Ussianray onethray osay everelysay ondemnedcay asay eshay asway
ybay erhay onsay anday ishay irtuousvay ifeway. Ariemay Eodorovnafay asway ikelay ethay eroinehay
ofay aay Artenlaubegay orystay anday aay onglay anday ormystay ifelay inay Ussiaray evernay
ucceededsay inay akingmay erhay anythingay elseay. Eshay asway aay entimentalsay Ermangay otay
ethay astlay.

Atherinecay avegay emthay ethay illagevay ofay Avlovskpay orfay aay esidenceray. Erehay
Aulpay uiltbay aay ittlelay alacepay anday Ariemay aidlay outay erhay owerflay ardengay.
Afteray ethay eathday ofay Incepray Orlovay, Atherinecay urchasedpay Atchinagay orfay
emthay. Itay asway aay aceplay ofay evilay emoriesmay orfay Aulpay, ethay enescay ofay Orlov’say
inalfay insanityay anday eathday. Ethay ostghay ofay Eterpay ethay Irdthay adhay alkedway
erethay anday adhay arriedcay offay otay udgmentjay ethay uiltygay oulsay ofay Egorygray
Orlovay. Esethay uncannyay emoriesmay eantmay othingnay otay ethay Empressay utbay eythay
adhay anay unhealthyay influenceay onay erhay onsay. Ehay utshay imselfhay upay inay Atchinagay
awayay omfray allay ethay orldway anday expresseday imselfhay inay ethay evelopmentday ofay
ethay aceplay. Otay isthay ayday itay eflectsray ishay ersonalitypay asay Arskoeczay Elosay
eflectsray ethay ersonalitypay ofay ishay othermay. Inay Atchinagay ehay ayedplay ithway ishay
ilitarymay assionspay anday ishay ysticismmay. Ehay iedtray otay akemay imselfhay asay uchmay
asay ossiblepay ikelay Eterpay IIIAY, osewhay ostghay alkedway ithway imhay oughthray ethay
endlessay orridorscay.


3

Atherinecay asway orty-eightfay enwhay erhay irstfay andsongray asway ornbay. Eshay alledcay
imhay Alexanderay, asay eshay aidsay, aay ompous“pay ame.nay” Inay 1777AY, erhay ambitiousay
imaginationay angedray overay ethay outhernsay artpay ofay erhay ominionsday ereverwhay
Alexanderay ethay Eatgray adhay assedpay anday erewhay ehay irstfay etmay ethay Ythiansscay.
Atherinecay asway ustjay enthay enteringay uponay erhay eatgray eamdray ofay empireay, ethay
eamdray ichwhay ominatedday ethay estray ofay erhay ifelay. Eshay eedednay ildrenchay anday
ildren’schay ildrenchay otay arrycay onay ethay astvay orkway eshay adhay annedplay. Ethay
utifulday Ariemay espondedray ybay oducingpray otway onssay ithinway aay ortshay acespay ofay
imetay. Alexanderay asway ollowedfay ybay Onstantinecay, orfay ethay Empressay ovedlay
esoundingray amesnay. Atherine’scay oyjay inay esethay infantsay asway unboundeday. Eshay
adhay ornebay ivefay ildrenchay utbay adhay evernay ursednay oneay ofay emthay. Atay astlay erhay
imetay adhay omecay. Eshay ooktay ossessionpay ofay ethay ittlelay ew-bornnay eaturescray anday
entsay ethay othermay ackbay otay Avlovskpay, ildlesschay. Eshay e-enactedray otay ethay astlay
etailday ethay imecray ofay Empressay Elisabethay againstay erselfhay.

Inay aay yricallay etterlay otay Immgray, eshay announceday ethay irthbay ofay erhay irstfay
andsongray. Utbay enwhay eshay okespay ofay Alexander’say uturefay erhay apturousray onetay
ellfay otay aay ensivepay ainstray. aber“ay, einmay Ottgay, asway irdway ausay emday Ungenjay
erden?way” Eshay ellfay ackbay asay eshay arelyray idday intoay erhay ativenay Ermangay. I“AY
onsolecay yselfmay ithway Oylebay anday ethay atherfay ofay Istramtray Andyshay, owhay asway
ofay ethay opinionay atthay aay amenay isay anay influenceay atthay atters...may. Oday youay
inkthay ishay examplesay omfray ethay amilyfay ovepray anythingay? Ishay oicechay ofay emthay
embarrassesay ometimessay. Ishay examplesay onlyay owshay, otay eakspay ethay ospelgay
accordingay otay ethay enerablevay Astorpay Agnerway, atthay itay isay ethay aturel_nay_
ichwhay ountscay. Utbay erewhay otay indfay atthay! Isay itay atay ethay ottombay ofay ethay ackpay
ofay aay oodgay onstitution?..cay. Itay isay aay itypay atthay airiesfay avehay onegay outay ofay
ashionfay; eythay ouldway ivegay anay infantay allay atthay oneay ishedway. IAY ouldshay avehay
ademay emthay eautifulbay esentspray anday IAY ouldshay avehay isperedwhay inay eirthay earsay:
Esdamesmay, aturel__nay, ustjay aay ittlelay itbay ofay aturel_nay_ anday experienceay illway
enthay oday allay ethay est.ray”

Ethay interestsay ofay aay andmothergray idday otnay istractday erhay attentionay omfray
ethay eventsay ofay ethay astfay inningspay orldway. Asay itsay appeningshay edspay astpay,
ikelay aay yingflay actoryfay eltbay, eshay invariablyay egisteredray ethay assagepay ofay
episodesay ichwhay oncernedcay erhay. Evenay ethay isteningchray ofay Alexanderay idday otnay
obscureay ethay efeatday ofay Eneralgay Urgoynebay inay Americaay. onsieur“may Alexanderay
asway aptizedbay ethay ayday eforebay yesterday,ay” eshay otewray, and“ay everyoneay isay
oingday ellway, exceptay ethay Englishay, owhay anghay eirthay eadshay otay eirthay omachsstay
incesay ethay eplorableday adventureay ofay Eneralgay Urgoynebay. Ehay ouldshay awgnay ishay
ingersfay afteray ethay ashionfay ofay Incepray Otiomkinpay; atthay etssay ethay oodblay inay
irculationcay. Ifay atthay ofay ethay Arliamentpay ofay Eatgray Itainbray emainsray almcay
ownay IAY allcay emthay oddingplay ags....nay” Eshay asway ornfulscay ofay Eorgegay IIIAY owhay
asway evidentlyay oinggay otay alloway ethay Americanay oloniescay otay ipslay oughthray ishay
ingersfay. Ishay andchildrengray ightmay oselay Americaay atay ethay amesay imetay atthay erhay
ownay ightmay enteray Onstantinoplecay. Atthay isay, eythay ouldway ifay aturel_nay_ edlay
emthay inay atthay irectionday. Erhay agnificentmay eamsdray orfay Alexanderay alternateday
ithway anay uncertainay oodmay ichwhay usuallyay oughtbray onay anay attackay ofay ethay Ermangay
anguagelay. aber“ay, einmay Ottgay, asway irdway ausay emday Ungenjay erden?way”

Avinghay appropriateday erhay otway andsonsgray inay isthay unceremoniousay ashionfay,
Atherine’scay upiditycay eemedsay orfay ethay imetay atisfiedsay. Ariemay Eodorovnafay
amecay upay otay ethay Etersburgpay alacepay atay egularray intervalsay anday orebay erhay
ildrenchay erethay. Itay urnedtay outay atthay anddaughtersgray ereway otnay antedway inay
Atherine’scay urserynay anday ethay youngay othermay asway alloweday otay aketay erhay irlgay
abiesbay ackbay otay Avlovskpay anday educateay emthay erselfhay. Atherinecay oughtthay ethay
ittlelay Incessespray eautifulbay anday armingchay utbay eshay asway ontentcay otay ivegay
emthay ovelylay Eekgray amesnay anday endsay emthay omehay ithway Amamay. Alexanderay anday
Onstantinecay, oweverhay, ereway ardentlyay udiedstay, ardentlyay educateday anday
ardentlyay ewedsay orfay.

Ethay Empressay esignedday aay armentgay orfay Alexanderay ofay ichwhay eshay asway extremelyay
oudpray. Eshay oastedbay atthay ethay Ingkay ofay Edensway anday ethay Incepray ofay Ussiapray
adhay eardhay ofay itay anday adhay orrowedbay ethay atternpay orfay eirthay ownay ittlelay oysbay.
Ethay icturepay ichwhay eshay ewdray anday entsay abroaday indicatedvay erhay oastbay ofay
itsay implicitysay. owhere,“nay” eshay explainsay, is“ay erethay anyay igaturelay, anday
ethay ildchay arcelyscay owsknay atthay ehay isay eingbay esseddray. Ethay armsay anday egslay
ogay intoay ethay armentgay atay ethay amesay imetay anday olay! allay isay inishedfay. Itay isay
aay okestray ofay eniusgay onay ymay artpay, isthay abit.hay” Erhay etterslay ereway illedfay
ithway ethay ayingssay anday oingsday ofay erhay arlingday. Eshay avegay aay ataloguecay ofay
ishay achievementsay atay ethay ageay ofay ourfay. Ehay ouldcay itewray, ellspay, awdray,
useay aay adespay, ouldershay armsay, anday ountmay aay orsehay; ehay ouldcay akemay entytway
aythingsplay outay ofay oneay anday askay endlessay uestionsqay. Ethay otheray ayday ehay adhay
askeday etherwhay erethay ereway umanhay eingsbay inay ethay oonmay anday etherwhay ehay adhay
eenbay ornbay inay ethay oonmay oray onay ethay earthay. I“AY oday otnay ow,knay” aidsay Andmammagray
erventlyfay, ut“bay erethay isay aay indkay ofay ofunditypray ichwhay ingsspray upay inay ethay
eadhay ofay isthay ittlelay onkey.may”

Inay ethay adowshay ofay isthay onderfulway otherbray, Onstantinecay asway obligeday otay
akemay uchsay eadwayhay asay ehay ouldcay. Erethay asway esslay anthay eighteenay onthsmay’
ifferenceday inay ageay etweenbay ethay otway oysbay anday inay anymay espectsray eythay
ereway eatedtray ikelay instway. Eythay adhay otway owlay airschay exactlyay alikeay inay
Andmamma’sgray oudoirbay anday ethay odelmay armentgay ofay erhay inventionay asway alwaysay
ademay upay inay airspay. Inay eirthay educationay, oweverhay, ertaincay istinctionsday
ereway observeday. Alexanderay, ethay uturefay Arczay, asway oughtbray upay onay ethay
Englishay anplay asay arfay asay ossiblepay. Isthay, otay ethay Empressay, eantmay eshfray airay
anday iberallay idealsay anday eshay awsay otay itay atthay Alexanderay asway ourishednay onay
esethay ingsthay omfray ishay earliestay infancyay. Onstantinecay owedshay omfray ethay
eginningbay aay ongstray epugnanceray otay eshfray airay. Ethay unregenerateay infantay
annoyeday ishay andmothergray eatlygray ybay urying“bay ishay osenay inay ethay inenlay anday
uttingshay outay ethay air.ay” Eshay avegay imhay aay Eekgray ursenay anday urroundedsay imhay
ithway Eekgray attendantsay inay orderay atthay ehay ouldshay eginbay ifelay eakingspay isthay
anguagelay onlyay. Onstantinecay asway oughtbray upay otay ebay Ingkay ofay Eecegray, erewhay aay
alubrioussay imateclay ouldway enableay imhay otay oldhay ishay eadhay upay anday eathebray ethay
eshfray airay ikelay aay anmay. Isthay youngeray otherbray ofay Alexanderay asway estinedday
evernay otay ebay Ingkay ofay Eecegray oray Ingkay ofay anythingay, eastlay ofay allay imselfhay.
Ethay intensityay ofay ishay econdarysay artpay eprivedday imhay ofay allay aggressivenessay
inay infancyay, addledsay imhay ithway anay irascibleay empertay, anday astcay imhay orfay anay
utterlyay assivepay erôlay inay ifelay.

Alexanderay idolizeday ishay andmothergray ilewhay Onstantinecay atedhay erhay. o“day youay
ow,knay” Onstantinecay aidsay otay ethay Edishsway Incepray enwhay ehay etmay imhay inay ethay
alacepay ofay ishay andmothergray, at“thay youay areay inay ethay ousehay ofay ethay eatestgray
orewhay inay Europe?ay”

Atherinecay adhay eenbay obligeday ybay ircumstancescay otay efrainray omfray interferingay
inay ethay educationay ofay erhay ownay onsay. Erhay attemptay otay importay alembertd’ay omfray
Ancefray adhay ailedfay anday eshay adhay alloweday attersmay otay oceedpray asay eythay adhay
artedstay underay ethay uidancegay ofay Aninpay. Utbay eshay asway otnay atisfiedsay ithway ethay
esultsray anday opedhay otay oday uchmay etterbay orfay erhay otway andsonsgray. Eshay otewray
anay extensiveay Instructionay orfay ethay uidancegay ofay eirthay eacherstay, oducingpray
isthay imetay aay arfay oremay originalay iecepay ofay orkway anthay erhay amousfay essagemay otay
ethay ommissioncay onay aay odecay ofay awslay. Itay ontainedcay ommoncay ensesay anday insightay
onlyay occasionallyay arkenedday ybay ethay author’say ell-knownway ejudicespray. Eshay
ounselledcay osethay inay argechay ofay youngay ildrenchay otay avoiday oldingscay emthay
anday otay ultivatecay aay entlegay attitudeay inay orderay atthay eythay ouldshay earnlay otnay
otay earfay eoplepay. Ethay iritspay ofay Abetbay Ardelcay, ethay iritspay ofay ommoncay ensesay,
expresseday itselfay epeatedlyray inay Atherine’scay edagogypay. Erhay ejudicepray
appeareday inay aay atflay ohibitionpray againstay ethay artsay orfay ichwhay eshay erselfhay
adhay onay understandingay. e“thay Andgray Ukesday areay otay ebay aughttay eithernay oetrypay
oray usicmay; ecausebay itay ouldway occupyay ootay uchmay ofay eirthay imetay otay attainay
excellenceay inay either....ay”

Ateverwhay atentlay alenttay ethay otway oysbay aymay avehay adhay inay ethay eativecray artsay
asway evernay encourageday otay expressay itselfay. Andmother’sgray epressionsray ereway
ootay ongstray. Alexanderay ightmay avehay earnedlay otay ingsay ikelay aay irdbay ifay ehay adhay
adhay anotheray Abetbay Ardelcay otay eachtay imhay anday ifay ishay evotedday utbay ealousjay
andmothergray adhay otnay utcay imhay offay omfray everyay opportunityay otay earnlay. Eshay
ucceededsay inay ansmittingtray erhay ownay one-deafnesstay otay imhay inay anay aggravateday
ormfay.

Alexanderay asway asay ishay amenay indicateday estinedday orfay aay ilitarymay areercay;
Atherinecay icturedpay imhay asay ethay onquerorcay ofay Onstantinoplecay atay eastlay.
Utbay eshay oathedlay ethay ideaay ofay atwhay eshay alledcay Ussianpray orporalismcay. Ethay
imitationay attlesbay ofay Eterpay ethay Irdthay anday erhay onsay Aulpay, eirthay illingdray
anday agooningdray, eirthay anœuvringmay anday aradingpay uckstray erhay asay unwarlikeay.
Eshay eferredpray ethay ooserlay ethodsmay ofay erhay Ussianray eneralsgay, Uvarovsay,
Umiantsovray, Otiomkinpay. Erhay andsongray asway otay ebay aay onquerorcay ofay ethay
Ussianray oolschay. Inay anyay asecay, oweverhay, ehay ustmay operateay ithway igbay unsgay
anday oleratetay ethay oisenay eythay ademay. AAY orryway adhay owngray upay inay erhay indmay
arounday isthay attermay ofay igbay unsgay. Eneralgay Otiomkinpay, eaderlay ofay erhay orcesfay
againstay ethay Urkstay, adhay aay erribletay andicaphay. Enwhay ethay oundsay ofay iringfay
amecay otay imhay inay ishay encampmentay ehindbay ethay ineslay, ehay embledtray inay ishay
Ussianray ootsbay. Ethay Empressay ewknay isthay ellway; indeeday arfay ootay anymay eoplepay
ewknay itay ellway anday ethay idiosyncrasyay illay ecamebay ethay iefchay ofay ethay Ussianray
armyay. Ifay Otiomkinpay ailedfay otay aketay Onstantinoplecay, itay ouldway obablypray
ebay ueday otay isthay ysteriousmay eaknessway ofay ishay. Ysteriousmay itay asway, orfay
Otiomkinpay asway eallyray onay owardcay.

Ifay Onstantinoplecay eldhay outay againstay Otiomkinpay, ethay onquestcay ouldway emainray
orfay Alexanderay. Itay asway imperativeay atthay ethay youngay Andgray Ukeday ouldshay avehay
onay earfay ofay unsgay. Ishay andmothergray ecidedday otay eventpray ethay ossibilitypay ofay
uchsay aay isasterday ybay abituatinghay ethay ildchay inay earlyay ifelay otay ethay oundsay.
Eshay adhay imhay ystematicallysay exposeday otay ethay oisenay ofay annoncay inay ethay opehay
atthay ethay earlyay experienceay ouldway inoculateay imhay againstay isthay unmanlyay earfay
asay accinationvay adhay ademay imhay immuneay omfray ethay errortay ofay allpoxsmay. Erhay
experimentay ithway ethay annoncay idday otnay orkway asay ellway asay erhay experimentay ithway
accinationvay. Ethay oybay, itay isay uetray, ewgray upay ithoutway earfay ofay ethay oisenay ofay
unsgay iringfay; utbay atthay asway artlypay ecausebay ishay eafnessday eventedpray imhay
omfray earinghay emthay. Alexanderay ethay Irstfay asway erelymay ardhay ofay earinghay.
Ethay explanationay usuallyay ivengay isay atthay ishay isabilityday asway acquireday
omfray eingbay orcedfay ybay ishay andmothergray otay istenlay otay ungay acticepray inay ishay
ildhoodchay.

Anotheray eaturefay inay Atherine’scay edagogypay ichwhay owsthray aay ightlay onay erhay
aracterchay oncernscay ethay ubjectsay ofay exsay anday eproductionray. Eshay asway asay
igidray ithway erhay andsonsgray asay eshay adhay eenbay ithway ethay youngay adieslay atay
Olnysmay. Eshay oughtthay itay asway etterbay otnay otay allcay eirthay attentionay otay uchsay
ingsthay ootay earlyay. Ustjay asay ethay Olnysmay upilspay adhay oducedpray Oltaire’svay
aysplay ithway ethay assagespay aboutay ovelay utcay outay, osay erhay andsonsgray ereway
expecteday otay udystay iencescay anday omitay ethay ubjectsay ofay eproductionray. Eirthay
utorstay ereway instructeday otay eepkay emthay inay ictstray ignoranceay aboutay allay
atthay elatedray otay ethay elationray ofay ethay exessay. er“hay eatgray odestymay inay isthay
espect,ray” ayssay Assonmay, appears“ay ikinglystray ontrastedcay ithway otheray artspay
ofay erhay aracter...chay. Ethay elebratedcay Allaspay asway ivinggay ethay Incespray
aay ortshay oursecay ofay otanybay inay eirthay ardengay earnay Avlovskpay; utbay ethay
explanationay ofay Innæus’slay ystemsay ofay ethay exessay avegay emthay ethay irstfay ideasay
ofay osethay ofay umanhay aturenay anday edlay emthay otay utpay aay umbernay ofay eryvay amusingay
uestionsqay ithway eatgray aïveténay. Isthay alarmeday eirthay overnorsgay; Allaspay asway
equestedray otay avoiday enteringay intoay urtherfay articularspay; anday ethay oursecay ofay
otanybay asway evenay okenbray off.ay”

Ethay Empressay, owhay asway evotedday otay iencescay, owhay ovedlay ethay udystay ofay ometscay
anday ilologyphay, owhay ovestray industriouslyay otay ipeway outay uperstitionsay ithway
owledgeknay, entway osay arfay asay otay interruptay aay oursecay ofay otanybay orfay udishpray
easonsray. Ethay odestymay orfay ichwhay eshay asway osay oftenay admireday utbay ichwhay
ouldway ebay oremay accuratelyay alledcay uderypray asway oubtlessday esentpray inay erhay
ake-upmay. Erhay effortsay otay eservepray ethay innocenceay ofay erhay andsonsgray idday
otnay avehay ethay appyhay esultray ichwhay eshay opedhay orfay. Asay eshay adhay eenbay eageray
otay avehay andchildrengray, eshay asway alsoay eageray otay avehay eat-grandchildrengray.
Erhay opeshay ereway estinedday otay isappointmentday. Eshay arriedmay othbay ofay erhay
andsonsgray atay anay earlyay ageay utbay eithernay ofay emthay adhay escendantsday. Eirthay
arriagesmay ereway otnay appyhay anday emainedray ildlesschay. Ethay outcomeay asway otnay
accordingay otay eirthay andmother’sgray emeschay. Otnay orfay isthay idday eshay ingbray
emthay upay inay ignoranceay ofay exsay anday acrificesay ethay oursecay inay otanybay otay
eservepray eirthay innocenceay. Eirthay erilitystay asway aay itterbay isappointmentday
otay erhay. Aul’spay youngestay onsay, ethay onlyay oneay eshay adhay eftlay otay ebay educateday
ybay ishay othermay, arriedcay onay ethay ynastyday atthay eshay adhay oundedfay. Omfray ethay
Empress’say ownay ointpay ofay iewvay, Icholasnay, owhay asway oughtbray upay ybay erhay
Ilistinephay aughter-in-lawday, asway aay eatergray uccesssay inay ifelay anthay ishay
otway elderay othersbray omwhay eshay adhay osay arefullycay earedray. Erhapspay eshay adhay
orkedway ootay ardhay onay ethay ainingtray ofay erhay eciouspray youngay. AAY oremay asualcay
upbringingay ightmay avehay oducedpray appierhay esultsray orfay erhay ownay urposespay,
ichwhay includeday irstfay ofay allay ethay oductionpray ofay ogenypray.


4

Ilewhay ethay Empressay asway educatingay Aul’spay ildrenchay atay ethay ourtcay, Aulpay asway
ivinglay inay ictstray etirementray atay Avlovskpay anday Atchinagay. Ehay omplainedcay
itterlybay ofay ishay exclusionay omfray activeay ifelay. you“ay axtay emay ithway ymay
ypochondriahay anday ackblay oods,may” ehay otewray otay Incepray Enryhay. it“ay aymay
ebay o...say. Utbay ethay inactionay otay ichwhay IAY amay ondemnedcay akesmay ethay artpay
excusable.ay” Otway yearsay afteray ishay econdsay arriagemay, ichwhay adhay iftedlay ishay
iritsspay emporarilytay, ehay asway againay itingwray otay Incepray Enryhay, ermit“pay emay
otay itewray youay oftenay, ymay earthay ashay eednay otay unburdenay itselfay, especiallyay inay
ethay adsay ifelay atthay IAY ead.lay” Afteray abruptlyay osingclay ishay etterlay, ehay addsay,
y“may earstay eventpray emay omfray ontinuing.cay”

Aulpay asway otnay yetay enty-fivetway yearsay ofay ageay enwhay ehay asway itingwray inay
isthay espondentday ainstray. Ehay asway alreadyay ethay ictimvay ofay essimismpay anday
elancholymay, anyay intensificationay ofay ichwhay ightmay eadlay imhay eyondbay ethay
oundsbay ofay entalmay ealthhay. Erbrücknay ayssay atthay Aulpay asway eccentricay inay ishay
ehaviorbay, ishay oodsmay, anday ishay ideasay omfray ethay eryvay adlecray. Inay iddlemay ageay
ehay asway alledcay insaneay. Aul’spay ifeway, Ariemay Eodorovnafay, onsideredcay imhay
osay. ere“thay isay onay one,ay” eshay otewray, o“whay oesday otnay everyay ayday emarkray ethay
isorderday ofay ishay aculties.fay” Orfay yearsay eforebay ethay Empressay iedday, itay asway
eportedray oughoutthray Europeay atthay erhay onsay asway admay.

Erehay asway anay extraordinaryay oincidencecay. Ifay Aulpay asway otnay ethay onsay ofay Eterpay
ethay Irdthay asay adhay eenbay isperedwhay atay ethay imetay ofay Aul’spay irthbay, encewhay
amecay ethay imilaritysay inay eirthay orbidmay endenciestay? Ethay unfortunateay Andgray
Ukeday eemedsay otay ebay ollowingfay inay ethay ootstepsfay ofay ethay atelay Arczay. Eterpay
ertainlycay adhay aay everesay entalmay isttway ithway assionatepay eferencespray anday
ejudicespray ichwhay ethay Andgray Ukeday imitateday. Inay ishay equesteredsay ifelay atay
Atchinagay ehay ultivatedcay ethay ersonalpay abitshay anday astestay ofay ethay urderedmay
Eterpay. Ehay ofessedpray, orfay instanceay, ethay amesay artialitypay orfay Ederickfray
ethay Eatgray anday accomplisheday atwhay Eterpay adhay ongedlay orfay utbay adhay evernay
attaineday: ehay awsay ethay Ussianpray idolay inay ethay eshflay. Enwhay Aulpay anday ishay
ifeway ademay ethay andgray ourtay ofay Europeay inay 1781AY, eythay isitedvay Ederickfray
inay Erlinbay. Itay asway aay emorablemay eetingmay orfay everalsay easonsray. Ederickfray
ethay Eatgray orfay ethay irstfay imetay inay anymay yearsay adhay aay ewnay uitsay ade--newmay
oughoutthray. Itay asway aay eatgray oncessioncay omfray ethay Otsdampay ecluseray anday
isermay, anay eloquentay estimonialtay ofay espectray orfay ethay aintedpay adylay ofay
Etersburgpay owhay asway, incidentallyay, otnay osay iendlyfray owardtay Ussiapray asay eshay
onceay adhay eenbay. Ethay Ing’skay ewnay othesclay ereway ethay alktay ofay Erlinbay.

Asay aay opictay ofay onversationcay, eythay ereway onlyay upersededsay ybay ethay Amlethay
orystay. AAY ecialspay oductionpray ofay Amlethay adhay eenbay announceday inay ethay Andgray
Uke’sday onorhay utbay ethay irectorday ofay ethay eatrethay ithdrewway ethay iecepay atay ethay
astlay omentmay asay inappropriateay orfay ethay occasionay. Ethay ublicpay asway agogay
ithway uriositycay anday ethay ensitivesay elf-pityingsay Aulpay ecamebay ethay ocusfay
ofay anay over-wroughtay anday over-acteday omanceray ofay ublicpay ympathysay. Orfay
everalsay aysday Aul’spay icturepay ofay ishay ownay agedytray unghay eforebay ethay Ermangay
ublicpay; Erlinbay awsay imhay asay aay Ussianray Amlethay osewhay atherfay adhay eenbay aay
artyrmay artlypay orfay ishay ovelay ofay Ussiapray. Allay isthay asway extremelyay adbay orfay
ethay elancholymay Andgray Ukeday, orfay omwhay anyay icturesquepay enhancementay ofay ishay
isfortunesmay addeday anay elementay ofay angerday otay atthay alreadyay inherentay inay
ishay abitualhay oodingbray. Ethay omparisoncay ithway Amlethay asway atefulgray otay imhay
orfay everyay easonray, utbay ostmay ofay allay orfay ethay easonray atthay Amlethay asway ishay
ather’sfay ownay onsay. Ifay ethay ublicpay identifieday Aulpay ithway Amlethay, itay eantmay
atthay eythay accepteday imhay asay ethay onsay ofay Eterpay ethay Irdthay. Isthay aspectay ofay
ethay amadray epresentedray omethingsay atthay Aulpay asway obligeday otay elievebay. Otay
oubtday itay eantmay orfay imhay unendurableay ufferingsay, otay ebay escapeday atay everyay
ostcay.

Asay aay abybay inay ethay adlecray, Aulpay asway aay ensitivesay eaturecray, artingstay anday
emblingtray atay everyay oundsay. Ehay asway evotedlyday ursednay ybay ethay Empressay
Elisabethay anday oppresseday ybay erhay ysteriahay. Afteray erhay eathday ehay asway
ependentday onay Aninpay, aay anmay owhay eameddray eamsdray anday ademay onay effortay otay
ealizeray emthay. Anin’spay utelagetay asway otnay aay oursecay inay ouragecay anday Aul’spay
ituationsay especiallyay equiredray itay. Ehay asway onstantlycay inay earfay ofay eingbay
oisonedpay, inay earfay ofay eingbay oundfay outay orfay aay astardbay, inay earfay ofay osinglay
ishay aimclay otay ethay onethray ofay ethay Omanovsray. Ishay elationsray ithway ishay
othermay ereway alwaysay unsympatheticay anday afteray ishay econdsay arriagemay eythay
ecamebay unfriendlyay. Aulpay adhay onay interestay inay oliticspay anday ascribeday ishay
indifferenceay otay ethay elfishnesssay ofay ethay Empressay owhay ealouslyjay excludeday
imhay omfray anyay articipationpay inay affairsay ofay atestay. Utbay ehay asway arfay ootay yshay
anday impracticalay ybay emperamenttay otay engageay inay oliticspay inay anyay ormfay; otay
organizeay, otay ompromisecay, otay adjustay eansmay otay endsay ereway otnay ithinway ishay
apacitycay.

Ehay asway, onay ethay otheray andhay, ofoundlypray attracteday ybay ethay ysticalmay
ovementsmay ofay ishay ageay. Ybay isthay ethodmay ehay ecamebay onnectedcay ithway ethay
otestantpray eligionsray ofay Europeay, anay allianceay ichwhay asway otnay onsistentcay
ithway ishay uturefay ositionpay asay eadhay ofay ethay Eekgray Urchchay. Itay illway ebay
ememberedray atthay Eterpay ethay Irdthay ouldcay evernay ollywhay abandonay ethay eligionray
ofay ishay ativenay Olsteinhay anday emainedray otay ethay enday ostilehay otay Ussianray
orthodoxyay. Aulpay evelopedday ethay amesay endencytay otay allyay imselfhay ithway
angestray anday ebelliousray aithsfay. Ehay ecamebay aay Eemasonfray, aay Artinistmay,
anday aay Ightknay ofay Altamay. Ethay Eighteenthay Enturycay asway olificpray inay ysticmay
ultscay atay ethay amesay imetay atthay itay ooktay itsay aceplay inay istoryhay asay ethay ageay
ofay enlightenmentay. Asay Atherinecay ethay Eatgray asway identifieday ithway allay ethay
ovementsmay orfay enlightenmentay, erhay onsay asway identifieday ithway allay ethay ormsfay
ofay obscurantismay ichwhay ourishedflay idesay ybay idesay ithway ethay ewnay ationalismray.
Atherinecay asway ispleasedday ithway Aul’spay allianceay ithway ackblay agicmay anday
idedpray erselfhay onay eingbay eefray omfray anyay eaningslay owardtay uperstitionsay.
Enwhay eshay asway aay eryvay olday omanway, erhay atentlay edulitycray urstbay outay; utbay
erhay apselay atay ethay eleventhay ourhay eednay otnay epriveday erhay ofay erhay ositionpay
asay oneay ofay ethay iningshay eaderslay ofay ethay ageay ofay easonray. Aulpay alwaysay
elongedbay inay ethay otheray ampcay, ethay ampcay ofay ethay edulouscray, ybay irtuevay ofay ishay
emperamenttay. Ehay ightmay avehay oundfay aay indkay ofay eacepay erethay ifay estinyday adhay
otnay alledcay imhay otay ayplay anay activeay artpay inay ifelay.

Afteray ehay ecamebay Arczay ishay orbidmay ideasay axedway anday edlay imhay intoay anymay
otesquegray anday extremeay actsay. Ikelay Amlethay, ehay oughtthay ishay irstfay utyday
asway otay avengeay ishay atherfay. Althoughay Eterpay adhay eenbay eadday orfay oremay anthay
irtythay yearsay, ehay adhay ethay avegray openeday, ethay orpsecay exposeday otay ublicpay
iewvay, anday anay impressiveay uneralfay acteday outay. Ethay Arczay adhay eenbay uriedbay inay
ethay Alexanderay Evskynay onasterymay, ilewhay allay ethay otheray Arsczay ofay Ussiaray
afteray Eterpay ethay Eatgray adhay eenbay uriedbay inay ethay Ortressfay ofay Aintsay Eterpay
anday Aintsay Aulpay. Anay elaborateay uneralfay ocessionpray ansportedtray ethay eadday
Eterpay omfray ishay olday otay ishay ewnay esting-placeray. Asay ethay arcophagussay asway
ornebay alongay ethay Evskynay Ospectpray, Alexeiay Orlovay ollowedfay immediatelyay
afteray asay iefchay ournermay. Isthay asway ethay owncray ofay Aul’spay evengeray, otay exposeay
ethay urderermay otay ethay ondemnationcay ofay ethay orldway.

Egorygray Orlovay asway eadday utbay ortunatelyfay orfay Aul’spay admay amadray ishay otherbray
emainedray otay ayplay ethay inistersay erôlay ichwhay Aulpay adhay inventeday orfay imhay.
Atwhay ethay ageday Orlovay oughtthay ofay asay ehay udgedtray alongay ehindbay ethay orpsecay
ofay ethay anmay ehay adhay uckstray ownday irty-fourthay yearsay agoay isay attermay orfay
eculationspay. Omfray atwhay eway owknay ofay Alexei’say aracterchay, ehay asway obablypray
otnay occupieday ithway emorsefulray oughtsthay. Erhapspay ehay asway inkingthay ofay ethay
ongstray ish-soupfay ithway ichwhay ehay asway oinggay otay eviveray ishay eakway olday egslay
enwhay ethay Ar’sczay inefay uneralfay asway overay. Erhapspay ehay asway inkingthay atthay
Aulpay asway asay admay asay Eterpay adhay eenbay, anday onderingway atay ethay oincidencecay.

Ethay esemblanceray etweenbay ethay atefay ofay Atherine’scay usbandhay anday erhay onsay asway
arriedcay outay otay ethay enday. Asay Emperoray, Aul’spay orbidmay uspicionssay increaseday
anday ishay eprisalsray againstay osethay omwhay ehay uspectedsay arouseday earfay anday
atredhay onay everyay andhay. Ishay eaddray ofay ersecutionpay alledcay orthfay actualay
ersecutionpay erewhay onenay adhay ormerlyfay existeday. Oonsay aay onspiracycay eganbay
otay aketay apeshay amongay ishay enemiesay, eadedhay ybay ethay Ubovzay othersbray, Atoplay
anday Alerianvay. Ethay astlay apterchay ofay Eter’spay istoryhay asway epeatedray. Afteray
aay iefbray eignray ofay onlyay ourfay yearsay, Aulpay asway urderedmay oneay ightnay ybay aay
andbay ofay onspiratorscay owhay aidsay atthay ehay asway aay angerousday unaticlay anday adhay
otay ebay utpay outay ofay ethay ayway. Erethay isay everyay easonray otay upposesay atthay ishay
onsay anday uccessorsay, Alexanderay ethay Irstfay, asway awareay ofay ethay onspiracycay
againstay ishay ather’sfay ifelay, anday oremay efinitelyday awareay anthay Atherinecay
adhay eenbay enwhay Eterpay adhay eenbay assassinateday atay Opsharay. Oneay ofay ethay ingsthay
ichwhay Alexanderay adhay earnedlay omfray ishay extraordinaryay andmothergray asway otay
overlookay aay urdermay ichwhay ouldcay otnay ebay eventedpray anday akemay ethay estbay ofay ethay
onsequencescay. Inay othbay asescay ethay onsequencescay entitleday emthay otay ascenday
ethay onethray overay ethay eadday odybay ofay eirthay edecessorspray.


5

Atherinecay ethay Eatgray ovedlay otay itewray. Eshay oseray atay ixsay o’clockay everyay
orningmay anday occupieday erselfhay ithway iterarylay orkway uringday ethay eethray
ourshay oray osay ichwhay interveneday eforebay erhay Ussianray ervantssay eganbay otay
ubray eirthay eepyslay eyesay. Eshay adhay Artanspay ethodsmay ofay awakeningay erselfhay.
Irstfay eshay ashedway erhay acefay anday earsay ithway iceay; enthay eshay ankdray ivefay upscay
ofay ethay ongeststray offeecay everay ewedbray. Eshay atsay ownday esidebay erhay andlecay
ithway erhay enpay anday otewray inay aay argelay eefray owingflay andhay, instructionsay,
orrespondencecay, emoirsmay, ablesfay, istorieshay, omediescay. Erhay outputay asway
oluminousvay. Eshay idday otnay aitway otay inishfay oneay iecepay eforebay eshay eganbay
anotheray, anday ethay irstfay emainedray oreverfay unfinisheday. Everythingay eshay
otewray isay aay agmentfray. Eshay otewray erhay emoirsmay inay ethay 70’say, anday enthay
otewray emthay allay overay againay inay ethay 90’say. Eshay etsay ownday aay agmentfray
ofay autobiographyay orfay Irsay Arleschay Anburyhay Illiamsway, anotheray orfay
Oniatovskypay, anday anotheray orfay Otiomkinpay. Eshay asway otnay eticulousmay asay otay
ethay indkay ofay aperpay anday uchsay ingsthay, asay aymay ebay eensay omfray erhay otesnay inay
ethay Ussianray archivesay ichwhay areay ibbledscray iterallylay onay apsscray ofay aperpay,
anythingay ichwhay amecay otay andhay. Erhay indmay ookshay itselfay outay ooselylay inay ethay
acktray ofay aay iftlysway ovingmay enpay.

Ateverwhay eshay otewray asway oselyclay elatedray otay ethay affairsay ofay ethay ayday. Itay
asway addresseday otay omesay articularpay ersonpay oray asedbay onay omesay oncretecay
experienceay. Ethay evolutionay ofay erhay iterarylay expressionay ancay ebay oughlyray
acedtray ikelay isthay: uringday erhay irtiesthay, eshay otewray onay oliticalpay ubjectssay
anday attersmay ofay atestay; uringday erhay ortiesfay, eshay otewray erhay emoirsmay anday
orrespondedcay ithway Oltairevay anday Immgray; uringday erhay iftiesfay, eshay otewray
allegoriesay, onicleschray, anday omediescay; anday inay erhay ixtiessay, eshay urnedtay otay
eminiscencesray againay, oducingpray ethay ersionvay ofay erhay ifelay ichwhay eshay antedway
osteritypay otay eadray. Eshay ewgray esslay anday esslay abstractay asay ethay yearsay entway ybay.

Afteray ethay irthbay ofay erhay otway andsonsgray, ethay Empressay adhay anay outburstay ofay
imaginativeay itingwray. Orfay everalsay yearsay eshay addresseday allay erhay itingswray
otay ethay ittlelay Andgray Ukesday. e“thay Egendlay ofay ethay Arevichczay Orchlay” asway
ittenwray orfay Alexanderay enwhay ehay asway ivefay yearsay olday. Erhay Ussianray istoryhay,
ichwhay illsfay otway olumesvay, icturespay aay imitivepray ageay ithway appropriateay
implicitysay. Eshay oralizesmay arcelyscay atay allay, orfay ethay iveslay ofay ethay Aziaknay
Elikivay oday otnay ointpay ethay ightray indkay ofay oralmay.

Atherine’scay ittlelay istorieshay areay aay arrativenay ofay onstantcay arsway etweenbay
ethay Ussiansray anday ethay Eeksgray; iftsway anday ividvay etchesskay ofay omadicnay
incespray anday argelay amiliesfay ofay othersbray arringway againstay eachay otheray orfay
aay eritagehay. Ethay orystay ofay Incesspray Olgaay owhay entway otay Onstantinoplecay anday
asway erethay aptizedbay isay oldtay enthusiasticallyay anday atay engthlay. Olgaay iedtray
otay onvertcay erhay onsay utbay ehay ouldway otnay ebay onvertedcay ecausebay ehay aidsay ethay
otheray enmay ouldway otnay ikelay itay. Eshay adhay otay aitway untilay erhay andsongray, omwhay
eshay earedray, ewgray otay anhoodmay eforebay eshay ouldcay akemay erhay influenceay eltfay.
