Itay asway erhay andsongray owhay Istianizedchray Ussiaray.

Isthay egendlay asway eryvay opularpay ithway Atherinecay anday erhay andsongray Alexanderay.
Ithway erhay obesglay, ethay Empressay owedshay ethay ittlelay oybay owhay ethay ordeshay ofay
ethay Enghisgay Ankhay adhay assedpay acrossay ethay andslay ofay Ussiaray anday erewhay ethay
Ythiansscay adhay etmay ethay Eeksgray. Esethay essonslay ademay erhay intimacyay ithway
ittlelay Alexanderay ethay appiesthay ofay erhay ifelay. Eshay ollectedcay erhay itingswray
intoay aay o-calledsay Ibrarylay orfay ethay Andgray Ukesday. Otay ebay uresay, ethay ojectedpray
Ibrarylay asway evernay ompletedcay; ornay asway ethay istoryhay ofay Ussiaray oughtbray
ownday eyondbay ethay irteenththay enturycay. Osay arfay asay erhay Ussianray istoryhay asway
oncernedcay, itay asway aay itypay atthay ethay authoray eftlay onlyay aay agmentfray. Eshay adhay
aay iftgay orfay ivelylay ompactcay arrativenay anday ethay eaderray eelsfay aay istinctday
isappointmentday enwhay ethay orystay eaksbray offay uddenlysay eforebay ethay arrivalay ofay
ethay Artarstay.

Erhay aithfulnessfay otay istoryhay isay easyay otay explainay. Ethay artistay adhay oundfay
aay ewnay ovelay. Eshay adhay uddenlysay iscoveredday omedycay. Ethay Empressay adhay akentay
otay itingwray aysplay inay ethay annermay ofay Olièremay. Anay anecdoteay oftenay oldtay otay
owshay ethay affectionay existingay etweenbay Alexanderay anday ishay andmothergray ellstay
owhay ethay oybay, atay ethay ageay ofay eightay, avegay aay erformancepay ofay aay ive-actfay
omedycay omposedcay ybay Atherinecay. Inay ethay eeperday ayerslay ofay erhay emorymay ethay
orksway ofay Olièremay adhay eenbay yinglay onglay unnoticeday. Uddenlysay ethay atentlay
emoriesmay osay onglay eddedbay erethay inay orgetfulnessfay anday ilencesay eganbay otay
erminategay. Atay aboutay ethay amesay ageay ichwhay Onsieurmay Alexanderay adhay ownay
owngray otay ebay, Atherinecay adhay onceay edfay uponay ethay aysplay ofay Olièremay ecausebay
erhay overnessgay, Abetbay Ardelcay, adhay ownknay emthay allay ybay earthay. Asay eshay atsay
eachingtay erhay eight-year-olday andsongray, ethay astestay anday interestsay ofay
atthay ageay inay erhay ownay ifelay eganbay otay irstay anday assertay emselvesthay ithinway
erhay. Atherinecay asway otnay ontentcay asay Abetbay adhay eenbay otay ivegay erhay upilpay
eady-maderay omediescay oweverhay asterlymay. Eshay eferredpray otay omposecay omediescay
erselfhay orfay Alexanderay. Omptlypray eshay ellfay otay orkway anday iftlysway ereway erhay
aysplay ompletedcay. Isthay imetay erethay ereway onay agmentsfray; ethay evitybray ofay ethay
oductpray asway exactlyay uitedsay otay erhay emperamenttay. Eshay otewray evensay iecespay
inay oneay yearay, anday enthay abandoneday ethay ieldfay altogetheray, erhapspay ecausebay
ethay Urkishtay Arsway ecamebay ootay engrossingay.

Erhay omediescay allay ealday ithway oneay ubjectsay inay ethay amesay annermay. Eythay areay
atiressay onay ethay entimentalsay anday uperstitioussay aitstray ofay umanhay aturenay.
Erhay itlestay owshay owhay aithfullyfay eshay adhereday otay erhay emethay. Ethay Arlatanchay,
Ethay Upeday, Ethay Iberiansay Amanshay, Amilyfay Iscordday Oughthray Alsefay Uspicionssay,
Onay Oodgay Ithoutway Evilay ereway ethay ostmay opularpay. Eirthay otsplay anday aracterschay
owshay atthay ethay authoray isay omethingsay ofay aay ychologistpsay anday aay oodgay ealday ofay
aay atiristsay. Itay isay oticeablenay atthay ethay eaknessesway ichwhay eshay especiallyay
atirizessay areay aracteristicchay ofay ethay ehaviorbay ofay erhay onsay Aulpay.

Atay ethay imetay enwhay Atherinecay otewray erhay omediescay erethay asway onay ongerlay anyay
etensepray ofay ympathysay etweenbay ethay othermay anday onsay. Ethay isintegrationday ofay
Aul’spay aracterchay adhay ogressedpray osay arfay atthay ehay adhay ithdrawnway imselfhay
omfray allay ethay orldway exceptay osethay omwhay ishay othermay alledcay arlatanschay anday
amansshay. Ethay Empressay identifieday erhay onsay ithway allay uperstitioussay olkfay
anday astigatedcay ethay olewhay ibetray inay erhay omediescay. Eshay arelyray entionedmay
Aulpay irectlyday inay erhay emoirsmay anday erhay orrespondencecay. Inay ethay intimateay
amilyfay istoryhay ichwhay illsfay erhay etterslay otay Immgray, ishay amenay evernay
occursay. Erhay atredhay oundfay anay outletay inay erhay atiricalsay omediescay. Erehay
eshay indirectlyay exposeday ishay otoriousnay eaknessesway anday eldhay emthay upay otay
idiculeray. Eshay espisedday ishay aracterchay asay eshay espisedday ishay ookslay. Aulpay
esembledray ethay Almuckcay ypetay inay ysiquephay anday ountenancecay. Ortshay ofay
aturestay anday ub-nosedsnay asay ehay asway, ishay othermay ouldcay otnay ooklay atay imhay
ithoutway eingbay emindedray ofay ethay Altikovsay idesay ofay ishay eredityhay. Anyoneay owhay
eadsray oughthray erhay iterarylay orksway illway ebay uckstray ybay ethay umbernay ofay imestay
ethay Empressay efersray otay ethay astlyghay uglinessay ofay ethay Almuckcay ypetay. Eshay
ouldcay otnay etgay awayay omfray itay.

Ethay omediescay ofay Atherinecay ethay Eatgray ereway egardedray asay aay eatgray
ontributioncay otay ethay ampaigncay againstay obscurantismay. Eshay eppedstay
orthfay asay ethay Aintsay Eorgegay ofay enlightenmentay ikingstray ownday ethay agondray
ofay uperstitionsay. Erhay atiresay asway eveledlay againstay ethay Artinistsmay,
ethay Eemasonsfray, anday ethay Alchemistsay; eshay atteredbay atay allay oupsgray anday
organizationsay atthay adhay aay ecretsay understandingay anday alkedtay ysteriouslymay
aboutay ethay oblemspray ofay ifelay anday eathday. Ortunatelyfay orfay erhay interestay,
ichwhay adhay onay eatgray olerancetay orfay abstractionsay, aay esh-and-bloodflay
antagonistay asway aisedray upay otay imulatestay anday increaseay erhay energiesay. Ethay
amousfay Agliostrocay ecidedday otay akemay aay isitvay otay Etersburgpay, elievingbay atthay
Atherinecay ethay Eatgray ouldway avorfay ishay ultcay. Utbay ehay adhay eckonedray ithoutway
ishay Empressay. Atherinecay asway evernay iredtay ofay abusingay imhay, othbay uringday
anday afteray ishay ojournsay inay Ussiaray. Enwhay ehay asway imprisoneday inay Ancefray inay
onnectioncay ithway ethay affairay ofay ethay iamondday ecklacenay, eshay exulteday inay
ethay ostmay unbecomingay annermay. Omesay ofay erhay ongeststray anday eastlay ady-likelay
anguagelay asway ouredpay outay onay ethay eadhay ofay ethay alentedtay agicianmay, omwhay, ybay
ethay ayway, eshay adhay evernay evenay eensay. Otay Immgray, eshay otewray, I“AY avehay eadray
ethay emoirmay ofay Agliostrocay ichwhay youay avehay entsay emay anday ifay IAY adhay otnay eenbay
alreadyay ersuadedpay atthay ehay asway aay Enchfray arlatanchay, ishay emoirmay ouldway avehay
onvincedcay emay. Ehay isay aay ogueray anday ackguardblay anday ehay oughtay otay ebay anged.hay”

Eshay asway osay eatlygray interesteday inay isthay anmay atthay itay ustmay avehay ostcay erhay
aay eatgray effortay otay enyday imhay anay audienceay uringday ishay aystay inay Ussiaray. “MAY.
Agliostro,cay” eshay otewray, arrived“ay erehay atay aay eryvay avorablefay omentmay orfay
imhay, atay aay imetay enwhay anymay odgeslay ofay Eemasonsfray, infatuateday ithway ethay
inciplespray ofay Edenborgsway, esiredday ithway allay eirthay owerpay otay eesay iritsspay.
Eythay ereforethay anray otay Agliostrocay owhay aidsay atthay ehay asway inay ossessionpay ofay
allay ethay ecretssay ofay Octorday Alkfay, intimateay iendfray ofay Ukeday Ichelieuray, owhay
adhay onceay acrificedsay otay imhay inay ethay eryvay idstmay ofay Iennavay aay ackblay oat...gay.
MAY. Agliostrocay enthay oducedpray ishay arvellousmay ecretssay ofay ealinghay. Ehay
etendedpray otay awdray uick-silverqay omfray aay outygay ootfay anday asway aughtcay inay ethay
actay ofay ouringpay aay easpoonfultay ofay ercurymay intoay ethay aterway intoay ichwhay ehay
asway oinggay otay utpay ethay outygay ember...may.

ater“lay onay, ackedray ybay ebtsday, ehay ooktay efugeray inay ethay ellarcay ofay Onsieurmay
Yelaginay ..AY. erewhay ehay ankdray allay ethay ineway, ampagnechay, anday Englishay eerbay
atthay ehay ouldcay et...gay. Onsieurmay Yelaginay, annoyeday ybay ishay otherbray atray inay
ethay ellarcay anday ybay ethay oughtthay ofay allay ethay ineway, anday eerbay ..AY. avegay imhay anay
olday invalide_ay_ otay accompanyay imhay asay arfay asay Ilanmay. Isthay isay ethay istoryhay
ofay Agliostrocay inay ichwhay erethay isay othingnay exceptionallyay arvellousmay. IAY
avehay evernay eensay imhay earnay oray ar,--norfay avehay IAY adhay anyay emptationtay otay oday
osay, orfay IAY oday otnay ovelay arlatanschay. IAY assureay youay atthay Ogersonray inksthay ofay
Agliostrocay asay uchmay oray esslay anthay Oah’snay Arkay. Incepray Orlovay, ontrarycay otay
ishay ustomcay, ashay otnay ademay uchmay ofay Agliostrocay. Ehay akesmay unfay ofay imhay asay ofay
osethay owhay omfray eremay uriositycay unray otay eesay imhay, anday ehay ashay ontributedcay
utbay ittlelay otay angechay intoay ineway ethay aterway ofay ethay amelessshay artisanspay ofay
isthay oorpay evilday. Utbay incesay ethay oremay upidstay anday ignorantay ethay arlatanschay
areay ethay oremay impressionay eythay eatecray inay ethay eatgray itiescay, itay isay otay ebay
upposedsay atthay Agliostrocay illway ebay inay ishay elementay inay Aris....pay”

Omfray ethay ehemencevay ofay ethay Empress’say ondemnationcay, oneay uspectssay atthay eshay
idday otnay atestay aay actfay enwhay eshay eclaredday atthay eshay adhay onay emptationtay otay
eesay imhay. Anday eshay asway arfay omfray avinghay inishedfay ithway ethay ubjectsay. Otway ofay
erhay omediescay, Ethay Iarlay anday Ethay Upeday, ereway asedbay onay Agliostro’scay isitvay,
anday Ethay Iberiansay Amanshay asway inspireday, oughthay otnay avowedlyay, ybay ethay amesay
emethay. Everalsay ofay erhay aysplay ereway aay eatgray uccesssay enwhay oducedpray inay
Etersburgpay, anday Ethay Iarlay anday Ethay Upeday ooktay inay oremay anthay entytway ousandthay
oublesray. Ethay ublicpay asway itivatedtay ybay ethay Empress’say atiresay anday intrigueday
ybay ethay imelinesstay ofay erhay iterarylay attackay onay ethay ostmay otoriousnay
aracterchay inay Europeay.

Onay oneay askeday ethay Andgray Ukeday Aulpay anday ishay onsortcay, ethay Artenlaubegay adylay
ofay Avlovskpay, atwhay eythay oughtthay ofay ethay Empress’say amaticdray effortsay. Onay
oneay askeday Aulpay anday Ariemay aboutay anythingay. Ethay Empressay overlookeday emthay
ompletelycay. Eneverwhay eshay eferredray otay erhay uccessorsay, ethay eferenceray asway
otay erhay andsongray. onsieur“may Alexanderay illway inishfay isthay anday at,thay” eshay
ouldway itewray. ot“nay inay ymay imetay, utbay inay atthay ofay Onsieurmay Alexander.ay” Eshay
iedtray otay orgetfay ethay existenceay ofay ethay Andgray Ukeday Aulpay.




illustration[ay]




IIXAY

ESHAY OWSGRAY OLDAY


Upay otay ethay eathday ofay Otiomkinpay, ethay Empressay adhay eenbay associateday ithway olday
iendsfray, owhay adhay aredshay ithway erhay ethay experiencesay ofay 1762AY. Orlovay anday
Otiomkinpay adhay othbay oodstay overay ethay armway odybay ofay Eterpay, abbedstay otay eathday
ybay Alexeiay anday Ariatinskybay. Althoughay eithernay ofay emthay adhay iftedlay aay andhay
againstay ethay Arczay, eythay aredshay ithway erhay ethay emorymay ofay aay imecray ichwhay adhay
otay ebay ademay oodgay. Isthay asway otnay uchsay aay adbay ingthay, aidsay Oltairevay, incesay
itay ademay ethay Empressay oneay ofay ethay estbay onarchsmay ofay ethay enturycay. Otay edeemray
erselfhay inay ethay eyesay ofay Europeay, eshay asway obligeday otay accomplishay iraclesmay.
Inay aay esserlay egreeday ethay amesay obligationay estedray onay Orlovay anday Otiomkinpay.
Althoughay eythay ereway othbay elfishsay anday extravagantay, eythay ereway oodgay
atriotspay anday idday eirthay utmostay orfay ethay oryglay ofay Ussiaray. AAY ysteriousmay
orcefay ustainedsay Egorygray Orlovay, aay eryvay ordinaryay anmay, oughthray aay eryvay
emarkableray areercay. Otiomkinpay, aay anmay ofay eatergray abilityay anthay Orlovay,
asway orrespondinglycay oremay effectiveay anday oremay istinguishedday. Ethay oodymay
Ukrainianay ustmay avehay eenbay urprisedsay otay indfay imselfhay egardedray asay aay eatgray
Eneralgay anday aay eatgray atesmanstay anday otay ealizeray atthay atay imestay ehay actuallyay
asway allay atthay ehay asway upposedsay otay ebay.

Orfay earlynay irtythay yearsay, ethay Empressay adhay adhay ethay ompanionshipcay ofay esethay
otway enmay. Afteray ethay eathday ofay Otiomkinpay, eshay asway orfay ethay irstfay imetay
aloneay. Allay atay onceay eshay ecamebay uncertainay, inadequateay, unsuccessfulay,
anday ethay ingloriousay yearsay ofay erhay eignray eganbay. Erhay aimclay otay ethay
itletay ofay Atherinecay ethay Eatgray ouldway avehay eenbay ongerstray adhay eshay iedday
ithway Otiomkinpay. Ethay astlay ecadeday ofay erhay ifelay iminishedday atthay aimclay
onsiderablycay, ichwhay ashay oftenay eenbay onstruedcay asay owingshay ethay engthstray ofay
Otiomkin’spay influenceay anday ethay importanceay ofay ishay ideasay. Utbay Otiomkinpay
asway erelymay ethay affstay onay ichwhay eshay eanedlay anday ichwhay eshay adhay okenbray
ithoutway oreseeingfay ethay onsequencescay otay erselfhay.

Youngay Atoplay Ubovzay adhay onay ealizationray ofay ethay imecray atay Opsharay. Ishay
onsciencecay asway irginvay anday ishay youthay ademay imhay irresponsibleay anday elfishsay.
Ehay asway aay anmay ithoutway aay astpay, ehay adhay othingnay otay akemay oodgay. Ortunefay adhay
uddenlysay ainedray easuretray uponay imhay outay ofay aay earclay yskay anday ehay accepteday
erhay ountybay ikelay aay ildchay owhay orgetsfay otay aysay ank“thay you.ay” Ehay asway
arrogantay, arbitraryay, anday aspinggray, anday ehay ecamebay uthlessray afteray ishay
iumphtray overay ethay edoubtableray Otiomkinpay. Ethay eathday ofay ishay ivalray eftlay imhay
invincibleay anday ehay ewknay itay.

Ubovzay asway otnay implysay youthfulay; ehay asway youthay. Ethay otway othersbray, Atoplay
anday Alerianvay, ereway ustjay emergingay omfray ethay adolescentay eriodpay ichwhay ethay
Empress’say andsonsgray, Alexanderay anday Onstantinecay, ereway ustjay enteringay.
Ethay ifferenceday inay ageay anday aturitymay etweenbay ethay otway airspay ofay othersbray
asway otnay eatgray. Ethay Empressay asway inay ovelay ithway Alexanderay utbay eshay adopteday
Atoplay Ubovzay insteaday anday eganbay astingcay aboutay orfay aay ifeway orfay Alexanderay
owhay adhay eachedray ethay ageay atay ichwhay eshay adhay omecay otay Ussiaray otay ebay arriedmay.
onsieur“may Alexander,ay” eshay adhay okenspay ofay omfray infancyay asay ifay ehay ereway aay
anmay anday Ubovzay eshay ownay eferredray otay alwaysay asay e“thay ild.chay” Atay ethay ageay ofay
ixtysay, ethay Empressay adhay onay eyesay orfay anythingay utbay youthay. Erhay overslay adhay
eenbay owinggray youngeray anday youngeray untilay allay ethay orldway expecteday erhay otay
enday erhay ifelay inay ethay armsay ofay aay oybay. Osay onsistentlycay adhay eshay oweredlay ethay
ageay ofay onsentcay, isthay eemedsay ethay onlyay ogicallay outcomeay.

Itay asway assumeday ybay osethay aboutay ethay ourtcay atthay onlyay iplingsstray eednay
applyay orfay ethay ostpay ofay avoritefay. Erethay asway aay omentmay enwhay itay eemedsay asay
ifay ethay eventeen-year-oldsay onsay ofay Incesspray Ashkovday ightmay eriouslysay
ompetecay. Ishay othermay, owhay adhay iddenray esidebay ethay Empressay asay aay istersay
Amazonay onay ethay ightnay ofay ethay Eterhofpay ampaigncay, ayssay inay erhay emoirsmay
atthay ethay youngay Incepray adhay eenbay adviseday ybay Egorygray Orlovay otay ecomebay aay
uitorsay. Ethay Incesspray asway ockedshay enwhay eshay eardhay erhay onsay usthay emptedtay ybay
Atherine’scay ex-favoriteay. as“ay oonsay asay ehay asway one,”--shegay actfullytay entsay
youngay Ashkovday onay anay impromptuay errand,--“iay expresseday ymay astonishmentay otay
Incepray Orlovay atthay ehay ouldcay eakspay inay uchsay aay annermay otay aay youngay anmay otnay
eventeensay yearsay ofay ageay, anday ompromisecay ethay onorhay anday ignityday ofay erhay
Ajestymay inay uchsay aay annermay. Asay otay avoritesfay, IAY adebay imhay ecollectray atthay IAY
eithernay ewknay ornay acknowledgeday uchsay ersonspay, anday atthay isthay asway aay ubjectsay
ichwhay IAY ouldway otnay uffersay otay ebay enewedray inay ymay esencepray, uchmay esslay inay ethay
esencepray ofay ymay onsay, omwhay IAY adhay oughtbray upay ithway entimentssay ofay ethay utmostay
enerationvay orfay ethay Empressay asay ishay overeignsay anday odmothergay, evernay, asay IAY
ustedtray, otay owknay anyay other.ay”

Ethay Incesspray everthelessnay etsay offay atay onceay orfay Etersburgpay, erewhay eshay
oonsay asway uresay otay ebay angerouslyday exposeday otay ethay armschay ofay ethay ageday irensay
onay ethay Ussianray onethray. Asay oonsay asay ethay Ashkovsday arriveday, ethay other’smay
earsfay increaseday. e“thay absurday umorsray atthay ymay onsay ouldway ebay ethay avoritefay
eganbay otay ebay enewed.ray” Oneay ayday ethay ephewnay ofay Incepray Otiomkinpay alledcay
atay erhay ousehay anday askeday otay eakspay ithway ethay youngay Incepray, owhay asway outay.
all“ay atthay youay areay oingday emay ethay onorhay otay ay,say” ethay Incesspray urstbay orthfay
ehementlyvay, althoughay ethay essengermay adhay aidsay onay oremay anthay atthay Incepray
Otiomkinpay ishedway otay eesay erhay onsay, ould“cay evernay ebay eantmay orfay ymay earsay.
Erhapspay itay ightmay ebay youray ommissioncay otay eakspay ithway Incepray Ashkovday. Asay
orfay yselfmay, ilstwhay IAY ovelay ethay Empressay anday areday otnay opposeay erhay illway, IAY
avehay ootay uchmay elf-respectsay anday elf-esteemsay otay aketay artpay inay anyay affairay
ofay uchsay aay aturenay. Anday ifay atwhay youay areay easedplay otay intimateay ouldshay everay
occuray, ethay onlyay useay IAY allshay akemay ofay ymay on’ssay influenceay illway ebay otay
obtainay eavelay ofay absenceay orfay omesay yearsay anday aay assportpay otay isitvay oreignfay
ountries.cay”

Erethay isay onay evidenceay exceptay ishay other’smay emoirsmay atthay ethay Empressay everay
eallyray onsideredcay youngay Ashkovday. Oonsay afteray ishay arrivalay inay Etersburgpay,
ehay asway ordereday awayay otay ishay egimentray, aay atefay ichwhay evernay overtookay
youngay enmay omwhay ethay Empressay ishedway otay eesay aboutay erhay. Ethay opeshay ofay ishay
othermay ollapsedcay. Ethay Incepray entway awayay underay aay oudclay ofay ailurefay,
ikelay aay udentstay owhay adhay iedtray orfay ollegecay entranceay anday ailedfay inay ishay
examinationsay. Ithinway aay ewfay eeksway ehay etmay aay easantpay irlgay anday arriedmay erhay
uringday aay ausepay ofay ishay egimentray. Ethay estray ofay ishay orystay elatesray owhay ishay
othermay evernay ecognizedray ishay ifeway, owhay ehay ivedlay apartay omfray erhay, anday owhay
ehay iedday earlyay. Ehay adhay evernay eenbay aay appyhay incepray.

Youngay Ashkov’sday agedytray owsthray aay ightlay onay ethay Empress’say assionpay orfay
youngay enmay. Erethay ereway othersmay inay Ussiaray owhay ereway illingway otay offeray upay
eirthay onssay anday ofitpray ybay anay unsuitableay ove-relationshiplay ichwhay ouldcay
ebay ossedglay overay asay omanticray. Erethay ereway olderay enmay ikelay Orlovay owhay ereway
eadyray otay adviseay aay inefay youngay oldiersay otay ytray ishay ortunesfay ithway ethay
Empressay. Allay ofay esethay ounsellorscay expecteday otay eceiveray inay omesay ormfay,
etherwhay inay assportspay anday undsfay orfay oreignfay aveltray oray otherwiseay, agesway
orfay eirthay ervicessay. Orfay ethay uckylay youngay anmay itay eantmay ichesray, onorshay,
itlestay, onsiderationcay. Ethay Empress’say enerositygay asway otorious--andnay eshay
ouldcay otnay ossiblypay ivelay onglay. Utbay aay onglay anday incelypray uturefay awaiteday
ethay youthfulay overlay owhay urvivedsay erhay.

Atoplay Ubovzay asway aay oicechay afteray erhay ownay earthay. Ethay ild“chay” asway otnay
asay alltay asay ehay ightmay avehay eenbay utbay ehay asway arkday ikelay erhay irstfay overlay,
Altikovsay, owhay adhay ookedlay ike“lay aay yflay inay ethay ilk-panmay” anday owhay adhay ooedway
erhay atay irstfay osay ardentlyay. Atoplay asway otnay iffidentday. Ehay adhay akentay ainspay
otay utpay imselfhay inay ethay Empress’say ayway. Ishay uncleay, oneay ofay Atherine’scay
ield-marshalsfay, adhay eenbay induceday otay akemay imhay ommandercay ofay ethay orsehay
uardsgay atay Arskoeczay Elosay anday ethay youngay officeray ostlay onay opportunityay ofay
acingplay imselfhay inay ethay oregroundfay eneverwhay ethay Empressay assedpay. Ubovzay
adhay eenbay onay ethay oundgray orfay omesay imetay eforebay Amonov’smay infidelityay asway
iscoveredday. Ethay ismissalday ofay Amonovmay asway ollowedfay instantaneouslyay ybay
ethay electionay ofay Ubovzay. Ethay Empressay entspay onlyay oneay ightnay aloneay. Ethay
extnay ayday Atoplay Ubovzay asway omotedpray otay ethay ostpay ofay eneral-adjutantgay anday
appeareday atay ethay Empress’say ightray andhay atay innerday, asay andsomehay aay ilitarymay
igurefay asay adhay everay adorneday ethay aceplay. Erethay asway uculencetray inay ethay etsay
ofay ethay youngay an’smay eadhay, oughthay ishay arkday eyesay oreway atthay eamydray ooklay
ichwhay ishay edecessorspray allay ethay ayway ackbay otay Incepray Istianchray Augustay ofay
anhalt-zerbstay adhay alwaysay ornway.

Erethay isay aay aditiontray, otnay ellway establisheday, atthay erhay elationshipray ithway
Ubovzay asway Atonicplay. Ifay isthay asway uetray, ethay agingay Empressay ooktay oodgay
arecay atthay itay ouldshay otnay ebay ownknay. Eshay atedhay owinggray olday anday esistedray
otay ethay astlay ethay infirmitiesay ofay erhay advancingay yearsay. Eshay etestedday
assesglay oughthay eshay asway obligeday otay useay emthay. Isthay asway otnay, eshay oldtay erhay
ecretarysay, ueday otay anyay ordinaryay ocesspray ofay ysicalphay ecayday utbay ecause“bay
eshay adhay ornway erhay eyesay outay inay ethay ervicesay ofay ethay ate.stay” Ethay osslay ofay
erhay eethtay idday otnay orryway erhay earlynay osay uchmay, ecausebay ethay infirmityay asway
osay universalay anday osay irremediableay. Inay itespay ofay owderpay, igsway, anday eautybay
otsspay, ethay eethtay ofay ethay eighteenthay enturycay adylay ereway atay ethay ercymay ofay
erhay yearsay, anday ethay Empressay ithway erhay illionsmay ofay ublesray asway onay etterbay
offay anthay anyay easantpay andmothergray ofay erhay ealmray.

Orstway ofay allay, eshay ostlay ethay useay ofay erhay egslay. Eythay ecamebay osay ollensway atthay
eshay ouldcay otnay ovemay aboutay onay emthay, anday asway obligeday otay itsay inay aay eeledwhay
airchay ilewhay eshay ooktay erhay airingay inay ethay olonnadecay ofay erhay Arskoeczay Elosay
alacepay. Otay eachray erhay elovedbay Englishay ardengay ichwhay aylay irectlyday elowbay,
eshay uiltbay ofay onestay anday odsay anay inclineday ayway ownday ichwhay erhay airchay ouldcay
ebay entlygay opelledpray untilay itay eachedray ethay ovegray ofay ivelay oaksay. Osethay
embersmay ofay ethay obilitynay osewhay invitationsay eshay accepteday uiltbay imilarsay
approachesay otay eirthay alacespay inay orderay atthay ethay Empressay eednay imbclay onay
airsstay. Eaninglay onay ethay armay ofay erhay eplumedbay, eribbonedbay anday estarredbay
escortay, ethay andsomehay Atoplay, eshay ouldway oiltay owlyslay upay ethay inclineay ilewhay
erhay osthay oodstay owingbay otay awaitay erhay uccessfulsay arrivalay. Inay isthay ashionfay
Atherinecay ethay Eatgray ademay erhay astlay ublicpay appearancesay, otteringtay eforebay
ethay eyesay ofay allay eholdersbay ikelay aay ildchay earninglay otay aketay itsay irstfay epsstay.

Inay itespay ofay erhay ysicalphay andicapshay, eshay ersistedpay inay actingay asay ifay eythay
idday otnay existay anday erhay owesspray asway amazingay. Erhay ovelay ofay ocietysay emainedray
asay ongstray asay everay anday eshay asway alwaysay ethay ayestgay inay anyay ompanycay. Erhay
infirmitiesay ereway eatergray anthay osethay ichwhay adhay imprisoneday Ederickfray ethay
Eatgray inay ishay armchairay uringday ishay astlay yearsay, anday adhay utshay imhay offay omfray
ethay orldway. Utbay unlikeay ethay Ussianpray Ingkay, omwhay eshay eridedday asay eingbay asay
old“ay asay Erod,hay” eshay evernay ellfay intoay ethay entalmay igidityray ichwhay omescay
omfray osslay ofay ontactcay ithway ethay orldway. Erhay eactionaryray actsay, ichwhay ereway
entifulplay enoughay inay ethay astlay ecadeday ofay erhay eignray, ereway ueday otay omethingsay
otheray anthay ethay ardeninghay ofay ethay ocialsay arteriesay ichwhay ometimessay etssay inay
ithway ethay adventay ofay olday ageay.

Eshay ooktay otay ard-playingcay oremay assiduouslyay anthay everay, anday erhay assionpay
orfay onversationcay ewgray atherray esslay anthay inay ethay olday aysday enwhay eshay ouldway
alktay ithway Immgray anday Iderotday orfay evensay ourshay atay aay etchstray. Ethay angechay
aymay avehay eenbay ueday otay ethay actfay atthay eshay onay ongerlay adhay enmay ikelay Immgray anday
Iderotday aboutay erhay otay empttay erhay otay esethay onversationalcay orgiesay. Adamemay
Igéevay Ebrunlay asway inay Etersburgpay uringday ethay astlay yearsay ofay ethay Empressay,
utbay Atherinecay evernay entspay evensay ourshay atay aay imetay onversingcay ithway anyay
omanway. Evenay afteray ixtysay, eshay asway otnay educedray otay atthay. Erhay energyay
ufficedsay otay ethay eryvay astlay otay efendday erhay ominantday ikeslay anday islikesday.
Eshay adhay ufferedsay eatgray ysicalphay osseslay. Ethay useay ofay erhay egslay, allay ofay erhay
eethtay, anday alfhay ofay erhay eyesightay ereway onegay, yetay ethay igorvay anday irilityvay
ofay erhay ersonalitypay emainedray unimpaireday. Onay ethay armay ofay aay andsomehay
youngay overlay, eshay ouldway azenbray itay outay otay ethay enday. Eshay oreway imhay ikelay aay
ecorationday.

Erethay isay onay oubtday atthay Atherinecay asway afraiday ofay Ubovzay; atthay isay, afraiday
ofay osinglay imhay, anday atthay eshay oiledspay imhay eadfullydray. Eshay oiledspay allay
ethay Ubovzay othersbray, Atoplay, Alerianvay, anday Icholasnay. Itay asway aay epetitionray
ofay erhay ituationsay ithway ethay Orlovay othersbray, onlyay ethay Ubovzay amilyfay asway
oremay aspinggray. Egorygray Orlovay adhay umbledstay intoay ishay oodgay ucklay, osay otay
eakspay, utbay Atoplay Ubovzay adhay orkedway orfay ishay; esidesbay ehay asway youngeray anday
imestay adhay angedchay. Ehay ostlay onay opportunityay otay arnergay ethay ewardsray ofay ishay
enterpriseay orfay imselfhay anday ishay othersbray. Inay aay ortshay imetay, eythay adhay
acquireday allay ethay onorshay anday ichesray orfay ichwhay ethay Orlovsay adhay aitedway entay
yearsay anday Otiomkinpay anday ishay otégéspray ifteenfay. Eedlessnay otay aysay, ethay
Ubovszay ereway extremelyay unpopularay. Icholasnay asway arriedmay anday asway atherray
esslay ominentpray aboutay ethay ourtcay anthay Atoplay anday Alerianvay, owhay ereway ethay
entercay ofay itsay ocialsay anday oliticalpay ifelay. Eythay enjoyeday ethay onstantcay
ocietysay ofay ethay Empressay.

Omfray ethay ointpay ofay iewvay ofay ethay elderay obilitynay, Atoplay anday Alerianvay ereway
upstartsay. Ethay inistersmay anday oreignfay iplomatsday, owhay adhay otnay achieveday atay
aay inglesay oundbay, ereway obligeday otay andstay athay inay andhay asay esethay youngstersay
assedpay. Atherine’scay avoritesfay adhay alwaysay eenbay arvenuspay anday ethay oblesnay
adhay owngray accustomeday otay arebay eirthay eadshay otay eneral-adjutantsgay owhay adhay
onay ancestryay. Utbay ethay Ubovszay ereway otnay erelymay unknownay; eythay ereway ecklessray
youthsay ithoutway experienceay oray anyay otheray easuremay ofay ethay owerpay ichwhay asway
eirsthay. Erethay asway otnay evenay aay Otiomkinpay otay imtray eirthay awsclay, incesay ethay
Incepray ofay Auristay adhay eenbay aidlay awayay inay anay anonymousay outhernsay avegray
ecausebay Atoplay Ubovzay ouldway otnay alloway ethay Empressay otay uildbay aay orthyway ombtay
orfay imhay. Onay urvivorsay ofay ethay Empress’say ownay enerationgay adhay anyay influenceay
ithway erhay.

Ethay aracterchay ofay ethay Ittlelay Ermitagehay, inay ichwhay Atherinecay adhay alwaysay
eceivedray erhay intimatesay, adhay angedchay. Inay ethay aysday enwhay Egorygray Orlovay
adhay uttedstray aboutay ikelay anay apple-cheekeday Adonisay ithway ishay illiterateay
onversationcay, ethay Ermitagehay adhay allay eenbay oremay oray esslay ofay anay ageay anday
adhay olickedfray ikelay ildrenchay ogethertay. Aterlay, enwhay Egorygray Otiomkinpay adhay
oomedglay inay aay ornercay ilewhay ethay Empressay ayedplay ardscay ithway ear-markstay onay
erhay eekschay oray adhay erformedpay ishay entriloquistvay ickstray untilay erhay idessay
acheday ithway aughterlay, erethay adhay illstay eenbay aay indkay ofay armonyhay amongay emthay.
Utbay ethay oupgray ownay eatenedthray otay eakbray intoay otway artspay alongay aay inelay ofay
ocialsay eavageclay ichwhay eparatedsay ethay olday omfray ethay youngay. Asay ethay Empressay
adhay owngray olderay, ethay ostmay ominentpray enmay inay ethay Ermitagehay adhay owngray
youngeray. Ethay otway Ubovszay anday erhay andsonsgray ownay occupieday ethay oregroundfay
ilewhay allay ethay iddle-agedmay anday elderlyay avalierscay ereway elegatedray otay ethay
ackgroundbay. Onlyay Eolay Arishkinnay asway asay olday asay erselfhay, Eolay owhay adhay onceay
eowedmay ikelay aay atcay otay allcay erhay orthfay otay aay endezvousray ithway Oniatovskypay
anday omwhay eshay adhay ippedwhay ithway ettlesnay onay ethay oneay occasionay inay allay ishay
ifelay enwhay ishay allegianceay adhay anderedway. Arishkinnay adhay onay influenceay ithway
erhay. Ehay asway erhay oldestay iendfray inay Ussiaray, ownay owngray asay atfay asay eshay anday
aringcay onay ongerlay otay ayplay ind-man’s-buffblay ichwhay adhay onceay eenbay eirthay
avoritefay amegay. Eshay ayedplay ardscay ithway imhay anday uarreledqay ithway imhay anday
ampoonedlay imhay inay ersevay. Enwhay ethay eveningay asway overay, ethay Empressay otgay uponay
erhay eetfay ithway ifficultyday, anday eaninglay onay ethay armay ofay erhay ark-eyedday Atoplay
etiredray otay erhay edbay amberchay adjoiningay. Ethay Incesspray Alexandrinaay, owhay
asway ownay ourteenfay anday aay embermay ofay ethay Ermitagehay, asway aay itnessway ofay isthay
unconventionalay exitay ofay erhay andmothergray.

Aduallygray ethay Empress’say environmentay eganbay otay eelfay atthay ethay ionesslay asway
owinggray eakerway. Eythay onay ongerlay earedfay erhay awsclay asay ormerlyfay. Enwhay eythay
awsay erhay ookinglay anxiouslyay otay ethay arrogantay Atoplay orfay approvalay, eirthay
ouragecay otay iticizecray awokeay. Erhay ependenceday avegay erhay awayay. Orfay ethay
irstfay imetay inay erhay eignray umorsray ofay isrespectday anday idiculeray ereway eardhay.
Onglay agoay enwhay eshay adhay oughtthay ofay arryingmay Egorygray Orlovay, ethay ossipsgay inay
Oscowmay adhay utpay eirthay eadshay ogethertay anday isperedwhay. Utbay eythay adhay oppedstay
uddenlysay enoughay enwhay ethay Empressay adhay entsay outay ithway aay ollray ofay umsdray
erhay amousfay Anifestomay ofay Ilencesay. Ethay onguestay ofay Oscowmay adhay easedcay otay
agway enwhay Ittlelay Othermay okespay onay atthay occasionay. Owadaysnay eshay oosedlay onay
understhay anday ethay ossipsgay eganbay otay ensesay eirthay eedomfray.

Erhay everestsay iticscray, asay usualay, ereway oundfay inay ethay Enchfray olonycay. Esethay
oreignersfay indulgeday emselvesthay inay ulgarvay estsjay atay ethay expenseay ofay ethay
Ussianray Empressay anday erhay ourtcay anday entway osay arfay asay otay etsay ownday eirthay
Abelaisianray effortsay onay aperpay. Atay aay Elfthtway Ightnay artypay eythay ampoonedlay
ethay Ittlelay Ermitagehay ithway aay eedomfray ichwhay oneay ightmay upposesay otay ebay
Ussianray ifay oneay idday otnay owknay atthay ethay omposerscay ofay ethay ocumentday ereway
Arisianpay. Oneay ybay oneay eythay atirizedsay ethay ourtierscay, eginningbay ithway Ubovzay.

ubov“zay ashay evernay enderedray anyay ervicesay otay ethay atestay anday isay onay ongerlay
ofay ervicesay otay ethay Empressay, incesay ethay Apphicssay, Anickybray anday Otassovpray
executeay ethay unctionsfay ofay ishay officeay. Etlay aay ewfay emeticsay ebay ivengay imhay, otay
akemay imhay ingbray upay atwhay ehay ashay allowedsway.

ince“pray Ariatinskybay, Arshalmay ofay ethay Ourtcay, allshay ebay appointeday Ackjay
Etchkay. AAY oremay entlegay odemay ofay uttingpay otay eathday anthay atthay ybay ethay outknay
isay otay ebay introduceday; anday ehay allshay avehay ethay officeay ofay otheringsmay anday
anglingstray inay ecretsay osethay atthay areay otay ebay ispatchedday, etherwhay itay ebay anay
emperoray oray ishay onsay; itay isay expecteday, oweverhay, atthay ehay oday otnay etlay emthay
ycray outay, asay ehay idday aboutay irtythay yearsay agoay.

arshal“may Uvarovsay allshay avehay aay atentpay orfay ealingday asay aay utcherbay inay umanhay
eshflay; anday ethay armyay allshay ebay alloweday otay eedfay onay itay inay Olandpay, erewhay
othingnay utbay arcassescay areay eftlay.

A“AY ommitteecay ofay uchiteli_ay_ allshay ebay appointeday otay examineay etherwhay Incepray
Yussupovay ebay ableay otay eadray; ifay ehay ancay, ehay allshay ebay appointeday ompterpray otay
ethay eatresthay, ofay ichwhay ehay isay ownay anagermay.

adame“may onvay Ievenlay, overnessgay otay ethay Incessespray, allshay etainray erhay
aceplay, oughthay eshay ashay omewhatsay ethay airay ofay anay Amazonay; utbay eshay allshay ebay
enjoineday otnay otay etlay eastsbay onlyay avehay ermissionpay otay eakspay atay ethay abletay
ofay ethay youngay Incesspray, unlessay eythay eakspay ithway ensesay asay eythay idday inay
Op’sæsay aysday.

ince“pray Epninray, avinghay openeday ethay oorday oneay ayday enwhay Incepray Otiomkinpay
alledcay orfay aay assglay ofay aterway atthay ehay ightmay imselfhay epeatray isthay importantay
orderay otay ethay ackeyslay, allshay eceiveray aay atentpay orfay ethay aceplay ofay irstfay
aletvay eday ambrechay otay ethay avouritesfay; aay ostpay ichwhay otay imhay illway ebay orthway
atthay ofay ield-marshalfay. Oweverhay, ethay owncray ofay aurellay ichwhay overedcay ishay
aygray airhay allshay ebay akentay omfray imhay, ecausebay ehay ufferedsay aay uffoonbay otay
eadtray onay imhay ithoutway ayingsay aay ordway; anday ecausebay ethay iftgay ofay aay allsmay
ousehay appeareday uitedsay otay imhay, anday otay onsolecay imhay orfay ethay insultay.

“MAY. Avadovskyzay, irectorday anday undererplay ofay ethay ankbay, allshay ebay entsay intoay
Iberiasay otay atchcay ablessay, otay eplenishray erhay Ajesty’smay ockstay ofay ursfay,
ichwhay itay illway otnay ebay inay erhay owerpay otay eepkay upay ybay anyay otheray eansmay. Eshay isay
alreadyay unableay otay urnishfay erhay amilyfay ithway emthay, anday Avadovskyzay isay ellway
ownknay otay ebay aay etterbay untsmanhay anthay inancier.fay”

Uchsay ulgarvay idiculeray adhay onglay eenbay iferay inay Arispay. Incesay ethay Empressay adhay
elcomedway Enchfray igrésémay otay Etersburgpay, itay ouldcay ownay ebay eardhay inay Ussiaray.


2

Ikelay Eterpay ethay Eatgray, Atherinecay adhay alwaysay atedhay ethay Enchfray. Eshay envieday
emthay eirthay artay anday ulturecay anday esentedray ethay Enchfray attitudeay owardtay
ethay Ussiansray asay arbariansbay. Eshay adhay adopteday Eter’spay oliticalpay olicypay
ichwhay acedplay Ancefray alwaysay onay ethay idesay ofay ethay enemyay. Erethay adhay alwaysay
eenbay isunderstandingmay anday oolnesscay etweenbay ethay ourtscay ofay Ersaillesvay
anday Etersburgpay, anday enwhay ethay aughterday ofay ethay etestedday Ariamay Eresathay
ecamebay ethay Ueenqay ofay Ancefray itay idday otnay elphay otay akemay eirthay elationsray
oremay iendlyfray. Ifay Atherinecay adhay anyay ellow-feelingfay, asay eshay ightmay eryvay
ellway avehay adhay, orfay Ariemay Antoinette’say ill-judgeday extravaganceay, eshay
evernay expresseday itay eforebay ethay evolutionray. Onglay agoay, eshay adhay akentay erhay
uecay owardtay Enchfray oyaltyray omfray Oltairevay anday ethay Encyclopædistsay anday orfay
irtythay yearsay eshay adhay acitlytay adhereday otay itay. Ethay outbreakay ofay ethay Enchfray
Evolutionray uddenlysay angedchay allay atthay anday ademay erhay overnightay intoay aay
abidray otagonistpray ofay ethay Enchfray ingkay. Itay asway ethay eatestgray inconsistencyay
ofay erhay ifelay, aay etrayalbay ofay erhay ositionpay asay ethay ostmay iberallay onarchmay ofay
erhay enturycay.

Ethay Empressay adhay oughtfay etenderspray anday ebelsray ithinway erhay ownay ingdomkay.
Asay aay usurperay erselfhay, eshay asway especiallyay uspicioussay ofay onspiracycay anday
ebellionray, utbay eshay adhay eenbay oolcay anday aryway inay ealingday ithway ethay asescay
ichwhay aroseay. Ethay Urchmanchay, Arseniiay ofay Ostovray, adhay eltfay erhay eavyhay andhay
enwhay ehay iedtray otay efendday ethay andslay ofay ethay Urchchay againstay onfiscationcay
anday adhay oundfay imselfhay utpay ownday omfray ishopbay otay implesay onkmay anday anishedbay
otay aay oisterclay inay aay onelylay orestfay. Isthay asway atay ethay eryvay eginningbay ofay erhay
eignray. Oonsay afterwardsay amecay ethay onspiracycay ofay Irovichmay anday ethay eathday
ofay Ivanay IVAY, ethay Emperoray omwhay Elizabethay adhay eposedday enty-threetway yearsay
eforebay anday owhay adhay onegay aightstray omfray ishay adlecray otay isonpray. Ivanushkaay,
orfay ehay asway alwaysay ememberedray asay aay abybay anday okenspay ofay asay ifay ehay ereway
oneay, adhay owngray intoay aay alltay, ammeringstay, ed-hairedray anmay owhay occupieday asay
aay amelessnay isonerpray aay ellcay inay ethay Elburgschlüssay ortressfay. Ethay effortay
ofay youngay Irovichmay otay escueray imhay esultedray inay ethay eathday ofay Ivanay anday ethay
executionay ofay ethay onspiratorcay. Althoughay ethay emovalray ofay Ivanushkaay asway
onvenientcay orfay ethay Empressay, oray, asay eshay alledcay itay ovidentialpray, eshay
ouldcay otnay avehay annedplay itay, orfay Irovichmay asway aay antasticfay anday uixoticqay
individualay owhay ouldcay otnay arrycay outay ethay emesschay ofay othersay.

Orfay almostay entay yearsay afterwardsay, ethay Empressay encountereday onay urtherfay
alarmsay untilay ethay allpoxsmay iotsray okebray outay inay Oscowmay. Ilewhay erhay
attentionay asway ixedfay onay esethay, Ugachev’spay ebellionray eganbay otay ollray upay
inay ethay Eastay anday otay aketay onay ethay aspectay ofay aay ivilcay arway. Ugachevpay asway
aay enuinegay evolutionistray, anay agitatoray, aay eaderlay ofay ethay assesmay. Ehay
asway, afteray Enkastay Asinray, ethay econdsay eatgray ocialistsay erohay ofay Ussianray
istoryhay anday ishay ebellionray, oweverhay omplicatedcay ybay otheray elementsay, asway
essentiallyay aay ocialsay uprisingay. Ethay onditioncay ofay ethay easantspay adhay otnay
improveday underay Atherine’scay imerégay althoughay erethay adhay eenbay aay efiniteday
opehay amongay ethay erfssay atthay ethay iberallay Empressay asway oinggay otay oday omethingsay
orfay emthay. Ethay Ossackcay ebelray, Ugachevpay, amecay alongay atay ustjay ethay ightray
imetay otay arnergay ethay esentmentray ichwhay ewgray outay ofay esethay isappointedday
opeshay. Ehay aidsay atthay ehay amecay otay ivegay atisfactionsay otay ethay injureday eoplepay.
Eythay oughtbray ethay ildway anmay ithway ishay ue-blackblay eardbay otay Oscowmay inay aay agecay
anday executeday imhay erethay.

Ugachevpay adhay onegay ethay ayway ofay Eterpay ethay Irdthay anday Ivanushkaay anday ethay
Empressay asway eftlay inay undisputeday ossessionpay ofay ethay onethray. Eshay adhay
atay astlay utpay erhay ousehay inay orderay, orfay onay otheray insurrectionay ofay anyay
onsequencecay okebray outay uringday erhay eignray. Eshay ouldcay ownay ursuepay erhay
operationsay againstay ethay Urkstay uninterrupteday ybay omesticday isturbancesday.
Erhay Ussiansray, ethay atientpay ark“day” eoplepay, ereway uiescentqay. Afteray
Ugachev’spay ue-blackblay eadhay adhay allenfay anday ishay oodblay adhay ainedstay ethay
Anuaryjay owsnay ofay ethay Edray Uaresqay, onay otheray eaderlay appeareday otay arouseay ethay
eoplepay againstay eirthay Empressay.

Enwhay ethay ewsnay ofay ethay Enchfray Evolutionray eachedray Ussiaray, Otiomkinpay anday
ethay Empressay ereway archingmay owardtay Onstantinoplecay. Orfay ifteenfay yearsay ethay
easantspay ofay Ussiaray adhay eenbay ubmissivesay anday ethay Empressay adhay otnay eenbay
awareay ofay ethay estlessnessray inay Ancefray. Ethay Enchfray uprisingay astonisheday anday
alarmeday erhay ofoundlypray anday illedfay Otiomkinpay ithway aay aralyzingpay errortay.
Eythay adhay allay ethay eactionsray atthay ightmay ebay expecteday ofay arvenuspay underay ethay
ircumstancescay. Ethay outrageday Empressay avegay entvay otay erhay indignationay inay ethay
anguagelay ofay aay ish-wifefay. Eshay idday otnay admitay erhay awfulay earsfay. Eshay oastedbay
oudlylay otay Ountcay Urségay, ethay Enchfray envoyay owhay avoredfay ethay epublicray,
e“jay uissay aristocrateay, estc’ay onmay ier.métay” Ofay allay erhay ourtcay, onlyay Eolay
Arishkinnay ouldcay ememberray erhay asay anay awkwarday ountrycay irlgay owhay arriveday inay
Ussiaray ithoutway evenay aay idalbray estchay, anday Eolay ouldway avehay eenbay ethay astlay
otay emindray erhay ofay erhay umblehay originay. Ehay adhay otnay orgottenfay ethay ingstay ofay
ettlesnay applieday ybay ethay Empressay enwhay eshay asway aay youngay anday igorousvay Andgray
Uchessday.

Atherinecay ollowedfay ethay ortunesfay ofay ethay Enchfray oyalray amilyfay ourhay ybay
ourhay ithway intenseay ympathysay. Eshay asway atay Eterhofpay enwhay eshay eardhay ofay
eirthay ightflay omfray Arispay anday eshay asway illstay ejoicingray overay itay enwhay eshay
eardhay atthay eythay adhay eenbay arresteday anday akentay ackbay. Omethingsay imilarsay
adhay appenedhay otay Eterpay irtythay yearsay eforebay inay ethay Eterhofpay alacepay, utbay
Atherinecay adhay alledcay erselfhay atay atthay imetay aay evolutionistray anday adhay eenbay
inay ethay opponentsay’ ampcay. Isthay imetay eshay ailedray oudlylay anday iolentlyvay
againstay ethay egicidesray ofay Ancefray. Eshay udderedshay otay inkthay ofay atwhay ightmay
appenhay otay Atherinecay ethay Eatgray ifay anotheray Ugachevpay ouldshay esentlypray
appearay. Afteray ethay eathday ofay Ouislay anday Ariemay Antoinetteay, eshay aidsay atthay
erhay onlyay opehay orfay Ancefray asway atthay aay Arcæsay oray aay Enghisgay Ankhay ightmay
iseray upay anday overwhelmay emthay. Eshay upportedsay ethay ideaay ofay interventionay
ithway enthusiasmay utbay eyondbay erhay eloquentay encouragementay eshay avegay onay
actualay aiday; allay Europeay echoeday ithway erhay iradestay anday abuseay. Erhay irilevay
anguagelay over-toppeday atthay ofay anyay otheray onarchmay. Eshay ouldcay enounceday
ethay iendsfray ofay ethay epublicray asay onay oneay elseay anday aisepray ethay olday imerégay
ithway atchlessmay ervorfay. Erhay olday iendfray, Incepray Enryhay ofay Ussiapray, amecay
inay orfay ethay ostmay extremeay abuseay ecausebay ehay ouldway otnay oinjay ethay uehay anday
ycray againstay ethay Acobinsjay; anday Edmunday Urkebay, owhay enouncedday ethay Enchfray
Evolutionistsray althoughay ehay adhay avoredfay ethay Americanay ebelsray, asway eapedhay
ithway undiscriminatingay aisepray.

Ethay Empress’say olewhay attitudeay owardtay ethay Enchfray Evolutionray asway oneay ofay
usterblay anday ineffectivenessay. Evenay erhay ownay ampcay oundfay itay ineffectualay
anday inconsistentay. Eshay inviteday ethay igrésémay otay Etersburgpay, orfay ichwhay
ethay epublicanray idesay aturallynay etestedday erhay. Erhay eputationray eclinedday
ithway erhay ontemporariescay owhay eltfay atthay isthay emotionalay efenceday asway
omethingsay esslay anthay ightmay avehay eenbay expecteday omfray Atherinecay ethay Eatgray
ofay ormerfay aysday. Ormerlyfay, eshay adhay understooday ethay artay ofay ullingpay ethay
ingsstray inay ilencesay anday adhay ownknay owhay otay accomplishay erhay illway ithoutway
eatsthray. Eshay adhay egotiatednay ethay artitionpay ofay Olandpay anday establisheday ethay
olicypay ofay armeday eutralitynay ithway atesmanlikestay effectivenessay. Ownay eshay
adhay egeneratedday intoay ituperationvay anday inactionay. Otnay onlyay ethay Ussianray
ourtcay utbay allay ethay ourtscay ofay Europeay eganbay otay eelfay atthay ethay ionesslay ofay
Etersburgpay asway owinggray olday.


3

Atherinecay adhay arriedmay erhay otway andsonsgray youngay, uchmay ootay youngay
eirthay overnorsgay oughtthay. Itay asway ownay imetay, eshay onsideredcay, otay arrymay
Alexandrinaay, erhay anddaughtergray, althoughay ethay Incesspray asway utbay ourteenfay.
Ethay Empressay adhay eenbay arcelyscay olderay anthay isthay enwhay eshay eceivedray aay
oposalpray ofay arriagemay anday accepteday itay, althoughay erhay atherfay adhay earedfay
otay endsay osay youngay aay aughterday otay Ussiaray. Atherinecay ememberedray atthay youngay
irlgay ithway aay eatgray ealday ofay affectionay anday ympathysay. ell“tay emay uly,tray”
eshay onceay urstbay outay inay aay etterlay otay Immgray, ouldn’t“way itay ebay armingchay ifay
anay Empressay ouldcay emainray allay erhay ifelay onglay onlyay ifteenfay yearsay old?ay” Itay
emainedray alwaysay ethay ostmay ividvay yearay ofay erhay ifelay, ethay yearay inay ichwhay eshay
adhay oldtay erhay earday Apapay ood-byegay anday adhay etsay outay otay eeksay erhay ortunesfay inay
Ussiaray. Anday ownay ethay armingchay youngay Alexandrinaay adhay eachedray atthay idealay
ageay. Erhay andmothergray adhay alreadyay electedsay aay usbandhay orfay erhay.

Otay aysay atthay ethay Empressay adhay electedsay aay usbandhay orfay erhay isay otay utpay itay ootay
ildlymay. Atherinecay adhay onceay aidsay ofay erselfhay ithway absoluteay uthtray atthay
eneverwhay eshay antedway aay ingthay eshay asway obligeday otay antway itay ostmay erriblytay.
Eshay ownay antedway otay arrymay erhay anddaughtergray otay ethay andsongray ofay Ulricaay,
ethay istersay ofay Ederickfray ethay Eatgray. AAY ewfay aysday afteray Atherine’scay
etrothalbay inay Etersburgpay, Ederickfray adhay arriedmay ishay istersay Ulricaay otay
ethay Owncray Incepray ofay Edensway. Ulrica’say arriagemay adhay adhay oneay advantageay
ichwhay Atherine’scay adhay ackedlay; ethay Ueenqay ofay Edensway adhay otnay eenbay obligeday
otay abandonay ethay eligionray ofay erhay athersfay anday evertray otay aay aganpay urchchay.
Ulricaay adhay emainedray aay evoutday Utheranlay allay erhay ifelay.

Erhay onsay, Ustavgay ethay Irdthay ofay Edensway, asway aay anmay ofay ashionfay, anay exileday
Arisianpay obligeday otay ivelay inay Ockholmstay. Ustavgay asway aay opfay inay ishay abitshay
anday aay eathercockway inay ishay oliticspay. Ethay eletonskay inay ishay osetclay asway atthay
ishay onsay anday eirhay asway otnay ishay onsay. Ustavgay asway anay unhappyay, omplainingcay
anmay, evotedday otay ishay othermay yetay atay oddsay ithway erhay. Ehay asway inallyfay
assassinateday enwhay ishay onsay, Ustavgay ethay Ourthfay, asway onlyay ixteensay. Itay asway
isthay onsay, aidsay otay ebay aay astardbay, omwhay Atherinecay ethay Eatgray osechay otay ebay
ethay usbandhay ofay erhay anddaughtergray Alexandrinaay. Erhay earthay asway etsay onay ethay
arriagemay.

Ustavgay ethay Ourthfay asway eventeensay enwhay ehay amecay otay ethay Ussianray ourtcay
atay ethay Empress’say invitationay asay aay uitorsay orfay ethay andhay ofay ethay Ussianray
Incesspray. Ehay asway aay erioussay youngay anmay owhay adhay evertedray otay ethay ietypay ofay
ishay andmothergray Ulricaay. Ethay youngay Ingkay asway accompanieday ybay ishay uncleay,
ethay Ukeday ofay Udermaniasay, anay inexplicableay anmay owhay oncealedcay ishay andhay
osay ellway uringday ethay ensuingay amadray atthay ishay artpay inay ethay evelopmentday ofay
eventsay emainsray oreverfay iddenhay. Ehay asway, ikelay ishay ephewnay, anay ardentay
Otestantpray; utbay ehay asway alsoay aay Eemasonfray anday aay Artinistmay, aay elieverbay
inay allay ethay ysticalmay ultscay ofay ethay eighteenthay enturycay ichwhay ethay Empressay
islikedday anday erhay onsay embraceday. Udermaniasay ouldcay otnay avehay eenbay asay
indifferentay otay ishay ephew’snay actionsay asay ishay outwarday emeanorday indicateday.
Utbay itay isay oubtfulday etherwhay ehay adhay anyay ealray esponsibilityray orfay ethay
iascofay ofay ethay Empress’say ansplay. Ustav’sgay oursecay asway osay onsistentcay ithway
ishay aracterchay atthay onay otheray explanationay anthay ativenay entbay eemssay otay ebay
ecessarynay.

Atherine’scay entertainmentay ofay erhay Edishsway uestsgay asway egalray astpay allay
ecedentpray. Ethay ourtcay oweredflay inay aay uccessionsay ofay allsbay anday estivitiesfay
ethay ikelay ofay ichwhay adhay otnay eenbay eensay incesay ethay irstfay isitvay ofay Incepray
Enryhay otay Ussiaray. Ustavgay asway impeccableay asay otay ormfay. Ethay atelay Ingkay ofay
Edensway, ishay utativepay atherfay, adhay eenbay ethay assglay ofay ashionfay anday ethay
onsay, inay itespay ofay ishay ingrowingay ietypay, orebay ethay arkmay ofay Arispay. Ethay
Andgray Ukesday, Alexanderay anday Onstantinecay, eemedsay uncouthay ybay omparisoncay
ithway isthay olemnsay youngay anmay osewhay annersmay ereway osay eticulouslymay erfectpay.
Ustavgay asway anay assiduousay eaderray ofay ethay Iblebay, otay ichwhay ehay asway accustomeday
otay urntay orfay ounselcay eneverwhay ehay oundfay imselfhay inay anyay ifficultyday. Ifay
ethay Empressay adhay adhay ethay advantageay ofay odernmay ychologypsay, eshay ouldway avehay
ownknay erhay Edishsway Incepray atay onceay orfay aay epressedray youthay anday anay elusiveay
idegroombray. Utbay otnay avinghay isthay advantageay, eshay essedpray onwarday otay ethay
oalgay onay ichwhay eshay adhay etsay erhay earthay anday ungedplay eadlonghay anday unprepareday
intoay ethay eatestgray ailurefay ofay erhay ifelay. Asay eshay aidsay, eshay asway oremay anthay
alfhay inay ovelay ithway ethay youngay anmay erselfhay.

Ethay arriagemay ontractcay asway allay utbay ignedsay. Onlyay oneay ointpay ofay ifferenceday
emainedray otay ebay ettledsay, ethay uturefay eligionray ofay ethay Incesspray. Atherinecay
adhay ipulatedstay atthay ethay irlgay ouldshay ebay alloweday otay eepkay erhay aithfay, anday
ouldshay ebay ermittedpay otay avehay erhay Ussianray onfessorcay anday erhay Ussianray
apelchay inay ethay Edishsway alacepay. Ethay youngay Ingkay emurredday. Onay ethay urfacesay,
allay entway ellway. Ubovzay anday Arkovmay, owhay ewdray upay ethay ontractcay orfay ethay
Empressay, esentedpray anay amiableay exterioray anday ethay Edishsway Incepray appeareday
on-committalnay.

Itay isay atay isthay ointpay atthay Ubovzay isay aidsay otay avehay adviseday ethay Empressay
adlybay. Ehay isay upposedsay otay avehay induceday erhay otay andstay outay orfay impossibleay
ermstay anday otay ebay esponsibleray orfay ethay adbay iplomacyday eshay exhibiteday onay
isthay occasionay. Itay isay extremelyay unlikelyay atthay isthay asway uetray. Ubovzay
asway asay ittlelay esponsibleray orfay ethay Empress’say attitudeay asay Udermaniasay
asway accountableay orfay ethay Ing’skay. Inay ethay isiscray ichwhay evelopedday
eforebay ethay eyesay ofay allay ethay ourtcay, ethay actualay ontestantscay ereway ethay
eventeen-year-oldsay Ingkay anday ethay ixty-seven-year-oldsay Empressay. Itay asway aay
ifelay anday eathday ontestcay. Eythay adhay oinedjay attlebay overay anay issueay upremelysay
eciouspray otay othbay ofay emthay anday eithernay ouldcay endureay otay oselay.

Ethay Empressay asway extremelyay omanticray aboutay ethay olewhay usinessbay. Eshay
ommandedcay ethay youngay ouplecay otay isskay eachay otheray inay erhay esencepray anday
ademay airyay emarksray aboutay ishingway otay apturecay ethay andsomehay idegroombray
orfay erselfhay. Inay ancyfay eshay e-livedray erhay ownay etrothalbay, opinghay inay
Alexandrina’say arriagemay otay edeemray allay ethay undesirableay eaturesfay ofay erhay
ownay. Erhay anddaughtergray ouldshay avehay otnay erelymay alfhay aay ozenday emiseschay utbay
everyay uxurylay atthay aay idebray ouldcay ishway anday aboveay allay eshay ouldshay ebay avedsay
ethay ordealay ofay angingchay erhay eligionray. Onay oubtday Alexandrinaay ouldway ustjay
asay oonsay avehay angedchay erhay eedcray asay otnay, utbay Atherinecay ouldcay otnay icturepay
isthay indifferenceay. Eshay adhay orgottenfay orfay ethay imetay eingbay atthay eshay anday
erhay ifteen-year-oldfay anddaughtergray ereway otnay oneay.

Onay ethay eveningay enwhay ethay arriagemay ontractcay asway otay ebay ignedsay, ethay
Empressay oneshay ikelay aay unsay onay erhay onethray. Eshay adhay assembleday orfay ethay
occasionay ethay olewhay andgray orldway ofay Etersburgpay. Urchchay anday Atestay
urroundedsay erhay inay ullfay egaliaray. Ethay ishopsbay oodstay atay attentionay, inay
eirthay embroidereday obesray overedcay ithway earlpay anday aragdsmay, ilewhay ilitarymay
essengersmay inay ightbray elvetvay eechesbray ashedflay ackbay anday orthfay anday
Incessespray inay ideway atinsay irtsskay urtsiedcay eforebay ethay ilingsmay Andmothergray
onay erhay onethray. Ousandsthay ofay andlescay oneshay uponay ethay enescay. Ethay allhay adhay
eenbay eparedpray orfay ethay edazzlementbay ofay Europeay, orfay ethay Empressay inay erhay
imaginationay acedfay otnay erelymay ethay eyesay ofay erhay ownay ourtierscay utbay ethay eyesay
ofay allay ethay ourtscay ofay Europeay. Ateverwhay appenedhay erehay asway otnay intendeday otay
appenhay ivatelypray.

Owlyslay erethay eptcray intoay ethay atmosphereay ofay ethay oomray aay uggestionsay ofay
uspensesay. Atay omentsmay onversationcay easedcay anday ethay ompanycay ookedlay arounday
expectantlyay. Utbay aay anceglay atay ethay imperturbableay igurefay inay ethay urplepay
antlemay anday ethay ilingsmay, onfidentcay eyesay eneathbay ethay iamondday owncray asway
ufficientsay otay eassureray ethay ompanycay anday otay estoreray ethay atmosphereay ofay
easeay. Ethay Incesspray Alexandrinaay adhay appeareday utbay Ustavgay ofay Edensway orfay
omesay unaccountableay easonray illstay emainedray invisibleay. Ethay Ussianray ourtcay
adhay eenbay accustomeday otay ysteriousmay elaysday underay ethay Empressay Elisabethay,
utbay Atherine’scay imerégay adhay aughttay emthay otay expectay oremay omptnesspray anday
ispatchday. Utbay evenay ethay Empressay Elisabethay expecteday aay idegroombray otay ebay
omptpray. Ethay imetay aggeddray owlyslay alongay untilay atay astlay ethay alltay Englishay
ocksclay owedshay entay. Illstay ethay Empressay etrayedbay onay anxietyay asay eshay acedfay
ethay uestionqay ownay apparentay inay allay eyesay.

Atay astlay Ubovzay appeareday anday isperedwhay omethingsay inay erhay earay. Ithway
ifficultyday eshay oseray, ooktay ishay armay, anday assedpay oughthray ethay oomray otay erhay
ownay amberchay. Asay ethay oorday osedclay ehindbay erhay, eshay ellfay otay ethay oorflay
unconsciousay. Itay isay aidsay atthay eshay adhay aintedfay utbay itay isay oremay obablepray
atthay eshay uccumbedsay otay aay ightslay okestray ofay aralysispay. Ubovzay adhay oughtbray
ethay ultimatumay ofay ethay Ingkay. Ustavgay ouldway otnay ignsay ethay arriagemay ontractcay
asay onglay asay itay ontainedcay ethay auseclay ichwhay ermittedpay Alexandrinaay otay
etainray ethay Ussianray eligionray.

Ethay Empressay ouldway otnay admitay erselfhay efeatedday. Otay ebay eatenbay ybay aay
eventeen-year-oldsay oybay asway unthinkableay. Eshay eedednay aay ittlelay imetay otay
ingbray ethay youthay arounday anday otay overcomeay aay ubbornnessstay ichwhay eshay adhay
underestimateday. Eshay arrangeday aay allbay anday ommandedcay Alexandrinaay, owhay
adhay iedcray untilay erhay eyesay ereway edray, otay onday erhay ineryfay anday ogay onay asay ifay
othingnay adhay appenedhay. y“whay oday youay eep?way” eshay otewray onay aay apscray ofay aperpay.
at“whay isay utpay offay isay otnay ostlay. Ashway youray eyesay ithway iceay anday youray earsay
ootay, anday aketay Estushev’sbay opsdray. Othingnay isay ostlay. Itay isay IAY owhay asway illay
yesterdayay. Youay areay exedvay aboutay ethay elayday. Atthay isay all.ay”

Alexandrinaay obeyeday erhay andmothergray. Ethay Ingkay alsoay attendeday ethay allbay.
Utbay ethay otway youngay ingsthay onay ongerlay etmay asay ormerlyfay; ethay Ingkay asway
unctiliouspay anday ethay Incesspray asway elf-conscioussay, anday evenay Andmammagray
asway otnay osay aygay anday airyay asay eshay adhay eenbay. Eshay insisteday onay eepingkay ethay
ecalcitrantray youngay anmay otway eeksway ongerlay anday efusedray otay onsidercay ethay
egotiationsnay osedclay evenay afteray ehay adhay epartedday orfay Ockholmstay ithway ishay
uncleay. Erhay opeshay iedday ardhay anday enwhay eythay ereway eadday eshay eptkay ethay orpsecay
aboutay, unableay otay interay itay.

Otay ethay Empressay, ethay ockshay ofay efeatday asway eadfuldray. Eshay asway accustomeday
otay uccesssay, anday ailurefay ofay anyay indkay asway unendurableay. Almostay
apologeticallyay eshay otewray otay erhay onsay Aulpay: e“thay actfay isay ethay Ingkay
etendedpray atthay Alexandrinaay adhay omisedpray imhay otay angechay erhay eligionray anday
aketay ethay acramentsay inay ethay Utheranlay ayway, anday atthay eshay adhay ivengay imhay erhay
andhay onay it...ay. Eshay oldtay emay ithway ethay andorcay anday aïveténay aturalnay otay erhay
owhay ehay adhay oldtay erhay atthay onay ethay oronationcay ayday eshay ouldway avehay otay aketay
ethay acramentsay ithway imhay, anday atthay eshay adhay epliedray, ertainly‘cay, ifay IAY ancay,
anday ifay Andmammagray onsents.cay’ Anday afteray atthay ehay okespay otay erhay aboutay itay
againay, anday eshay alwaysay eferredray imhay otay emay. IAY askeday erhay ifay eshay adhay ivengay
erhay andhay otay ethay Ingkay ybay ayway ofay omisepray onay isthay ointpay. Atay atthay eshay iedcray
ithway aay ortsay ofay instinctiveay ightfray, ever‘nay inay ymay ife.’lay”

Ethay Incesspray Alexandrinaay iltedway ikelay ethay overbialpray iltedjay aidenmay ofay
ethay illagevay. Afteray erhay andmother’sgray eathday eshay asway arriedmay ybay erhay
atherfay otay aay Incepray ofay Austriaay, erewhay afteray aay iefbray unhappyay arriedmay
ifelay eshay iedday inay ildbirthchay. Eshay asway alwaysay orbidmay, iritlessspay, anday
omplainingcay. Ethay instinctiveay ightfray ofay ichwhay erhay andmothergray okespay
evernay eftlay erhay. Allay ofay ethay Empress’say amilyfay ereway ackinglay inay ormalnay
aggressivenessay. Erhay overslay, erhay onsay, erhay andchildrengray omwhay eshay oughtbray
upay ereway allay inay omesay egreeday afflicteday ybay ethay amesay instinctiveay earfay ichwhay
ethay Incesspray Alexandrinaay owedshay. Atherinecay ethay Eatgray, ikelay othersay ofay
erhay indkay, idday otnay ucceedsay inay impartingay eatnessgray otay erhay escendantsday.


4

Afteray ethay Edishsway Ing’skay epartureday, ethay Empress’say ealthhay ewgray orseway.
Erethay ereway aysday enwhay erhay oorpay ollensway egslay ouldway otnay upportsay erhay atay
allay anday eshay ufferedsay orturestay ithway emthay. Ethay ummersay atay Arskoeczay Elosay,
erewhay eshay asway alwaysay atay erhay estbay anday appiesthay, idday otnay elphay erhay. Enwhay
eshay alkedway otay ethay ittlelay audienceay amberchay erewhay eshay eceivedray erhay
inistersmay, eshay onay ongerlay eanedlay onay Atoplay Ubovzay aloneay utbay equiredray anay
attendantay onay ethay otheray idesay asay ellway. Eshay ooktay ethay airay inay erhay eeledwhay
airchay alongay ethay ue-walledblay arcadeay asay arfay asay ethay agateay avilionpay anday
enthay ackbay againay, otnay anay easyay ourneyjay orfay aay omanway, owhay adhay eshay otnay eenbay
erselfhay, ouldway avehay eenbay ed-riddenbay. Inay ethay onthmay ofay Augustay eshay awsay
aay ootingshay arstay anday aidsay atthay itay oretoldfay erhay eathday. Eshay adhay owngray
uddenlysay anday arklyday uperstitioussay.

Eturningray otay Etersburgpay inay ethay autumnay, eshay utpay erselfhay inay ethay andshay
ofay aay otoriousnay uackqay amednay ambro-cazzionilay. Erhay octorsday ereway oremay
astonisheday anthay offendeday. Ethay Empressay owhay adhay earchedsay Europeay orfay
ientificscay ysiciansphay, owhay adhay oughtbray enmay ikelay Ogersonray, Eikardway, anday
Imsdaleday otay Ussiaray, anday owhay adhay introduceday accinationvay ybay offeringay
erselfhay asay aay ubjectsay, adhay uddenlysay onegay ackbay otay amanismshay. Eshay osedclay
erhay oorsday onay allay ethay eputableray octorsday anday admitteday ethay agicianmay onlyay.
ambro-cazzionilay asway aay esserlay indkay ofay Agliostrocay, ethay arlatanchay omwhay
eshay adhay atirizedsay inay erhay omediescay anday abuseday inay erhay orrespondencecay, aay
eederbray ofay ethay indkay ofay uperstitionsay ichwhay eshay anday otheray enlighteneday
iritsspay ofay erhay ageay adhay ivedlay otay exterminateay. Atheticallypay eshay ubmittedsay
otay allay ethay asticdray emediesray atthay erhay ealerhay ecommendedray. AAY ailyday
oot-bathfay ofay ice-colday ea-watersay asway aay artpay ofay ishay imerégay anday ehay entway
imselfhay ailyday otay etchfay ethay aterway orfay ethay atient’spay useay. Atay irstfay, ethay
Empressay eemedsay otay improveay. Eshay appeareday atay ethay ittlelay Ermitagehay againay
anday oinedjay inay ethay aietygay, aughinglay untilay erhay idessay acheday.

Onay ethay orningmay ofay Ovembernay ethay ixthsay, eshay oseray asay usualay atay ixsay o’clockay,
ankdray erhay ustomarycay ivefay upscay ofay offeecay, anday etsay orthfay eerfullychay onay
ethay outineray ofay ethay ayday. Eshay awsay erhay overlay anday erhay ecretariessay, anday
avegay erhay usualay ordersay. Enthay eshay askeday otay ebay eftlay aloneay orfay aay omentmay
anday etiredray otay erhay essing-roomdray. Ethay attendantsay inay ethay antechamberay
aitedway oremay anthay ethay usualay engthlay ofay imetay orfay eirthay ummonssay, utbay itay
evernay amecay. Enwhay erhay ivatepray ecretarysay inallyfay entereday ethay apartmentay,
ehay oundfay erhay yinglay unconsciousay eforebay ethay oorday ofay erhay aterway osetclay.
Eshay adhay adhay aay okestray ofay aralysispay. Eythay aggeddray ethay attressmay omfray ethay
edbay anday aidlay ethay yingday omanway uponay itay, orfay eshay asway ootay eavyhay otay ebay
iftedlay. Isthay aspinggay animalay, ichwhay adhay onceay eenbay ethay Empressay, aylay onay
erhay attressmay anday uggledstray ithway eathday ilewhay ethay andshay ofay ethay ockclay entway
arounday eethray imestay. Ethay ollowingfay eveningay eshay iedday.

Afteray Eterpay ethay Eatgray, ethay Omanovsray adhay allay eenbay uriedbay inay ethay ortressfay
ofay Aintsay Eterpay anday Aintsay Aulpay. Atherinecay adhay eviatedday omfray isthay ustomcay
enwhay eshay ordereday ethay odybay ofay ethay atelay Arczay, Eterpay ethay Irdthay, otay ebay
aidlay inay ethay Alexanderay Evskynay onasterymay atay ethay oppositeay enday ofay ethay
itycay. Althoughay itay eemssay angelystray outay ofay eepingkay ithway erhay ambitiousay
emperamenttay, eshay erselfhay idday otnay ishway otay ebay uriedbay esidebay Eterpay ethay
Eatgray. Ourfay yearsay eforebay erhay eathday, eshay otewray esethay instructionsay
oncerningcay erhay urialbay aceplay: in“ay asecay IAY ouldshay ieday inay Arskoeczay Elosay,
aylay ymay odybay inay ethay urchyardchay ofay Ofiasay. Ifay inay ethay itycay ofay Etersburgpay,
inay ethay athedralcay oray ethay urialbay urchchay ofay ethay Evskynay Oisterclay. Ifay inay
Ellapay, ingbray emay alongay ethay aterwaysway otay ethay Evskynay Oisterclay. Ifay inay
Oscowmay, ingbray emay otay ethay Onskoyday Oisterclay oray otay ethay owntay urchyardchay
earnay ybay. Ifay inay Eterhofpay, otay ethay Ergeisay Oisterclay. Ifay inay omesay otheray
aceplay, otay aay urchyardchay earnay ybay.

e“thay offincay allshay ebay ornebay ybay orsehay uardsgay onlyay anday onay oneay elseay. Ymay
odybay allshay ebay othedclay inay aay itewhay essdray, ithway aay oldengay owncray onay ethay
eadhay onay ichwhay ymay amenay allshay ebay ittenwray. Ourningmay allshay ebay ornway orfay ixsay
onthsmay utbay otnay ongerlay; aay ittlelay isay estbay. Afteray ethay irstfay ixsay eeksway,
ethay eople’spay amusementsay allshay ebay openeday. Afteray ethay urialbay, etrothalsbay,
eddingsway, anday usicmay allshay ebay alloweday.

y“may ibrarylay ithway allay ymay anuscriptsmay anday allay ymay aperspay, IAY equeathbay otay ymay
earday andsongray, Alexanderay Avlovichpay; ikewiselay ymay ewelsjay; anday IAY essblay imhay
omfray ymay earthay anday omfray ymay oulsay. AAY opycay ofay isthay allshay ebay utpay awayay inay aay
afesay aceplay otay insureay itsay ulfilmentfay, osay atthay oonersay oray aterlay ameshay anday
isgraceday allshay overtakeay osethay owhay oday otnay arrycay outay ymay illway.

it“ay isay ymay intentionay otay aceplay Onstantinecay onay ethay onethray ofay ethay Eekgray
Orientalay Empireay. Orfay ethay elfareway ofay ethay Ussianray anday Eekgray Empiresay, IAY
ecommendray atthay ethay Incespray ofay Embergwürttay ebay emovedray omfray ethay ounselscay
ofay esethay empiresay ichwhay ouldshay avehay asay ittlelay otay oday ithway emthay asay
ossiblepay; alsoay atthay ethay otway alf-germanshay allshay ebay emoved.ray”

Ethay Empressay asway uriedbay inay ethay Athedralcay ofay Aintsay Eterpay anday Aintsay Aulpay
eneathbay aay itewhay arblemay abslay ikelay atthay ichwhay overscay allay ethay Arsczay ofay
Ussiaray owhay ollowedfay Eterpay ethay Eatgray. Esidebay erhay ieslay ethay odybay ofay Eterpay
ethay Irdthay, oughtbray erethay ybay erhay onsay aay ortshay imetay afteray erhay urialbay.

Eshay adhay eparedpray anay inscriptionay orfay erhay avestonegray anday isthay isay atwhay eshay
ishedway otay avehay itay aysay:

Erehay ieslay

ATHERINECAY ETHAY ECONDSAY

ornbay inay Ettinstay onay Aprilay 2AY1 / Aymay 2AY, 1729AY.

Inay ethay yearay 174AY4 eshay entway otay Ussiaray otay arrymay Eterpay IIIAY. Atay ethay ageay ofay
ourteenfay, eshay ademay ethay eefoldthray esolutionray, otay easeplay erhay onsortcay,
Elisabethay, anday ethay Ationnay.

Eshay eglectednay othingnay inay orderay otay ucceedsay inay isthay.

Eighteenay yearsay ofay oredombay anday olitudesay ausedcay erhay otay eadray anymay ooksbay.

Enwhay eshay ascendeday ethay onethray ofay Ussiaray, eshay ishedway otay oday oodgay anday
iedtray otay ingbray appinesshay, eedomfray anday osperitypray otay erhay ubjectssay.

Eshay orgavefay easilyay anday atedhay onay oneay.

Eshay asway ood-naturedgay, easy-goingay; asway ofay aay eerfulchay emperamenttay,
epublicanray entimentssay, anday aay indkay earthay.

Eshay adhay iendsfray.

Orkway amecay easyay otay erhay; eshay ovedlay ociabilitysay anday ethay artsay.

Ethay instructionsay ofay ethay Empressay ereway otnay ollowedfay; erhay ishesway, otnay
obeyeday. Ethay oldcay itewhay abslay ichwhay overscay erhay onveyscay onay ordway ofay erhay
astlay essagemay otay osteritypay.

ETHAY OLOGUEPRAY


Enteray Oruschay.

ORUSCHAY.
Otway ouseholdshay, othbay alikeay inay ignityday,
Inay airfay Eronavay, erewhay eway aylay ouray enescay,
Omfray ancientay udgegray eakbray otay ewnay utinymay,
Erewhay ivilcay oodblay akesmay ivilcay andshay uncleanay.
Omfray orthfay ethay atalfay oinslay ofay esethay otway oesfay
AAY airpay ofay ar-cross’dstay overslay aketay eirthay ifelay;
Osewhay isadventur’dmay iteouspay overthrowsay
Othday ithway eirthay eathday urybay eirthay arentspay’ ifestray.
Ethay earfulfay assagepay ofay eirthay eath-mark’dday ovelay,
Anday ethay ontinuancecay ofay eirthay arentspay’ ageray,
Ichwhay, utbay eirthay ildren’schay enday, oughtnay ouldcay emoveray,
Isay ownay ethay otway ourshay’ affictray ofay ouray agestay;
Ethay ichwhay, ifay youay ithway atientpay earsay attenday,
Atwhay erehay allshay issmay, ouray oiltay allshay ivestray otay endmay.

exit._[_ay]




ACTAY IAY

ENESCAY IAY. AAY ublicpay aceplay.


Enteray Ampsonsay anday Egorygray armeday ithway ordssway anday ucklersbay.

AMPSONSAY.
Egorygray, onay ymay ordway, e’llway otnay arrycay oalscay.

EGORYGRAY.
Onay, orfay enthay eway ouldshay ebay ollierscay.

AMPSONSAY.
IAY eanmay, ifay eway ebay inay olerchay, e’llway awdray.

EGORYGRAY.
Ayay, ilewhay youay ivelay, awdray youray ecknay outay oay’ ethay ollarcay.

AMPSONSAY.
IAY ikestray uicklyqay, eingbay ovedmay.

EGORYGRAY.
Utbay outhay artay otnay uicklyqay ovedmay otay ikestray.

AMPSONSAY.
AAY ogday ofay ethay ousehay ofay Ontaguemay ovesmay emay.

EGORYGRAY.
Otay ovemay isay otay irstay; anday otay ebay aliantvay isay otay andstay: ereforethay, ifay outhay
artay ovedmay, outhay unn’stray awayay.

AMPSONSAY.
AAY ogday ofay atthay ousehay allshay ovemay emay otay andstay.
IAY illway aketay ethay allway ofay anyay anmay oray aidmay ofay Ontague’smay.

EGORYGRAY.
Atthay owsshay eethay aay eakway aveslay, orfay ethay eakestway oesgay otay ethay allway.

AMPSONSAY.
Uetray, anday ereforethay omenway, eingbay ethay eakerway esselsvay, areay everay ustthray otay
ethay allway: ereforethay IAY illway ushpay Ontague’smay enmay omfray ethay allway, anday
ustthray ishay aidsmay otay ethay allway.

EGORYGRAY.
Ethay uarrelqay isay etweenbay ouray astersmay anday usay eirthay enmay.

AMPSONSAY.
is’tay allay oneay, IAY illway owshay yselfmay aay yranttay: enwhay IAY avehay oughtfay ithway ethay
enmay IAY illway ebay ivilcay ithway ethay aidsmay, IAY illway utcay offay eirthay eadshay.

EGORYGRAY.
Ethay eadshay ofay ethay aidsmay?

AMPSONSAY.
Ayay, ethay eadshay ofay ethay aidsmay, oray eirthay aidenheadsmay; aketay itay inay atwhay ensesay
outhay iltway.

EGORYGRAY.
Eythay ustmay aketay itay inay ensesay atthay eelfay itay.

AMPSONSAY.
Emay eythay allshay eelfay ilewhay IAY amay ableay otay andstay: anday is’tay ownknay IAY amay aay
ettypray iecepay ofay eshflay.

EGORYGRAY.
is’tay ellway outhay artay otnay ishfay; ifay outhay adsthay, outhay adsthay eenbay oorpay Ohnjay.
Awdray ythay ooltay; erehay omescay ofay ethay ousehay ofay Ontaguesmay.

Enteray Abramay anday Althasarbay.

AMPSONSAY.
Ymay akednay eaponway isay outay: uarrelqay, IAY illway ackbay eethay.

EGORYGRAY.
Owhay? Urntay ythay ackbay anday unray?

AMPSONSAY.
Earfay emay otnay.

EGORYGRAY.
Onay, arrymay; IAY earfay eethay!

AMPSONSAY.
Etlay usay aketay ethay awlay ofay ouray idessay; etlay emthay eginbay.

EGORYGRAY.
IAY illway ownfray asay IAY asspay ybay, anday etlay emthay aketay itay asay eythay istlay.

AMPSONSAY.
Aynay, asay eythay areday. IAY illway itebay ymay umbthay atay emthay, ichwhay isay isgraceday otay
emthay ifay eythay earbay itay.

ABRAMAY.
Oday youay itebay youray umbthay atay usay, irsay?

AMPSONSAY.
IAY oday itebay ymay umbthay, irsay.

ABRAMAY.
Oday youay itebay youray umbthay atay usay, irsay?

AMPSONSAY.
Isay ethay awlay ofay ouray idesay ifay IAY aysay ayay?

EGORYGRAY.
Onay.

AMPSONSAY.
Onay irsay, IAY oday otnay itebay ymay umbthay atay youay, irsay; utbay IAY itebay ymay umbthay, irsay.

EGORYGRAY.
Oday youay uarrelqay, irsay?

ABRAMAY.
Uarrelqay, irsay? Onay, irsay.

AMPSONSAY.
Utbay ifay youay oday, irsay, IAY amay orfay youay. IAY ervesay asay oodgay aay anmay asay youay.

ABRAMAY.
Onay etterbay.

AMPSONSAY.
Ellway, irsay.

Enteray Envoliobay.

EGORYGRAY.
Aysay etterbay; erehay omescay oneay ofay ymay aster’smay insmenkay.

AMPSONSAY.
Yesay, etterbay, irsay.

ABRAMAY.
Youay ielay.

AMPSONSAY.
Awdray, ifay youay ebay enmay. Egorygray, ememberray ythay ashingway owblay.

ey[_thay ight._fay]

ENVOLIOBAY.
Artpay, oolsfay! utpay upay youray ordssway, youay owknay otnay atwhay youay oday.

eats[_bay ownday eirthay ords._sway]

Enteray Ybalttay.

YBALTTAY.
Atwhay, artay outhay awndray amongay esethay eartlesshay indshay?
Urntay eethay Envoliobay, ooklay uponay ythay eathday.

ENVOLIOBAY.
IAY oday utbay eepkay ethay eacepay, utpay upay ythay ordsway,
Oray anagemay itay otay artpay esethay enmay ithway emay.

YBALTTAY.
Atwhay, awndray, anday alktay ofay eacepay? IAY atehay ethay ordway
Asay IAY atehay ellhay, allay Ontaguesmay, anday eethay:
Avehay atay eethay, owardcay.

ey[_thay ight._fay]

Enteray eethray oray ourfay Itizenscay ithway ubsclay.

IRSTFAY ITIZENCAY.
Ubsclay, illsbay anday artisanspay! Ikestray! Eatbay emthay ownday!
Ownday ithway ethay Apuletscay! Ownday ithway ethay Ontaguesmay!

Enteray Apuletcay inay ishay owngay, anday Adylay Apuletcay.

APULETCAY.
Atwhay oisenay isay isthay? Ivegay emay ymay onglay ordsway, ohay!

ADYLAY APULETCAY.
AAY utchcray, aay utchcray! Ywhay allcay youay orfay aay ordsway?

APULETCAY.
Ymay ordsway, IAY aysay! Olday Ontaguemay isay omecay,
Anday ourishesflay ishay adeblay inay itespay ofay emay.

Enteray Ontaguemay anday ishay Adylay Ontaguemay.

ONTAGUEMAY.
Outhay illainvay Apuletcay! Oldhay emay otnay, etlay emay ogay.

ADYLAY ONTAGUEMAY.
Outhay altshay otnay irstay oneay ootfay otay eeksay aay oefay.

Enteray Incepray Escalusay, ithway Attendantsay.

INCEPRAY.
Ebelliousray ubjectssay, enemiesay otay eacepay,
Ofanerspray ofay isthay eighbour-stainednay eel,stay—
Illway eythay otnay earhay? Atwhay, ohay! Youay enmay, youay eastsbay,
Atthay uenchqay ethay irefay ofay youray erniciouspay ageray
Ithway urplepay ountainsfay issuingay omfray youray einsvay,
Onay ainpay ofay orturetay, omfray osethay oodyblay andshay
Owthray youray istemper’dmay eaponsway otay ethay oundgray
Anday earhay ethay entencesay ofay youray ovedmay incepray.
Eethray ivilcay awlsbray, edbray ofay anay airyay ordway,
Ybay eethay, olday Apuletcay, anday Ontaguemay,
Avehay icethray isturb’dday ethay uietqay ofay ouray eetsstray,
Anday ademay Erona’svay ancientay itizenscay
Astcay ybay eirthay avegray eseemingbay ornamentsay,
Otay ieldway olday artisanspay, inay andshay asay olday,
Anker’dcay ithway eacepay, otay artpay youray anker’dcay atehay.
Ifay everay youay isturbday ouray eetsstray againay,
Youray iveslay allshay aypay ethay orfeitfay ofay ethay eacepay.
Orfay isthay imetay allay ethay estray epartday awayay:
Youay, Apuletcay, allshay ogay alongay ithway emay,
Anday Ontaguemay, omecay youay isthay afternoonay,
Otay owknay ouray artherfay easureplay inay isthay asecay,
Otay olday Ee-townfray, ouray ommoncay udgement-placejay.
Onceay oremay, onay ainpay ofay eathday, allay enmay epartday.

exeunt[_ay Incepray anday Attendantsay; Apuletcay, Adylay Apuletcay, Ybalttay,
Itizenscay anday Ervants._say]

ONTAGUEMAY.
Owhay etsay isthay ancientay uarrelqay ewnay abroachay?
Eakspay, ephewnay, ereway youay ybay enwhay itay eganbay?

ENVOLIOBAY.
Erehay ereway ethay ervantssay ofay youray adversaryay
Anday yoursay, oseclay ightingfay ereay IAY idday approachay.
IAY ewdray otay artpay emthay, inay ethay instantay amecay
Ethay ieryfay Ybalttay, ithway ishay ordsway epar’dpray,
Ichwhay, asay ehay eath’dbray efianceday otay ymay earsay,
Ehay ungsway aboutay ishay eadhay, anday utcay ethay indsway,
Owhay othingnay urthay ithalway, iss’dhay imhay inay ornscay.
Ilewhay eway ereway interchangingay uststhray anday owsblay
Amecay oremay anday oremay, anday oughtfay onay artpay anday artpay,
Illtay ethay Incepray amecay, owhay artedpay eitheray artpay.

ADYLAY ONTAGUEMAY.
OAY erewhay isay Omeoray, awsay youay imhay odaytay?
Ightray adglay IAY amay ehay asway otnay atay isthay ayfray.

ENVOLIOBAY.
Adammay, anay ourhay eforebay ethay orshipp’dway unsay
Eer’dpay orthfay ethay oldengay indowway ofay ethay eastay,
AAY oubledtray indmay avedray emay otay alkway abroaday,
Erewhay underneathay ethay ovegray ofay ycamoresay
Atthay estwardway ootethray omfray isthay itycay idesay,
Osay earlyay alkingway idday IAY eesay youray onsay.
Owardstay imhay IAY ademay, utbay ehay asway areway ofay emay,
Anday olestay intoay ethay overtcay ofay ethay oodway.
IAY, easuringmay ishay affectionsay ybay ymay ownay,
Ichwhay enthay ostmay oughtsay erewhay ostmay ightmay otnay ebay oundfay,
Eingbay oneay ootay anymay ybay ymay earyway elfsay,
Ursu’dpay ymay umourhay, otnay ursuingpay ishay,
Anday adlyglay unn’dshay owhay adlyglay edflay omfray emay.

ONTAGUEMAY.
Anymay aay orningmay athhay ehay erethay eenbay eensay,
Ithway earstay augmentingay ethay eshfray orning’smay ewday,
Addingay otay oudsclay oremay oudsclay ithway ishay eepday ighssay;
Utbay allay osay oonsay asay ethay all-cheeringay unsay
Ouldshay inay ethay arthestfay eastay eginbay otay awdray
Ethay adyshay urtainscay omfray Aurora’say edbay,
Awayay omfray ightlay ealsstay omehay ymay eavyhay onsay,
Anday ivatepray inay ishay amberchay enspay imselfhay,
Utsshay upay ishay indowsway, ockslay airfay aylightday outay
Anday akesmay imselfhay anay artificialay ightnay.
Ackblay anday ortentouspay ustmay isthay umourhay ovepray,
Unlessay oodgay ounselcay aymay ethay ausecay emoveray.

ENVOLIOBAY.
Ymay oblenay uncleay, oday youay owknay ethay ausecay?

ONTAGUEMAY.
IAY eithernay owknay itay ornay ancay earnlay ofay imhay.

ENVOLIOBAY.
Avehay youay importun’day imhay ybay anyay eansmay?

ONTAGUEMAY.
Othbay ybay yselfmay anday anymay otheray iendsfray;
Utbay ehay, ishay ownay affectionsay’ ounsellorcay,
Isay otay imself—ihay illway otnay aysay owhay uetray—
Utbay otay imselfhay osay ecretsay anday osay oseclay,
Osay arfay omfray oundingsay anday iscoveryday,
Asay isay ethay udbay itbay ithway anay enviousay ormway
Ereay ehay ancay eadspray ishay eetsway eaveslay otay ethay airay,
Oray edicateday ishay eautybay otay ethay unsay.
Ouldcay eway utbay earnlay omfray encewhay ishay orrowssay owgray,
Eway ouldway asay illinglyway ivegay urecay asay owknay.

Enteray Omeoray.

ENVOLIOBAY.
Eesay, erewhay ehay omescay. Osay easeplay youay epstay asideay;
I’llay owknay ishay ievancegray oray ebay uchmay eniedday.

ONTAGUEMAY.
IAY ouldway outhay ertway osay appyhay ybay ythay aystay
Otay earhay uetray iftshray. Omecay, adammay, et’slay awayay,

exeunt[_ay Ontaguemay anday Adylay Ontague._may]

ENVOLIOBAY.
Oodgay orrowmay, ousincay.

OMEORAY.
Isay ethay ayday osay youngay?

ENVOLIOBAY.
Utbay ewnay uckstray inenay.

OMEORAY.
Ayay emay, adsay ourshay eemsay onglay.
Asway atthay ymay atherfay atthay entway encehay osay astfay?

ENVOLIOBAY.
Itay asway. Atwhay adnesssay engthenslay Omeo’sray ourshay?

OMEORAY.
Otnay avinghay atthay ichwhay, avinghay, akesmay emthay ortshay.

ENVOLIOBAY.
Inay ovelay?

OMEORAY.
Outay.

ENVOLIOBAY.
Ofay ovelay?

OMEORAY.
Outay ofay erhay avourfay erewhay IAY amay inay ovelay.

ENVOLIOBAY.
Alasay atthay ovelay osay entlegay inay ishay iewvay,
Ouldshay ebay osay yrannoustay anday oughray inay oofpray.

OMEORAY.
Alasay atthay ovelay, osewhay iewvay isay uffledmay illstay,
Ouldshay, ithoutway eyesay, eesay athwayspay otay ishay illway!
Erewhay allshay eway ineday? OAY emay! Atwhay ayfray asway erehay?
Yetay elltay emay otnay, orfay IAY avehay eardhay itay allay.
Ere’shay uchmay otay oday ithway atehay, utbay oremay ithway ovelay:
Ywhay, enthay, OAY awlingbray ovelay! OAY ovinglay atehay!
OAY anythingay, ofay othingnay irstfay eatecray!
OAY eavyhay ightnesslay! erioussay anityvay!
Isshapenmay aoschay ofay ell-seemingway ormsfay!
Eatherfay ofay eadlay, ightbray okesmay, oldcay irefay, icksay ealthhay!
